Svacchandatantra [or Svacchandabhairavatantra]
kailāsaśikharāsīnaṃ bhairavaṃ vigatāmayam 
caṇḍanandimahākālagaṇeśavṛṣabhṛṅgibhiḥ ।। 

kumārendrayamādityabrahmaviṣṇupuraḥsaraiḥ 
stūyamānaṃ maheśānaṃ gaṇamātṛniṣevitam ।। 

sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāraṃ vilayasthitakārakam 
anugrahakaraṃ devaṃ praṇatārtivināśanam ।। 

muditaṃ bhairavaṃ dṛṣṭvā devī vacanamabravīt 
yattvayā kathitaṃ mahyaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvara ।। 

śatakoṭipravistīrṇaṃ bhedānantyavisarpitam 
catuṣpīṭhaṃ mahātantra catuṣṭayaphalodayam ।। 

na śaknuvanti manujā alpavīryaparākramāḥ 
alpāyuṣo alpavittāśca alpasattvāśca śaṃkara ।। 

tadarthaṃ saṃgrahaṃ tasya svalpaśāstrārthavistaram 
bhuktimuktipradātāraṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। 

kīdṛśaṃ vai guruṃ vidyāt sādhakaṃ ca maheśvara 
bhayābhayapradātāraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhūmiṃ ca kīdṛśīm ।। 

mantrāṃścaiva samāsena kālaṃ caiva samāsataḥ 
yajanaṃ havanaṃ caiva adhivāsaṃ rajāṃsi ca ।। 

pañcagavyaṃ caruṃ caiva dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca maṇḍalam 
dīkṣā cādhvābhiṣekau ca samayānsādhanāni ca ।। 

kalimāsādya sidhyanti tathā brūhi maheśvara 
sādhu sādhu mahābhāge yattvayā paricoditam ।। 

anugrahāya martyānāṃ sāmprataṃ kathayāmi te 
ādau tāvatparīkṣeta ācāryaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।। 

āryadeśasamutpannaṃ sarvāvayavabhūṣitam 
śivaśāstravidhānajñaṃ jñānajñeyaviśāradam ।। 

devakarmarataṃ śāntaṃ satyavādidṛḍhavratam 
sattvavadvīryasampannaṃ dayādākṣiṇyasaṃyutam ।। 

tyāginaṃ dambhanirmuktaṃ śivaśāstreṣu bhāvitam 
īdṛśaṃ tu guruṃ prāpya siddhimuktī na dūrataḥ ।। 

krodhanaścapalaḥ kṣudro dayādākṣiṇyavarjitaḥ 
kekaro danturaḥ kāṇaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ śāstravarjitaḥ ।। 

atidīrghastathā hrasvaḥ kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ kṣayānvitaḥ 
tārkiko dambhasaṃyuktaḥ satyaśaucavivarjitaḥ ।। 

anyaśāstrarato yastu nāsau muktiphalapradaḥ 
śiṣyo dayānvito dhīro dambhamāyāvivarjitaḥ ।। 

devāgnigurubhaktaśca śāstrabhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ 
guruśuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ suśāntendriyasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

īdṛśo vai bhavecchiṣyaḥ so atrānugrahabhājanam 
māyānvitaḥ śaṭhaḥ krūro niḥsatyaḥ kalahapriyaḥ ।। 

kāmī ca lobhasampannaḥ śivabhaktivivarjitaḥ 
dūṣako guruśāstrāṇāṃ dīkṣito api na muktibhāk ।। 

santāpaṃ krodhane vindyāc capale capalāḥ śriyaḥ 
mantrasiddhiṃ haret kṣudra ācāryastu varānane ।। 

dayāhīnena daurbhāgyam adakṣe dasyupīḍanam 
kekareṇa bhavedvyādhir danturaḥ kalikārakaḥ ।। 

kāṇo vidveṣajananaḥ khalvāṭaścārthanāśanaḥ 
śāstrahīne na siddhiḥ syād dīkṣādau vīravandite ।। 

dīrghe rājabhayaṃ jñeyaṃ hrasvaḥ putravināśanaḥ 
kṛśaḥ kṣayakaro jñeyaḥ sthūla utpātakārakaḥ ।। 

kṣayānvitena mṛtyuḥ syāt tārkike vadhabandhanam 
dāmbhikaḥ pāpajanako veditavyo varānane ।। 

mantāstasya na siddhyanti yaḥ satyādivivarjitaḥ 
sarve te na śubhā devi iha loke paratra ca ।। 

sitaraktapītakṛṣṇāṃ bhūmiṃ plavaviśodhitām 
viśalyāṃ lakṣaṇairyuktāṃ sarvakāmārthasādhikām ।। 

sugandhigandhasaṃyuktāṃ puṣpaprakaralālitām 
sudhūpāmodabahalāṃ vitānopariśobhitam ।। 

ācāryastu śucirbhūtvā candanāgurucarcitaḥ 
sudhūpitaḥ prasannātmā khaṭikākarasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ 
mātṛkāṃ prastarettatra ādikṣāntāmanukramāt ।। 

ādiḥ ṣoḍaśabhedena sākṣādvai bhairavaḥ smṛtaḥ 
kavargaścaṭavargau ca tapayāḥ śastathaiva ca ।। 

saṃhāreṇa samopetau yonirvai bhairavī smṛtā 
mātṛkābhairavaṃ devam avargeṇa prapūjayet ।। 

bhairavī kādinā pūjyā mātṛvargaiḥ prapūjayet 
avarge tu mahālakṣmīḥ kavarge kamalodbhavā ।। 

cavarge tu maheśānī ṭavarge tu kumārikā 
nārāyaṇī tavarge tu vārāhī tu pavargikā ।। 

aindrī caiva yavargasthā cāmuṇḍā tu śavargikā 
etāḥ sapta mahāmātṛḥ saptalokavyavasthitāḥ ।। 

sarvān kāmānavāpnoti devyevaṃ bhairavo abravīt 
ante asya uddharenmantrān yathākramaniyogataḥ ।। 

trayodaśaṃ binduyutam anantāsanamuttamam 
anena yojayetsarvaṃ somasūryāgnimadhyagam ।। 

brahmaviṣṇumaheśānaṃ śavāntaṃ parikalpayet 
mūrtiṃ haṃsākṣareṇaiva bindubhinnena kalpayet ।। 

ardhacandrakṛtāṭopāṃ svasvanāṃ tuhinaprabhām 
tadūrdhve sakalaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ parikalpayet ।। 

oṃkāramuccaretpūrvam aghorebhyo anantaram 
tha ghorebhyo samālikhya tato anyattu samālikhet ।। 

ghoraghoratarebhyaśca sarvataḥ śarva uccaret 
sarvebhyaḥ padamanyacca namaste rudra eva ca ।। 

rūpebhyaśca samālikhya namaskārāvasānakam 
mantrarājaḥ samākhyātaḥ aghoraḥ surapūjitaḥ ।। 

sakṛduccārito devi nāśayet sarvakilbiṣam 
janmakoṭīsahasraistu bhramadbhiḥ samupārjitam ।। 

smaraṇānnāśayeddevi tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā 
yakārādivakārāntāḥ saṃhāreṇa samāyutāḥ ।। 

bindumastakasambhinnā bhairavasya mukhāni ca 
brahmabhaṅgyā niyojyāni mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi ।। 

punaścordhvaṃ mukhaṃ kalpyaṃ prāgdakṣiṇamathottaram 
aparaṃ kalpayitvā tu kalābhedena vinyaset ।। 

pūrvaṃ ca dakṣiṇaṃ caiva uttaraṃ paścimaṃ tathā 
ūrdhvamūrdhnā tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣakāraṃ tvīśarūpiṇam ।। 

evaṃ vaktraṃ caturdhā tu vaktreṣveva niyojayet 
pañcamaṃ yadbhavedvaktraṃ kṣakāreṇaiva nirdiśet ।। 

hṛdi grīvāṃsapṛṣṭhe tu nābhau ca jaṭhare tathā 
pṛṣṭhe corasi vinyased aghoreṇa yathākramam ।। 

guhye tathā gude caiva tathorvorjānunorapi 
jaṅghayośca sphijoḥ kaṭyāṃ pārśvayorubhayorapi ।। 

vinyaseccaiva vāmena śarīre tu yathākramam 
pādau hastau tathā nāsāṃ śiraścaiva bhujāvatha ।। 

sadyena kalpayeddevi sarvametadyathākramam 
tāsāṃ nāmāni vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

tārā sutārā taraṇī tārayantī sutāraṇī 
īśānasya kalā pañca nirañjanapadānugā ।। 

nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntistathaiva ca 
puruṣasya kalā hyetāś catasraḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। 

tamā mohā kṣudhā nidrā mṛtyurmāyā bhayā jarā 
aghorasya kalā hyetā aṣṭau vai varavarṇini ।। 

rajā rakṣā ratiḥ pālyā kāmyā tṛṣṇā matiḥ kriyā 
ṛddhirmāyā ca rātriśca bhrāmiṇī mohanī tathā ।। 

manonmanī kalā hyetā vāmadeve trayodaśa 
siddhirṛddhirdyutirlakṣmīr medhā kāntiḥ sudhā sthitiḥ ।। 

sadyojātakalāstvevam aṣṭau samparikīrtitāḥ 
punaśca sādhako devi sarvāṅgeṣu yathākramam ।। 

navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca dhruveṇa parikalpayet 
vidyāṅgāni punarnyasya teṣāṃ mantrān śṛṇu priye ।। 

aghorebhyo samālikhya tha ghorebhyo dvitīyakam 
ghoraghoratarebhyaśca tṛtīyaṃ parikalpayet ।। 

sarvataḥ śarva sarvebhyo caturthaṃ parikalpayet 
namaste rudrarūpebhyaḥ pañcamaṃ ca vidhānataḥ ।। 

oṃkāramuccaretpūrvaṃ juṃ saśca tadanantaram 
netratrayaṃ prakalpeta vidyādehasya bhāmini ।। 

vidyāṅgāni vijānīyāt nāmāni ca nibodha me 
sarvātmā tu brahmaśiro jvālinī piṅgalaṃ tathā ।। 

durbhedyaṃ pāśupatyaṃ ca jyotīrūpaṃ tathaiva ca 
kriyā jñānaṃ tathaivecchā tāsāṃ mantrānnibodha me ।। 

caturthasvarasaṃyuktaṃ hāntaṃ binduvibhūṣitam 
kriyāśaktiḥ samākhyātā sarvasṛṣṭiprakāśikā ।। 

śakārasya tṛtīyaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhayuktaṃ sabindukam 
jñānaśaktiḥ smṛtā hyeṣā prabodhajananī śubhā ।। 

kṣādiṃ dvisvarasambhinnaṃ tripañcena tu mūrchitam 
icchāśaktiḥ samākhyātā bhairavasyāmitātmikā ।। 

haṃsākhyo bindusaṃyuktaḥ ṣaṣṭhasvaravibheditaḥ 
bālendunādaśaktyantaḥ svacchando niṣkalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

asyoccaraṇamātreṇa ye yuktāḥ sarvapātakaiḥ 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśāḥ padaṃ gacchantyanāmayam ।। 

sāntaṃ dīrghasvaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir bhinnajātivibheditam 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma locanāstraṃ prakalpayet ।। 

oṃkāro dīpanasteṣām ante jātiṃ prakalpayet 
namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ krameṇa tu ।। 

eṣa bhairavarājastu sarvakāmārthasādhakaḥ 
hara īma akāraśca ṅādirosvarasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

yānta ekārasaṃyuktaḥ ṣādirlāntavibheditaḥ 
lādistrisvarasambhinno haṃso bindusamāyuktaḥ ।। 

ṣaṣṭhasvarasamopetaḥ phaṭkārāntavikalpitaḥ 
aghoreśvarīti vikhyātā svacchandotsaṅgagāminī ।। 

bhairavāṅgasamopetā vaktrapañcakasaṃyutā 
hānto yādiryakārānto rādiḥ ṣaṣṭhakalānvitaḥ ।। 

bindunādasamāyogāt kapāleśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
sānto binduradho hyagniḥ ṣaṣṭhayuktastu kīrtitaḥ ।। 

śikhivāhanasaṃjñastu jñātavyo asau varānane 
saṃhāraḥ ṣaṣṭhasaṃyuktaḥ ṣaḍantena samanvitaḥ ।। 

krodharājaḥ samākhyātaḥ - - - - - - - - 
- - - - - - - tathānyaṃ kathayāmi te 
ñādiḥ ṣaṣṭhasvaropetas tripadena samāyutaḥ ।। 

bindumastakasambhinno vikarālo varānane 
sāntaḥ śādyena saṃyuktaḥ ṣaṣṭhasvarayuto apyadhaḥ ।। 

caturdaśasvarākrānto bindunādāntabhūṣitaḥ 
manmathaḥ kathito hyeṣa surasiddhanamaskṛtaḥ ।। 

yenedaṃ tu nijaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam 
hararādisamāyuktaḥ ūkārādhaḥ sabindukaḥ ।। 

meghanādeśvaro hyeṣa bhairavaḥ samprakīrtitaḥ 
kṣasāntarbindusaṃyuktaḥ pañcamena vibheditaḥ ।। 

someśvaraḥ samākhyāto janmamṛtyuvināśanaḥ 
kṣādiryāntasamopeto hāntenādhoniyojitaḥ ।। 

bhānto vādirlakārānto rādyo adho rudrayojitaḥ 
bindvardhendusamāyukto nādaśaktisamanvitaḥ ।। 

vidyārājaḥ samākhyāto mahāpātakanāśanaḥ 
bhairavāṣṭakametaddhi parivāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

lokapālāṃstathoddhṛtya svanāmapraṇavādikān 
namaskārāvamānāṃśca sāstrānsamparikalpayet ।। 

iti svacchandatantre mantroddhāraprakāśanaṃ nāma prathamaḥ paṭalaḥ

dvitīyaḥ paṭalaḥ

athārcanaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
śaucaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ snānaṃ kartavyaṃ tu mṛdambhasā ।। 

śucisthānānmṛdaṃ pūrvaṃ gṛhītvāstreṇa śodhitām 
prakṣālya jalatīraṃ tu sthāpayettāṃ varānane ।। 

bhāgadvayaṃ tato astreṇa kartavyaṃ tu kṛśodari 
bhāgārdhena kaṭiṃ corū jaṅghe pādau tathaiva ca ।। 

kṣālayeta yathānyāyaṃ trirantaritayogataḥ 
avaśiṣṭaṃ tu bhāgārdhaṃ gṛhītvāstrābhimantritam ।। 

saptavārānvarārohe arkadīptaṃ tu kārayet 
śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntam āguṣṭhya snānamācaret ।। 

uttīryodakamadhyāttu upaspṛśya yathākramam 
saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryāc chāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। 

malasnānaṃ bhavedevaṃ vidhisnānaṃ pracakṣmahe 
bhāgārdhaṃ yatsthitaṃ pūrvaṃ tato bhāgatrayaṃ kuru ।। 

vāmahastasya pūrve ca dakṣiṇe cottare kramāt 
pūrvabhāgaṃ tato astreṇa saptavārāṃstu mantrayet ।। 

dakṣiṇasthaṃ tathā vaktrair abhimantrya varānane 
uttaraṃ cābhimantryaivaṃ devenāṅgayutena ca ।। 

pūrvabhāgaṃ gṛhītvā tu daśadikṣu vinikṣipet 
uttareṇa tu bhāgena jalaṃ caivābhimantrayet ।। 

bāhumātrapramāṇena bhairaveśamanusmaran 
ātmānaṃ guṇṭhayitvā tu dakṣabhāgena suvrate ।। 

snāyādrājopacāreṇa sugandhāmalakādibhiḥ 
prāṇāyāmābhiṣekau tu kartavyau bhairaveṇa ca ।। 

uttīryodakamadhyāttu tadvāsaḥ parivartayet 
upaspṛśya kṛtanyāso mūlamantramanusmaran ।। 

tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya deveśi ātmano agre nidhāpayet 
tatrastho vandayetsaṃdhyāṃ mārjanādiranukramāt ।। 

aghamarṣaḥ prakartavya upasthānaṃ divākare 
japaṃ kṛtvā nivedyaivaṃ praṇamya ca varānane ।। 

mantrāṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā devānāmṛṣibhiḥ saha 
sarveṣāṃ bhūtasaṃghānāṃ tatastīrthaṃ tu saṃharet ।। 

mūlamantramanusmṛtya bhasmasnānamataḥ param 
malasnānaṃ prakartavyaṃ bhāvitenāntarātmanā ।। 

parivṛttya tato vāsaḥ saṃdhyāṃ prāgiva vandayet 
vidhisnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād bhairaveśamanusmaran ।। 

śiro vaktraṃ ca hṛdguhyaṃ pādāntaṃ ca vibhāgaśaḥ 
bhairaveṇāṅgayuktena samuddhūlyaṃ yathākramam ।। 

abhiṣekaṃ prakurvīta paraṃ tattvamanusmaran 
saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryād yathāpūrvaṃ varānane ।। 

tato yāgagṛhaṃ gatvā hastau pādau ca kṣālayet 
śikhāṃ baddhvā śikhāṃ smṛtvā upaspṛśya vidhānataḥ ।। 

sakalīkṛtadehastu puṣpamādāya suvrate 
diṅmātṛbhyo namaskṛtya dvāraṃ saṃprokṣya yatnataḥ ।। 

śivāmbhasāstramantreṇa vighnaproccāṭanaṃ bhavet 
dvāraśākhordhvato devaṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca śriyaṃ tathā ।। 

saṃpūjya gandhapuṣpādyair dhūpādibhiranukramāt 
arghyapādyopahāraiśca tato dvārasya cottare ।। 

nandigaṅge samabhyarcya mahākālaṃ ca dakṣiṇe 
kālindīṃ caiva saṃpūjya yathānukramayogataḥ ।। 

bhairavāstraṃ samuccārya puṣpaṃ saṃgṛhya bhāvitaḥ 
saptābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā jvaladagniśikhākulam ।। 

nārācāstraprayogeṇa praviśedgṛhamadhyataḥ 
nivāritaṃ tena sarvaṃ vighnajālamanantakam ।। 

tato rakṣārthamantraṃ ca daśadikṣu vinikṣipet 
madhye sampūjya brahmāṇaṃ gandhaiḥ puṣpairanukramāt ।। 

dakṣiṇāyāṃ tato mūrtau praṇavāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
upaviśyāsanaṃ baddhvā svabhyastaṃ vai puraḥsthitam ।। 

gandhadigdhau karau kṛtvā astreṇa pariśodhayet 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau plāvayedamṛtena tu ।। 

parāṃ śaktiṃ tu saṃkṣobhya tato anantaṃ prakalpayet 
mūrtiṃ nyasyānuvaktrāṇi svacchandaṃ parikalpayet ।। 

aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ vinyasedaṅgapañcakam 
bhairavānapi saṃkalpya paraṃ tattvamanusmaret ।। 

prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kāryaṃ dehasaṃśuddhikāraṇam 
aśuddhaḥ svamarudrecyaḥ śuddhenāpūrayettanum ।। 

kumbhakaṃ recakaṃ kṛtvā vyomnyātmānaṃ nidhāpayet 
khadyotakanibhaṃ sūkṣmaṃ karaṇaistu vivarjitam ।। 

kāryeṇaiva vihīnaṃ ca māyāpradhvastagocaram 
śivīkāryastathātmaiva yathā bhavati tacchṛṇu ।। 

paraṃ bhāvaṃ tu saṃgṛhya tataḥ śoṣyā tanuḥ priye 
saṃhāreṇa yabhinnena rudrabījayutena ca ।। 

tenaiva dahanaṃ kāryam ūrdhvādho agniyutena ca 
adho viṣṇusamāyukto vāyuvarṇaḥ sabindukaḥ ।। 

utpūyanakaro hyeṣa plāvane vāruṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
bindumastakasaṃbhinnaḥ śaktinyāsastato bhavet ।। 

ānayettaṃ yathānītaṃ plāvayedamṛtena tu 
malapradhvastacaitanyaṃ kalāvidyāsamāśritam ।। 

rāgeṇa rañjitātmāna kālena kalitaṃ tathā 
niyatyā yamitaṃ bhūyaḥ puṃbhāvenopabṛṃhitam ।। 

pradhānāśayasaṃpannaṃ guṇatrayasamanvitam 
buddhitattvasamāsīnam ahaṅkārasamāvṛtam ।। 

manasā buddhikarmākṣais tanmātraiḥ sthūlabhūtakaiḥ 
praṇavena tu sarvaṃ tac charīrotpattikāraṇam ।। 

nyasetkrameṇa deveśi triṃśadekaṃ ca saṃkhyayā 
ṣaṭtattvī tvātmasaṃbaddhā jñātavyātra varānane ।। 

pradhānāvaniparyantaṃ śarīraṃ ca vinirmitam 
caturviṃśatitattvāni caitanyarahitāni tu ।। 

draṣṭavyāni varārohe puruṣādhiṣṭhitāni tu 
sacetanāni sarvāṇi jñātavyāni sadaiva hi ।। 

pañcaviṃśakametacca prākṛtaṃ samudāhṛtam 
tato mūrtiṃ nyaseddevi mūlamantrasulakṣitam ।। 

sakalaṃ bhairavaṃ nyasya dvātriṃśārṇaṃ sulocane 
mukhāni kalpayetpaścān mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi ।। 

vaktrāṇi kalpayetpaścād ūrdhvaṃ pūrvaṃ ca dakṣiṇam 
uttaraṃ paścimaṃ caiva yathāvatpravibhāgaśaḥ ।। 

kalābhedaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ śodhyādhvānaṃ prakalpayet 
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca vidyāṅgā locanatrayam ।। 

vargātītena kṣurikām ūrdhvādho agnipradīpitām 
ṣoḍaśāntarhatā sā tu rakṣi"kā vighnanāśikā ।। 

navakaṃ kalpayetpūrvaṃ mūrdhni vaktre ca kaṇṭhake 
hṛdaye nābhideśe ca guhya ūrvośca jānutaḥ ।। 

pādāntaṃ caiva vinyasya svadhyānaguṇasaṃyutam 
kriyājñāne tathecchā ca dakṣe vāme ca madhyataḥ ।। 

vidyārājaḥ smṛto hyeṣa bhairavo mantranāyakaḥ 
niṣkalaṃ tu tathāvāhya aṅgānyevaṃ yathākramam ।। 

gandhairdhūpaistathā puṣpair vividhairbhakṣyabhojanaiḥ 
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ manasaiva prakalpitaiḥ ।। 

ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyātvā tato hṛdyāgamācaret 
nābhau kandaṃ samāropya nālaṃ tu dvādaśāṅgulam ।। 

hṛdantaṃ kalpayedyāvat tatra padmaṃ vicintayet 
aṣṭapatraṃ mahādīptaṃ kesarālaṃ sakarṇikam ।। 

kandaṃ śaktimayaṃ tatra nāle vai kaṇṭakāstu ye 
bhuvanāni ca tānyeva rudrāṇāṃ varavarṇini ।। 

māyātmako bhavedgranthir aśuddhādhvavyavasthitaḥ 
vidyāpadmaṃ mahādīptaṃ karṇikābījarājitam ।। 

puṣkarāṇi ca deveśi tatra vidyeśvarāḥ smṛtāḥ 
evaṃ dhyātvā mahāpadmaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ śubham ।। 

śaktinyāso bhavetpūrvaṃ kandaṃ tu tadanantaram 
aṅkuraṃ nālavinyāsam anantaṃ parikalpayet ।। 

tejomayaṃ mahāśubhraṃ sphuratkiraṇabhāsvaram 
dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca kramānnyaset ।। 

sitaraktapītakṛṣṇā āgneyyādīśadiggatāḥ 
pādakāḥ siṃharūpāste trinetrā bhīmavikramāḥ ।। 

śivaśaktimayā mantrā nyastavyā vīravindate 
adharmājñānāvairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca prāgdiśaḥ ।। 

uttarāntaṃ niveśyaṃ tu gātrakāḥ sitavarṇakāḥ 
saṃdhānakīlakāścaiva atasīpuṣpasaṃnibhāḥ ।। 

vedā yugāśca te caiva jñātavyāḥ kramaśaḥ priye 
adhaśchādanamūrdhvaṃ ca raktaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet ।। 

madhye tamo vijānīyād guṇāstvete vyavasthitāḥ 
sitaṃ padmaṃ vijānīyāt kesarāṇi vicintayet ।। 

sitaraktaprapītāni mūlamadhyāgradeśataḥ 
karṇikā hemasaṃkāśā bījāni haritāni tu ।। 

vāmāṃ pūrvadale nyasya jyeṣṭhāṃ vahnidalāśritām 
raudrīṃ dakṣiṇapatre tu kālīṃ nairṛtagocare ।। 

kalavikaraṇīṃ devīṃ vinyasyedvāruṇe dale 
balavikaraṇīṃ devīṃ vāyavyadalamāśritām ।। 

balapramathanīṃ devīm uttare viniyojayet 
sarvabhūtadamanīṃ ca aiśānyāṃ viniyojayet ।। 

madhye manonmanīṃ devīṃ karṇikāyāṃ niveśayet 
śakracāpanibhaṃ devi dhyātavyaṃ śaktimaṇḍalam ।। 

madhye sūryasahasrābhāṃ cintayettu manonmanīm 
sūryādhvamaṇḍalaṃ patre somaṃ saṃyojya kesare ।। 

vahnimaṇḍalakaṃ devi karṇikāyāṃ niveśayet 
brahmā viṣṇurharaścaiva maṇḍaleṣvadhipāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

brahmā caturmukho raktaś caturbāhuvibhūṣitaḥ 
kṛṣṇājinottarīyaśca rājīvāsanasaṃsthitaḥ ।। 

kamaṇḍaludharo devi daṇḍahastastathaiva ca 
akṣamālādharo devaḥ padmahastaḥ sulocanaḥ ।। 

dhyātvā patreṣu taṃ nyasyet sarvakilviṣanāśanam 
atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। 

pītāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam 
sphuranmukuṭamāṇikyaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam ।। 

divyakuṇḍaladhartāraṃ garuḍāsanasaṃsthitam 
dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ mahātmānaṃ kesareṣu niveśayet ।। 

śaṅkhakundendudhavalaṃ śūlahastaṃ trilocanam 
daśabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam ।। 

siṃhacarmaparīdhānaṃ śaśāṅkakṛtabhūṣaṇam 
nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣārūḍhaṃ rudraṃ dhyātvā varānane ।। 

niveśayetkarṇikāyāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam 
mahāpretaṃ nyasetpaścāt prahasantaṃ sacetanam ।। 

raktavarṇaṃ sutejaskaṃ netratrayavibhūṣitam 
praṇavena nyasetsarvam āsanaṃ bhairavasya tu ।। 

gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya tato mūrtiṃ prakalpayet 
kadambakusumākārāṃ tuṣārakiraṇatviṣam ।। 

mūrtyūrdhve bhairavaṃ devaṃ sakalaṃ parikalpayet 
dvātriṃśadvarṇakacitaṃ sphurattaḍidivojjvalam ।। 

vaktrāṇi kalpayeddevi svadhyānena maheśvari 
mūrdhādicaraṇaṃ yāvat praṇavādinamontataḥ ।। 

aṣṭātriṃśatkalābhedaṃ śodhyādhvānaṃ prakalpayet 
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca navakaṃ bhairavābhidham ।। 

vidyāṅgā locanaṃ caiva kṣurikāṃ ca prakalpayet 
śaktitrayaṃ tato nyasyed dakṣadigvāmagocare ।। 

madhyapradeśe deveśi tato rūpamanusmaret 
tripañcanayanaṃ devaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam ।। 

candrakoṭipratīkāśāṃ candrārdhakṛtaśekharam 
pañcavaktraṃ viśālākṣaṃ sarpagonāsamaṇḍitam ।। 

vṛścikairagnivarṇābhair hāreṇa tu virājitam 
kapālamālābharaṇaṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇam ।। 

pāśāṅkuśadharaṃ devaṃ śarahastaṃ pinākinam 
varadābhayahastaṃ ca muṇḍakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇam ।। 

vīṇāḍamaruhastaṃ ca ghaṇṭāhastaṃ triśūlinam 
vajradaṇḍakṛtāṭopaṃ paraśvāyudhahastakam ।। 

mudgareṇa vicitreṇa vartulena virājitam 
siṃhacarmaparīdhānaṃ gajacarmottarīyakam ।। 

aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ sutejasam 
ūrdhvavaktraṃ maheśāni sphaṭikābhaṃ vicintayet ।। 

āpītaṃ pūrvavaktraṃ tu nīlotpaladalaprabham 
dakṣiṇaṃ tu vijānīyād vāmaṃ caiva vicintayet ।। 

dāḍimīkusumaprakhyaṃ kuṅkumodakasaṃnibham 
candrārbudapratīkāśaṃ paścimaṃ tu vicintayet ।। 

svacchandabhairavaṃ devaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam 
dhyāyate yastu yuktātmā kṣipraṃ sidhyati mānavaḥ ।। 

tataḥ paramabījena paraṃ paramakāraṇam 
suśāntaṃ niṣkalaṃ devaṃ sarvavyāpinirañjanam ।। 

āvāhayetsuhṛṣṭātmā tava devi vadāmyaham 
hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhyanādāntāntasamāśritam ।। 

niṣkampaṃ kāraṇātītam āvāhya parameśvaram 
saṃsthāpya vidhivaddevam aṅgaṣaṭkaṃ tato nyaset ।। 

pādyamācamanaṃ cārghaṃ svāgataṃ tadanantaram 
saṃnidhānaṃ ca deveśi niṣṭhurayā nirodhayet ।। 

gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpair dhūpayitvā tamarcayet 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। 

tataḥ snānādikaṃ karma kṛtvā caiva varānane 
paridhāpya suvastrāṇi netrapaṭṭodbhavāni ca ।। 

vilipyāgurukarpūrair mukuṭādyairvibhūṣayet 
puṣpairnānāvidhaiḥ śubhrair arcayedbhūṣayetpunaḥ ।। 

arghaṃ dattvā maheśāni punarmudrāṃ pradarśayet 
praṇamya bhairavaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ viśvanāyakam ।। 

tato hyābharaṇaṃ bāhye viniveśyaṃ varānane 
aiśānyāṃ pūrvato yāmyāṃ uttarāpyāvasānakam ।। 

vinyasetpañca vaktrāṇi pañcavaktrayutāni ca 
bāhubhirdaśabhiścaiva śaśāṅkamukuṭaiḥ saha ।। 

dhyātavyāni svarūpāṇi varābhayakarāṇi tu 
agnīśarakṣovāyavyacaturdikṣu ca taṃ nyaset ।। 

hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma astraṃ ca pravibhāgaśaḥ 
hṛdayaṃ raktavarṇābhaṃ śiro gorocanaprabham ।। 

taḍidvalayasaṃkāśāṃ śikhāṃ devīṃ vicintayet 
ādhūmraṃ kavacaṃ vidyāt kapiśaṃ cāstrameva ca ।। 

jyotīrūpapratīkāśaṃ netraṃ madhye ca saṃsthitam 
pañcavaktrāḥ smṛtāḥ sarve daśabāhvindubhūṣitāḥ ।। 

nānābharaṇasaṃyuktā nānāsraggandhalepanāḥ 
nānāvastraparīdhānā mukuṭairujjvalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। 

ratnamālāvanaddhāśca hārakeyūrabhūṣitāḥ 
dviraṣṭavarṣakākārāḥ surūpāḥ sthirayauvanāḥ ।। 

bhairavādyāḥ smṛtā mantrāḥ pīṭheśāḥ pīṭhamardakāḥ 
yā sā pūrvaṃ mayā khyātā aghorī śaktiruttamā ।। 

bhairavaṃ pūjayitvā tu tasyotsaṅge tu tāṃ nyaset 
yādṛśaṃ bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ bhairavyāstādṛgeva hi ।। 

īṣatkarālavadanāṃ gambhīravipulasvanām 
prasannāsyāṃ sadā dhyāyed bhairavīṃ vismitekṣaṇām ।। 

dvitīyāvaraṇe devi vinyasedbhairavāṣṭakam 
kapālīśaṃ tu pūrvāyām āgneyyāṃ śikhivāhanam ।। 

dakṣiṇe krodharājaṃ tu vikarālaṃ tu nairṛte 
manmathaṃ paścime bhāge meghanādeśvaraṃ tathā ।। 

vāyavye devi vinyasya somarājaṃ tathottare 
vidyārājaṃ tathaiśānyāṃ vinyasettu subhāvitaḥ ।। 

pañcavaktrāstrinetrāśca daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ 
kapālamālābharaṇāḥ sphuranmāṇikyamaṇḍitāḥ ।। 

pūrvaṃ pītaṃ smṛtaṃ devi raktamāgreyagocare 
dakṣiṇe nīlameghābhaṃ nairṛtyāṃ jvalanaprabham ।। 

śyāmaṃ cāparadigbhāge dhūmraṃ vāyavyagocare 
candrabimbaprabhaṃ saumye īśāne sphaṭikaprabham ।। 

tṛtīye caiva lokeśān sāstrānsaṃparikalpayet 
nāmāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

indrāgniyamanirṛtivaruṇāśca samīraṇaḥ 
somarājaḥ kuberaśca īśānaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

bhairavāṣṭakarūpeṇa dhyātavyāstu varānane 
vajraṃ śaktistathā daṇḍaḥ khaḍgaḥ pāśastathaiva ca ।। 

dhvajo gadā triśūlaṃ ca lokapālayudhāni vai 
vajraṃ cānekavarṇāḍhyaṃ śaktiṃ hemasamaprabhām ।। 

daṇḍaṃ bhinnāñjanābhaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ nīlotpalaprabham 
kiṃśukābhaṃ tathā pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet ।। 

gadāṃ tu vidrumābhāṃ vai śūlaṃ vidyutsamaprabham 
saṃpūjyāvaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ saṃdhānaṃ mantranāyake ।। 

astrāṇi lokapālāśca bhairavāṣṭakameva ca 
pañca brahmānyathāṅgāni etānyāvaraṇāni tu ।। 

krameṇoccārayetsarvaṃ yāvattadgarbhamaiśvaram 
mūlamantreṇa kartavyaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānameva ca ।। 

parāntaṃ yāvadābhāvya naivedyāni nivedayet 
ghārikā vaṭakāṃścaiva śaṣkulīrmodakāṃstathā ।। 

khaṇḍalaḍḍuśarāvāṇi bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca 
śālyodanaṃ mudgasūpam ājyāktaṃ saṃprakalpayet ।। 

kauśalyāṃ maṇḍakāpūpāṃs tathā kṣaudraśirāṃsi ca 
ghṛtāktāṃścillakāṃścaiva lavaṇānparikalpayet ।। 

avadaṃśānyanekāni kaṭūni madhurāṇi ca 
rasālāṃ ca dadhi kṣīram āsavaṃ vividhaṃ tathā ।। 

matsyamāṃsānyanekāni lehyapeyāni yāni ca 
agramāpūrayecchaṃbhor vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। 

paścādarghaḥ pradātavyaḥ surayā susugandhayā 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। 

praṇipātaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japaṃ paścātsamācaret 
akṣamālāṃ tu saṃgṛhya gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samarcitām ।। 

vāṅnirudvaḥ sucittātmā rājīvāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya nāde līnaṃ vicintayet ।। 

unmīlyākṣāṇi saṃcintya tatastu japamārabhet 
akṣarākṣarasantānaṃ na drutaṃ na vilambitam ।। 

japaḥ prāṇasamaḥ kāryaḥ dinastho muktikāṅkṣibhiḥ 
saṃhāraḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śivadhāmaphalapradaḥ ।। 

vyomni prāpto yadā nādaḥ punareva nivartate 
śarvarī sā tu vijñeyā hṛdabjaṃ yāvadāgataḥ ।। 

sṛṣṭireṣā samākhyātā sarvasiddhiphalodayā 
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ sadā bhāvyaṃ varānane ।। 

tasya vighnā vinaśyanti japaśca saphalo bhavet 
japtvā nivedayeddevi bhairavāya varānane ।। 

pūrakeṇa prayogeṇa tristhaṃ ca tritayānvitam 
trisiddhisiddhidaṃ devi sarahasyamudāhṛtam ।। 

śāntike mānaso japya upāṃśuḥ pauṣṭike smṛtaḥ 
saśabdaścābhicāre asau prāgudagdakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।। 

ātmā na śṛṇute yaṃ tu mānaso asau prakīrtitaḥ 
ātmanā śrūyate yastu tamupāṃśuṃ vijānate ।। 

pare śṛṇvanti yaṃ devi saśabdaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ 
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva akṣamālā samerukā ।। 

rudrākṣaśaṅkhapadmākṣaputrajīvakamauktikaiḥ 
sphāṭikī maṇiratnotthā sauvarṇī vaidrumī tathā ।। 

daśākṣamālā deveśi gṛhasthānāṃ prakīrtitāḥ 
sūtraṃ dhyātvā parāṃ śaktim adhvabhāgāṃstato maṇīn ।। 

vyaktisthānaṃ śivasyādhvā tatastaddharmiṇīṃ smaret 
saptaviṃśatibhiḥ kuryād dviguṇairvā caturguṇaiḥ ।। 

samaistu saṃhatairekaṃ śivatattvātmakaṃ mukhe 
na taṃ vilaṅghayedvidvān sṛṣṭisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। 

vīrasthānaratānāṃ hi vīrāṇāṃ varavarṇini 
mahāśaṅkhākṣasūtraṃ tu sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। 

gṛhasthena na kartavyam udvegajananaṃ param 
tasmāttu sphāṭikī mālā japtavyā sādhakottamaiḥ ।। 

sādhayedvividhānkāmān adhamānmadhyamottamān 
evaṃ hṛdambujāvastho yaṣṭavyo bhairavo vibhuḥ ।। 

sabāhyābhyantaraṃ kṛtvā paścādyajanamārabhet 
tatrārghapātramādau vai sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tathā ।। 

śāṅkhaṃ śāmbūkaṃ śauktaṃ vā tāmraṃ mṛṇmayameva vā 
padmapatrapalāśotthaṃ gṛhītvā kṣālya vāriṇā ।। 

astrajaptena deveśi pralipyāgurucandanaiḥ 
mṛṣṭadhūpena saṃdhūpya vāriṇāpūrayettataḥ ।। 

vastrapūtena śuddhena tāḍayedastramuccaran 
varmāvaguṇṭhitaṃ kṛtvā yāgaṃ tatraiva vinyaset ।। 

pūrvoktena vidhānena prokṣyastena samāsataḥ 
yāgārtho dravyasaṃghātaḥ tato yajanamārabhet ।। 

śaktiṃ nyasya tataścādau vyomākārāṃ sujājvalām 
sakalavyāpikāṃ sūkṣmāṃ śivādhārāṃ tu sarvagām ।। 

oṃkāradīpitāṃ devīṃ namaskārāvasānikām 
anantaṃ caiva vinyasya dharmaṃ jñānaṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

vairāgyaṃ ca tathaiśvaryam āgneyyādikrameṇa tu 
adharmaṃ ca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram ।। 

saṃdhānakīlakāṃścaiva adhaśchādanamūrdhvagam 
padmaṃ sakesaraṃ devi karṇikāṃ puṣkarāṇi ca ।। 

maṇḍalatritayaṃ devāñ śaktīścāpi śivāntakam 
mūrtiṃ brahmakalājālaṃ navatattvaṃ tritattvakam ।। 

bhairavāṣṭakavidyāṅgalocanaṃ kṣurikāṃ tathā 
śaktitrayaṃ paraṃ devam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam ।। 

vinyasya bhāvayeddevi satataṃ vidhipūrvakam 
nirvartya tu yathānyāyaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। 

svāgataṃ cārdhyapādyaṃ ca sannidhānaṃ tathaiva ca 
rodhaṃ niṣṭhurayā kuryān mūlamantramanusmaran ।। 

pūjā suvipulā kāryā gandhadhūpasragādibhiḥ 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। 

tata āvaraṇaṃ bāhye viniveśyaṃ varānane 
īśapūrvayāmyasaumyavaruṇāntaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

vaktrāṇāṃ pañcakaṃ devi svadhyānaguṇasaṃyutam 
āgneyaiśānarakṣaḥsu sāmīraindradiśorapi ।। 

uttarāntaṃ niveśyaṃ tu aṅgānāṃ pañcakaṃ tathā 
netraṃ tu karṇikāyāṃ vai pūrvasyāṃ diśi saṃsthitam ।। 

svamantreṇa tu sarveṣām ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ samāhitaḥ 
mantrasaṃkarapuṣpāṇi na kuryātsādhakaḥ sadā ।। 

na bāhuṃ pṛṣṭhato vāpi mantrāṇāṃ parikalpayet 
paripāṭyā tu dātavyaṃ na mantrāṃllaṅghayetkvacit ।। 

svamudrāmantrasaṃyuktān yugapatparikalpayet 
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca nityaṃ tāvatsamācaret ।। 

sarveṣāmeva mantrāṇāṃ vidhireṣa prakīrtitaḥ 
bhairavāṣṭakalokeśān sāstrānsaṃparikalpayet ।। 

bāhye śmaśānavinyāsaṃ praṇavādinamontagam 
pūrvādīśānaparyantaṃ kalpayeta vidhānataḥ ।। 

āmardakaṃ ca pūrvaṃ vai śmaśānādhipatiṃ vibhum 
śmaśānaiḥ sakabandhaiśca saśūlodbandhabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।। 

citibhiḥ prajvalantībhiḥ śivārāvaiḥ subhīṣaṇaiḥ 
agnikaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge kālākhyaṃ paścime tathā ।। 

ekapādaṃ tathā saumye āgneyyāṃ tripurāntakam 
nairṛtyāmagnijihvaṃ tu vāyavyāṃ tu karālinam ।। 

aiśānyāṃ bhīmavaktraṃ tu śmaśāneśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tarpayenmatsyamāṃsādyair āsavairvividhaistathā ।। 

gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ tu pradāpayet 
praṇipātaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japtvā mantraṃ subhāvitaḥ ।। 

recakena prayogena nivedya vidhipūrvakam 
huḍḍuṅkāranamaskārān kṛtvā caiva tato vrajet ।। 

agnikuṇḍasamīpaṃ tu arghahastaḥ subhāvitaḥ 
kuṇḍaṃ tu lakṣaṇopetaṃ prokṣayedastravāriṇā ।। 

kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitad astradarbheṇa collikhet 
uddhṛtya prokṣayetpaścād astramantreṇa bhāmini ।। 

pūraṇaṃ tena kartavyaṃ samīkaraṇameva ca 
secanaṃ kuṭṭanaṃ caiva lepanaṃ tena kārayet ।। 

prokṣaṇaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ caiva tathāstreṇaiva kārayet 
pūjanaṃ gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ asinā cābhimantraṇam ।। 

vajrīkaraṇamastreṇa rekhāḥ pūrvāparāstrayaḥ 
yāmyasaumyamukhī caikā vajrametatprakīrtitam ।। 

vajrīkaraṇamastreṇa rekhāstisrastu pūrvagāḥ 
yāmyasaumyamukhā tvekā vajrametatprakīrtitam ।। 

asinaivāgnikuṇḍaṃ tad darbhaiḥ pūrvāgrasaṃstaraiḥ 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ chādyaṃ gṛhahetvarthamīśvari ।। 

kuṇḍasya dakṣiṇe bhāge śuṣkagomayamāsanam 
darbheṇa viṣṭaraṃ puṣpaṃ praṇavena prakalpayet ।। 

svanāmapadasaṃyuktaṃ svadhyānena namontagam 
āmantraṇapadenaiva brahmāṇaṃ sthāpya pūjayet ।। 

puṣpādibhiḥ sudhūpādyair dhruveṇa tu yathākramam 
catuṣpathaṃ kuṇḍamadhye darbhābhyāṃ praṇavena tu ।। 

pūrvasaubhyāgrabhāgābhyāṃ viṣṭaraṃ tasya copari 
puṣpaṃ tasyopariṣṭāttu hṛdayenaiva pūjayet ।। 

vāgīśīṃ ca samāhūya praṇavādinamontagām 
nīlotpaladalaśyāmām ṛtumaccārulocanām ।। 

sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇāṃ sarvāvayavabhūṣitām 
dhyātvā caivaṃvidhāṃ devīṃ sthāpayetkuṇḍamadhyataḥ ।। 

ṛtukāla ivottānāṃ śirasaiśānasaṃsthitām 
pūjayedgaṃdhapuṣpādyair bhavamantramanusmaran ।। 

tato mudrāṃ darśayeta saṃnidhānāya mantravit 
tato agnipātramādāya śivāmbho astreṇa prokṣayet ।। 

kavacenāvaguṇṭhyāpi praṇavenaiva pūjayet 
araṇyādisamudbhūtaṃ lokāgnyantaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। 

agniṃ tu śukravaddhyātvā caitanyaṃ praṇavena tu 
ṣaḍaṅgenaiva saṃpūjya amṛtatvaṃ dhruveṇa tu ।। 

ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyātvā agniṃ dhyātvā tu bījavat 
dhruveṇa kuṇḍabāhye tu tridhābhrāmyāvatārayet ।। 

yonau tu bījavatkṣiptvā bhairaveṇa śivāmbhasā 
astramuccārya saṃprokṣya yoniṃ pracchādayedbudhaḥ ।। 

darbheṇa dhruvamantreṇa akṣavāṭaṃ tato nyaset 
astreṇaiva caturdikṣu darbhaireva prakalpayet ।। 

saptavārāstramantreṇa darbheṇaiva tu kaṅkaṇam 
dakṣahaste tu badhnīyād astramantramanusmaran ।। 

rakṣārthamagnigarbhasya garbhādhānamato bhavet 
aparāsyatrirāhutyā pūjanaṃ hṛdayena tu ।। 

hṛdā trirāhutiṃ dattvā garbhādhānaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet 
hṛdā vai jalabinduṃ tu darbhāgreṇātra pātayet ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjāṃ śikhayā kārayet tataḥ 
trirāhutiṃ cottareṇa śikhayā ca trirāhutim ।। 

puṃsaḥ kalpanamevaṃ hi na strī garbhe tu janyate 
sīmantaṃ dakṣiṇāsyena darbhāgreṇa prakalpayet ।। 

grīvāmaṃsau kaṭiṃ caiva bāhū jaṅghe prakalpayet 
pratyaṅgāni ca saṃkalpya sīmantonnayanaṃ bhavet ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjā śirasā cāhutitrayāt 
pūrvamadhyāparānvahnau trīnbhāgānparikalpayet ।। 

mukhahṛtpādadeśāṃstu homāttacca tritattvakam 
śirāṃsi pañcāhutyaiva ūrdhvāsyena tribhistribhiḥ ।। 

pañcavaktraṃ tu saṃkalpya madhyaprāgyāmyasaumyakam 
aparaṃ cāpyāhutibhiḥ pūrvāsyena trisaṃkhyayā ।। 

vaktrāṇāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ tadvad āhutīnāṃ trisaṃkhyayā 
netraṃ netreṇa saṃkalpya mukheṣvevaṃ trayaṃ trayam ।। 

āhutitritayenaiva tilaiḥ sarvaṃ tu kārayet 
tataḥ kalāsamūhaṃ ca pañca cātha catuṣṭayam ।। 

aṣṭāṅgāni tathā trīṇi daśa cāṣṭāvanukramāt 
śeṣāsyaiḥ saṃprakalpyaivaṃ kalāmūrtistato bhavet ।। 

aṅgāni vinyasetpaścāt hṛdādyāni yathākramam 
trirāhutiṃ dakṣiṇena śirasā cāhutitrayam ।। 

sīmantonnayanaṃ hyevaṃ jātakarma tvathocyate 
astreṇa vījayedagnim astreṇaiva tu pūjayet ।। 

trirāhutiṃ tu pūrveṇa astreṇaivāhutitrayam 
evaṃ mantradvayenaiva jātakarma kṛtaṃ bhavet ।। 

astreṇa prokṣayetkuṇḍaṃ sadyaḥ sūtakaśuddhaye 
vaktrāṇyuddhāṭayetpaścād vaktreṇaivāhutitrayāt 
vaktrāṇi śodhyānyasinā āhutitrayayogataḥ ।। 

vaktrābhighāro vaktraistu vaktre vaktre trayaṃ trayam 
prokṣayetkuṇḍapārśvāni sāstreṇaiva śivāmbhasā ।। 

darbhānāstīrya pūrvāgrān dakṣiṇottarasaṃsthitān 
saumyāgrānpūrvavāruṇyoḥ paridhīnviṣṭarāṃstathā ।। 

astramantreṇa te sarve brahmāṇaṃ pūrvaviṣṭare 
rudra ca dakṣiṇe sthāpya viṣṇuṃ paścimaviṣṭare ।। 

sadāśivaṃ cottare atha svanāmapadacihnitam 
ādau dhruvaṃ smareddevi namaścānte prakalpayet ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjyāḥ svarūpaṃ teṣvanusmaret 
mekhalopari lokeśān pūjayetpraṇavena tu ।। 

rakṣārthaṃ jātabālasya brahmādyāḥ pūjitāstu ye 
tataḥ kaṅkaṇakaṃ muktvā dakṣahastavyavasthitam ।। 

puṣpaṃ saṃgṛhya devena śivāgnernāma kalpayet 
kavacenopacāraṃ tu gandhapuṣpādidhūpakaiḥ ।। 

ūrdhvāsyenāhutīstisraḥ kavacena trayaṃ punaḥ 
śivanāmāṅkitaṃ vahniṃ janayitvā surāṃstataḥ ।। 

visarjayettu svasthānaṃ sāvitrīṃ praṇavena tu 
puṣpādibhiḥ samabhyarcya homaireva tribhistribhiḥ ।। 

dhāmnaivedhmāstu hotavyā hastamātrapramāṇataḥ 
caturviṃśatisaṃkhyātāḥ śivāgnestarpaṇāya tu ।। 

srukstruvau saṃpratāpyāgnau śivāmbho astreṇa prokṣayet 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau śivāgnau bhrāmayettridhā ।। 

astreṇa mārjayedadbhir darbhāgreṇātha saṃspṛśet 
punaragnau paribhrāmya prokṣayettau śivāmbhasā ।। 

darbhamadhyena saṃspṛśya bhūyo agnau bhrāmya tāpayet 
śivāmbhasā mārjayitvā darbhamūlena saṃspṛśet ।। 

sruksruvābhyāṃ tato mūlaṃ sthāpayettāvadhomukhau 
darbhāṇāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pūjyau dakṣiṇe agneḥ sadā budhaiḥ ।। 

ājyasaṃskaraṇaṃ kuryād ājyādhiśrayaṇādikam 
ājyaṃ saṃprokṣya cāstreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।। 

śivāgnau tāpyamastreṇa udvāsyaṃ kavacena tu 
kuṇḍasya parito devi tridhā bhrāmya tu sthāpayet ।। 

yonisaṃsthaṃ cājyapātraṃ udplavaṃ saṃplavaṃ tataḥ 
darbhāgradvayamādāya prādeśaṃ madhyagranthitam ।। 

pavaitrametadvihitam utplavaṃ tena saṃplavam 
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu gṛhītvaitatpavitrakam ।। 

parāṅmukhaṃ tu trīnvārān saṃmukhaṃ trīṃstathaiva ca 
astreṇaiva tu mantreṇa avadyotaḥ śivāgninā ।। 

darbholmukaṃ tu saṃgṛhya ājyapātraṃ nirīkṣayet 
nīrājanaṃ tataḥ kuryāt paryagnikaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। 

dhāmnāstramantramuccārya tamagnāvulmukaṃ kṣipet 
dhāmnaiva vidhinā mantrī prokṣayedastravāriṇā ।। 

abhimantrya ṣaḍaṅgena amṛtatvaṃ śivena tu 
sakṛduccārayogena pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।। 

vaktrasaṃdhānakaṃ vaktrair āhutitritayena tu 
aparāsyena tadvaktrasaṃdhānaṃ tu samācaret ।। 

evaṃ saumyasya vaktrasya saṃdhānaṃ tu kṛtaṃ bhavet 
trirāhutiprayogeṇa dakṣiṇasyāpyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। 

pūrvavaktre apyathaivaṃ syād ūrdhvavaktraṃ śivānvitam 
trirāhutiprayogeṇa vaktrasaṃdhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

mukhyamūrdhvaṃ smṛtaṃ vaktraṃ guṇatvamitareṣu tu 
muktikāmasya dīkṣāyām ūrdhvavaktrasya mukhyatā ।। 

pādalepāñjanādyā vai siddhīstu vividhāśca yāḥ 
sadāśivāntagāḥ sarvāḥ pūrvavaktre tu homayet ।। 

māraṇoccāṭanādau tu vidveṣe stambhane tathā 
dakṣiṇe caiva vaktre tu homātsiddhiḥ parā bhavet ।। 

śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ caiva saubhāgyākarṣaṇāni ca 
saubhāgyārohasiddhiṃ tu uttare homayetsadā ।। 

paścime nityakarmāṇi viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
ājyabhāgo hi hotavya ūrdhvavaktre tu paścime ।। 

ājyapātrasya madhye tu darbho vai bhairaveṇa tu 
nyasitavyo varārohe tato vai vartmakalpanā ।। 

uccārya bhairavaṃ pātre saṃpātaṃ pātya vartmanā 
nāḍītrayeṇa yugapat pātre bhāgatrayaṃ nyaset ।। 

suṣumnāṃ madhyamārgasthāṃ dakṣe piṅgāṃ prakalpayet 
iḍābhāge tu yattejo vāme saumyaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

evaṃ tribhāgaṃ saṃkalpya sruvamāpūrya homayet 
bhairaveṇaiva mantreṇāgnaye svāhāntameva ca ।। 

agnibhāgāttu saṃgṛhya sruveṇājyāhutiṃ kṣipet 
somabhāgastu somāya svāhetyante samuccaran ।। 

dhāmādipraṇavādyaṃ ca sruveṇājyāhutiṃ kṣipet 
agnīṣometi saṃjñe dve svāhānte dhāma cāditaḥ ।। 

praṇavādyājyamadhyāttu sruvamāpūrya homayet 
śuklapakṣe vidhirhyeṣa kṛṣṇapakṣe anyathā bhavet ।। 

somabhāge bhavetsūryo hy agnisaṃjñā tu pūrvavat 
agneḥ sūryasya madhyādvai āhutiṃ pratipādayet ।। 

yataḥ sūryasya madhye vai amāvasyāṃ viśecchaśī 
prāśanārthamato homo vaktrāṇāṃ bhairaveṇa tu ।। 

cūḍādyā ye tu saṃskārā agnerbālāntasaṃsthitāḥ 
prāpaṇārthāya sarveṣāṃ pūrṇāmekāṃ pradāpayet ।। 

bhairavaṃ tu samuccārya śivāgniḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ 
agniṃ tu proddharetpaścāt pātre saṃsthāpya rakṣayet ।। 

kuṇḍasya cottare bhāge viṣṭarasya ca bāhyataḥ 
praṇītaṃ kalpayettatra camasaṃ vāripūritam ।। 

puṣpākṣatatilairyuktaṃ pavitraṃ tatra vinyaset 
praṇavādi samāvāhya viṣṇunāma tato namaḥ ।। 

āmantraṇapadenaiva viṣṇuṃ saṃsthāpya pūjayet 
svāgatāsanapādyārghaiḥ tato vijñāpayettu tam ।। 

paśvarthaṃ yajña ārabdha ātmārthaṃ vātha sādhakaiḥ 
bhagavaṃstvatprasādena yāge niśchidratāstu naḥ ।। 

tato agnau yajanaṃ kṛtvā bhairavaṃ tu prapūjayet 
sthaṇḍiloktavidhānena anantādīnprakalpayet ।। 

dhyātvā vaktrāṇi pañcādau yena yatkarma vāñchitam 
tanmukhyavaktraṃ saṃkalpya mukhaṃ kuṇḍapramāṇataḥ ।। 

bhāvayennava jihvāsatu vaktrevaktre pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
prāgādyaṣṭau madhya ekā kāmyārthe diggatāstu yāḥ ।। 

rājyārthā dāhajananī mṛtyudā śatrukārikā 
vaśīkartryuccāṭanī syād arthadā muktidāyikā ।। 

sarvasiddhipradā madhye tasmānmadhye tu homayet 
pūṇā tu bhairaveṇaiva jihvānāṃ kalpanāya ca ।। 

punaḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ caiva bhairaveṇa pradāpayet 
jvālāgraṃ tu hṛdāgṛhya vahnicaitanyakalpitam ।। 

ātmahṛtsthaṃ tu saṃkalpya yogapīṭhaṃ tu kalpayet 
madhyajihvānusāreṇa agninābhau tu kandakam ।। 

nālaṃ hṛdavadhi dhyātvā padmaṃ tatra vicintayet 
patrāṣṭakasamopetaṃ sitavarṇaṃ sutejasam ।। 

anantaṃ kalpayettatra dharmādicaraṇāntikam 
oṃkāreṇa śivāntaṃ ca agnimūrtiṃ prakalpayet ।। 

śikhā hṛdi sthitā yā tu dhruveṇotkīlayetpunaḥ 
recakeṇa kṣipedvahnau sā mūrtirbhairavātmikā ।। 

mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpyaivam aṣṭātriṃśatkalāyutam 
śodhyādhvānaṃ tu vinyasyed dīkṣākāle varānane ।। 

bhairavaṃ pūjayitvā tu śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā 
vaktrasaṃdhiśca vaktrabhyāṃ śivavaktrāgnivaktrayoḥ ।। 

saṃdhāya caivaṃ jihvābhyāṃ nāḍīsaṃdhirato bhavet 
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya agnināsāvinirgatam ।। 

sthaṇḍilasthaśivālīnam ekārthaṃ caiva saṃdhayet 
śuddhājyenāhutiśatam aṣṭotkṛṣṭaṃ varānane ।। 

bhairavasya tu hotavyaṃ vaktrāṅgānāṃ daśāṃśakam 
bhairavāṣṭakalokeśān daśamāṃśena homayet ।। 

mūlamantraṃ samuccārya pūrṇāmekāṃ prapātayet 
bhairavāpyāyanārthāya tathā pūrṇāṃ prapātayet ।। 

punarnyūnātiriktārthaṃ niśchidrakaraṇāya ca 
paścāddhomaḥ prakartavyo yathecchaṃ tu varānane ।। 

sarvakāmaprado homas tilaiḥ śasto ghṛtānvitaiḥ 
dhānyairdhanārthasiddhyarthaṃ ghṛtaguggulahomataḥ ।। 

jāyate vipulā siddhir adhamā madhyamottamā 
śvetāravindairājyāktaiḥ bilvaiśca śriyamāpnuyāt ।। 

kśīrāktatilahomena śāntikarma varānane 
sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaiḥ śamanākṛṣṭipauṣṭikam ।। 

māraṇaṃ ca varārohe krameṇa parikalpayet 
kundapuṣpaiḥ sutārthāya aśokaiḥ priyasaṃgamaḥ ।। 

jātikuṭmalakaiḥ kanyā gāndharvī bakulodbhavaiḥ 
nāgaistu nāgakanyā vai siddhārthaiḥ siddhakanyakā ।। 

caṇyakaiścāpyapsaraso narendraḥ phalguṣeṇa tu 
ghṛtāktena varārohe samantrī sapurohitaḥ ।। 

rājñī putrasamopetā vaśaṃ yāti varānane 
yakṣiṇī vaśamāyāti puṣpaiścaiva kadambajaiḥ ।। 

vidyādharī kuyyakaiśca sādhayennātra saṃśayaḥ 
mṛgīṃ baddhvā tilairhomaḥ padmabilvairadhiṣṭhitam ।। 

bhakṣyairgrāsapramāṇaistu dhanyaiḥ prasṛtisaṃmitaiḥ 
evaṃ homānusāreṇa sādhako vidhisaṃsthitaḥ ।। 

pūjāhomarato nityaṃ yānyānkāmānsamīhate 
tāṃstānsa sādhayatyeva bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। 

iti śrīsvacchandatantre dvitīyaḥ paṭalaḥ

tṛtīyaḥ paṭalaḥ

adhivāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
vāriṇā suviśuddhātmā kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।। 

bhasmoddhūlitadehastu mudrālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ 
jihmajenopavītena savāsā vā digambaraḥ ।। 

sugandhigandhaliptāṅgaḥ puṣpasragdāmabhūṣitaḥ 
divyābharaṇasampannaḥ suprasannaḥ subhāvitaḥ ।। 

sudhūpitaḥ sutāmbūlaś candanāgurucarcitaḥ 
mahadvārapradeśe tu sthitvā prāgiva bhāvitaḥ ।। 

dvārādhyakṣān pūjayitvā puṣpaprakṣepaṇaṃ tataḥ 
humphaṭkāraprayogeṇa tālāśabdaṃ vidhāya ca ।। 

pārṣṇyadhohastasaṃyogād vighnaproccāṭanāya vai 
pārṣṇyā bhūmigatān hanyāt tālayā cāntarikṣagān ।। 

mantrairdivyān viśodhyaivaṃ yāgaharmyaṃ viśettataḥ 
rakṣāṃ pūrvavadastreṇa paritaḥ parikalpayet ।। 

varmaṇā māyārūpeṇāc chādyaiva tu makhālayam 
tato dakṣiṇadigbhāge upaviśya varānane ।। 

karanyāsaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ dahanotpūyane tathā 
plāvanāpyāyane caiva sakalīkaraṇaṃ tathā ।। 

pūrvavanmānasaṃ yāgam antardehe samācaret 
śaktyādhāramanantaṃ ca dharmādicaraṇāvadhi ।। 

gātrakāṇi tvadharmādyas tathā sandhānakīlakān 
adhaśchādanamūrdhvaṃ ca padmakesarakarṇikāḥ ।। 

puṣkarāṇi ca śaktīśca maṇḍalān maṇḍalādhipān 
śivāntamāsanaṃ dadyāt pūrvarūpaṃ dhruveṇa tu ।। 

mūrtibrahmakalāvyūhaṃ navatattvaṃ tritattvakam 
dvātriṃśadakṣaraṃ devaṃ bhairavāṣṭakameva ca ।। 

vidyāṅgāni tathā devīṃ kṣurikāṃ locanatrayam 
śaktitrayaṃ paraṃ devam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam ।। 

mudrāmantrāṃśca dravyāṇi yathāsthānaṃ prakalpayet 
saṃkalpya ca yathānyāyaṃ yathāyogaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

sadyojātaṃ ca vāmaṃ ca aghoraṃ ca yaduktavān 
puruṣeśau ca devasya dalasthāṃścopakalpayet ।। 

hṛdayādīṃstataḥ pañca diśāsu vidiśāsu ca 
pūrvato yāvadīśāntaṃ bhairavāvaraṇaṃ bahiḥ ।। 

lokapālāṃstadastrāṇi pūrvādīśāntakāvadhi 
astrāṇi lokapālāṃśca bhairavāṣṭakameva ca ।। 

pañcabrahmāṇyathāṅgāni etānyāvaraṇāni hi 
krameṇoccārayet sarvān yāvattadgarbhamaiśvaram ।। 

mantrasandhānametaddhi paramīkaraṇaṃ śṛṇu 
uccārayettato devaṃ hrasvadīrghaplutānvitam ।। 

tāvaduccārayenmantraṃ yāvannirvāṇagocaram 
adhaḥśakteryāvadūrdhvaṃ somasūryapathāntarā ।। 

piṅgalāmadhyamārgeṇa varṇoccārakrameṇa tu 
devatāpañcakaṃ śaktiṃ vyāpinīṃ samanonmane ।। 

bhedayitvā kramāt sarvaṃ yāvadvai nidhanāntikam 
nistaraṅgaṃ niradhvākhyaṃ sakalavyāpi conmanam ।। 

tadadhyāsyānulomyena hṛtpadme viniveśayet 
sarveṣvāvaraṇeṣvevaṃ devi tadvyāpakaṃ nyaset ।। 

tena cādhiṣṭhitāḥ sarve sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ 
yathā svarūpasaṃsthānavarṇā ye kathitā mayā ।। 

tathā te viniyoktavyā mānase mānasena tu 
karṇikāyāṃ tu saṃsthāpya dvidhāvasthaṃ ca bhairavam ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ sarvamantrairalaṃkṛtam 
tatrāpi parito jñeyam anirdeśyamanāmayam ।। 

yatra nāsti dvidhābhāvo na mantrādiprakalpanā 
oṃkārabindunādānāṃ vilayaṃ taṃ vinirdiśet ।। 

tatsthānaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā sambhavenna kadācana 
yasya nāgraṃ ca mūlaṃ ca diśo vidiśastathā ।। 

na śabdo nāpi cākāśaṃ dhyātvā tattu vimucyate 
prathamaṃ mānasaṃ yāgaṃ paścāddravyasamanvitam ।। 

ya evaṃ satataṃ kuryād daiśiko yāgatatparaḥ 
svahaste sthaṇḍile liṅge maṇḍale caruke tathā ।। 

jale cāgnau ca sampūjya samyag dīkṣāphalaṃ labhet 
akṛtvā mānasaṃ yāgaṃ yo anyaṃ yāgaṃ samārabhet ।। 

aśivaḥ sa tu vijñeyo na mokṣāya vidhīyate 
ātmayāge kṛte caiva dehaśuddhiḥ prajāyate ।। 

adhiṣṭhitaṃ śivenaiva tamācāryaṃ vinirdiśet 
ātmanirdahanaṃ caiva mānasaṃ ca yaduktavān ।। 

viditvā samyagācāryaḥ pāśahā sa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ 
yatra yatra sthito deśe yaścaivaṃ tu vidhiṃ yajet ।। 

brahmahāpi sa mucyeta kiṃ punaḥ śivatatparaḥ 
sarvāvasthāgataścaiva viṣayairanurañjitaḥ ।। 

sakṛt sampūjya mucyeta kiṃ punaryo dine dine 
etattantroktavidhinā yaduktaṃ vidhipūrvakam ।। 

ijyādi cānyatantre api tadvaitat kāmikaṃ bhavet 
nānāsiddhiguṇairyuktaṃ nānākāmaphalapradam ।। 

yogasiddhiśca jāyeta muktiṃ ca labhate dhruvam 
sadāśivo api jānāti devāścaivāsurādayaḥ ।। 

evaṃ tu mānasaṃ yāgaṃ kṛtvā bāhyaṃ samācaret 
parāṃ vṛttimanudhyāyan dravyāṇyādau vilokayet ।। 

sitacandanakarpūraṃ sudhūpaṃ sitavāsasī 
puṣpāṇi divyagandhīni tilavrīhighṛtādikam ।। 

cūtapallavadarbhāṃstu siddhārthān khaṭikāṃ tathā 
karaṇīṃ kartarīṃ caiva pāśabandhanasūtrakam ।। 

vārdhānīṃ śivakumbhaṃ ca tathedhmān paridhīnapi 
samidho dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca carusthālīṃ srucaṃ sruvam ।। 

taṇḍulāṃśca tathā kṣīram evamādīnyanekaśaḥ 
tato arghapātramādāya kṣālayedastravāriṇā ।। 

kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaiva praṇavena tu pūjayet 
udakādibhiraṣṭāṅgaḥ pūrayettu varānane ।। 

udakaṃ kṣīrakusumaṃ kuśasarṣapataṇḍulāḥ 
praṇavenāsanaṃ sarvaṃ tato mūrtiṃ nyaset priye ।। 

bhairavāvaraṇairyuktāṃ pūjayettāṃ yathākramam 
gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpair mantrasandhānapūrvakam ।। 

mantavyaṃ paramaṃ tattvaṃ tataścaivāmṛtībhavet 
pātrāṇāṃ tritayaṃ kalpyaṃ nirodhārthe vidhau tathā ।। 

paśvarghe ca prakalpyaivaṃ śivahastaṃ prakalpayet 
mantrasandhānakaṃ prāgvan nāḍīsandhānameva ca ।। 

mūlamantramanusmṛtya hṛtkaṇṭhatālumadhyagam 
bhrūmadhyaṃ śabdakūṭaṃ tat turyasthānaṃ vibhedayet ।। 

vāmadakṣiṇamadhye tu viṣuvatsthena bhedayet 
dvādaśāntaṃ paraṃ nītvā karastho mantravigrahaḥ ।। 

tasyāpyanena nyāyena vilomena viśeddhṛdi 
ātmano recakenaiva pūrakeṇa viśeddhṛdi ।। 

nāḍīsandhānametaddhi śivena parikīrtitam 
vyāpakaṃ tu śivaṃ dhyāyen mantramūrtimadhiṣṭhitam ।। 

darbhaṃ saṃgṛhya cāstreṇa saptavārābhimantritam 
pañcagavyāya pātraṃ tu śodhayettu śivāmbhasā ।। 

astreṇa kṣālayettacca kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
darbhāsanaṃ dhruveṇaiva maṇḍalaṃ tu prakalpayet ।। 

tasyopari nyaset pātraṃ gomayādīni cāharet 
pṛthakpātrasthitānyeva prokṣyāstreṇa śivāmbhasā ।। 

gomayaṃ tu hṛdāmantrya gomūtraṃ śirasā dadhi 
śikhayā varmaṇā kṣīram astreṇājyaṃ kuśodakam ।। 

dhāmnā ca mantrayet paścād gomayādīni yojayet 
pūrvasaṃskṛtapātre tu svamantrairgomayādikam ।। 

saṃyojya mantrayetpaścāt taireva hṛdayādibhiḥ 
praṇavena tu saṃkalpya anantaṃ mūrtivigraham ।। 

dhāmāṅgāni ca bāhye tu sampūjyāvaraṇasthitim 
mantrasandhānakaṃ kṛtvā amṛtīkaraṇaṃ tathā ।। 

śivāmṛtaṃ tatsaṃcintya sampūjya sthāpayettataḥ 
astrābhimantritaṃ darbhaṃ gṛhītvollekhanaṃ kuru ।। 

yāvadbhūmau samantāttu saumyāsyo dakṣiṇe sthitaḥ 
tataścaivoddharecchalyam ājalāntaṃ vyavasthitam ।। 

recitaṃ bhāvayecchuddhaṃ mauktikādyaiḥ prapūrayet 
samīkaraṇamastreṇa kavacena tu secanam ।। 

ākoṭanamathāstreṇa tato mārjanalepane 
astreṇa pañcagavyena gandhatoyena copari ।। 

śivāmbhasāstrayuktena vikirāṇyabhimantrayet 
saptakṛtvo astramantreṇa sthitvā mantre tu prāgdiśaḥ ।। 

ūrdhvādho vikireddhānyāny astrabhūtāni cintayet 
cāmareṇa suśubhreṇa astramantreṇa saṃharet ।। 

aiśānyabhimukhānyeva nairṛtyā yāvadaiśvaram 
pañcagavyena samprokṣya gandhāmbhobhiḥ śivāmbhasā ।। 

dhruveṇa śriyamāvāhya padmahastāṃ sulocanām 
śuklapuṣpāṇi muñcantīṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām ।। 

nīlotpaladalaśyāmāṃ yāgaharmyāvalokinīm 
brahmasthānopaviṣṭāṃ tu dvārābhimukhabhadradām ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya śivakumbhaṃ prakalpayet 
aiśānīṃ diśamāśritya pañcagavyena maṇḍalam ।। 

gandhodakena saṃlipya śivāmbho astreṇa prokṣayet 
anantādyāsanaṃ dattvā dhruveṇāmaṇḍalāvadhi ।। 

sarvadoṣavinirmuktaṃ kumbhaṃ candanalepitam 
svastikādyaiścārcayitvā yavasiddhārthadūrvabhiḥ ।। 

sitasūtreṇa saṃveṣṭya vastrapūtena cāmbhasā 
sampūrya sarvataśchannaṃ cūtāśvatthādipallavaiḥ ।। 

ratnagarbhauṣadhīyuktaṃ sahadevādibhirgaṇaiḥ 
prokṣya cāstreṇa saṃgṛhya kavacenāvaguṇṭhitam ।। 

āsanasyopari nyasyen mūlamantramanusmaran 
kalādhvabhairavādīni nyasyārghādīn prakalpayet ।। 

mudrāṃ baddhvā hṛdādīni pūjyānyagnidalādiṣu 
gandhapuṣpapavitrādyaiḥ sitavastreṇa bhūṣayet ।। 

vāmabhāge tu kumbhasya pañcagavyena maṇḍalam 
śivāmbhasā tu samprokṣya praṇavenāsanaṃ nyaset ।। 

samprokṣya ca śivāmbhobhir vārdhānīṃ maṅgalānvitām 
kumbhavaccārcayitvā tām āsanasyopari nyaset ।। 

gandhapuṣpapavitrādyaiḥ pūjayitvā tu vārdhanīm 
uccāryāstraṃ krameṇāgre dravyāṇāṃ vārdhanīṃ nayet ।। 

acchinnāmanulomena jaladhārāṃ tu pātayan 
tatsthānāttu samuddhṛtya yāvatkoṇaṃ tu śāṅkaram ।। 

ācāryaḥ kalaśaṃ paścād bhairaveṇa samuddharet 
nayedvārdhānimārgeṇa tasmin saṃsthāpayetpunaḥ ।। 

vārdhānīṃ sthāpayetpaścād astramantramanusmaran 
viśeṣapūjāmubhayor gandhapuṣpapavitrakaiḥ ।। 

mantrasandhānakaṃ kuryān nāḍīsandhimathobhayoḥ 
vikirān saṃhitān pūrvaṃ vārdhānyāḥ kalpayedadhaḥ ।। 

akṣatāstrāṇyanekāni śarakuntāsimudgarāḥ 
cakrapaṭṭisavajrāditriśūlāntānyanekaśaḥ ।। 

yogauko vyāpya sarvaṃ tu tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥ sthitāḥ 
vārdhānyastrasya sarve te raśmibhūtā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

śiṣyasya dakṣiṇe haste vārdhānyastraṃ tu saṃhitam 
tenaitaṃ yajñarakṣārthaṃ yāgādau kalaśaṃ nyaset ।। 

naivedyaṃ vividhaṃ dattvā nutvā vijñāpayedvibhum 
bhagavaṃstvatprasādena yāgaṃ nirvartayāmyaham ।। 

sannidhānaṃ sadā tubhyam avighnārthaṃ sadā bhava 
anujñātotthito yāyād arghahasto digīśvarān ।। 

svanāmapadavinyāsān oṃkārādinamontagān 
gandhapuṣpapavitrādyaiḥ pūjayettān prayatnataḥ ।। 

indrādyanantaparyantāṃl lokapālān prapūjayet 
tato maṇḍalakaṃ madhye yāgabhūmau prakalpayet ।। 

pañcagavyena liptvādau gandhatoyena copari 
śivāmbhasāstramantreṇa samprokṣya tvavaguṇṭhayet ।। 

brahmasthānasya pūrveṇa gurūn pūjya vināyakam 
vāyavye pūjayeddevi gandhapuṣpairanukramāt ।। 

athaitāṃstu namaskṛtya ājñāṃ dattāṃ vibhāvayet 
tatastu madhyadeśasthaṃ yogapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

pūrvoktena vidhānena bhairaveśaṃ varānane 
pūjayitvā pavitrādyais trirāvaraṇasaṃyutam ।। 

svadhyānaguṇasaṃyuktaṃ mudrālaṅkārabhūṣitam 
mantrasandhānakaṃ pūrvaṃ nāḍīsandhānameva ca ।। 

paramīkaraṇaṃ kuryād vyāpakena pareṇa tu 
naivedyān vividhākārān dattvā mudrāṃ pradarśayet ।। 

praṇipātaṃ japaṃ kṛtvā nivedya vidhipūrvakam 
paścādbaliḥ pradātavyo mātṛṇāṃ bhūtasaṃhate ।। 

bhūteśvarāṇāṃ deveśi kṣetrapālasya sarvataḥ 
tataḥ snāyādathoddhūlya athavācamya suvrate ।। 

tato agnikuṇḍaṃ gatvā tu pūrvavacchodhanaṃ tathā 
bhairavaṃ pūjayettatra vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। 

agneḥ santarpaṇaṃ kuryāt sahasreṇa śatena vā 
tataścaruṃ ca śrapayet sthālīṃ saṃgṛhya nirvraṇām ।। 

śivāmbhasā tu prakṣālya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
candanādyairvilimpettāṃ mṛṣṭadhūpena dhūpayet ।। 

sūtreṇa veṣṭayet kaṇṭhe varmabhūtena suvrate 
darbheṇāstrasvarūpeṇa kalpayenmaṇḍalaṃ priye ।। 

prokṣya caiva śivāmbhobhiḥ kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
āsanaṃ tatra vinyasyed anantādiśivāntakam ।। 

mūrtibhūtāṃ nyasetsthālīṃ tatrasthaṃ bhairavaṃ yajet 
trirāvaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ gandhapuṣpairanukramāt ।। 

mānasena prayogeṇa bhāvapuṣpairvarānane 
cullīṃ samprokṣya cāstreṇa kuṇḍavaccārcayettataḥ ।। 

tatra sthālīṃ samāropya paścādagniṃ nyasedadhaḥ 
kṣīraṃ prokṣya śivāmbhobhis taṇḍulāṃśca samāsataḥ ।। 

mantreṇāṣṭaśatenaiva prakṣipya pācayecchanaiḥ 
mūlamantreṇa deveśi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। 

cālanodghāṭanādīni astramantreṇa kārayet 
taptābhidhāraṃ susvinne aṅgaiścaiva prakalpayet ।। 

tribhistribhirghṛtenaiva sruveṇa juhuyāt priye 
bhūmau maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā praṇavenāvatārayet ।। 

sthālīmājyopaliptāṃ tu śītāghāraṃ ca homayet 
bhairaveṇa ṣaḍaṅgena vaṣaḍjātiyutena ca ।। 

maṇḍalaṃ kuṇḍasāmīpye kṛtvā darbhāsanaṃ nyaset 
sthālyāṃ tasyopari nyasya sampātaṃ mantrasaṃhitām ।। 

japannekaikayāhutyā pātayed bhairaveṇa tu 
aṣṭotkṛṣṭaśatenaiva parāmṛtamanusmaran ।। 

rajasyādau tato devi kartaryāṃ karaṇau tathā 
khaṭikātilājyasampātaṃ mūlamantreṇa kārayet ।। 

tribhāgaṃ kalpayitvā taṃ caruṃ sthālyāṃ tu saṃsthitam 
śivāgnisādhakebhyaśca śivāyāgraṃ nivedayet ।। 

dvitīyaṃ homayedagnau sādhakebhyastṛtīyakam 
caruṃ pātre tu saṃgṛhya pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।। 

puṣpadhūpādibhirnītvā dhāmnaitaṃ vinivedayet 
hṛdādyāvaraṇasthānāṃ daśamāṃśaṃ nivedayet ।। 

kalaśe apyevamevaṃ tu agnau homyaścaruḥ srucā 
bhairavasya śataṃ homyam aṅgānāṃ tu daśāṃśakam ।। 

sādhakebhyastu yaccheṣaṃ pidhāya sthāpayet priye 
vināyake śataṃ homyaṃ bhūparigrahaṇe tathā ।। 

adhivāse tathaiveha aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutiḥ 
prāyaścittanimittaṃ tu anulomavilomake ।। 

nyūnātirikte deveśi aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutiḥ 
bhairavaṃ pūjayitvātha prārthyānujñāṃ varānane ।। 

śiśoḥ karma prakartavyaṃ yathā bhavati tacchṛṇu 
dvāre maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā darbhaṃ tasyopari nyaset ।। 

praṇavenāsanaṃ kalpyaṃ śiṣyaṃ tasminniveśayet 
samapādaṃ stabdhakāyaṃ saumyānanakṛtāñjalim ।। 

guruḥ pūrvamukho astreṇa prokṣayettaṃ śivāmbhasā 
bhasmanā tāḍayenmūrdhni astramantreṇa cālabhet ।। 

nābhyūrdhvaṃ trīṃstathā vārān nabhyadhastrīn prakalpayet 
śivaṃ nyāsāṅgasahitaṃ pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।। 

vastraṃ samprokṣya cāstreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
pūjayedbhairaveṇaiva mukhaṃ pracchādayettathā ।। 

hastābhyāṃ taṃ gṛhītvātha viśejjavanikāntaram 
devasyābhimukhaṃ kṛtvā puṣpaṃ prāṇau pradāpayet ।। 

prakṣepayettato dhāmnā mukhamudghāṭya darśayet 
vidyāmantragaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ kāraṇaṃ sasadāśivam ।। 

ajñānapaṭanirmuktaḥ prabuddhaḥ paśurīkṣate 
daṇḍavaddharaṇīṃ gatvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā prahṛṣṭanayanaṃ śiśum 
utthāpya hastān saṃgṛhya dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtimānayet ।। 

tatra maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā puṣpeṇa praṇavāsanam 
tasyopari śiśuṃ nyasya ūrdhvakāyamudaṅmukham ।। 

guruḥ pūrvānanaḥ sthitvā prokṣaṇādīni kārayet 
upaveśya tataḥ kṛtvā sakalīkaraṇe vidhim ।। 

viśeṣaphalasiddhyarthaṃ mumukṣoḥ sādhakasya vā 
gandhadigdhau karau kṛtvā astreṇa pariśodhayet ।। 

kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau plāvayedamṛtena tu 
anantamāsanaṃ kalpyaṃ bhairavāṅgāni vinyaset ।। 

vyomnyātmānaṃ yojayitvā śiśoḥ śoṣyā tanuḥ priye 
āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ dhyātvā nirdahyāstreṇa taṃ śiśum ।। 

dhūmajvālāvinirmuktaṃ dagdhakāyaṃ vibhāvayet 
bhasmībhūtaṃ tataḥ śāntaṃ plāvayedamṛtena tu ।। 

vyomavaccintayeddehaṃ caitanyaṃ kanakāgnivat 
śaktinyāsaṃ nyasetpūrvaṃ kamalaṃ praṇavena tu ।। 

tasyopari tadātmānaṃ dhyāyejjyotirmayaṃ śubham 
mūrtimantraṃ samuccārya mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

pūrvoddhṛtena mantreṇa plāvayedamṛtena tu 
mantranyāso yathāpūrvam aṣṭātriṃśatkalāvadhi ।। 

kalādhvānaṃ nyaset paścāc chāntyatītādyanukramāt 
sphaṭikābhā tathā kṛṣṇā raktā śuklā ca pītakā ।। 

śāntyatītādikā jñeyās tattvabhūtāstu tāḥ kalāḥ 
dhāmnāvāhya tathāṅgāni nyasyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ bhavet ।। 

ātmāntaḥkaraṇe yadvat tadvatpūjāṃ samārabhet 
dhāma proccārya sandadhyāt sabāhyābhyantaraṃ punaḥ ।। 

śivahaste vibhuṃ dhyātvā mantragrāmaṃ sujājvalam 
dhāmoccārya ca sandhāya śiṣyamūrdhni karaṃ nyaset ।। 

adhomukhena hṛtpṛṣṭhe śivahastena cālabhet 
utthāpya dattvā puṣpaṃ tu añjalau bhairaveṇa tu ।। 

praveśyābhyarcayecchambhuṃ śivamuccārya nikṣipet 
nirgatya vandayeddevaṃ daṇḍavat triḥ pradakṣiṇam ।। 

śivakumbhāgnimadhyasthaṃ sthaṇḍilasthaṃ ca vandayan 
śivapūjāgnikāryādau sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ ।। 

nānyathā prāksvarūpeṇa pūjanārho bhavettu saḥ 
nītvā kuṇḍasamīpaṃ taṃ śiṣyahastāviyogataḥ ।। 

ātmasavye atha digbhāge maṇḍalaṃ praṇavena tu 
praṇavenāsanaṃ dattvā tasyopari śiśuṃ nyaset ।। 

upaveśya kare darbhaṃ bhairaveṇa samarpayet 
mūlaṃ śiṣyasya hastasthaṃ sāgramācāryajaṅghayoḥ ।। 

piṅgalā madhyamā nāḍī śiṣyadehādvinirgatā 
saivātra darbhabhūtā tu gurunāḍyāṃ layaṃ gatā ।। 

nāḍīsandhānahetvarthaṃ bhairaveṇāhutitrayam 
tayā nāḍyā praveṣṭavyaṃ śiṣyasya hṛdaye sakṛt ।। 

grahaṇākarṣaṇārthaṃ tu gṛhṇan muñcan punaḥ punaḥ 
dīkṣākāle yataścaivaṃ tadarthaṃ nāḍisaṃhatiḥ ।। 

śiṣyasyātha śirobhūmau bhairaveṇa vidhāya tu 
sampātaṃ sarvamantraistu dhruveṇājyāhutiṃ kṣipet ।। 

mūlamantraṃ samuccārya svā ityagnau prapātayet 
heti śiṣyasya śirasi sampātaḥ śivacoditaḥ ।। 

śiṣyadehe tu ye mantrāḥ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ sthitāḥ 
kuṇḍasthāḥ pūjitā ye tu dhāmādyāvaraṇāntagāḥ ।। 

yugapattarpaṇaṃ teṣāṃ sampātastena kīrtitaḥ 
ekaikasyātra mantrasya āhutitritayena tu ।। 

utthāpya ca tataḥ śiṣyaṃ tadarthaṃ mantratarpaṇam 
bhairavāya śataṃ hutvā hṛdādau daśakaṃ hutiḥ ।। 

dhāmnā cotthāya hotavyaṃ pūrṇāhutyānutarpayet 
mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ kuryād dhāmādyastrāvadhi kramāt ।। 

huṃkāradvayamadhye tu mūlamantraṃ samuccaran 
praṇavādiphaḍantena āhutīḥ pratipādayet ।। 

hṛdādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ jātiruktātra dīpane 
pāśānāṃ bandhanārthāya mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ smṛtam ।। 

mantrāḥ karaṇabhūtāstu paśukāryasya sādhane 
ācāryaḥ karaṇaṃ proktaḥ śivarūpo yataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

krūrakārye tu kartavye mantrān sandīpya yojayet 
krūrajātyanurūpeṇa vācakān yojayet sadā ।। 

bhrukuṭīkarālavadanān vācyarūpān vicintayet 
saumyajātiyutān saumye saumyarūpān vicintayet ।। 

pāśakarma tato vakṣye kanyākartitasūtrakam 
triguṇaṃ triguṇīkṛtya pāśabandhanasūtrakam ।। 

śivāmbho astreṇa samprokṣya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
pūjayitvā vidhānena gandhapuṣpādidhūpakaiḥ ।। 

prasārayedgṛhītvā tan mūrdhādyaṅguṣṭhakāvadhi 
śiṣyasya stabdhadehasya nāḍībhūtaṃ vicintayet ।। 

suṣumnā madhyamā nāḍī sarvanāḍīsamanvitā 
oṃkārādi svanāmnā tu namaskārāvasānakam ।। 

śiṣyadehasthitāṃ nāḍīṃ sūtre saṃgṛhya yojayet 
gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।। 

sannidhānāhutīstisraḥ svanāmapadajātikāḥ 
śivāmbho astreṇa samprokṣya śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ punaḥ ।। 

tāḍayedastrapuṣpeṇa hṛdi citsaṃhṛtā bhavet 
huṃkāroccārayogena recakena viśeddhṛdi ।। 

nāḍīrandhreṇa gatvā tu caitanyaṃ bhāvayecchiṣoḥ 
kadambagolakākāraṃ sphurattārakasannibham ।। 

hṛtsthaṃ chittvāstrakhaḍgena humphaṭkārāntajātinā 
dhāmnā cāṅkuśarūpeṇa karṣecchaktyavadhi kramāt ।। 

dvādaśāntaṃ tu saṃgṛhya sampuṭya hṛdayena tu 
saṃhāramudrayā yojyaṃ sūtre nāḍīprakalpite ।। 

vyāpakaṃ bhāvayitvā tu kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ sannidhānasya hetave ।। 

dvitīyaḥ sūtradehastu pāśā yatra sthitāstvime 
bandyāścedyāstathā dāhyāḥ sūtrasthāne na vigrahe ।। 

pāśāstu trividhā bhāvyā māyīyāṇavakarmajāḥ 
caitanyarodhakāstvete kāryakāraṇarūpiṇaḥ ।। 

malaḥ karma nimittaṃ tu naimittikamataḥ param 
ādhārarūpaṃ naimittaṃ śarīrabhuvanādikam ।। 

nimittamabhilāṣākhyaṃ vicitrairheturūpakaiḥ 
tāṃścāvalokayet sūtre bandhyabandhanahetutaḥ ।। 

pāśānāṃ tāḍanaṃ kāryaṃ humphaṭkārāntajātinā 
svanāmapraṇavādyena śāntyatītādyanukramāt ।। 

puṣpeṇa tāḍayenmūrdhni grāhyaṃ hūmādi yojayet 
huṃphakārāntayogenāgṛhya saṃhāramudrayā ।। 

dhāmnā tu yojayet sūtre namaskārāntayoginā 
evaṃ śāntyādikān pāśān sthānāt saṃgṛhya yojayet ।। 

bhāvayettrividhān pāśān pañcatattvādhvavyāpakān 
trayāṇāṃ vyāpikā śaktiḥ kriyākhyā pārameśvarī ।। 

śāntyatītādibhedena pañcasaṃjñāpratiṣṭhitā 
ādheyagraha ādhāraṃ gṛhītaṃ bhāvayet paśoḥ ।। 

gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya sūtre pāśāṃśtu tarpayet 
śāntyatītākrameṇaiva āhutīnāṃ trayaṃ trayam ।। 

sannidhānāya pāśānām ataḥ pāśāṃstu dīpayet 
svanāmajātiphaṭkāradhāmabhiśca trayaṃ trayam ।। 

viśleṣakaraṇārthaṃ tu pāśānāṃ dīpanaṃ bhavet 
dīptāḥ pāśāstato bandhyās tāḍanagrahaṇādinā ।। 

sūtrasthāṃstāḍayetpuṣpaiḥ svadehasthāniva kramāt 
dhāmnā ca sampuṭīkṛtya svanāmnā ca sakṛtsakṛt ।। 

bandhane tu prayogo ayaṃ sūtre granthīn pradāpayet 
bandhane parimāṇaṃ ca karmaṇo viṣayasya ca ।। 

ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamadhyastho bhuṅkte bhogaṃ na cānyathā 
pāśān saṃsthāpya pātre tu saṃpātaṃ juhuyāt sakṛt ।। 

pātrasampuṭamadhyasthān sthaṇḍile vinivedayet 
nītvā samarpayet kumbhe pāśān saṃrakṣa he vibho ।। 

darbhaṃ vimocayecchiṣyaṃ puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet 
shtaṇḍile śivakumbhe ca śivāgnau ca prapūjayet ।। 

tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍavannipatedbhuvi 
utthāpya pañcagavyādīn dadyādvai bhairaveṇa tu ।। 

gomayena śucau deśe kāryaṃ maṇḍalakatrayam 
ekasmin maṇḍale viṣṭaḥ pañcagavyaṃ śiśuḥ pibet ।। 

upaviśya dvitīye tu carukaṃ prāśayedbudhaḥ 
ācamya dantakāṣṭhaṃ tu tṛtīye maṇḍale sthitaḥ ।। 

bhakṣayitvā ca deveśi tataścaiva vinikṣipet 
pūrvaṃ paścāttathaiśordhvaṃ cottarasyāṃ ca śobhanam ।। 

anyasyāmaśubhaṃ viddhi tasya homaḥ śataṃ bhavet 
ācāryo juhuyāt paścāt prāyaścittaṃ śivena tu ।। 

vidhernyūnātiriktasya cittavikṣepakarmaṇi 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā prāyaścittād viśuddhyati ।। 

paścātsantarpayeddhomasahasreṇa śatena vā 
mantrāṃśca daśabhāgena vahnau naivedyadāpanam ।। 

viśeṣapūjanaṃ cārghaṃ mudrābandhaṃ varānane 
stotraṃ vādyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā caruṃ prāśya visarjayet ।। 

nirodhārgheṇa cārghaṃ tu dattvā caiva varānane 
recakena tu saṃgṛhya bhairavaṃ tamanusmaran ।। 

muṣṭinā pūritaṃ nītvā pūjayitvā varānane 
agniṣṭhaṃ vai pūrakeṇa gṛhītvā sthāpayet punaḥ ।। 

tatrasthaṃ pūjayitvā ca kalaśe tu vinikṣipet 
kusumādibhirabhyarcya kumbha eva tu bhairavam ।। 

prakṣipya caiva nirmālyaṃ gomayena spṛśet priye 
śivāmbhasā tu samprokṣya śiṣye śayyāṃ prakalpayet ।। 

gṛhiṇo darbhaśayyāṃ tu yatervai bhasmanā priye 
pūrvāśirā gṛhī kāryo yatirvai dakṣiṇāśirāḥ ।। 

tatra sthitasya śiṣyasya śikhābandhaṃ varānane 
siddhārtharocanādyaiśca rakṣāṃ kuryādasiṃ smaran ।। 

bhasmanā rocanādyaiśca astraprākāracintanam 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaiva śiṣyaṃ tu svāpayettataḥ ।। 

tataścaiva tu nirgatya balikarma samārabhet 
balistu kalpitaḥ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūteṣvathādarāt ।। 

taṃ tu saṃgṛhya deveśi pūrvādīśāntakaṃ kṣipet 
bhūtā ye vividhākārā divyabhaumāntarikṣagāḥ ।। 

pātālatalasaṃsthāśca śivayāge subhāvitāḥ 
dhruvādisarvabhūtāśca aindrādyāśāsthitāśca ye ।। 

svāhākārasamāyogāt tṛpyantūccārayan kṣipet 
namaskāreṇa sampūjya gandhairdhūpairanukramāt ।। 

pūrvādīśānaparyantam adhaścordhvaṃ samantataḥ 
koṇasthān kṣetrapālāṃśca patitāñchvapacānapi ।। 

baliṃ dattvā tu sarvebhya ācamya ca varānane 
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā krameṇa prāśayeccarum ।। 

sahāyaiḥ sahito vīra ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ 
prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vā maṇḍalasthaḥ pṛthakpṛthak ।। 

pañcagavyaṃ pibet pūrvaṃ carukaṃ dantadhāvanam 
prāśyaivaṃ sakalīkṛtya rakṣāṃ pūrvavadeva ca ।। 

yāgabūmau svapet pāścāc chiṣyaiḥ saha varānane 
bhairavadhyānayogena samādhau jāgradeva vā ।। 

svacchandatantre adhivāsapaṭalastṛtīyaḥ

caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ

pratyūṣe vimale kṛtvā śaucādyān purrvavatkramāt 
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pūrvavat praviśedgṛham ।। 

śiṣyaśca śucirācāntaḥ puṣpahastaḥ guruṃ tataḥ 
praṇamya śirasā hṛṣṭo guroḥ svapnānnivedayet ।। 

śubhān svapnān pravakṣyāmi aśubhāṃśca varānane 
svapneṣu madirāpānam āmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam ।। 

krimiviṣṭhānulepaṃ ca rudhireṇābhiṣecanam 
bhakṣaṇaṃ dadhibhaktasya śvetavastrānulepanam ।। 

śvetātapatraṃ mūrdhasthaṃ śvetasragdāma bhūṣaṇam 
siṃhāsanaṃ rathaṃ yānaṃ dhvajaṃ rājyābhiṣecanam ।। 

ratnāṅgābharaṇādīni tāmbūlaṃ phalameva ca 
darśanaṃ śrīsarasvatyoḥ śubhanāryavagūhanam ।। 

narendrairṛṣibhirdevaiḥ siddhavidyādharairgaṇaiḥ 
ācāryaiḥ saha saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā svapne prasiddhyati ।। 

nadīsamudrataraṇam ākāśagamanaṃ tathā 
bhāskarodayanaṃ caiva prajvalantaṃ hutāśanam ।। 

grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ candrabimbasya darśanam 
harmyasyārohaṇaṃ caiva prāsādaśikhare api vā ।। 

narāśvavṛṣapotebhataruśailāgrarohaṇam 
vimānagamanaṃ caiva siddhamantrasya darśanam ।। 

lābhaḥ siddhacaroścaiva devādīnāṃ ca darśanam 
guṭikāṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca khaḍgapādukarocanāḥ ।। 

upvītāñjanaṃ caiva amṛtaṃ pāratauṣadhīḥ 
śaktiṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ padmam akṣasūtraṃ manaḥśilām ।। 

prajvalatsiddhadravyāṇi gairikāntāni yāni ca 
dṛṣṭvā siddhyati svapnānte kṣitilābhaṃ vraṇaṃ tathā ।। 

kṣatajārṇavasāṃgrāmataraṇaṃ vijayaṃ raṇe 
jvalatpitṛvanaṃ ramyaṃ vīravīreśibhirvṛtam ।। 

vīravetālasiddhaiśca mahāmāṃsasya vikrayam 
mahāpāśoḥ saṃvibhāgaṃ labdhvā devebhya ādarāt ।। 

ātmanā pūjayan devaṃ japan dhyāyan stuvannapi 
suhutaṃ cānalaṃ dīptaṃ pūjitaṃ vā prapaśyati ।। 

haṃsasārasacakrāhvamayūraśavarohaṇam 
mātṛbhirbhairavaścaiva mātṛrudragaṇaiḥ saha ।। 

bhairavaṃ bhairavīṃ dṛṣṭvā siddhyatyatra na saṃśayaḥ 
śubhāḥ svapnā mayākhyātā aśubhāṃśca nibodha me ।। 

tailābhyaṅgastathā pānaṃ viśanaṃ ca rasātale 
andhakūpe ca patanam atha paṅke nimajjanam ।। 

vṛkṣavāhanayānebhyaḥ patanaṃ harmyaparvatāt 
kartanaṃ karṇanāsābhyām atha vā hastapādayoḥ ।। 

patanaṃ dantakośānām ṛkṣavānaradarśanam 
vetālakrūrasatvānāṃ tathaiva kālapūruṣāḥ ।। 

kṛṣṇordhvakeśā malināḥ kṛṣṇamālyāmbaracchadāḥ 
raktākṣī strī ca yaṃ svapne puruṣaṃ tvavagūhayet ।। 

mriyate nātra saṃdeho yadi śāntiṃ na kārayet 
gṛhaprasādabhedaṃ ca śayyāvastrāsaneṣu ca ।। 

ātmano abhibhavaṃ saṃkhya ātmadravyāpahāraṇam 
kharoṣṭraśvasṛgāleṣu kaṅkagṛdhrabakeṣu ca ।। 

mahiṣolūkakākeṣu rohaṇam ca pravartanam 
bhakṣaṇam pakvamāṃsasya raktamālyānulepanam ।। 

kṛṣṇaraktāni vastrāṇi vikṛtātmā prapaśyati 
hasanaṃ valganaṃ svapne mlānasragdāmadhāraṇam ।। 

svamāṃsotkartanaṃ bandhaṃ kṛṣṇasarpeṇa bhakṣaṇam 
udvāhaṃ ca tathā svapne dṛṣṭvā naiva prasidhyati ।। 

aśubhā hyevamākhyātā vijñeyā deśikottamaiḥ 
śubhāstatrānumedyāstu aśubheṣu tu homayet ।। 

aṣṭottaraśataṃ dhāmnā prāyaścittādviśuddhyati 
pūrvavat sakalīkṛtya vighnoccāṭanarakṣaṇam ।। 

veṣṭanaṃ pūrvavat kuryāc chivambhaḥ śivahastakam 
lokapālāṃstu saṃpūjya śivakumbhaṃ ca sthaṇḍilam ।। 

agnikāryaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pūrṇāhutiprapātanam 
prāyaścittaṃ tataḥ paścād dusvapnārthaṃ yaduktavān ।। 

evaṃ pūjādikaṃ kṛtvā visṛjya sthaṇḍilacchivam 
nirmālyāpanayaṃ kṛtvā bhūmiṃ saṃśodhya pūrvavat ।। 

nityakarma tataḥ kuryāt pūjāhomajapādikam 
nityāhnike samāpte tu naimittikamathācaret ।। 

upalipya śivāmbhobhir bramhmasthānaṃ prapūjayet 
bhāvena gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ tato maṇḍalamālikhet ।। 

karaṇīṃ khaṭikāṃ caiva bhairaveṇa prapūjayet 
dhāmnā tu rajasāṃ pātaḥ sitādyaśvāgamoditaḥ ।। 

niṣpanne maṇḍale snātvā nityakarma samācaret 
nityakarmasamāptau tu kuryānnaimittikaṃ budhaḥ ।। 

snānādi pūrvamantraiḥ sakalīkaraṇādikam 
ātmarakṣāstraprākāradvārapālādipūjanam ।। 

vighnoccāṭanadigbandhau bhūpātālakhavāsinām 
astraprākāramāropya kavacenāvaguṇṭhanam ।। 

udaṅmukhaṃ tūpaviṣṭaḥ karaśuddhyādi pūrvavat 
śivāmbhaḥ śivahastaṃ ca arghatrayaprakalpanam ।। 

lokapālāṃstu saṃpūjya śivakumbhaṃ prapūjayet 
maṇḍalasyāgrato bhūtvā maṇḍalaṃ prokṣya cāsinā ।। 

varmaṇā veṣṭayet paścāt praṇavenābhimantrayet 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ dhāmnā rajodoṣairviśuddhyati ।। 

caturdikṣvastraṃ saṃpūjya dvāre gandhādibhiḥ kramāt 
prākāraṃ bhāvayedastraṃ maṇḍalaṃ praviśet tataḥ ।। 

gurūn saṃpūjya vighneśaṃ puṣpādyaiḥ praṇavena tu 
anantamāsanaṃ prāgvac chivāntaṃ praṇavena tu ।। 

mūrtyādi pūrvannyasyed dhṛdādyāvaraṇāntagam 
pūrvoktavidhinā pūjya naivedyāni nivedayet ।। 

nirodhārgheṇa cārdhaṃ tu datvā caiva nirodhayet 
japadhyānādikaṃ kṛtvā agniṣṭhaṃ bhairavaṃ yajet ।। 

nāḍīsaṃdhānakaṃ triṣṭhaṃ kṛtvā saṃtarpayedvibhum 
ātmano niṣkaloccāraṃ kṛtvā kumbhe niveśayet ।। 

kalaśasthasya vāmena rocayet pūrayettataḥ 
maṇḍalasthasya savyena punarvāmena rocayet ।। 

agniṣṭhasya tu tattejo dakṣiṇena viśan smaret 
evaṃ sādhanakaṃ kṛtvā tatastarpaṇamārabhet ।। 

daśabhāgavibhāgena hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet 
prāyaścittaviśuddhyarthaṃ kuryādaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।। 

vidheḥ pūrṇātiriktasya dhāmnā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ 
ācāryoṭhārdhahastastu maṇḍalaṃ praviśettataḥ ।। 

saṃpūjya parameśānaṃ puṣpādyairardhapaścimam 
mudrāṃ baddhvā praṇamyādau jānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ ।। 

vijñāpayeta paśvarthaṃ prārabdhyoyaṃ makhottamaḥ 
snānādhivāsanādyaṃ yan maṇḍale agnau ca yatkṛtam ।। 

vidhānaṃ puṣkalaṃ samyak tvatprasādādihāstu tat 
idānīṃ śiṣyadehe tu sakalīkaraṇādikā ।। 

yojanyantādhvaśuddhistu tvatprasādāt prasiddhyatu 
evamastvityanujñātaḥ parameśena vīrarāṭ ।। 

labdhānujñaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā niṣkrāmenmaṇḍalādbahiḥ 
paśvarthāya kṛtaṃ yattu tadgṛhītvārdhapātrakam ।। 

dhāmnastu dakṣiṇe bhāge kārayenmaṇḍalaṃ guruḥ 
praṇavāsanaṃ kuśairnyasya śuciṃ śiṣyaṃ niveśayet ।। 

śivāmbho astreṇa saṃtāḍya bhasmanā ca kuśaiḥ kramāt 
maṇḍale kalpite śiṣyaṃ mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

upaviśya karanyāsaṃ nirdāhādyastrapūrvakam 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ nyāsaṃ mantrasaṃdhānameva ca ।। 

śivahastaḥ pradātavyo dhyātvā devaṃ sujājvalam 
mūrdhni saṃpātayettejaḥ pāśāṅkuravināśanam ।। 

utthāpya ca tato nītvā maṇḍalaṃ tu praveśayet 
vastraṃ saṃprokṣya toyena kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।। 

pūjayedgandhapuṣpādyair bhairaveṇābhimantrayet 
netre baddhā tu netreṇa puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet ।। 

akāmānnikṣipetpuṣpaṃ devasyābhimukhaṃ sthitaḥ 
puṣpapātavaśānnāma kuryādvai sādhakasya ca ।। 

mumukṣorgururicchātaḥ nāma vai sādhakasya vā 
mukhamudghāṭya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivāya praṇipātayet ।। 

pradakṣiṇamataḥ kṛtvā maṇḍalegnau praṇamya ca 
agnikuṇḍasamīpe tu ācāryaḥ paśunā saha ।। 

ātmasavyetha digbhāge maṇḍalaṃ praṇavena tu 
pūrvannāḍisaṃdhānaṃ tad arthaṃ cāhutitrayam ।। 

saṃpātābhihutiṃ kṛtvā aṇutarpaṇameva ca 
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato dattvā prāyaścittāni homayet ।। 

dhāmnā cāṣṭaśataṃ paścāt pātayedāhutitrayam 
jātyuddhāre dhruveṇaiva dvijatvāpādane tathā ।। 

bījāhāre tathā deśabhāvaśuddhau dvijo bhavet 
praṇavenāhutīstisro rudrāṃśāpādane tathā ।। 

astreṇa prokṣayecchiṣyaṃ puṣpayuktena tāḍayet 
recakena tato gatvā śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi ।। 

oṃkārādi śivaṃ japtvā astramantraṃ phaḍantagam 
viśleṣakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā caitanyasya vidhānataḥ ।। 

chedayedastramantreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
aṅkuśena samākṛṣya dvādaśānte tu kārayet ।। 

tatrasthaḥ pudgalo grāhyaḥ saṃpuṭyaiva dhruveṇa tu 
saṃhāramudrayā samyak pūrakeṇa viśeddhṛdi ।। 

saṃskubhya sarasīkṛtya recayetpudgalaṃ punaḥ 
tyajantaṃ devatāṣaṭkaṃ tataścāpi svakaṃ padam ।। 

tatrasthaṃ pudgalaṃ gṛhya saṃpuṭya ca bhavena tu 
saṃhāramudrayoddhṛtya śiṣyasya hṛdi yojayet ।। 

bhairaveṇābhimantrya evam upavītaṃ śiśordadet 
ādhānādyāvadantyeṣṭiṃ dvijatve saṃskṛto bhavet ।। 

piṇḍasyāpādanaṃ jāteḥ āhutitritayena tu 
caitanyasyāpi saṃskāram ādhānāntyeṣṭitaḥ param ।। 

sūkṣmavijñānataḥ kṛtvā dvijatve saṃskṛto bhavet 
śatahomaṃ sahasraṃ vā hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।। 

samayī saṃskṛto hyevaṃ vacaneṣyārhatā bhavet 
śravaṇe adhyayane home pūjanādau tathaiva ca ।। 

caryādhyānaviśuddhātmā labhate padamaiśvaram 
atha dīkṣādhvaśuddhyarthaṃ bhuktimuktiphalārthinām ।। 

vidhānamucyate sūkṣmaṃ pāśavicchattikārakam 
guruḥ saṃpṛcchate śiṣyaṃ dvividhaṃ phalakāṅkṣiṇam ।। 

phalamākāṅkṣase yādṛk tādṛk sādhanamārabhe 
vāsanābhedataḥ prāptiḥ sādhyamantrapracoditā ।। 

mantramudrādhvadravyāṇāṃ homaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
vāsanābhedato bhinnaḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā ।। 

sādhako dvividhastatra śivadharmyekataḥ sthitaḥ 
śivamantraviśuddhādhvā sādhyamantraniyojitaḥ ।। 

jñānavāṃścābhiṣiktaśca mantrārādhanatatparaḥ 
trividhāyāstu siddhervai so atrārhaḥ śivasādhakaḥ ।। 

dvitīyo lokamārgastha iṣṭāpūrtavidhau rataḥ 
karmakṛtphalamākāṅkṣañ śubhaikastho aśubhojjhitaḥ ।। 

tasya kāryaṃ sadā mantrair aśubhāṃśavināśanam 
gṛhastho vā yatirvāsāv āśramaikatamasthitaḥ ।। 

mumukṣurdvividhaḥ prokto nirbījo bījavānpunaḥ 
bālabāliśavṛddhastrībhogabhugvyādhitātmanām ।। 

eṣāṃ nirbījikā dīkṣā samayadivivarjitā 
vidvaddvandvasahānā tu sabījā kīrtitā priye ।। 

dīkṣānugrāhikā teṣāṃ samayācārasaṃyutā 
viśeṣasamayācārā mantrākhye ye prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

te atra pālyāḥ prayatnena mokṣasiddhimabhīpsatā 
sabījā sā tuvijñeyā putrakācāryayoḥ sthitā ।। 

gṛhastho vāśramī vātha yatiḥ saṃkalpya dīkṣayet 
pāśasūtrakamādāya śiṣyadehe avalambayet ।। 

adhvānaṃ saṃdhayedagnau dhāmnā caiva vicakṣaṇaḥ 
kumbhamaṇḍalavahnisthaś cādhvātmasthaḥ śiśośca yaḥ ।। 

sūtrasthaścāpi caikatra adhvasaṃdhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
ṣaḍvidhasyādhvamārgasya sādhāraṇagatasya tu ।। 

kuṇḍe saṃkalpya saṃśodhyamadhvasaṃdhau tu homayet 
mūlamantrāṣṭaśatikamadhvasaṃdhānahetutaḥ ।। 

adhvāvalokanaṃ paścād vyāpyavyāpakabhedataḥ 
bhuvanavyāptitā tattveṣv anantādiśivāntake ।। 

vyāpakāni ca ṣaṭtriṃśat mantravarṇapadātmakāḥ 
tattvāntarbhāvinaḥ sarve vācyavācakayogataḥ ।। 

kalāntarbhāvinaste vai nivṛttyādyāśca tāḥ smṛtāḥ 
hṛdādyā vācakāstāsāṃ bījāmantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

ekikasyāḥ kalāyāśca pṛthagvyāptiṃ vibhāvayet 
pṛthivyādikalā jñeyā brahmādyāḥ kāraṇāśca te ।। 

evaṃ vyāptiṃ bhāvayitvā adhvopasthāpanaṃ bhavet 
trirāhutiṃ dhruveṇaiva adhvaśuddhirato bhavet ।। 

agnau tu pūjite deve adhvanyāse kṛte sati 
tadeva pādādārabhya pṛthivyādikramānnyaset ।। 

dhāmādhiḥ praṇavādiśca nivṛttyai ca namaḥ punaḥ 
upasthāpanamantro ayaṃ vyāptiṃ dhyātvādhvasaṃsthitām ।। 

nivṛttyabhyantare pṛthvī śatakoṭipravistarā 
tasyāṃ ca bhuvanānāṃ ca śatamaṣṭottarāvadhi ।। 

aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ padāni varṇa eko atra saṃsthitaḥ 
mantrau dvāveva vijñeyau adhvaṣaṭkaṃ vibhāvayet ।। 

puṣpagandhādinā pūjya saṃnidhāvāhutitrayam 
māyīyā bhuvanākārā malāḥ karma ca saṃsthitāḥ ।। 

śarīrabhuvanākārā māyīyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
bhogahetuśca karma syād abhilāṣo malo atra tu ।। 

evaṃ pāśatrayaṃ bhāvyaṃ dīkṣāyāmadhvasaṃsthitam 
tadviśuddhyai ca dīkṣā ca kriyate sā yathāvidhi ।। 

ādau śaktiṃ nyaseddevi kalātattvasamanvitām 
hṛdā saṃkalpya vāgīśīṃ vyāpikāṃ sarvayoniṣu ।। 

śatarudrādyanantāntaṃ yonayo vividhāḥ sthitāḥ 
samakālamṛtutvena vāgīśīṃ saṃnidhāpayet ।। 

dhruveṇa pūjayetpuṣpair gandhadhūpairanukramāt 
oṃkāreṇāhutistisro vāgīśīsaṃnidhāpane ।। 

śiṣyaṃ saṃprokṣya cāstreṇa tāḍayedastramuccaran 
recakenātmano gatvā chindyāttasyāsinā hṛdaḥ ।। 

dhāmnākṛṣya tadātmānaṃ dvādaśānte nidhāpayet 
dhruveṇa tatsthaṃ saṃpuṭya caitanyaṃ mudrayātmani ।। 

pūrayedbhairaveṇaiva kumbhayedrecayettataḥ 
dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya yojayedbhavamudrayā ।। 

ātmānamīśvaraṃ dhyātvā māyāṃ vāgīśvarīmapi 
saṃyojya tasyāṃ caitanyaṃ śarīrāṇyadhvani sṛjet ।। 

prākkarmavāsanāśeṣaphalabhogatvahetave 
yugapadbhinnabhogāni deśakālaśarīrataḥ ।। 

mantraśaktyā vipacyante pudgalāśca tathāvidhāḥ 
bhinādehā visṛjyante garbhe vāgīśiyoniṣu ।। 

dhāmnā ca yojayitvā ca juhuyādāhutitrayam 
yugapatsarvagarbheṣu dehā vividharūpakāḥ ।। 

bhairavecchāsusaṃpannaḥ śatarudrādyanantagāḥ 
garbheṣu garbhaniṣpatti bhairaveṇāhutitrayam ।। 

hutvā tu jananaṃ kāryaṃ punastenāhutitrayāt 
sarvayoniṣu dehāste yugapadvṛddhimāgatāḥ ।। 

bhoganiṣpattaye karma vyāparasahakāraṇam 
tadabhāvānna bhogaḥ syāt tadarthaṃ mārjanaṃ smṛtam ।। 

arjite [ārjite] sati bhoktavyo bhogo duḥkhasukhātmakaḥ 
layaḥ paramayā prītyā sukhaduḥkhādike apyalam ।। 

tisṛbhistisṛbhirhomaṃ dhāmnaiva triṣu kārayet 
āhutīnāṃ śataṃ homyaṃ dhāmnā niṣkṛtaye punaḥ ।। 

yatkarmabhogyarūpaṃ tu jātyāyurbhogalakṣaṇam 
niṣkṛtyante viśuddhyettad bhūlokasamavasthitam ।। 

saṃsārā daśacatvāraḥ saṃskārā aṣṭabhiḥ saha 
catvāriṃśad dvijatvāya vakṣyante bhuvanādhvani ।। 

yonirbījaṃ tathā bhāva āhāro deśa eva ca 
eteṣāṃ śodhanaṃ devi rudrāṃśāpādanaṃ tathā ।। 

atrāvalokanaṃ kṛtvā niṣkṛtyāmeva śuddhyati 
viṣayā bhuvanākārā ye kecidbhogyarūpiṇaḥ ।। 

bhuktakarmaphalāśeṣā niṣkṛtistena sā smṛtā 
viśleṣo niṣkṛterbhogāt bhogābhāve sa hi smṛtaḥ ।। 

bhoktṛtvaṃ viṣayāsaktir malakāryaṃ prakīrtitam 
bhoktṛtvābhāvastatraiva śarīreṇa tu yatkṛtam ।। 

viśleṣaḥ kriyate tasya paśormantraiḥ śivājñayā 
dhāmnā cāhutayastisro viśleṣakaraṇāya ca ।। 

āhutitritayaṃ dhāmnā pāśacchede api dāpayet 
pāśā dehe tu māyīyāḥ kalādyā bhūtakāvadhi ।। 

śarīrakaraṇākārāḥ puruṣārthaprasiddhaye 
bhogābhāvādvipadyante śarīrāṇi sahasradhā ।। 

pāśacchede vidhistasya mantraiśca vidhicoditaiḥ 
evaṃ pāśatrayasyāpi viśleṣo dīkṣayocyate ।। 

śarīraśeṣabhaṅgena ekacaitanyabhāvanā 
pūrṇāhutiṃ śivenaiva vauṣaḍjātiyutena ca ।। 

śuddhatattvāgrasaṃsthaṃ tac caitanyaṃ kanakaprabham 
uddhārāyāhutīstisraḥ punardhāmnā tu dāpayet ।। 

tasmāt tattvādgṛhītvā tu caitanyaṃ malasaṃyutam 
mudrayā prāgvidhānena ātmasthaṃ pūrayedddhṛdi ।। 

kumbhitvā recya saṃgṛhya dvādaśāntād dhruveṇa tu 
śiṣyadehe niveśyaitan nāḍīrandhreṇa pūrvavat ।। 

tatsthīkaraṇahetvarthaṃ dhāmnā caivāhutitrayam 
kalāśuddhyavasāne tu brahmāṇaṃ kāraṇādhipam ।। 

svanāmapraṇavāhvānapūrvaṃ saṃtarpya cārpayet 
śabdasparśo tyajet tasmin dhruvādyau nāmasaṃyutau ।। 

svāhākāraprayogena tau brahmaṇi nivedayet 
tisṛbhistisṛbhirhomāt puryaṣṭāṃśaṃ nivedayet ।। 

āmantraṇavibhaktyā tu śrāvaṇāṃ tasya kārayet 
brahmāṇaṃ pūjayitvā tu homaṃ kṛtvā visarjayet ।। 

dhruveṇābhyarcya vāgīśīṃ saṃtarpya ca visarjayet 
hutvāvalokayettatra viśuddhaṃ pāśajālakam ।। 

prākkarmabhāvikasyātha abhāvaṃ bhāvayettadā 
mumukṣornirapekṣatvāt prārabdhrekaṃ na śodhayet ।। 

sādhakasya tu bhūtyarthaṃ prākkarmaikaṃ tu śodhayet 
prākkarmāgāmi caikasthaṃ bhāvayitvā ca dīkṣayet ।। 

śivadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā lokadharmiṇyato anyathā 
prāktanāgamikasyāpi adharmakṣayakāriṇī ।। 

lokadharmiṇyasau jñeyā mantrārādhanavarjitā 
prārabdhadehabhede tu bhuṅkte sa hyaṇimādikān ।। 

bhuktvā vrajedūrdhvaṃ guruṇā yatra yojitaḥ 
sakale niṣkale vāpi śiṣyācāryavaśādbhaved ।। 

nirvāṇe api sabījāyāṃ karmābhāvādvipadyate 
samayācārapāśaṃ hi dīkṣitaḥ pālayettu yaḥ ।। 

taṃ pāśaṃ naiva śuddhyeta sā sabījā prakīrtitā 
samayācārapāśaṃ tu nirbījāyāṃ viśodhayet ।। 

dīkṣāmātreṇa muktiḥ syād bhakrimātrādguroḥ sadā 
sadyonirvāṇadā dīkṣā nirbījā sā dvitīyakā ।। 

atītanāgatārabdhapāśatrayaviyojikā 
dīkṣāvasāne śuddhiḥ syād dehatyāge paraṃ padam ।। 

evaṃ bhāvānusāreṇa śiṣyāṇāṃ guruṇā sadā 
phalaṃ tu vividhākāraṃ niṣpādyeta sudīkṣayā ।। 

acintyā mantraśaktirvai parameśamukhodbhavā 
kriyā kāle prayoktavyā guruṇā bhaktipūrvikā ।। 

viṣāṇamiva pāśānāṃ mantraiḥ kavalanaṃ dhruvam 
karoti mantratattvajñaḥ śivāveśī guruḥ kṣaṇāt ।। 

kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ kuryāc chuddhāśuddhadvirūpagam 
śuddhamuccārayedhrasvam aśuddhaṃ dīrghameva ca ।। 

ekatvaṃ bhāvayitvā tu līnaṃ śuddhaṃ vibhāvayet 
praṇavādinivṛttistu pratiṣṭhā tadanantaram ।। 

namaskārastadante tu kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ smṛtam 
āvāhya sthāpya saṃpūjyāhutīstisraḥ prapātayet ।। 

kalāsaṃdhānametaddhi vyāptiṃ tasyāvalokayet 
gulphādārabhya nābhyantaṃ śiṣyadehe adhvakalpanam ।। 

pratiṣṭhāyā bhavedvyāptiś caturviṃśatitattvikā 
ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanikā trayoviṃśativarṇikā ।। 

jñeyaikaviṃśatipadā trimantrā ca vidhīyate 
mukhyā hyete smṛtāḥ pāśāḥ sūkṣmānantarvibhāvayet ।। 

anyattantraprasiddhiṃ tu tanmātrendriyaśodhanam 
ṣaṭkośānviṣayān pañca tadantarbhāvayetsadā ।। 

viśeṣasthāpanaṃ kṛtvā pūjyā gandhādibhistataḥ 
bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ tasyā vāgīśikalpanā ।। 

svanāmāvāhanādyasya ardhahomādi pūrvavat 
prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ cheda ākarṣagrahaṇe tathā ।। 

dhāmnāpūrya kumbhayitvā chittvātha grāhayetpunaḥ 
yojanaṃ garbhadhāritvaṃ jananaṃ pūrvavatkramāt ।। 

aiśvarīṃ mūrtimāsthāya tāḍanādīni kārayet 
adhikārasthathā bhogo layo niṣkṛtireva ca ।। 

śivarūpeṇa kartavyāḥ niṣkṛtiḥ śirasā punaḥ 
viśleṣaśca hṛdā homyaḥ pāśacchedastathāsinā ।। 

pūrṇāhutisamuddhāraṃ pūrvavadbhairaveṇa tu 
sadāśivatanau sthitvā viśleṣādīni kārayet ।। 

ātmasthaṃ pūrakeṇaiva tatsthaṃ recakavṛttitaḥ 
svanāmnoccārayedviṣṇuṃ dhyātvāvāhya tu sthāpayet ।। 

pūjayetpuṣpagandhādyaiḥ tarpaṇāhutitrayam 
rasaṃ puryaṣṭakāṃśaṃ tu arpayedviṣṇave sadā ।। 

visarjayettato viṣṇuṃ vāgīśīṃ ca visarjayet 
kalāsaṃdhiryathāpūrvaṃ hrasvadīrghaprayogataḥ ।। 

abhāvaṃ bhāvayettasmin pāśajāle tvanantake 
kalādvayavinirmuktaḥ paśurūrdhvagamotsukaḥ ।। 

tasyedānīṃ tṛtīyasyāṃ vidyāyāṃ yojya śodhayet 
sthāpayitvā saṃpūjya juhuyādāhutitrayam ।। 

evaṃ tu saṃmukhīkṛtya prāgivādhvāvalokanam 
puṃstattvādyāvanmāyāntaṃ vidyāyā vyāptiriṣyate ।। 

sapta tattvāni bhuvanasaptaviṃśatireva ca 
padaviṃśatirākhyātā varṇāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

mantrau dvau ṣaḍvidhādhvānaṃ jñātvā vāgīśikalpanam 
praṇavena samāvāhya vyāpinīṃ sarvayoniṣu ।। 

samakālamṛtutvena dhyātvā saṃpūjya tarpayet 
tataḥ śivāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya cāstreṇa tāḍayet ।। 

tenaiva cāstrabhūtena huṃphaṭkārayutena tu 
ātmano revakenaiva śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi ।। 

astramantreṇa saṃchedya viśeṣāśleṣyāstreṇa karṣayet 
dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya ātmasthaṃ pūrvavatkuru ।। 

pūrakeṇātha saṃkumbhya recayitvā tu yojayet 
pūrvavaddvyāpakaṃ tasya caitanyaṃ sarvayoniṣu ।। 

yogādyaṃ layaparyantaṃ dhāmnā caivātra pūrvavat 
śikhayā śatahomāttu vidyāyā niṣkṛtirbhavet ।। 

praṇavādi tato rudram āvāhya sthāpya pūjayet 
tato asya vinyaseddevi gandharūpe dhruvāhutī ।। 

puryaṣakāṃśaṃ vinyasya visarjya rudradevatām 
vāgīśīṃ ca visarjyaivaṃ kalāsaṃdhiśca pūrvavat ।। 

hrasvadīrghavibhāgena vidyāṃ śāntau niyojayet 
saṃdhānārthaṃ tu mūlena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।। 

svanāmnāvāhanaṃ śānter vidhipūrvaṃ nivedanam 
prameyabhāvanāṃ kṛtvā pūjayet kusumādibhiḥ ।। 

trirāhutiṃ tu mūlena vidyātattvātsadāśivam 
tattvānāṃ tritaye vyāptir varṇānāṃ traya eva ca ।। 

padaikādaśikā jñeyā purāṇi daśa sapta ca 
mantrau dvau ṣaḍvidho adhvaivaṃ mukhyāḥ pāśā ime smṛtāḥ ।। 

sūkṣmapāśānanekāṃśca tadantarbhāvayetsadā 
vagīśīṃ kalpayettatra pūrveṇa vidhināhutiḥ ।। 

pūjanaṃ mūlamantreṇa tataḥ prokṣaṇatāḍanam 
chedākarṣagrahaṃ caiva yogadhāritvajanma ca ।। 

adhikārastathā bhogo layo vai pūrvavadbhavet 
sarve te mūlamantreṇa āhutitritayena tu ।। 

niṣkṛtau śatahomaṃ tu kavacena tu kārayet 
viśleṣaṃ pāśachedaṃ tu kuryādastreṇa daiśikaḥ ।। 

uddhārakaraṇātmasthatatsthīkārānbhavena tu 
svanāmnā praṇavādyena īśamāvāhya pūjayet ।। 

saṃpūjya hutvā saṃtarpya buddhyahaṃkṛtidyaṃśakam 
svanāmnā praṇavādyaṃ tu svāhānte buddhimarpayet ।। 

ahaṃkāraṃ tathāpyevaṃ hutvedaṃ kṣamayettataḥ 
vāgīśīṃ pūjayitvā tu tarpayitvā visarjayet ।। 

kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ pūrvaṃ śāntyatīte tu yojayet 
hrasvadīrghavibhāgena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।। 

dhruveṇa tattvasaṃdhānaṃ kartavyaṃ vidhivedinā 
kalopasthāpanaṃ paścād dhruveṇa juhuyātpriye ।। 

trirāhutiprayogeṇa svanāmapadamuccaran 
śāntyatītāṃ samāvāhya sthāpayetpūjayetpunaḥ ।। 

vyāptimālokya cādhvasthāṃ śivatattvagatāśca ye 
bindurnādastathā śaktiḥ śivatattve vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

padamekaṃ mantra eko varṇāḥ ṣoḍaśa kīrtitāḥ 
bhuvanāni tu sūkṣmāṇi śāntyatīte tu bhāvayet ।। 

śodhanīyā varārohe yāvatte śivaraśmayaḥ 
śivasyordhve śivo jñeyo yatra yukto na jāyate ।। 

ṣaḍadhvā caikato jñeyaḥ tasya saṃkhyāṃ punaḥ śṛṇu 
kalāśca pañca vijñeyās tattvaṣaṭtriśadeva tu ।। 

sacaturviṃśati jñeyaṃ bhuvanānāṃ śatadvayam 
ekāśītipadānyatra varṇārdhaśatikā smṛtā ।। 

mantrā ekādaśā jñeyā ityetaccādhvamaṇḍalam 
etasmiñśuddhimāpane muktimāpnoti dīkṣitaḥ ।। 

dhruveṇāvāhya vāgīśīṃ vinyaset pūrvavaddhutiḥ 
saṃpūjya kusumādayistu tadyonau pūrvavatpaśum ।। 

dhruveṇa sarvaṃ kartavyaṃ jananādilayāntakam 
niṣkṛtau śatahomaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa kalpayet ।। 

viśleṣapāśacchedābhyāṃ prāgvatkuryāddhruveṇa tu 
graheṇātmasthatatsthatvaṃ praṇavena paśoḥ smṛtam ।। 

sadāśivamathāvāhya mūlamantraṃ samuccaran 
namaskāreṇa saṃsthāpya puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjya tarpayet ।। 

manaḥ puryaṣṭakāṃśaṃ tu vinyasetkāraṇeśvare 
praṇavādi samuccārya manaḥsaṃjñāṃ namastathā ।। 

vinyasya pūjayetpaścāt saṃjñāsvāhāntameva ca 
āhutitritayaṃ hutvā puryaṣṭāṃśādviśuddhyati ।। 

tato visarjayeddevaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca sadāśivam 
puṣpādibhiḥ samabhyarcya vāgīśīṃ tadanantaram ।। 

tā tu saṃpūjya saṃtarpya vijñāpyā bhaktibhāvitā 
kṣamasva devadeveśi paśvarthaṃ kheditā mayā ।। 

idānīṃ noparoddhavyaṃ gaccha devi svaviṣṭapam 
visarjyaivaṃ kalā bhāvyā śāntyatītā layaṃ gatā ।। 

svaśaktyādhāraparyante susūkṣmābhāvasaṃsthite 
ātmatattvavibhāgena dhāmnā vai juhuyācchatam ।। 

saśaboccārayogena ātmatattve tu homayet 
māyātattvāvadhi jñeyaṃ daiśikena mahādhvare ।। 

vidhivaikalyakarmārthaṃ prāyaścittaviśuddhaye 
vidyātatve tu hotavyaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ priye ।। 

upāṃśūccarayogena vidyātattve tu homayet 
sadāśivāntamadhvānaṃ vidyātattvaṃ vinirdiśet ।। 

mantroccaravolomena prāyaścittaṃ tu yadbhavet 
tadviśuddhyai sa homaḥ syād vidyātattve tu yaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 

manovijñānavaikalyāt prāyaścittaṃ tu yadbhavet 
tacchuddhyarthaṃ śive tattve mūlamantreṇa homayet ।। 

mānasena prayogena śaktyante adhvani saṃsthitam 
tattvatrayaviśuddhyante śikhācchedaṃ tu kalpayet ।। 

adhvāntasthāṃ parāṃ śāntām anaupamyāmanāmayām 
vyāpinīṃ sarvatattvānāṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।। 

dhyātvā śiśoḥ śikhāgre tu puṣpāgre jalabinduvat 
kartarīṃ śikhayāmantrya śikhayā cchedayecchikhām ।। 

śikhāṃ samarpya cānyasya nirgacchetsa saśiṣyakaḥ 
snānaṃ samācarecchiṣyaḥ gurorācamanaṃ bhavet ।। 

snānamuddhūlanaṃ vātha ācaretsvecchayā guruḥ 
praviśya sakalīkṛtya pūrṇayā juhuyācchikhām ।। 

hutvā nirgamya cācamyākṣālya sruksruvakartarīḥ 
praviśya sakalīkṛtya śivahastānupūjanam ।। 

tatastu maṇḍale paścāt pūjayetparameśvaram 
puṣpādibhiraśeṣaistu tato vijñāpayecchivam ।। 

bhagavaṃstvatprasādena adhvaṣṭakavyavasthitam 
paśuṃ saṃgṛhya saṃśodhya śikhācchedāvasānakam ।। 

tvanmukhoktavidhānaṃ tu leśato vartitaṃ mayā 
tvacchaktyaiva tu gantavyam āśu dhruvapadaṃ śivam ।। 

idānīṃ yojane karma tavājñānuvidhāyinaḥ 
ājñā me dīyatāṃ nātha śiṣyaṃ saṃyojayāmyaham ।। 

labdhānujñātamātmānaṃ prahṛṣṭo nirgataḥ purāt 
ardhahasto vrajedagnim śiṣyamāhūya prokṣayet ।। 

pūrvavaccāsanasthasya sakalīkaraṇādikam 
antaḥkaraṇavinyāsaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānapūrvakam ।। 

pūjanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ cāgnau mantrāṇāṃ ca śivasya ca 
daśabhāgavibhāgena yathā dravyānusārataḥ ।। 

mantrānsaṃśodhayetpaścāt sakalīkaraṇe sthitān 
sakṛdāhutiyogena adhikāro vivarjyatām ।। 

sakalīkaraṇatvena na kadācitpaśoḥ punaḥ 
yojanīyaṃ prayogaṃ tu adhunā kathayāmi te ।। 

jñātvā cārapramāṇaṃ tu prāṇasaṃcārameva ca 
ṣaḍvidhādhvavibhāgaṃ tu prāṇaikatra yathāsthitam ।। 

haṃsoccāraṃ tu varṇaiśca kāraṇatyāgameva ca 
śūnyaṃ samarasaṃ jñeyaṃ tyāgaṃ saṃyogamudbhavam ।। 

bhedanaṃ ca padārthānāṃ bhāvaprāptivaśātpunaḥ 
ātmavidyāśivavyāptim evaṃ jñātvā tu yojayet ।। 

tadvibhāgaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathā jñāyeta tattvataḥ 
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaścāro hṛtpadmādyāvaśaktitaḥ ।। 

tuṭiṣoḍaśamānena kālena kalitaḥ priye 
saṃcarantaṃ vibhāgena yathāvattaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। 

hṛtpadmādyāvadayanaṃ bhāgamekaṃ tyajettu saḥ 
nāsikāgre dvitīyaṃ tu śaktyante tu tṛtīyakam ।। 

tatrastho vinivarteta yāvattattvaṃ na vindati
