vidite tu pare tattve tatrastho api na bādhyate ।। 

śaktyā cādho yadā gacched abudhastu tadā bhavet 
hṛdgataḥ punaruttiṣṭhed budhyamānaḥ sa ucyate ।। 

śaktiṃ prāpya budho jñeyaḥ vyāpinyaṃśe prabuddhatā 
atītaḥ suprabuddhastu unmanastvaṃ tadā bhavet ।। 

na kālo na kalā cāro na tattvaṃ naca kāraṇam 
sunirvāṇaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ gurupāramparāgatam ।। 

tadvoditvā vimucyeta gatvā bhūyo na jāyate 
adhvaṣṭkaṃ yathā prāṇe saṃsthitaṃ kathayāmi te ।। 

āpādānmūrdhaparyantaṃ citeḥ saṃvedanaṃ hi yat 
bhuvanādhvā sa vijñeyas tattvādhvā ca tathaiva hi ।। 

kalākalitasaṃtānaḥ prāṇaḥ saṃcarate sadā 
nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca adhobhāge pravartike ।। 

vidyā śāntistathā cordhve śāntyatītā tvadhiṣṭhikā 
tadatītaḥ paro bhāvaḥ tadūrdhvam padamavyayam ।। 

evaṃ bindukalā jñeyā nādaśaktyātmikāśca yāḥ 
vyāpinyādyātmikā yāśca vyāpyavyāpakabhedataḥ ।। 

prāṇaikasaṃsthitāḥ sarvāḥ ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
kalādhvaivaṃ samākhyāto varṇādhvānaṃ nibodha me ।। 

varṇāḥ śabdātmakāḥ sarve jagatyasmiṃścarācare 
sthitāḥ pañcaśatā bhedaiḥ śāstreṣvānantyakoṭiṣu ।। 

śabdātprāṇaḥ samākhyātas tasmādvarṇāstu prāṇataḥ 
utpadyante layaṃ yānti yatra śabdo layaṃ gataḥ ।। 

śabdātīto varārohe tattvena saha yujyate 
yuktaḥ sarvagato devi dharmādharmavivarjitaḥ ।। 

nādho nirīkṣate bhūyaḥ śivatattvaṃ gato yadā 
adho vai yātyadharmeṇa dharmeṇordhvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ ।। 

vijñānena dvayaṃ tyaktvā sarvagastu bhavediha 
varṇādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ padādhvā procyate adhunā ।। 

ekāśītipadānyeva vidyārājasthitānyapi 
varṇātmakāni tānyatra varṇāḥ prāṇātmakāḥ sthitāḥ ।। 

tasmādevaṃ padānyatra tāni prāṇakrameṇa tu 
padādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ mantrādhvānaṃ nibodha me ।। 

mantrikādaśikā yā tu sā ca haṃse vyavasthitā 
padikādaśikā sā ca prāṇe carati nityaśaḥ ।। 

akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca 
ardhacandro nirodhī ca nādo nādānta eva ca ।। 

śaktiśca vyāpinī caiva samanaikādaśī smṛtā 
unmanā ca tato atītā tadatītaṃ nirāmayam ।। 

mantrā evaṃ sthitāḥ prāṇe haṃsoccārastathocyate 
hakārastu smṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ svapravṛtto halākṛtiḥ ।। 

akāreṇa yadā yukta ukāracaraṇena tu 
makāramātrayā yukto varṇoccāro bhavetsphuṭaḥ ।। 

binduḥ śiraḥsamāyogāt susvaratvaṃ prapadyate 
nādo asya vadanaṃ proktaḥ vadanaṃ śabdamīrayet ।। 

anenaiva ca yogena haṃsaḥ puruṣa ucyate 
brahmaviṣṇvīśamārgeṇa caranvai sarvajantuṣu ।। 

śaktitattve layaṃ yāti vijñānenordhvatāṃ vrajet 
vyāpinīṃ samanāṃ tyaktvā vrajedunmanayā śivam ।। 

śivatattvagato haṃso na caret vyāpako bhavet 
haṃsoccāraḥ samākhyātaḥ kāraṇaiśca samanvitaḥ ।। 

hakāraḥ prāṇaśaktyātmā akāro brahmavācakaḥ 
hṛdi tyāgo bhavettasya ukāro viṣṇuvācakaḥ ।। 

kaṇṭhe tyāgo bhavettasya makāro rudravācakaḥ 
tālumadhye tyajettaṃ tu binduścaiveśvaraḥ svayam ।। 

tyāgastatra bhruvormadhye nāde vācyaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
lalāṭānmūrdhaparyantaṃ tyāgastasya vidhīyate ।। 

śaktivyāpinīsamanās tāsāṃ vācyaḥ śivo avyayaḥ 
mūrdhamadhye tyajecchaktiṃ tadūrdhve vyāpinīṃ tyajet ।। 

samanāṃ unmanāṃ tyaktvā ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
sūkṣmasūkṣmatarairbhāvair evamevaṃ tyajetpriye ।। 

sthūlasthūlatarairbhāvair nānāsiddhiphalapradaiḥ 
sūkṣmo atyantaṃ paro bhāvas tv abhāvaḥ sa vidhīyate ।। 

unmanā tvaparo bhāvaḥ sthūlastasyāparo mataḥ 
tasyāparaṃ punaḥ śūnyaṃ saṃsparśaṃ ca tato aparam ।। 

śabdo jyotiḥ tato mantrāḥ kāraṇā bhuvanāni ca 
pañcabhūtātmabhuvanaṃ kāraṇaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitam ।। 

bhuvanaṃ cintayedyastu vakṣyamāṇaikarūpakam 
bhuvaneśatvamāpnoti śivaṃ dhyātvā tu tanmayaḥ ।। 

brahmādikāraṇānāṃ ca sādhane vigrahaṃ smaran 
pūrvoktalakṣaṇaṃ yaśca tanmayatvamavāpnuyāt ।। 

mantriśca mantrasiddhistu japahomārcanādbhavet 
pūrvoktarūpakadhyānāt siddhyantyatra na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

jyotirdhyānāttu yogīndro yogasiddhimavāpnuyāt 
tanmayatvaṃ yadāpnoti yogināmadhipo bhavet ।। 

śabdadhyānācca śabdātmā vāṅmayāpūrako bhavet 
sparśadhyānācca sparśātmā jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet ।। 

śūnyadhyānācca śūnyātmā vyāpī sarvagato bhavet 
samanadhyānayogena yogī sarvajñatāṃ vrajet ।। 

unmanyā tu paraṃ sūkṣmam abhāvaṃ bhāvayetsadā 
sarvendriyamanotītas tv alakṣyo abhāva ucyate ।। 

abhāvaṃ bhāvyaṃ bhāvena bhāvaṃ kṛtvā nirāśrayam 
sarvopādhivinirmuktam abhāvaṃ labhate padam ।। 

eṣa te kāraṇatyāgaḥ kālatyāgaṃ nibodha me 
tuṭiṣoḍaśasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇastu samudāhṛtaḥ ।। 

tuṭadvayaṃ samāśritya ekaiko bhairavaḥ sthitaḥ 
ahorātravibhāgena kurvantyudayameva te ।। 

navamastu paro devaḥ tejasastūdayanti te 
sarvaṃ kālaṃ tyajetprāṇe yathāvatkathayāmi te ।। 

tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśaivoktāḥ kālasya karaṇaṃ tu tāḥ 
tadādiḥ saṃsthitaḥ kālaḥ sarvaṃ carati vāṅmayam ।। 

tuṭirlavo nimeṣaśca kāṣṭhā caiva kalā tathā 
muhūrtaścāpyahorātraḥ pakṣo māsa ṛtustathā ।। 

ayanaṃ vatsaraścaiva yugaṃ manvantaraṃ tathā 
kalpaścaiva mahākalpaḥ śaktyante taṃ parityajet ।। 

vyāpinyante paraḥ kālaḥ sa tadaṅgī tyajettu tam 
sa ca saptadaśo jñeyaḥ parārdhaparataḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

so api cāṣṭādaśo devi samanānte tu taṃ tyajet 
sarvakālaṃ tu kālasya vyāpakaḥ paramo avyayaḥ ।। 

unmanyante pare yojyo na kālastatra vidyate 
nityo nityodito vyāpī ādirūpaṃ na saṃtyajet ।। 

taṃ ca nityoditaṃ prāpya tanmayo jāyate sadā 
kālatyāgo bhavedevaṃ śūnyabhāvastvathocyate ।। 

ūrdhvaśūnyamadhaḥśūnyaṃ madhyaśūnyaṃ tṛtīyakam 
śūnyatrayaṃ calaṃ hyetat tadadho madhya ūrdhvataḥ ।। 

caturthaṃ vyāpinīśūnyaṃ samanāyāṃ ca pañcamam 
unmanāyāṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣaḍete sāmayāḥ sthitāḥ ।। 

tattvenādhiṣṭhitāḥ sarve sāmayā api siddhidāḥ 
ṣaṭ śūnyāni parityajya saptame tu layaṃ kuru ।। 

tacchūnyaṃ tu paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ sarvāvasthāvivarjitam 
aśūnyaṃ śūnyamityuktaṃ śūnyaṃ cābhāva ucyate ।। 

abhāvaḥ sa samuddiṣṭo yatra bhāvāḥ kṣayaṃ gatāḥ 
sattāmātraṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ tatpadaṃ kimapi sthitam ।। 

yatra yatra ca nādādisthūlā anye api saṃsthitāḥ 
tatra tatra paraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। 

tadeva bhavati sthūlaṃ sthūlopādhivaśātpriye 
sthūlasūkṣmaprabhedena tadekaṃ saṃvyavasthitam ।। 

tatprāpya tanmayatvaṃ ca labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śūnyabhāvaḥ samākhyātaḥ sāmarasyaṃ nibodha me ।। 

ātmanyekaḥ samaraso mantre jñeyo dvitīyakaḥ 
tṛtīyaṃ nāḍigaṃ kuryāc chaktau kuryāccaturthakam ।। 

vyāpinyāṃ pañcamaṃ proktaṃ samanāyāṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam 
tātvaḥ samaraso devi saptamastu vidhīyate ।। 

śiṣyātmānaṃ tu saṃgṛhya pūrvoktavidhinā kramāt 
paścādātmani saṃyojya lolībhūtaṃ vicintayet ।। 

pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā samānena nirodhayet 
yāvatyo nāḍayo devi tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥsthitāḥ ।। 

samānena samākṛṣṭā ekībhūtā bhavanti tāḥ 
tāsu ye vāyavaste api prāṇe samarasīgatāḥ ।। 

nāḍayastu suṣumnāyām ekībhūtā vyavasthitāḥ 
tato vai uccarenmantraḥ nāde līnaṃ vicintayet ।। 

mantra ātmā tathā nāḍī evaṃ samarasībhavet 
vāmadakṣiṇamadhye tu tato nādaṃ pramocayet ।। 

setubandhaṃ ca taṃ mārgaṃ yatra gatvā na jāyate 
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraḥ śiva eva ca ।। 

ete atra samatāṃ yānti anyathā tu pṛthak pṛthak 
tasminsamuccarennādaṃ yāvacchaktau layaṃ gataḥ ।। 

śaktimadhyagato nādaḥ śaktyātmā tu vidhīyate 
sarvaṃ śaktimayaṃ tatra sarvaṃ samarasībhavet ।। 

tadūrdhvaṃ vyāpinīṃ prāpya sarvaṃ tanmayatāṃ vrajet 
samantādvyāpnuyādyasmād vyāpinītyabhidhīyate ।। 

tadūrdhvaṃ samanāṃ vyāpya tanmayatvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ 
sā ca sarvagatā jñeyā sāmarasyena saṃsthitā ।। 

ṣaṣṭhaṃ samarasaṃ tyaktvā saptamaṃ tu tato vrajet 
taṃ prāpya tanmayatvaṃ hi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

sa ca sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhāvatatvendriyeṣu ca 
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva cetanācetanasthitam ।। 

adhvānaṃ vyāpya sarvaṃ tu sāmarasyena saṃsthitaḥ 
prasahya cañcalītyeva yogināmapi yanmanaḥ ।। 

yasya jñeyamayo bhāvaḥ sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ 
mano na calate tasya sarvāvasthāgatasya tu ।। 

yatra yatra mano yāti jñeyaṃ tatraiva cintayet 
calitvā yāsyate kutra sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ ।। 

viṣayeṣu ca sarveṣu indriyārtheṣu ca sthitaḥ 
yatra yatra nirūpyeta nāśivaṃ vidyate kvacit ।। 

evāṃ samarasaṃ jñātvā nāsau muhyet kadācana 
yasyaivaṃ sarvato bhāvaḥ so api sarvagato bhavet ।। 

evaṃ samarasaḥ prokto viṣuvattu nibodha me 
prathamaṃ prāṇaviṣuvan mātraṃ jñeyaṃ dvitīyakam ।। 

tṛtīyaṃ nāḍiviṣuvat praśāntaṃ ca caturthakam 
pañcamaṃ śaktiviṣuvat ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai kāla ucyate ।। 

saptama tattvaviṣuvat pravibhāgastvathocyate 
ātmānaṃ ca manaḥ prāṇe saṃyojya viṣuvadbhavet ।। 

prāṇe viṣuvadākhyātaṃ māntraṃ viṣuvaducyate 
mantramuccārayettāvad yāvannānyamanā bhavet ।। 

parāparavibhāgena mantrātmā tu taducyate 
māntraṃ viṣuvadityuktaṃ nāḍisthaṃ tannibodha me ।। 

sarvāsāmeva nāḍīnāṃ madhye yā saṃvyavasthitā 
suṣumnā nāma sā jñeyā nābheḥ śaktyā śivaṃ gatā ।। 

tatra pravāhayennādaṃ nāḍīviṣuvaducyate 
praśāntaṃ viṣuvaccaivam adhunā kathayāmi te ।। 

ayane ṣaḍaṅgulaścāraḥ kāraṇānyaṅgule aṅgule 
tānyadhastātparityajya kāraṇāni ṣaḍeva tu ।। 

saptame tu praśāntaṃ vai praśāntendriyagocaram 
praśāntaḥ stimito jñeyaḥ stimito niścalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

niścalo nistaraṅgaśca sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ 
evaṃbhāvaṃ samāsthāya dīkṣā kāryā tu daiśikaiḥ ।। 

etatpraśāntaviṣuvat śaktyupādhiṃ nibodha me 
śaktimadhyagato nādo nādordhvaṃ ca caredyadā ।। 

tāvattu śaktiviṣuvat kālākhyaṃ tu nibodha me 
tuṭiḥ ṣoḍaśakā yā tu prāṇānte saṃvyavasthitā ।। 

kālo bhrūkṣepamātrastu tatrānte kīrtito mayā 
taṃ parāparabhāgena punareva tridhā kuru ।। 

aparaḥ ṣoḍaśo yāvat kālaḥ saptadaśaḥ paraḥ 
parāparastu yaḥ kālaḥ sa priye aṣṭādaśaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

prāṇa evaṃ tridhā kālaṃ kṛtvā caiva tyajetpunaḥ 
aparaḥ śaktimūrdhastho vyāpinyāṃ ca dvitīyakaḥ ।। 

tṛtīyaḥ samanāsthāne tatkālaviṣuvatsmṛtam 
etatṣaṣṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ saptamaṃ tātvvamucyate ।। 

unmanā parato devi tatrātmānaṃ niyojayet 
tasminyuktastato hyātmā tanmayaśca prajāyate ।। 

tattvākhyaṃ viṣuvaddevi sarveṣāṃ parataḥ sthitam 
viṣuvadevaṃvidhaṃ jñātvā ko na mucyeta bandhanāt ।। 

viṣuvatte samākhyātaṃ padārthabhedanaṃ śṛṇu 
tyāgaṃ cānubhavaṃ caiva yojanaṃ ca pare pade ।। 

padārthaikādaśī jñeyā unmanāntaḥ paro bhavet 
bhedayejjñānaśūlena jñānaṃ jñeyasya jñāpakam ।। 

jñāpakaṃ bodhamatulaṃ dīpavadyotanaṃ yataḥ 
dīpahasto yathā kaścid dravyamālokya cāharet ।। 

evaṃ jñānena ca jñeyaṃ tasmin kuryāttu saṃsthitam 
jñānaṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ jñeyatatvasya suvrate ।। 

lakṣaṇaṃ guṇa ākhyātaḥ kalā tattvasya sarvadā 
na guṇena vinā tattvaṃ na tattvena vinā guṇaḥ ।। 

guṇaṃ gṛhṇanti sarvatra na tattvaṃ gṛhyate kvacit 
gṛhyate hyanumānena pratyakānubhavena ca ।। 

arthipratyarthibhāvena āgamena tu labhyate 
āgamo jñānamiyuktam anantāḥ śāstrakoṭayaḥ ।। 

śāstraṃ śabdātmakaṃ sarvaṃ śabdo haṃsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
haṃsayogaḥ purākhyātaḥ mātrāsaṃkhyā tvathocyate ।। 

mātrāyogo yathā cāsya pramāṇaṃ hṛdayādisu 
nābherūrdhvaṃ vitastyante kaṇṭhādhastātṣaḍaṅgule ।। 

hṛdayaṃ madhyadeśe tu caturaṅgulasaṃmitam 
caturviṃśatitattvaistu brahmā tatra vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

kaṇṭhamaṣṭāṅgulaṃ viddhi viṣṇustatra vyavasthitaḥ 
tattvāṣṭakena saṃyuktaḥ tadūrdhvaṃ caturaṅgulam ।। 

māyātattvaṃ samāśritya rudrastālutale sthitaḥ 
aṅguladvayamānaṃ tu bhruvormadhyaṃ prakīrtitam ।। 

tatreśvaraḥ sthito devi tattvadvayasamanvitaḥ 
ekādaśāṅgule caiva mūrdhvaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।। 

tattvadvayasamāyukto yāvadbrahmabilaṃ gataḥ 
tadūrdhvaikāṅgulā śaktiḥ śivastatra vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

tvakcheṣe vyāpinī proktā samanā conmanā tataḥ 
tatparaṃ tu paraṃ tattvaṃ pramāṇaparivarjitam ।। 

mātrāsaṃkhyā ca yogaścādhunā haṃsasya kathyate 
akāraśca hakāraśca dvāvetāvekataḥ sthitau ।। 

vibhaktirnānayorasti mārutāmbarayoriva 
ekamātraḥ sa vijñeyo hṛdayātsaṃpravartate ।। 

ukārastu dvimātro vai kaṇṭhasthāne samuccaret 
trimātrastu makāro vai tālumadhyagataścaret ।। 

binduścaivārdhamātrastu mātrārdhaṃ hi sa ucyate 
bhruvormadhye sa uccāras tasya devi vidhīyate ।। 

taccheṣāccārdhacandrastu pādamātrastvasau bhavet 
nirodhī cārdhapādastu lalāṭānte samuccaret ।। 

nādaḥ ṣoḍaśakāṃśastu mūrdhāntaṃ yāvaduccaret 
dvātriṃśadaṃśā śaktistu ṣaṭtriṃśānte samuccaret ।। 

vyāpinī catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśā śaktestu parataḥsthitā 
samanā conmanā cordhvam amātraḥ paramo avyayaḥ ।। 

mātrāsaṃkhyā ca yogaśca pramāṇaṃ parikīrtitam 
evaṃ jñātvā varārohe padārthān bhedayettataḥ ।। 

bhedayenmatraśūlena mudrābhāvayutena ca 
mantro vai jñānaśaktiśca mudrā caiva kriyātmikā ।। 

bhāvaśca mana ityuktaṃ tanmano buddhipūrvakam 
paraśca manasā gamya icchāśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। 

yatra yatra bhavedicchā jñānaṃ tatra pravartate 
kriyākaraṇasaṃbandhāt tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ bhavet ।। 

kriyākaraṇahīnasya na caivoccāraṇaṃ bhavet 
kriyā karaṇabhedena sā caiva trividhā smṛtā ।। 

ekenoccārayettattvaṃ karaṇena vicakṣaṇaḥ 
nāḍīścātha dvitīyena dvārāṇi ca nirodhayet ।। 

tṛtīyaṃ karaṇaṃ divyaṃ kṛtvā vai tattvamuccaret 
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā sarvadvārāṇi rodhayet ।। 

gudadvāreṇa ruddhena ruddhānyatra bhavanti hi 
dvāramekaṃ tataścordhve pravahattadvicintayet ।। 

nāḍayo granthipadmāśca ye adhomukhagatāḥ priye 
te kumbhakena saṃruddhā vikasanti samantataḥ ।। 

karaṇaṃ tu tataḥ kṛtvā lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vai śṛṇu 
jihvā tu tāluke yojyā kiṃcidūrdhvaṃ na saṃspṛśet ।। 

īṣatprasārya vaktraṃ tu kiṃcidoṣṭhau na saṃspṛśet 
dantapaṅktī tathaiveha dṛṣṭiścādhordhvavarjitā ।। 

kāyaṃ samunnataṃ kṛtvā karaṇaṃ divyamucyate 
divyaṃ ca karaṇaṃ kṛtvā tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ kuru ।। 

kumbhitaścaiva yaḥ prāṇo recayettaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ 
nāḍayo granthipadmāśca dehe yāḥsaṃvyavasthitāḥ ।। 

recakena samākṣiptā ūrdhvasroto bhavanti te 
tato vai jñānaśūlena granthīnbhindan samuccaret ।। 

bhitvā hṛtpadmagranthiṃ tu tataḥ śabdaḥ prajāyate 
yadākāśasamāyogāt ghoṣaśabdopamo bhavet ।। 

kaṇṭhastho viramecchabdaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ prāpya varānane 
bhindataḥ kaṇṭhadeśaṃ tu śabdo dhugadhugāyate ।। 

tālumadhyagataḥ prāṇo yadā bhavati suvrate 
bindatastālugranthiṃ tu śabdo ghumaghumāyate ।। 

evaṃ te anubhavāḥ proktāḥ prāṇe carati suvrate 
trayaste aṣṭakalāḥ proktā uparyuparitaḥ kramāt ।। 

tiṣṭhetsa yatra vai prāṇa ātmā tadgatimāpnuyāt 
tattadrūpaṃ bhavettasya sthānabhāvānurūpataḥ ।। 

bhruvormadhyaṃ yadā gacchet sphoṭaśabdastu jāyate 
binduṃ bhedayato devi śabdo dhumadhumāyate ।। 

kapirvai nārikīlena ācāryaḥ saha bindunā 
abhinnena kuto mokṣaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ priye ।। 

bhitvā binduṃ tato devi ardhacandraṃ vibhedayet 
bhidyataścārdhacandrasya lalāṭe jhimijhimāyate ।। 

ardhacandraṃ tu bhittvā vai bhedayettu nirodhinīm 
tasyāstu bhidyamānāyāḥ śabdaḥ simisimāyate ।। 

sthanatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam 
prāṇasya caratastatra yasminsthāne sa tiṣṭhati ।। 

tattadrūpo bhavedātmā tāṃ tāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt 
nirodhinīṃ bhedayitvā tato nādaṃ vrajedbudhaḥ ।। 

vaṃśaśabdasamaḥ śabdas tatra sūkṣmaḥ prajāyate 
bhedayennādasaṃsthānaṃ brahmarandhraṃ sudurbhidam ।। 

bhidyato brahmarandhrasya śabdaḥ śumaśumāyate 
śaktimadhyagataḥ prāṇo vaṃśanādāntasaṃnibhaḥ ।। 

tāṃ vai tu bhedayecchaktiṃ durbhedyāṃ sarvayoginām 
bhidyate ca yadā śaktiḥ śāntaḥ śumaśumastataḥ ।। 

śaktiṃ bhitvā tato devi yaccheṣaṃ vyāpinī bhavet 
anubhāvo bavettatra sparśo yadvatpipīlikā ।। 

sthānatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam 
yatra yatra caretprāṇas tattadrūpamavāpnuyāt ।। 

yatra yatrāvatiṣṭheta tāṃ tāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt 
tasmādvai suprayatnena bhitvā yāti parāṃ gatim ।। 

bhitvā vai vyāpinīṃ devi samanāyāṃ manastyajet 
manasā tu manastyaktvā jīvaḥ kevalatāṃ vrajet ।। 

jīvo vai kevalastatra ātmajñānakriyānvitaḥ 
bandhanāśeṣanirmuktaḥ sattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ ।। 

samastādhvapadātītaḥ śuddhavijñānakevalaḥ 
gṛhāṇāti nāparaṃ bhāvaṃ na paraṃ ca śivātmakam ।। 

parāparavinirmuktaḥ svātmanyātmā vyavasthitaḥ 
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptirataḥ param ।। 

bandhanāśeṣabhāvena sarvādhvopādhivarjitā 
aviditvā paraṃ tattvaṃ śivatvaṃ kalpitaṃ tu yaiḥ ।। 

ta ātmopāsakāḥ śaive na gacchanti paraṃ śivam 
ātmatattvagatiṃ yānti ātmatattvānurañjitāḥ ।। 

tasmādātmā parityājyo yadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ 
ātmatattvaṃ tatastyājyaṃ vidyātatve niyojayet ।। 

unmanā sā tu vijñeyā manaḥ saṃkalpa ucyate 
saṃkalpaḥ kramato jñānam unmānaṃ yugapatsthitam ।। 

tasmāt sā tu parā vidyā yasmādanyā na vidyate 
vindate hyatra yugapat sārvajñyādiguṇān parān ।। 

vedanānādidharmasya paramātmatvabodhanā 
varjanā paramātmatve tasmādvidyeti socyate ।। 

tatrastho vyañjayettejaḥ paraṃ paramakāraṇam 
parasmiṃstejasi vyakte tatrasthaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet ।। 

supradīpte yathā vahnau śikhā dṛśyeta cāmbare 
dehaprāṇasthito hyātmā tadvallīyeta tatpade ।। 

tadvadevābhimānastu kartavyo daiśikottamaiḥ 
ahameva paro haṃsaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

matprāṇe sa tu paśvātmā līnaḥ samarasīgataḥ 
mantrakaraṇakriyāyogād yojayāmi pare śive ।। 

evaṃ yo vetti tattvena agnivaddehamadhyataḥ 
yadvadvahniśikhātītā tadvadyojayate pare ।। 

tasminyuktaḥ pare tattve sārvajñyādiguṇānvitaḥ 
śiva eko bhaveddevi avibhāgena sarvataḥ ।। 

tattvatrayaṃ paraṃ khyātam aparaṃ cādhvamadhyagam 
bhedanaṃ tu padārthānāṃ tyāgānubhavayojanam ।। 

pūrvoktaṃ ca idaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā tattve niyojayet 
saṃkṣepeṇa tu tattvasya vyāptiṃ śṛṇu sureśvari ।। 

vidyātattvāspadaṃ baddhvā bindutattvāsane sthitaḥ 
nādaśaktitanuścaiva vyāpinīkaraṇānvitaḥ ।। 

sarvajñatvāvabodhena samanāntaścarā tu sā 
tritatvaṃ yatparaṃ proktaṃ tena cāpūritā tanuḥ ।। 

aparā sā tanuḥ sthūlā ṣaṭviṃśattattvakalpitā 
tattvatrayaṃ paraṃ yacca sarvatattvādhvavarjitam ।। 

tena cāpūritāśeṣaṃ sā tattvādhvaparā tanuḥ 
evamācarate yastu ācāraṃ tu śivātmakam ।। 

śivena sahacāritvād ācāryastena cocyate 
tasya darśanasaṃbhāṣāsparśanātsmaraṇādapi ।। 

bhavatyevaiśvarī vyāptir na bhavettadadhogatiḥ 
tena saṃyojito jantuḥ brahmahāpi śivo bhavet ।। 

tatastena samo nāsti jagatyasmiṃścarācare 
śiva ācāryarūpeṇa lokānugrahakārakaḥ ।। 

tasmānna mānavīṃ buddhiṃ kārayeddeśakaṃ prati 
ācāryasya ca mantrasya śivajñāne śivasya ca ।। 

nānātvaṃ naiva kurvanti vidyeśāścakranāyakāḥ 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā vai vīravandite ।। 

ācāryatve niyuktā ye te sarve tu śivāḥ smṛtāḥ 
anyathā prāksvarūpeṇa ye paśyanti narādhamāḥ ।। 

narake te prapacyante sādākhyaṃ vatsaratrayam 
na tena saha saṃbhāṣā kartavyā tu śivārthinā ।। 

kṛtvā saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ tena narakaṃ so api gacchati 
tasmācchivasamāḥ sarve draṣṭavyā muktimicchatā ।। 

bhuktimuktiphalāvāptir bhavatyeva tadājñayā 
ācāryaḥ svajānānāṃ ca kulakoṭisahasraśaḥ ।। 

jñānajñeyaparijñānāt samastāstārayiṣyati 
evamuktavidhānajño bhāvajñaścāpi daiśikaḥ ।। 

pūrṇāhutyaikayaivāsau paśūnyojayate pare 
pūrṇāhutiprayogaṃ tu kathayāmyadhunā tava ।। 

ūrdhvakāya ṛjugrīvaḥ samapādo vyavasthitaḥ 
nābhisthāne sruco mūlam uttānāgramukhaṃ samam ।। 

srucyupari sruvaṃ devi kṛtvā caivamadhomukham 
puṣpaṃ dattvā srugagre tu darbheṇa sahitau karau ।। 

muṣṭinā caiva hastābhyāṃ gṛhītvā yatnato api ca 
agrato dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ vai pṛṣṭataḥ priye ।। 

muṣṭibhyāṃ saṃgṛhītvā vai uttānakarayogataḥ 
tato ghṛtena saṃplāvya abhimānaṃ tu kārayet ।। 

ahameva paraṃ tattvaṃ parāparavibhāgataḥ 
tattvamekaṃ hi sarvatra nānyaṃ bhāvaṃ tu kārayet ।। 

yatkumbhe adhvātra vinyastaḥ ṣaṭprakāro varānane 
maṇḍale agnau śiśorantaḥ sādhāraṇavikalpitaḥ ।। 

srucyadhvānaṃ tamāropya prāṇasthaṃ nāḍimadhyagam 
prāṇadhāre samīkṛtya srucā dhārāṃ vinikṣipet ।। 

vasudhāraprayogeṇa prakṣipejjātavedasi 
nābhisthāne sruco mūlaṃ nayannāsāntagocaram ।। 

yathā yathā tyajeddhārāṃ tathā prāṇaṃ samuccaret 
prāṇo api varṇatāṃ yāti ṣaḍvidhādhvamayastu saḥ ।। 

ṣaḍvidhedhvani nāto anyaḥ prameyo vidyate kvacit 
tasmānmāntre parāmarśe heyopādeyataḥ sthitāḥ ।। 

varṇaiḥ kāraṇaṣaṭkaṃ tu ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca ।। 

ardhacandro nirodhī ca nādaścaivordhvagāminī 
śaktiśca vyāpinī hyetāḥ samanā ca tataḥ param ।। 

samanāntaṃ varārohe pāśajālamanantakam 
kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhirākrāntaṃ mantrasthaṃ heyalakṣaṇam ।। 

atra pāśopari hyātmā vyomavadbindu[ccitsu]nirmalaḥ 
śivatattvaguṇāmodāc chivadharmāvalokakaḥ ।। 

pāśāvalokanaṃ tyaktvā svarūpālokanaṃ hi yat 
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptistato anyathā ।। 

sarvajñyādiguṇā ye arthā vyāpakānbhāvayedyadā 
śivavyāptirbhavedeṣā caitanye heturūpiṇī ।। 

ato dharmisvabhāvo hi śivaḥ śāntaśca paṭhyate 
unmanāśca manogrāhyaḥ ātmabodhe sthitonmanāḥ ।। 

vyāpāraṃ mānasaṃ tyaktvā bodharūpeṇa yojayet 
tadā śivatvamāyāti paśurmukto bhavārṇavāt ।। 

pare caiva niyuktasya sruvamāpūrayetpunaḥ 
sruco randhreṇa taddravyaṃ yāvadvahnau prayujyate ।। 

bahisthāṃ kumbhakaṃ tāvat pare tattve tu bhāvayet 
bahirnirodhabhāvena sāmarasyaṃ śivena ca ।। 

anyathā na bhaveddevi nadīvega ivārṇave 
sthitaḥ sa sāgaredbhistu sindhuḥ samarasībhavet ।। 

punarvibhāgaṃ nāpnoti tathātmā tu śivārṇave 
srucastu pūraṇaṃ yāvat tāvatkālaṃ samādiśet ।। 

anenaiva tu kālena bahiḥ kumbhakavṛttinā 
ātmā samarasatvena śivībhavati sarvagaḥ ।। 

guṇānāpādayetpaścāt ṣaṭ aṅgaparimāhutīn 
yathā nṛpatve saṃprāpte kalaśaiścābhiṣicyate ।। 

vandibhiśca guṇāste api khyāpyante vasudhātale 
tathā śivatve saṃprāpte guṇānāpādayedbudhaḥ ।। 

sarvajño vai bhava svāhā paritṛptastathaiva ca 
anādibodho bhava ca tataḥ svātantryaśaktikaḥ ।। 

tathā tvaluptaśaktiścānantaśaktistataḥ punaḥ 
guṇānāpādya sarvāṃstān mūlamantramanusmaret ।। 

oṃhūmātmapadopetaṃ sarvajñāyetyapaścimam 
svāhākāraprayogeṇa āhutīḥ pratipādayet ।। 

tisraḥ pañca daśaikā vā tilairvātha ghṛtena vā 
dadyāt tato abhiṣekaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa suvrate ।। 

paraṃ śaktyamṛtaṃ kṣobhya śiṣyamūrdhni nipātayet 
turyadvāraṃ viśettaddhi sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret ।। 

mantraśaktibhirugrābhiḥ śeṣanirdahanādibhiḥ 
śarīraṃ śoṣyate tābhis tadarthamabhiṣecanam ।। 

dīkṣānirvartanātpūrvaṃ puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet 
darbhaṃ vimocayitvā ca śivāgnau kalaśe gurau ।। 

pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍavannipatedbhuvi 
kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā bhavottīrṇaḥ sunirmalaḥ ।। 

protphullanayanaḥ śāntas tṛptātmānaṃ tu bhāvayet 
iyaṃ nairvāṇakī dīkṣā nirbījā vā sabījikā ।। 

yeṣāṃ sabījikā dīkṣā kuryātteṣvabhiṣecanam 
śrutaśīlasamācārān deśakatve niyojayet ।। 

athābhiṣeka ācārye śivayogādanantaram 
pañcabhiḥ kalaśairbhadre sitacandanalepitaiḥ ।। 

śivakumbhavadabhyarcya ratnagarbhāmbupūritaiḥ 
ṛddhivṛddhyādibhiḥ pūtair oṣadhyakṣatapūritaiḥ ।। 

sitapadmamukhodgāraiś cūtapallavasaṃyutaiḥ 
pṛthivyādīni tattvāni pañca pañcasu vinyaset ।। 

kalaśeṣu mahādevi punaścaiva kalā nyaset 
nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāḥ pañca teṣu caivātra vinyaset ।। 

ekaikakalaśo vyāpyo hy anantādiśivāntakaḥ 
pūjayedbhairavaṃ devaṃ sarvasaṃbhārakaiḥ kramāt ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgāvaraṇopetaṃ mantrasaṃdhānasaṃyutam 
bhairaveṇābhimantreta ekaikaṃ kalaśaṃ priye ।। 

aṣṭottaraśatenaiva paratattvamanusmaran 
vāruṇyāṃ saumyayamyāyam endryāmaiśyāṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

saṃpūjyaivaṃ vidhānena abhiṣekaṃ samācaret 
yāgaharmyasya aiśānyāṃ pīṭhaṃ saṃkalpyayebudhaḥ ।। 

tatra maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā svastikādivibhūṣitam 
vitānoparisaṃchannaṃ dhvajaiśca pariśobhitam ।। 

tatrāsanaṃ nyaseddevi śrīparṇīcandanodbhavam 
tatrānantāsanaṃ nyasya mūrtibhūtaṃ śiśuṃ nyaset ।। 

pūrvavatsakalīkṛtya aiśānyabhimukhaṃ sthitam 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya nirbhartsyaḥ kāñcikaudanaiḥ ।। 

mṛdbhasmagomayaiḥ piṇḍair dūrvāṅkurasamāśritaiḥ 
siddhārthadadhitoyaiśca nirājanasamanvitaiḥ ।। 

nirbhartsyaivaṃ vidhānena abhiṣekaṃ pradāpayet 
pṛthivyādighaṭāsayirvā dhāmānusmṛtya secayet ।। 

kramāddhyātvā kalaśeṣu ācāryaḥ susamāhitaḥ 
abhiṣikto anyavāsastu paridhāpyācanettataḥ ।। 

praviśya dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtiṃ yogapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet 
saṃsthāpya sakalīkṛtya adhikāraṃ prakalpayet ।। 

uṣṇīṣaṃ mukuṭādyāṃśca chatraṃ pādukamāsanam 
hastyaśvaśivikādyāṃśca rājāṅgāni hyaśeṣataḥ ।। 

karaṇīṃ kartarīṃ khaṭikāṃ sruksruvau darbhapustakam 
akṣasūtrādikaṃ dattvā caturāśramasaṃsthitāḥ ।। 

dīkṣyānugrahamārgeṇa dīkṣā vyākhyā tvayā sadā 
adyaprabhṛti kartavyety adhikāraḥ śivājñayā ।। 

utthāpya hastau saṃgṛhya maṇḍale tu praveśayet 
jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā saṃpūjya bhairavaṃ tataḥ ।। 

vijñāpya bhagavannevam abhiṣiktastvadājñayā 
ācāryapadasaṃsthena tavānujñāvidhāyinā ।। 

kartavyaṃ yattadāyātam adhikāraṃ tu deśake 
śivatattvārthakathanaṃ śivasya purataḥ shitaḥ ।। 

nirgatya bhavanādaganau kalādhvānaṃ tu homayet 
mantratarpaṇakaṃ kṛtvā kalānāṃ pañca cāhutīḥ ।। 

pañca pañcasu sarvāsu hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ guruḥ 
arghapūjādikaṃ kṛtvā praṇamya khyāpayetprabhoḥ ।। 

abhiṣikto mayācāryas tadarthaṃ mantratarpaṇam 
hṛdādyaiḥ pañcabhiścāṅgair dakṣiṇaṃ lāñchayetkaram ।। 

darbholmukaṃ śivāgnau tu kānīyasyādi lāñchayet 
puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradadyāttu maṇḍalāgnau prapātayet ।। 

bhairavaṃ kalaśaṃ cāgniṃ namaskṛtya tu daṇḍavat 
labdhādhikāro hṛṣṭātmā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalānvitaḥ ।। 

sa guruḥ śivatulyastu śivadhāmaphalapradaḥ 
śāntyante bhūtidīkṣā ca sadāśivapadātmikā ।। 

śivadharmiṇyasau jñeyā lokadharmiṇyatoṇyathā 
śivadharmiṇyasau yeṣāṃ sādhakānāṃ prakīrtitā ।। 

teṣāṃ kṛtvābhiṣekaṃ tu sādhakatve niyojayet 
sādhakasyābhiṣeko ayaṃ vidyādīkṣāta uttaraḥ ।। 

vidyādīkṣā bhavetsā tu vāsanābhedataḥ sthitā 
karmabhedo na vidyeta sarvatrādhvani saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

kṛtāni yāni karmāṇi sarvāṇyadhvagatāni tu 
tāni saṃśodhya vidhivat kalāpañcasthitāni tu ।। 

yojanyavasare bhedo vimarśaḥ sādhakasya tu 
prārabdaṃ karma pāścātyaṃ na caikasthaṃ tu bhāvayet ।। 

sādhakasya tu bhūtyarthaṃ prāk karmaikaṃ tu śodhayet 
dhāma proccārya sakalaṃ sadāśivatanau nyaset ।। 

vidyādehasvarūpeṇa dhyātvā devaṃ sadāśivam 
pūrṇāhutiprayogena aṇimādiguṇairyutam ।। 

aṇimādiguṇāvāptau mūlamantrasvasaṃjñayā 
aṣṭāvevāhutīrdattvā abhiṣiñcettu sādhakam ।। 

kalaśaiḥ pañcabhiḥ kuryāt nivṛtyādyāstriṣu nyaset 
śāntyatītāṃ pañcame ca śāntiṃ paścāccaturthake ।। 

śāntyā tu saṃpuṭīkṛtya pṛthivyādyaiśca pañcabhiḥ 
ekaikakalaśe paścāt sādhyamantraṃ tu vinyaset ।। 

vidyāṅgaiḥ sakalīkṛtya vidyāṅgāvaraṇaṃ nyaset 
saṃmantryāṣṭaśatenaiva ekaikaṃ kalaśaṃ tataḥ ।। 

bahirmaṇḍalake nyasya āsanaṃ praṇavena tu 
sādhakaṃ tatra saṃsthāpya sakalīkaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। 

nirbhatsya pūrvavatsarvaiḥ sādhyamantreṇa secayet 
nivṛtyāditribhiḥ kumbhaiḥ snāpayetpūrvadiṅmukham ।। 

śāntyatītaṃ ghaṭaṃ paścād gṛhītvā secayecchiśum 
śāntiṃ paścāttu gṛhṇīyāt saṃpuṭenābhiṣecayet ।। 

sādhakasyābhiṣeko ayam anulomavilomataḥ 
abhiṣicya praveśyainaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtimāsthitam ।। 

praṇavenāsanaṃ dattvā sakalīkaraṇaṃ bhavet 
sādhakasyādhikārārtham akṣamālādi kalpayet ।। 

mantrakalpākṣasūtraṃ ca khaṭikāṃ chatrapāduke 
uṣṇīṣarahitaṃ datvā praviśya śivasaṃnidhau ।। 

vijñāpya parameśānaṃ sādhako ayaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ 
bhūyātsiddhistvadājñātas triprakārasya bhaktitaḥ ।। 

sādhyamantraṃ dadetpaścāt puṣpodakasamanvitam 
tasya haste samarpyeta siddhyarthaṃ sādhakasya tu ।। 

praṇamyobhau gṛhītvā tu mantraṃ hṛdi niveśayet 
prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ śiṣyo guruścāpi praharṣavān ।। 

agnyāgāre sāvadhānau tarpayenmantrasaṃhitām 
sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vāpi sādhyamantrasya tarpaṇam ।। 

evaṃ saṃtarpayitvā tu puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet 
tristhaṃ saṃpūjya devaṃ tu tato api triḥpradakṣiṇam ।। 

praṇamya bhaktiyuktātmā aṇimādiphalaṃ labhet 
utthāpya sādhakaṃ brūyāt samayānpāhi yatnataḥ ।। 

dīkṣāvasāne te devi śrāvaṇīyā vipaścitā 
evaṃ dīkṣāṃ tu nirvartya sarvadaiva varānane ।। 

ātmatyāgaḥ prakartavyo yathā bhavati tacchruṇu 
vaijñānakī prākṛtī vā ācāryasya yadṛcchayā ।। 

vaijñānikīṃ susūkṣmāṃ tu vidhinānena kārayet 
tilājyādisamāyuktā adhvavāgīśikalpanā ।। 

kalābhiḥ pañcabhirvyāptam adhvānaṃ yugapannyaset 
pūjāhomopacārādyān kṛtvātmānaṃ niyojayet ।। 

śiṣyacaitanyavat yogād adhvānaṃ yugapannyaset 
puṣpādyaiḥ pūjayitvā taṃ yogārthamāhutitrayam ।। 

garbhadhāritvajanane arjane bhogatallaye 
yugapaddhomayeddevi mūlamantreṇa suvrataḥ ।। 

āhutīnāṃ trayaṃ homyaṃ pratikarma varānane 
hotavyā niṣkṛtirbhinnā pañcasthānakalātmasu ।। 

śatamekaṃ tadarthaṃ vā niṣkṛtiḥ parikīrtitā 
viśleṣapāśacchedādye dhāmnaiva yugapaddhutiḥ ।। 

uddhāre cātmatattvasthe pūrṇāhutiṃ tu pātayet 
ātmānaṃ yojayettattve śive paramakāraṇe ।। 

guṇān pūrvavadāpādya amṛtānpūrvavat kuru 
ātmadīkṣā samāptau tu prāyaścittanivṛttaye ।। 

atha vijñānarūpeṇa sakṛduccāralakṣaṇā 
heyopādeyapāśānāṃ yugapadbhairaveṇa tu ।। 

śāśvatī saṃsthitiḥ paścāt sūkṣmadīkṣā prakīrtitā 
viśeṣapūjanaṃ homaṃ yathāśakti prakalpayet ।। 

vādyagītasunṛtyādyaiḥ stutibhiḥ pūjayeddharam 
triḥ pradakṣiṇamāvartya kalaśāgnisamaṇḍalam ।। 

aṣṭāṅgapatanaṃ kṛtvā vijñapetparameśvaram 
bhagavanpaśuhetvarthaṃ yenmayāvāhito bhavān ।। 

tatkṣantavyaṃ sadā deva vidhisthasya mama prabho 
vidhinyūnamakāmasya pūjā śāstoditā yathā ।। 

na bhavedatibhūyiṣṭhā prākṛtairdravyasaṃcayaiḥ 
avalambya bhaktimātraṃ vidhānaṃ yatkṛtaṃ mayā ।। 

tatsarvaṃ saphalaṃ me astu suprasanne vibho tvayi 
prasannavadano hṛṣṭo varaṃ dattaṃ vibhāvayet ।। 

upaviśya tato yāgaṃ saṃhareta kramāt priye 
agraṃ saṃprārthya gṛhṇīyāt sthāpayeccāstrarakṣitam ।। 

viśeṣapūjanaṃ cārdhaṃ praṇipātaṃ tataḥ punaḥ 
nirodhārdhaṃ tato gṛhya ardhaṃ savyāpasavyataḥ ।। 

datvā visarjayeddevaṃ dhāmamantramanusmaran 
ātmano recakaṃ kṛtvā puṣpaṃ devāya nikṣipet ।। 

saṃhāriṇyā ca saṃgṛhya mantrān pārśvavyavasthitān 
vidyudvaccalitān dhyātvā dhāmadehe tu vinyaset ।। 

vidyādehaṃ bhairavasya tallīnaṃ binduvigrahe 
binduṃ tu nādaśaktisthaṃ śaktirūpaṃ tu grāhayet ।। 

śaktirūpaṃ vyapakena praṇavobhayasaṃpuṭam 
saṃhāriṇyā tu saṃgṛhya dvādaśāte tu yojayet ।। 

pūrakeṇa hṛdi nyasya svasthānasthaṃ tu bhāvayet 
sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ rūpaṃ tathā sakalaniṣkalam ।। 

bhinnāvasthaṃ tu mantreṣu hṛtsthaṃ tatsaṃsmaretpriye 
visarjanavidhirhyevaṃ agnāvevaṃ prapūjayet ।। 

aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ prapātayet 
ardhāmācamanaṃ datvā praṇipatya kṣamāpayet ।। 

maṇḍalasthaprayogena recakāpūrakeṇa tu 
saṃgṛhya mantrasaṃghātaṃ yathāsthānaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

jāgarayettadāgniṃ tu nityakarmanimittataḥ 
nirmālyanayanaṃ kuryād rajāṃsyapaharetpriye ।। 

tataḥ praviśya vasudhāṃ prokṣayettaṃ śivāmbhasā 
bahirnirgatya bhūtānāṃ balikarma tu pūrvavat ।। 

ācamya sakalīkṛtya liṅginastarpayettataḥ 
guruṃ saṃpūjayecchiṣyo yathāvibhavavistaraiḥ ।। 

deśādhyakṣo grāmaśataṃ maṇḍaleśastadardhakam 
śatabhukpañca vai dadyād grāmaṃ viṃśatibhuktathā ।। 

dadyāttu grāmabhuk kṣetraṃ kṣetrabhoktā tu viṃśatim 
yena yena gurustuṣyet tatsarvaṃ vinivedayet ।। 

tatastvanṛṇatāṃ yāti vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
tatastu samayāñśrāvyas tantre bhairavanirgate ।। 

carukaṃ prāśayetpaścāc cumbakaḥ sādhakaiḥ saha 
vāṅniruddhaḥ prasannātmā pṛthak pātravyavasthitaḥ ।। 

anukrameṇa dātavyaḥ tataḥ siddhimavāpnuyāt 
anenaiva vidhānena dīkṣitā ye varānante ।। 

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdraścānye athavā priye 
sarve te samadharmāṇaḥ śivadharme niyojitāḥ ।। 

sarve jaṭādharāḥ proktā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ 
ekapaṅktibhujaḥ sarve samayinastu varānane ।। 

putrakāṇāṃ bhavedekā sādhakānāṃ tathā bhavet 
cumbakānāṃ bhavedekā na prāgjātivibhedataḥ ।। 

ekaiva sā smṛtā jātir bhairavīyā śivāvyayā 
tantrametatsamāśritya prāgjātiṃ na hyudīrayet ।। 

putrakāṇāṃ sādhakānāṃ tathā samayināmapi 
prāgjātyudīraṇāddevi prāyaścittī bhavennaraḥ ।। 

dinatrayaṃ tu rudrasya pañcāhaṃ keśavasya ca 
pitāmahasya pakṣaikaṃ narake pacyate tu saḥ ।। 

avivekī bhavettasmād yadīccheduttamāṃ gatim 
avivekena deveśi siddhirmuktirdhruvaṃ bhavet ।। 

svacchandatantre caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ

pañcamaḥ paṭalaḥ

kalādīkṣā sureśāna kathitā parameśvara 
tattvadīkṣā samāsena kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। 

samāsāt kathayiṣyāmi tvatpriyārthaṃ varānane 
ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamukhyāni yathā śodhyāni pārvati ।। 

pṛthivyādiśivāntāni svavyāptyānuguṇaiḥ saha 
yathā śuddhyānti deveśi tathā te kathayāmyaham ।। 

vidyārājasya ye varṇā navasaṃkhyopalakṣitāḥ 
vācakāste ca tattvānāṃ kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

dharitryādipradhānāntam ūkāro vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
puruṣasya yakāro vai rāgatattvānvitasya ca ।। 

niyāmikāṃ vakāreṇa vidyātattvasamanvitām 
kālaṃ kalāṃ lakāreṇa kalpayettu varānane ।। 

māyātattvaṃ makāreṇa vidyātattvaṃ kṣakārataḥ 
repheṇa caiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ hakāreṇa sadāśivaḥ ।। 

praṇavena tathā śaktir nyasitavyā varānane 
vyāpinīṃ samanāṃ cordhvaṃ tatraiva tu viśodhayet ।। 

śodhayitvā krameṇaiva mūlamantreṇa suvrate 
yojya ātmā pare tattve unmanātītasarvage ।। 

nirābhāse pare śānte īśāne cāvyaye tvaje 
ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamākhyātaṃ navatattvaṃ pracakṣmahe ।। 

prakṛtiḥ puruṣaścaiva niyatiḥ kāla eva ca 
māyā vidyā tatheśaśca sadāśivaśivau tathā ।। 

śodhayitvā tu vidhivad vyāptyātmānaṃ niyojayet 
pañcatattvī yadā śodhyā vaktramantrāstu vācakāḥ ।। 

dharitryādi khaparyantaṃ śodhayet tatkrameṇa tu 
kalānāṃ yāvatī vyāptis tattvānāṃ tāvadeva hi ।। 

tritattvamadhunā vakṣye yathā śodhyaṃ varānane 
akāra ātmatattvasya vācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

māyāntaṃ tadvijānīyāt vidyākhyasyāpyukārakaḥ 
sakalāvadhi tajjñeyaṃ śivasya tu makārakaḥ ।। 

khasvaraḥ khasvarūpasya śivatattvasya vācakaḥ 
śodhayitvā krameṇaiva pare tattve niyojayet ।। 

tattvadīkṣā samākhyātā caturbhedavyavasthitā 
paradīkṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

vidyārāje tu ye varṇā navasaṃkhyopalakṣitāḥ 
pṛthagbhedena teṣāṃ tu vinyāsaṃ kathayāmi te ।। 

navanābhaṃ puraṃ kṛtvā navapadmopalakṣitam 
navahastaṃ likhedveśma aṣṭaparvādhikaṃ budhaḥ ।। 

saptabhāgīkṛtaṃ tattu dakṣiṇottarabhājitam 
caturaśraṃ vibhajyādau matsyaiścaivātra cihnitam ।। 

koṣṭhakaikonapañcāśat sūtreṇa tu samālikhet 
madhyame koṣṭhake sūtraṃ dvātriṃśāṅgulasammitam ।। 

samālikhya mahādevi caturbhāgavibhājite 
prathame karṇikāṃ kuryāt kesarāṇi dvitīyake ।। 

tṛtīye dalasandhīṃśca dalāgrāṇi caturthake 
dikṣu rekhāṣṭakaṃ dattvā pratidikṣu tathaiva ca ।। 

bhrāmayeccaturo vṛttāṃś caturaṅgulasammitān 
dvābhyāṃ pratidigrekhābhyāṃ madhye sūtraṃ nidhāpya tat ।। 

sūtrāgraṃ tu tato bhrāmyam ardhacandravidhānataḥ 
madhyasūtraṃ ca dātavyaṃ kiñjalkasthaṃ vipaścitā ।। 

pūrvapatraṃ prasādhyavam itarāṇyevameva hi 
kesarāṇi ca saṃlikhya caturviṃśatisaṃkhyayā ।। 

patrāgrato nyasellekhāṃ vartulāṃ tu suśobhanām 
tasyāntaṃ caturaśraṃ tu kartavyaṃ tatpramāṇataḥ ।। 

pūrvaṃ brahma prasādhyaṃ tu viṣuvatsthena helinā 
pūrvapaścāttataṃ sūtraṃ śaṅkunā sādhayet priye ।। 

dvādaśāṅgulamānena madhye śaṅkuṃ praropya tam 
pārśveṣu bhrāmayedrekhāṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulasammitām ।। 

pūrvāhne grāhayecchāyām aparasthāṃ sucihnitām 
aparasthena sūryeṇa prākchāyāṃ lāñchayet priye ।। 

dhruveṇottaradakṣasthāṃ lāñchayettu varānane 
tataḥ samālikhet padmam aṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam ।। 

dikkoṣṭhakāṃśca saṃgṛhya aṣṭasaṃkhyopalakṣitam 
śeṣā lopyā varārohe ekāntaritayogataḥ ।। 

padmāṣṭakaṃ tato dikṣu bāhye dvārāṇi cālikhet 
vīthyardhasammitāṃ devi śobhāṃ caiva prakalpayet ।। 

upaśobhāṃ ca tanmānāṃ kapolāntaṃ samālikhet 
tathā kaṇṭhaṃ ca tanmānaṃ dvārametatprakīrtitam ।। 

dvārāṣṭakavibhāgena navanābhaṃ puraṃ smṛtam 
snātvā tu vidhivad devi praviśedbhavanaṃ guruḥ ।। 

pūrvoktena vidhānena sakalīkaraṇādikam 
tataḥ sampūjayeddevaṃ bhairavaṃ parameśvaram ।। 

praṇavenāsanaṃ dattvā śivāntaṃ varavarṇini 
madhye sampūjayeddevaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvaram ।। 

pūrvoktena vidhānena aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam 
patrāṣṭake nyasedvarṇān pūrvādīśāṃśtataḥ kramāt ।। 

sadāśivaṃ hakāreṇety evamādi varānane 
prakṛtyantaṃ vijānīyān madhye pīṭheśakalpanā ।। 

dikpadmakarṇikāsaṃsthān aṣṭau devān prapūjayet 
tatsthāne bhairavaḥ pūjyaḥ śeṣā varṇairyathākramam ।। 

śodhayecca prakṛtyādiśivāntaṃ surasundari 
īśānadiśa ārabhya madhyapīṭhaṃ viśodhayet ।। 

yojayettu pare tattve śive paramakāraṇe 
evaṃ varṇāstathā mantrān bhuvanāni viśodhayet ।। 

kālāgnyādi śivāntaṃ tu kalāvidhi samāśrayet 
samayān śrāvayetpaścāt tantrāmnāyotthitān priye ।। 

na nindedbhairavaṃ devaṃ śāstraṃ vānyasamudbhavam 
sāṃkhyaṃ yogaṃ pāñcarātraṃ vedāṃścaiva na nindayet ।। 

yataḥ śivodbhavāḥ sarve hy apavargaphalapradāḥ 
smārtaṃ dharmaṃ na nindettu ācārapathadarśakam ।। 

brahmādidevatā yāśca mātaraścumbako giriḥ 
vīrāścaiva bhaginyaśca gāvo bhūtagaṇāstathā ।। 

devadravyaṃ na hiṃsyāttu siddhānte yadvyavasthitam 
gurorannaṃ na bhuñjīta adattaṃ parameśvari ।। 

madyaṃ māṃsaṃ tathā matsyān anyāni ca varānane 
sācārāśca nirācārāṃl liṅgino na jugupsayet ।। 

carukaṃ prāśayannityaṃ gurūn sampūjayet sadā 
upaskarān mahādevi pādena tu na saṃspṛśet ।। 

saṃhitāṃ cintayennityaṃ bhaktānāṃ śrāvayet sadā 
āhnikaṃ na vilumpettu sandhyākarma varānane ।। 

adīkṣitānāṃ purato noccarecchāstrapaddhatim 
trikālaṃ pūjayeddevaṃ japadhyānarataḥ sadā ।। 

samayān pālayannityam ubhayārthaphalepsayā 
ato vijñānadīkṣāṃ tu pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

adhyātmagaticāreṇa kevalena viśodhikām 
śiṣyātmānaṃ gṛhītvā tam ātmaprāṇe niyojayet ।। 

abhimānaṃ tathoccārya kuryādvai pūrvavattadā 
udghātaiśca tato adhvānaṃ śiṣyasya tu viśodhayet ।। 

tataḥ samuccaraṃstattvaṃ pṛthivyādyaṃ tu suvrate 
bhinnābhinnasvarūpeṇa ekaikaṃ tu yathākramam ।। 

sasvaraṃ hyakṣaroccāraṃ devatābhiḥ samanvitam 
bindunā śaktisaṃyogād udghātaḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

devatātrayanirmuktaḥ caturthāntasamanvitaḥ 
udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

haṃsākṣarasamuccāraḥ sudīrgho bindusaṃyutaḥ 
ardhacandrānnirodhinyām udghātastu tṛtīyakaḥ ।। 

bhinnodghātau yadā devi nādāntastu tadā bhavet 
udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi caturthaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

sa eva cākṣaroccāro vyāpinyante vyavasthitaḥ 
udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi pañcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

pañcodghātāṃstato dattvā pṛthivīṃ śodhayedbudhaḥ 
akārokāramakārāntam evaṃ śuddhyati nānyathā ।। 

śuddhe atha pārthive tattve cintitavyaṃ tu yogibhiḥ 
jalībhūtaṃ tadevaitad ātmanā saha yogataḥ ।। 

jalībhūte punarmantrī tadeva caturuccaret 
bindvantaṃ dhāraṇāyuktaṃ śiṣyādātmani cintayet ।। 

śodhite toyasaṃghāte tejobhūtaṃ vicintayet 
tejodghātāstrayasteṣu nirodhyantamavasthitāḥ ।। 

nāsti tejastato vāyur udghātadvayaśodhitaḥ 
ākāśe līyamānaṃ tam udghātena tu cintayet ।। 

naṣṭe vāyau tataḥ śūnyam udghātaikena yojayet 
vyāpinī sā tu vijñeyā pañcamānte vyavasthitā ।। 

samanāyāṃ tato hyātmā tattvavyāpī sa ucyate 
ātmavyāpī tataścordhvaṃ sarvavyāpī tataḥ punaḥ ।। 

tattvāntasaṃsthito hyātmā udghātaikena yogavit 
yojayetparame tattve unmanātītasarvage ।। 

yojanāṃ tu pare tattve śṛṇu devi vadāmyaham 
mantramuccārayeddevi hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ param ।। 

parāparavibhāgena yāvattattvaṃ paraṃ gatam 
tridevaṃ bindusaṃyuktam ardhacandraṃ nirodhikām ।। 

nādaṃ ca śaktisaṃyuktaṃ vyāpinīsamanonmanāḥ 
unmanā ca paraścaiva sarvavyāpī śivo avyayaḥ ।। 

jñātvā sarvamaśeṣeṇa vidhimeṣāṃ yathākramam 
tadā tu yojayenmantrī anyathā naiva yojayet ।। 

bindusthaṃ tritayaṃ śabde caturtho bindureva hi 
brahmā viṣṇustathā rudraḥ trimāṇaṃ varṇa ucyate ।। 

īśvaro bindudevastu kaṇṭhe śabdaḥ pravartate 
tatra śabdaḥ kriyāntasthaḥ kriyāśaktiriti smṛtā ।। 

sa śabdastāluke devi īritaḥ sampravartate 
tasya kiṃcidgataḥ śabdo nāsikānte pravartate ।। 

jñānaśaktistuvijñeyā yatnataḥ parameśvari 
mūrdhasthānagataḥ śabdo lalāṭāntamavasthitaḥ ।। 

varṇaḥ śabdagataḥ teṣām udghātaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ 
tatrasthā vinivartante śivajñānavivarjitāḥ ।। 

pañcadhāvasthito bindur ardhacandro nirodhikā 
tasyātīto bhavennādaḥ avicchinnastvasau bhavet ।। 

īṣatprasārite vaktre devadevaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
caturvidho bhavecchabdo yaḥ suvegavahaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

pañcamo na vahecchabdaḥ ūrdhvagāminyasau smṛtā 
tasyātītā bhavecchaktiḥ pañcadhā tu vyavasthitā ।। 

sparśastatra bhaveddevi ātmavittatra pūrvavat 
vyāpinī parataścaiva pañcadhā tu vyavasthitā ।। 

vālāgramāśritaṃ sparśaṃ kadācidvetti vā na vā 
vyāpinī sā samuddiṣṭā na jñānaṃ parameśvari ।। 

tasyāpi samanātītā manastatra na kārayet 
unmanāpadamārohan śuddhātmā tu tato bhavet ।। 

śiṣyātmānaṃ guruvara unmanyante niyojayet 
tatra yuktaḥ pare śānte mahāśāntimavāpnuyāt ।। 

gurupāramparāyātaḥ sampradāyaḥ prakāśitaḥ 
yojane tu pare tattve upāyaḥ kathitastava ।। 

evaṃ jñātvā varārohe sarvakarmāṇi kārayet 
tattvādhvānaṃ kalādhvānaṃ bhuvanādhvānameva ca ।। 

varṇamantrapadādhvānaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ śuddhyati priye 
eṣā vai dhāraṇādīkṣā kartavyā yoginātra tu ।। 

mantrasiddhena vā devi kṛtā vai sukṛtā bhavet ।। 

iti svacchandatantre tattvadīkṣāprakāśanaṃ nāma pañcamaḥ paṭalaḥ

ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ

samayācārayuktasya sādhakasya varānane 
jāyate vividhā siddhiḥ girigahvaramāśrite ।। 

suśuddhe bhūpradeśe tu sarvaśalyavivarjite 
pracchanne vijane ramye bhairavaṃ tatra pūjayet ।। 

japitvākṣaralakṣaṃ tu bahurūpasya suvrate 
pañcapraṇavasaṃyogāj japataḥ siddhyate dhruvam ।। 

mucyate na tu sandeho bhedanāt praṇavasya tu 
hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ sūkṣmam atisūkṣmaṃ paraṃ śivam ।। 

praṇavaṃ pañcadhā jñātvā bhittvā mokṣo na saṃśayaḥ 
praṇavaḥ pañcadhāvasthaḥ haṃsena saha saṃyuktaḥ ।। 

yatkiñcidvāṅmayaṃ loke śivajñāne pratiṣṭhitam 
śivajñānaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ haṃsaḥ praṇavasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

vinā praṇavasaṃyogāj jīva eko vyavasthitaḥ 
yathāprakṛti saṃyukto na ca tiṣṭhati caikataḥ ।। 

tathā ṣaṣṭhena sambhinno dehe jīvaḥ pravartate 
coditastu yadā tena tadā cordhvaṃ pravartate ।। 

pratyakṣamapi tattattvaṃ mahāmāyāvimohitāḥ 
kathitaṃ nābhijānanti vinā śāstreṇa codanām ।। 

ṣaṣṭhaścordhvavaho jñeyaḥ svabhāvamukhasaṃsthitaḥ 
aprakāśaḥ svadehastho guṇabhūtaḥ pravartate ।। 

nirguṇastu yadā deva ekākī kālavarjitaḥ 
vijñātavyaṃ na kiñcitsyāt kevalo niṣkalastu saḥ ।। 

tasya rūpaṃ śarīraṃ ca nāsti varṇaḥ kriyā tathā 
sa kathaṃ gṛhyate sūkṣma agrāhyo nityamavyayaḥ ।। 

etasmātkāraṇāddevi ṣaṣṭhaṃ bījaṃ niyojitam 
pañcapañcakasaṃyukto dehe sakalaniṣkalaḥ ।। 

grahaṇaṃ tu yadā tasya yogī yogavicintakaḥ 
yogenāvāhitasyāpi bhāvamātraṃ tu bhāvayet ।। 

yadā karoti sṛṣṭiṃ ca ūrdhvaṃ binduḥ pravartate 
bindūpari ca yacchāntaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

tatra bindurlayaṃ yāti tatsthānaṃ durlabhaṃ suraiḥ 
ṣaṣṭhasvarasamāyogād abhyāsādacirāllabhet ।। 

ṣaṣṭhaśca pañcamaścaiva tasya devi guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ 
saguṇaḥ sakalo jñeyo nirguṇo niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ ।। 

sakalo grahasaṃyukto niṣkalo bhāvamāśritaḥ 
sakale japyamāne tu japto bhavati niṣkalaḥ ।। 

surāsurāṇāṃ devena yajanopāyahetunā 
rūpaṃ tu sakalaṃ tasya dvidhāvasthaṃ prakāśitam ।। 

prathamaṃ prākṛtaṃ rūpaṃ vikṛtaṃ ca dvitīyakam 
prakṛtirvikṛtiścaiva ubhe ṣaṣṭhena saṃyute ।। 

ye padārthāḥ purā proktās tatrāsāvucchvasan muhuḥ 
pravartate ca etena punastena nivartate ।। 

praṇavaḥ pañcadhāvasthaḥ trivarṇaśca tridaivataḥ 
bindunādasamāyuktaḥ praṇavaḥ paripaṭhyate ।। 

akāraśca ukāraśca makāraśca tṛtīyakaḥ 
varṇatrayamidaṃ proktaṃ brahmādyā devatāstrayaḥ ।। 

bindunādasamāyogād īśvaraśca sadāśivaḥ 
ete vai praṇavāḥ pañca haṃsaḥ prāṇayutaḥ sadā ।। 

paramātmā śivo haṃsas tv apareṇa samanvitaḥ 
parataḥ praṇavān pañca punareva vadāmyaham ।। 

śaktiśca vyāpinī caiva samanātmā ca niṣkalaḥ 
unmanā ca tathā devi praṇavāḥ pañca kīrtitaḥ ।। 

parataḥ paramo haṃsaḥ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ 
ete vai praṇavāḥ pañca parāparavibhāgaśaḥ ।। 

parāpareṇa haṃsena nityameva praṇāmitāḥ 
pravartante hi sarvatra bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ ।। 

pañcabhistu yutastvebhiḥ sa pañcapraṇavātmakaḥ 
tatrasthaḥ ekarūpastu niṣkalastattvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

tadyogādapi tadbījaṃ sarvabījaprarohakam 
pravartate ayato yasmād devāsuraniketanam ।। 

tatra mantrāśca varṇāśca pratiṣṭhāṃ yānti nānyathā 
tasya boddhādvimucyante ahikañcukavat priye ।। 

tāvadbhramati saṃsāre yāvattattvaṃ na vindati 
vidite tu pure tattve na bhūyo jāyate kvacit ।। 

akṛtārtho narastāvad yāvaddhaṃsaṃ na vindati 
praṇavena samāyuktaṃ kṛtārtha iti nirdiśet ।। 

uccāraṃ ca tato jñātvā uccarettaṃ varānane 
uccārastrividho devi haṃsasya samudāhṛtaḥ ।। 

hakārokārasaṃyuktabindvante tu tṛtīyakaḥ 
sṛṣṭinyāsena tūccāraḥ saṃhārayoga ucyate ।। 

evamādikrameṇaiva mantramuccārayedbudhaḥ 
bindusthaṃ tritayaṃ kṛtvā vaktramudghāṭayettataḥ ।। 

īṣadudghāṭite vaktre tadā nādaṃ vijānata 
nādasthaṃ pañcadhā caiva śaktisthaṃ pañcadhā punaḥ ।। 

vyāpinyāṃ pañcadhā caiva samanāniṣkalātmanoḥ 
unmanā ca paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। 

evaṃ jñātvā vimucyante śivatattvavido janāḥ 
anyathā naiva mucyante bindvante ye vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

jyotīrūpaṃ tu bindusthaṃ nādasthaṃ śabdarūpakam 
śaktisthaṃ sparśagaṃ caiva tadūrdhvaṃ śūnyarūpakam ।। 

brahmādipañcakaṃ yacca teṣāṃ śūnyaṃ ca tatpadam 
parāparavibhāgena te sarvatra vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

śūnyātītā tu samanā śuddhātmā tūnmanā tathā 
sarvātītaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। 

mantrarūpāśca vijñeyā bindudharmāttu devatāḥ 
tatrasthā sarvakarmāṇi sādhayanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

tattvaṃ ca unmanātmā tu samanā śūnyameva ca 
sparśaścaiva tathā śabdo rūpaṃ ca tadanantaram ।। 

mantrātmani sthitāḥ sarve jñātavyā daiśikena tu 
tatrasthā jñānayogaṃ ca prayacchanti varānane ।। 

karmakāle tu sakalān śiraḥ pāṇyādibhiryutān 
japet tu sakalān devi niṣkalena samanvitān ।। 

dhyāyejjyotirmayān sarvān śabdasiddhipradāyakān 
śaktisthāḥ śaktidāḥ proktāḥ śūnyasthā vyāpakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

kramājjñānapradāste vai samanāsthā varānane 
kaivalyadāstataścordhve sarvajñāśconmane pade ।। 

tattvena vedhitāḥ sarve ye mayā parikīrtitāḥ 
tajjñātvā siddhidāḥ sarve muktidāśca na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

pañcapraṇavasaṃyuktaṃ tattvaṃ te kathitaṃ mayā 
pañcapraṇavapūrveṇa oṃkārādyayutena tu ।। 

namaskārāvasānena bahurūpeṇa suvrate 
japataḥ siddhimāpnoti lakṣenākṣarasaṃkhyayā ।। 

praṇavādyena saṃyuktaṃ mantramevaṃ japet sadā 
japānte tu punarhomaṃ daśamāṃśena kārayet ।। 

nṛmāṃsaṃ purasaṃyuktaṃ ghṛtena ca pariplutam 
tataḥ siddhimavāpnoti adhamāṃ madhyamottamam ।। 

triguṇena tu japyena svacchandasadṛśo bhavet 
brahmaviṣṇvindradevānāṃ siddhadaityorageśinām ।। 

bhayadātā ca hartā ca śāpānugrahakṛd bhavet 
darpaṃ harati kālasya pātayed bhūdharānapi ।। 

sphoṭayedbilvayantrāṇi diggajānapi cālayet 
brahmarākṣasavetālān krūragrahavināyakān ।। 

smaraṇānnāśayeddevi avadhyastridaśairapi 
prākṛtānyapi karmāṇi siddhyanti japalakṣataḥ ।। 

tāni samyakpravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
mohanā sahadevā ca bhūdhātrī cakralāñchanā ।। 

rāmavallyā sahaikatra ātmabījena poṣayet 
bhakṣe pāne ca dātavyaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam ।। 

uttavāraṇimūlaṃ tu puṣyarkṣeṇa tu grāhayet 
ātmendriyeṇa saṃyuktaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam ।। 

śravaṇākṣimalaṃ lālā rudhirendriyasaṃyutam 
bhūkadambasamopetaṃ dātavyaṃ payasā niśi ।। 

apravāse pradātavyaṃ mriyate viraheṇa sā 
ṣaṣṭiṃ kanakabījāni ṣoḍaśa maṇicandrikāḥ ।। 

naragodantasaṃyuktāḥ pradadyādyasya bhāminī 
eṣa kāpāliko yogo gacchantamanugacchati ।। 

śvetārkamūlaṃ mañjiṣṭhā caṭakasya śirastathā 
gṛhodbhavasya kuṣṭhaṃ ca svaraktendriyasaṃyutam ।। 

bhakṣye pāne pradātavyaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam 
mohanā caiva kāntārī mayūraśikhayā yutā ।। 

ātmalālendriyairyuktaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam 
lajjālukā ca gorambhā caṇḍālīkarmakaṃ tathā ।। 

nāgendrapadamiśraṃ tad ātmabījasamanvitam 
eṣa yogavaro divyo dīyate yasya suvrate ।। 

madhureṇa samāyukto yāvadāyurvaśī sa tu 
caṇakā māṣamudgāśca apānena vinirgatāḥ ।। 

vāntaṃ ghṛtaṃ tathā retaḥ strīrajo hṛnmalaṃ tathā 
mūtraṃ raktaṃ tathā keśo lālā caiva varānane ।। 

putrajāniḥ kṛtāhvā ca nāgendrapadasaṃyutā 
mohanā viṣṇukrāntā ca dhātrī caivaikataḥ sthitā ।। 

puṣyarkṣeṇa niyuñjīta garvitānāṃ varānane 
bhakṣye pāne pradātavyo yogastridaśapūjitaḥ ।। 

uccāṭanaṃ pravakṣyāmi śatrūṇāṃ garvitātmanām 
kākolūkasya pakṣāṃśca kharoṣṭramūtramṛttikā ।। 

kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ prājñaḥ kākaraktena lepayet 
kākolūkasya pakṣāṃśca gude tasya vinikṣipet ।। 

tāṃ catuṣpathe nikhanet śmaśānāgnimathopari 
prajvālya homayettatra kākapakṣāṃśca suvrate ।। 

udbhrāntapatrasahitān kharamūtreṇa bhāvitān 
yasya nāma samuddiśya yakārādyantarodhitam ।। 

mantrāvasāne vinyastaṃ visargāntaṃ pracāṭayet 
bhramate kākavat pṛthvīṃ śatrurvyādhinipīḍitaḥ ।। 

piṇyākaṃ nimbapattrāṇi mṛtkiṇvaṃ tu tuṣāṇi ca 
śatroḥ pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā akṣapuṣpaistu veṣṭitām ।। 

śmaśāne nikhanettāṃ tu vahniṃ prajvālya copari 
puṣpairvibhītatarujair yasya nāmnā tu homayet ।। 

vidviṣṭo vai bhavecchatruḥ kāmadevasamo api yaḥ 
priyaṅgulatikāmiśraṃ gugguluṃ ghṛtavedhitam ।। 

hṛtvā tvaṣṭaśataṃ devi subhagaḥ samprajāyate 
jātikuṭmalakairmiśrais trimadhvaktaistilairhutaiḥ ।। 

subhagatvamavāpnoti rūpahīno api yo naraḥ 
tilairlavaṇasammiśrais trimadhvaktairhutaiḥ priyaiḥ ।। 

saptāhādvaśamāyāti yā strī rūpeṇa garvitā 
rājikā lavaṇaṃ caiva madhukṣīraghṛtaplutam ।। 

homayennāmasammiśraṃ yasyākarṣettu taṃ drutam 
narasya rocanāṃ gṛhya dviradasya madena tu ।। 

bhāvayitvābhimantryaitan mantreṇāṣṭaśataṃ japet 
snāne vilepane madye gandhe vā yasya dīyate ।। 

sa vaśyo bhavati kṣipraṃ dhanadaḥ prāṇadastathā 
athavā mārayetkṣipraṃ śatruṃ niścitamātmanaḥ ।। 

apakāraśatairyuktaṃ kṛtaghnaṃ duṣṭacetasam 
kapāladvayamādāya nāma śatroḥ samālikhet ।। 

kapālasampuṭasthaṃ tad viṣāṅgāreṇa bhāvitam 
rudhireṇa samāyuktaṃ humphaṭkāravidarbhitam ।। 

mahāpretavanaṃ gatvā svacchandaṃ pūjayettataḥ 
kṛṣṇamālyopahāraiśca tataḥ karma samārabhet ।। 

vijñāpya bhairavaṃ devaṃ śatruṃ me vinipātaya 
anujñātastu devena gṛhittvā tacchirodvayam ।। 

tatra gatvā mahādevi kapālāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
tatrastho roṣasampūrṇo dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ jñātvā ghoraṃ subhīṣaṇam 
kruddhaḥ samuccarenmantrī dvātriṃśākṣarasammitam ।। 

vilomena mahābhāge śatrunāma tato antagam 
humphaḍdvayaṃ samuccārya kādye cāsphālayedbhṛśam ।। 

khaṇḍaśaścūrṇite yāvat tāvacchaturvinaśyati 
saptarātreṇa deveśi prayogastvanivartakaḥ ।। 

evaṃ śatasahasrāṇi anyakalpotthitāni ca 
prayogāṇāṃ karotyeṣa mantrarājeśvareśvaraḥ ।। 

anulomagataṃ devaṃ vauṣatkārāntasaṃsthitam 
kṣīraṃ tu homayeddevi śāntyarthe hitakārakam ।। 

vaṣadāpyāyane śastaṃ svāhāntaṃ vaśakarmaṇi 
mantrāṇāṃ tarpaṇārthaṃ ca natyantaṃ cārcane smṛtam ।। 

etaddhi kathitaṃ devi sādhakasya sumedhasaḥ 
kriyākālāṃśayuktasya akleśāttu sukhāvaham ।। 

iti svacchandatantre pañcapraṇavādhikāraḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ

saptamaḥ paṭalaḥ

kriyā jñātā mayā deva tvatprasādānmaheśvara 
kālāṃśakaṃ ca deveśa kathayasva prasārataḥ ।। 

kālo dvidhātra vijñeyaḥ sauraścādhyātmikaḥ priye 
suvārakaraṇe lagne suyoge sudine priye ।। 

tejo apacayarāśau tu dakṣiṇāyanamuttaram 
grahaṇaṃ candrasūryābhyāṃ kālaśca ṛtavastathā ।। 

pakṣo māsaśca velā viṣuvadrāśyantaraṃ tathā 
puṇyāpuṇyodayo devi saura eṣa prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

ādhyātmikaṃ punardevi kathayāmi nibodha me 
ṣāṭkośikastu yo deho bhūtatanmātrasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

sa manobuddhyahaṅkārabuddhikarmendriyairguṇaiḥ 
sarvatattvaistathā devaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitavigrahaḥ ।। 

tatrātmā prabhuśaktiśca vāyurvai nāḍibhiścaran 
nābhyadhomeḍhrakande ca sthitā vai nābhimadhyataḥ ।। 

tasmādvinirgatā nāḍyas tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥ priye 
cakravat saṃsthitāstatra pradhānā daśa nāḍayaḥ ।। 

dvāsaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍyastābhyo vinirgatāḥ 
punarvinirgatāścānyā ābhyo apyanyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

yāvatyo romakoṭyastu tāvatyo nāḍayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
yathā parṇa palāśasya vyāptaṃ sarvatra tantubhiḥ ।। 

śarīraṃ sarvajantūnāṃ tadvadvyāptaṃ tu nāḍibhiḥ 
mārutāpūritāḥ sarvā ātmaśakticarāḥ sadā ।। 

pṛthagvṛttiprabhedena bhinnāścāraprabhedataḥ 
cāravṛttiprabhedena saṃjñābhedo varānane ।। 

nāḍināṃ caiva vāyūnāṃ bhedo jñeyaḥ sahasraśaḥ 
pradhānā daśa yāḥ proktā nāḍayaśca varānane ।। 

tāsāṃ madhye tu deveśi vāyavo ye vyavasthitāḥ 
nāḍīnāṃ caiva vāyūnāṃ saṃjñāvṛttīrnibodha me ।। 

iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva suṣumnā ca tṛtīyakā 
gāndhārī hastijihvā ca pūṣā caiva yaśasvinī ।। 

alambusā kuhūścaiva śaṃkhinī daśamī smṛtā 
etāḥ prāṇavahāḥ proktāḥ pradhānā daśa nāḍayaḥ ।। 

prāṇo apānaḥ samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca 
nāgaḥ kūrmo atha kṛkaro devadatto dhanañjayaḥ ।। 

vāyavo nāḍayaścaiva cakravatsaṃsthitāḥ priye 
tāsu saṃcarataḥ siddhiṃ yogaṃ caiva varānane ।। 

japataśca varārohe japasiddhimavāpnuyāt 
daśānāṃ tu paraṃ devi nāḍītrayamudāhṛtam ।। 

bindunādātmake dve vai madhye śaktyātmikā smṛtā 
hṛccakre tu samākhyātāḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāvahāḥ ।। 

prāṇo vai carate tāsu ahorātravibhāgataḥ 
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi pravibhajya yathāsphuṭam ।। 

prabhuśaktisamākṛṣṭā marutprāṇātmasaṃsthitāḥ 
traya ete avibhāgena saṃcarante samantataḥ ।। 

adha ūrdhvaṃ vahedyasmāt sarvanāḍīḥ pravāhayan 
vṛttisaṃjñāprabhedena varṇarūpāṇyanekadhā ।। 

dvāsaptatisahasrebhyo jāyante daśa vai priye 
koṭidhāto varārohe sa ekaḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। 

prāṇāpānamayaḥ prāṇo visargāpūraṇaṃ prati 
nityamāpūrayanneva prāṇināmurasi sthitaḥ ।। 

prāṇanaṃ kurute yasmāt tasmāt prāṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
ahorātragatiṃ prāṇe adhunā kathayāmi te ।। 

tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśa prāṇe pūrvaṃ hi kathitā mayā 
bāhye naiva tu kālena te lavāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। 

tābhiścatasṛbhirdevi prāṇe yāmo vidhīyate 
taireva praharairdevi caturbhistu dinaṃ bhavet ।। 

rātriścaturbhirvijñeyā ahorātrastvato aṣṭabhiḥ 
śivo dharmeṇa haṃsastu sūryā haṃsaḥ prabhānvitaḥ ।। 

ātmā vai haṃsa ityuktaḥ prāṇo haṃsasamanvitaḥ 
tasyodayātkaletkālaḥ grahāṇāmudayo bhavet ।। 

ṛkṣāṇi rāśayaścaiva tārāstvaṃśāstathaiva ca 
prāṇe vai udayantyete ahorātreṇa suvrate ।। 

ahorātrodayastyaiva vibhāgaṃ kathayāmi te 
hṛdayordhve tu kaṇṭhādho yāvadvai pravahet priye ।। 

aṅgulena vihīne tu prathamaḥ praharaḥ smṛtaḥ 
dvitīya ūrdhve vijñeyo madhyāhnastālumadhyataḥ ।। 

atra homo japo dhyānaṃ kṛtaṃ vai mokṣadaṃ bhavet 
nāsāgryatryaṅgulordhve tu yāvatprāptastu suvrate ।। 

praharastu tṛtīyo asau bhavedvai varavarṇini 
śaktyante ca caturthastu praharo ahaḥ prakīrtitam ।। 

caturthānte tu deveśi prāṇasūryaḥ sadāstagaḥ 
tato astamayasandhyātra tuṭyardhaṃ tu bhavet priye ।। 

tatkālaṃ tu vilambyaivaṃ punaścādhaḥ pravartate 
sa ca candrodayo devi rajanī ca vidhīyate ।। 

pūrvoktakramayogena yāmeṣvevaṃ caratyasau 
tāluke cārdharātrastu punarevaṃ vidhīyate ।। 

hṛtpadmaṃ tu yadā prāptaḥ prabhātasamayastadā 
tuṭyardhaṃ tu varārohe pūrvasaṃdhyā bhavettataḥ ।। 

tasmātsamudayaścaiva sūryasya sa bhavetpunaḥ 
pūrvavat kramayogena sa careddhi sadā śubhe ।। 

vāsare tu caretsūryo dhārāyāṃ saṃcarecchaśī 
candrasūryodayo hyeṣa mayā te parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

bhaumādyāśca grahā hyevaṃ caranti pravibhāgaśaḥ 
prāṇe cāpyudayantyete prahare prahare priye ।। 

velā vāro bhavedyasya sa caretpraharadvayam 
rāhuścarati somena ketuścarati bhāsvatā ।। 

ye grahāste ca vai nāgā lokapālāṣṭakaṃ ca te 
mūrtayaścaiva te cāṣṭāv aṣṭau te ca gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। 

te ca pañcāṣṭakā rudrās tathā yogāṣṭakāḥ pare 
anantādiśikhaṇḍyantās te ca vidyeśvarāṣṭakāḥ ।। 

sakalādyāni tattvāni sthitāni paratastviha 
pūrvoktā bhairavāścāṣṭau sarve te ca vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

grahādīnsamadhiṣṭhāya sarveṣūdayakārakāḥ 
rāśibhiḥ saha nakṣatrais ta udyanti aharniśam ।। 

madhyāhne cārdharātre ca udayo abhijito bhavet 
abhīpsitaṃ phalaṃ tatra sādhakānāṃ bhavediha ।। 

ahorātravibhāgo ayam evaṃ te kathito mayā 
adhunā pakṣamāsāṃśca varṣāṇi kathayāmi te ।। 

ādhyātmikāhorātreṇa bāhye kāṣṭhā vidhīyate 
māsenādhyātmikenaiva bāhye caiva kalā bhavet ।। 

tatra triṃśadahorātrā māsastu varavarṇini 
māsaidvadaśabhiścaiva bāhye atha ghaṭikā bhavet ।। 

śatāni trīṇyahotrātrāḥ ṣaṣṭireva tathādhikā 
varṣametat samākhyātaṃ bāhye vai ghaṭikā ca sā ।। 

ghaṭikāḥ ṣaṣṭistvahorātre bāhye tu pravahanti vai 
tā evāntaracāreṇa ṣaṣṭiḥ saṃvatsarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

prāṇasaṃkhyāṃ punasteṣu kathayāmyadhunā tava 
ṣaṭ śatāni varārohe sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।। 

ahorātreṇa bāhyena adhyātmaṃ tu saradhipe 
prāṇasaṃkhyā samākhyātā jñātavyā sādhakena tu ।। 

praṇahaṃse sadā līnaḥ sādhakaḥ paratattvavit 
tasyāyaṃ japa uddiṣṭaḥ siddhimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। 

adhaḥ pravahaṇe siddhir hṛtpadmaṃ yāvadāgataḥ 
muktiścaiva bhavedūrdhve paratattve tu suvrate ।। 

mano apyanyatra nikṣiptaṃ cakṣuranyatra pātitam 
yathā pravartate prāṇas tv ayatnādeva sarvadā ।। 

nāsyoccārayitā kaścit pratihantā na vidyate 
svayamuccarate haṃsaḥ prāṇināmurasi sthitaḥ ।। 

māsavatsarasaṃkhyā tu eṣā te kathitā mayā 
candrasūryoparāgaṃ tu kathayāmi tataḥ param ।। 

ahorātrastu yaḥ proktaḥ prāṇe asminsurasundari 
sa eva pakṣadvitayaṃ māsaṃ ca kathayāmi te ।। 

tuṭyardhaṃ cāpyadhaścordhvaṃ viśramaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
madhye pañcadaśoktā yās tithayastāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

prathamodaye tu hṛtpadmāt tuṭyardhaṃ tu dinaṃ bhavet 
dvitīye caiva tuṭyardhe yadā carati śarvarī ।। 

rāśayo grahanakṣatrāṇy udayanti yathākramam 
asminnevamahorātre pūrvavacca varānane ।। 

tuṭibhiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ pakṣaḥ sa tu vidhīyate 
tithicchede ṛṇaṃ jñeyaṃ vṛddhau caiva dhanaṃ bhavet ।। 

ṛṇaṃ caiva bhavetkāso niḥśvāso dhana ucyate 
kṛṣṇapakṣordhvacāreṇa saṃhāraḥ saṃkṣayo bhavet ।। 

krūrakarmāṇi vai tatra kurvansiddhimavāpnuyāt 
śubhakarmāṇi kṛṣṇe ca na ca siddhyanti suvrate ।। 

śaktiṃ vai viśati prāṇe yā tuṭistu vidhīyate 
amāvasyā tu sā jñeyā kṛṣṇapakṣe varānane ।। 

śaktermadhyordhvabhāge tu tuṭyardhaṃ yatprakīrtitam 
pakṣasaṃdhistvasau jñeyo amāvasyārdhapratipadā ।। 

tithicchedena vai tatra sūryasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet 
ravibimbāntare devi candrabimbaṃ tadā bhavet ।। 

tadantare bhavedrāhur amṛtārthī varānane 
amṛtaṃ sravate candro rāhuśca grasate tu tam ।। 

pītvā tyajati tadlimbaṃ tadā muktaḥ sa ucyate 
ādityagrahaṇaṃ caiva loke tadupadiśyate ।। 

rāhurādityacandrau ca traya ete grahā yadā 
dṛśyante samavāyena tanmahāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ।। 

sa kālaḥ sarvalokānāṃ mahāpuṇyatamo bhavet 
tatra snānaṃ tathā dānaṃ pūjāhomajapādikam ।। 

yatkṛtaṃ sādhakairdevi tadanantaphalaṃ bhavet 
tāṃ caivārdhatuṭiṃ tyaktvā śuklapakṣodayo bhavet ।। 

śaktigarbhādadhaḥ sṛṣṭis tasmādvṛddhiḥ prajāyate 
tadārabhya ca karmāṇi śubhānyabhyudayāni ca ।। 

dhyānamantrādiyuktasya siddhinte nātra saṃśayaḥ 
prāṇahaṃso yadā prāptas tv adhastāṃ prathamāṃ tuṭim ।। 

pūrvamardhaṃ tvahaḥ proktaṃ tuṭyardhamaparaṃ niśā 
rāśayo graha ṛksāṇi yogāśca karaṇāni ca ।। 

pūrvavatkramayogena tānyudyanti tvaharniśam 
pratipatsā tu vijñeyā candraścaikakalo bhavet ।। 

dvitīyāyāṃ dvitīyā tu vṛddhimeti krameṇa tu 
tithayaścaivamārabhya yāvatpañcadaśī tuṭi ।। 

paurṇamāsī tu vijñeyā tithirvai sādhakena tu 
tatra pūjā japo dhyānaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet ।। 

saṃpūrṇaśca bhavettasyāṃ candro vai cārulocane 
tasyāścārdhatuṭiryā tu pakṣasaṃdhyā tu sā smṛtā ।। 

tasyārdhaṃ paurṇamāsī tu pratipadardhena saṃsthitā 
hṛtpadmasaṃdhimadhye tu somasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet ।। 

ādityena vinā loke somagrahaṇamucyate 
tatraiva ca mahatpuṇyaṃ dhyānahomajapādibhiḥ ।। 

pakṣadvaye api deveśi grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ 
nānādiddhipradaṃ hyetat sādhakasyābhiyoginaḥ ।। 

mokṣaścaiva punarbhadre pakṣadvayasamujjhitaḥ 
pakṣadvayaṃ parityajya pūvoktakaraṇena tu ।। 

unmanyante sthito nityaṃ paravṛttyavalambakaḥ 
parityajya tvadhaḥ sarvaṃ dhyānamāsthāya yojayet ।। 

tasya muktirna saṃdehas tv anyathā siddhibhāgbhavet 
pakṣadvaye api grahaṇaṃ bhavedvai sarvadehinām ।। 

evametatsamākhyātaṃ yāvadāyurvarānane 
atraivādhyātmāhorātre tv athābdodaya ucyate ।। 

hṛtpadmādūrdhvaparyantaṃ rāśayaḥ ṣaḍ vyavasthitāḥ 
aṅgulaiḥ ṣaḍbhirekaiko hṛtpadmādyāva śaktitaḥ ।। 

aṅgule aṅgule hyatra tithayaḥ pañca saṃsthitāḥ 
tasyāpyardhaṃ dinaṃ pūrvam aparārdhaṃ niśā bhavet ।। 

ṣaṭpañcakāstithīnāṃ ye te ḥorātrāstu māsikāḥ 
triṃśatā tairahorātrair dvipakṣo māsa ucyate ।। 

māsi rāśyudaye hyeṣa adhordhvaprāṇasaṃcare 
hṛdayādudayasthānāt saṃkrāntirmakare sthitā ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgulānyadhastyaktvā kumbhe saṃkramate punaḥ 
kaṇṭhordhve dvyaṅgulaṃ tyaktvā mīne saṃkramate punaḥ ।। 

galordhvādyāvattālvantaṃ tyaktvā meṣe atha saṃkramet 
nāsāntaṃ yāvatsaṃkrāntir aṅgulāni ṣaḍeva hi ।। 

eṣā vai viṣusaṃkrāntir uttare saṃvyavasthitā 
japahomārcanadhyānān mahābhyudayakārikā ।। 

nāsāgraṃ tu parityajya prāṇahaṃso vṛṣe caret 
ṣaḍaṅgulāni saṃtyajya saṃkramenmithune punaḥ ।। 

śaktyantaṃ yāvadadhvānaṃ saṃkrāntirmithune smṛtā 
makarācca samārabhya mithunāntaṃ ca suvrate ।। 

uttarayaṇamatraitad aihikīsiddhivarjitam 
snānaṃ dhyānaṃ tathā dānaṃ pūjāhomajapādikam ।। 

sādhakādyaiḥ kṛtaṃ yacca sahastrānekadhā bhavet 
iha janmani nāpnoti paratraivopatiṣṭhate ।। 

dināni tatra vardhante makarānmithunāntikam 
tatkāle saṃharedvīryaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācare ।। 

haṃso raśmibhirākṛṣya garbhasthaṃ kārayettu tam 
garbhasthānekadhārūpaṃ yadgṛhītaṃ purātanam ।। 

karkaṭādeḥ samārabhya sarvaṃ varṣati tatpunaḥ 
tasmādārabhya makarād dhyānahomajapādikam ।। 

paralokanimittāya tadanantaphalaṃ bhavet 
puraścaryānimittāya mantragrahavrataṃ ca yat ।। 

mīnādāvārabhetsarvaṃ mantrasiddhyarthamātmanaḥ 
bāhye api taravo loke ṛtuṣaṭkasamīritam ।। 

kusumānandamāyānti kusumāyudhadīpakam 
mantrāḥ kālānurūpeṇa vratacaryādineritāḥ ।। 

jñeyabodhapradīptāśca siddhimuktiprasādhakāḥ 
adhyātmaśabdarūpātmā ṣaḍrasāsvādaneritaḥ ।। 

haṃsabodhapradīptastu galake mīnamāśritaḥ 
śabdasaṃvedanaṃ tasya sphuṭaṃ tatra bhavedyataḥ ।। 

tadārabhya japāttasya sarvameva pravartate 
mithunāntaṃ ca deveśi tataḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate ।। 

sahaṃso binduśaktisthaḥ siddhidvārairadhomukhaḥ 
karkaṭādau sa varṣettu tulāntaṃ tālukāntare ।। 

kaṇṭhādadhastato dehī hṛtpadmātsarvato vrajet 
tasmādihātmasiddhyarthaṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ caiva sādhayet ।। 

dakṣiṇāyanaje kāle yasmātsṛṣṭiḥ prajāyate 
śaktyadho hṛdaye haṃsaḥ saṃkrametkarkaṭe priye ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgulāni saṃtyajya siṃhe vai saṃkrametpunaḥ 
ṣaḍaṅgulaiḥ punastyaktaiḥ kanyāṃ saṃkramate punaḥ ।। 

nāsikāgrāttu tālvantaṃ tyaktvaivaṃ viṣuvadbhavet 
tulāsaṃkrāntireṣoktā dakṣiṇaṃ viṣuvadbhavet ।। 

sādhanaṃ yat kṛtaṃ tatra iha janmani kāmadam 
mṛtyorjayaṃ tathā śāntiṃ puṣṭiṃ tasmātsamārabhet ।। 

tasmātsa ṣaḍrasāhāro galādhaḥ prīṇayettanum 
ṣaḍaṅgulāni tyaktvā tu vṛścike kramate punaḥ ।। 

kaṇṭhordhvaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ tyaktvā kaṇṭhādhaścaturaṅgulam 
vṛścikaṃ tu parityajya dhanvisaṃkrāntirucyate ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgulādadhastāttu dhanvisthaścarate hṛdi 
hṛtpadmāntaṃ tu vai haṃsaś caritvā ūrdhvagodayaḥ ।। 

makarādiṣu saṃkrāntau dvādaśaivaṃ caretsadā 
amunoktakrameṇaiva āyurvai sarvadehinām ।। 

aihikāmuṣmikī siddhir adhamā madhyamottamā 
ayanadvayamākhyātaṃ mokṣasiddhirdvayojjhitā ।। 

ayanadvayaparyanta unmanyante sadā sthitaḥ 
tatrastho vai japadhyānān mokṣasiddhimavāpnuyāt ।। 

mokṣaṃ gatvā tu nāgacchet pratijñā bhairavasya tu 
asminnabdodaye bhūyo dvādaśābdodayaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

caitrasaṃvatsare yasmān māsānāmudayo bhavet 
tadādi sādhakaistasmāt kartavyaṃ mantrasādhanam ।। 

dvādaśābdaḥ sa vijñeyaś caitramāsādvarānane 
lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi prāṇo asminpravibhāgaśaḥ ।। 

tatra saṃvatsareṇaiva amunoktena suvrate 
ahorātrastu yaḥ prokto dvādaśāṃśaṃ bhajetpriye ।। 

dvādaśa te ahorātrā dvādaśābde bhavanti vai 
pañcabhistāṃstu saṃguṇya dvādaśābda ṛturbhavet ।। 

tameva dviguṇaṃ kṛtvā kālastu sa vidhīyate 
triguṇenaitadayane vatsaraḥ ṣaṅguṇena tu ।। 

saṃkrāntayo dvādaśātra yadvadabde prakīrtitāḥ 
dvādaśābdodaye prāṇe vatsarāste prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

dvādaśābde tvahorātrāḥ teṣāṃ saṅkhyāṃ nibodha me 
sahasrāṇi tu catvāri triśatī viṃśatistathā ।। 

dvādaśābdodaye devi prāṇe asminkathitā mayā 
ṣaṣṭyabdodayamatraiva punaśca kathayāmi te ।। 

ānandādyāstu te jñeyāḥ ṣaṣṭyabdāstu varānane 
te cādha ūrdhvage prāṇe ekasminsurasundari ।। 

caranti pravibhāgena tathā te kathayāmyaham 
ānandaprabhṛterdevi mantramārādhayettu yaḥ ।। 

tasyānandastu deveśi mantreṇa saha jāyate 
dvādaśābde tvahorātraṃ pañcadhā bhedayecca tam ।। 

ṣaṣṭyabde te tvahorātrāḥ pañcaiva parikīrtitāḥ 
te vai ṣaṅguṇitāstatra māsa ekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

taiśca dvādaśabhirdevi varṣamekaṃ vidhīyate 
aṅgule tu sapañcāṃśe mānametatprakīrtitam ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgulaistu pañcābdāḥ ṣaṣṭyabda udayanti te 
hṛtpadmādyāva śaktyūrdhvaṃ triṃśadabdodayo bhavet ।। 

śaktyadho yāvaddhṛtpadmaṃ triṃśadabdodayo bhavet 
ṣaṣṭyabde ye tvahorātrāḥ saṅkhyāṃ teṣu vadāmyaham ।। 

viṃśatistu sahasrāṇi sahasraṃ ṣaṭśatādhikam 
ahorātrāstu ṣaṣṭyabde saṅkhyātāstu varānane ।। 

ṣaṣṭyabdodaya ākhyātaḥ prāṇa ekatra te mayā 
candrasūryoparāge ca pakṣamāsāyaneṣu ca ।। 

yugādiṣu yugānteṣu yacca saṃvatsare apyatha 
varṣadvādaśake caiva ṣaṣṭyabde atha varānane ।। 

snānadānena yajñaiśca pūjāhomajapena ca 
jñānayogādibhiścaiva bāhye kāle tu yatkṛtam ।। 

amunokte varārohe tatphalaṃ labhate mahat 
prāṇahaṃsagatiṃ cāre jñātvaikasmiṃstu tadbhajet ।। 

svasaṃvedyo bhaveccāro nāḍīcārajayātsphuṭam 
athavā sa japādevam atyarthamupabṛṃhitaḥ ।। 

mantrī yogaṃ vijānāti jñātvā sarvajñatāṃ vrajet 
punareva pravakṣyāmi nāḍitrayavibhāgataḥ ।। 

dakṣinottarasaṃkrāntau viṣuvaccāratastathā 
yathā caratyasau haṃso jagatyasmiṃścarācare ।। 

antaḥsthaḥ kālarūpeṇa kalābhiḥ kalayañjagat 
nāḍitrayakṛtādhāro mārgatrayavyavasthitaḥ ।। 

guṇatrayasamāviṣṭas tridhāvasthāvyavasthitaḥ 
kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhirākrāntaḥ śaktitritayasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

icchājñānakriyāviddhaḥ somasūryāgnimadhyagaḥ 
dakṣanāsāpuṭe caiva nāḍī vai piṅgalā smṛtā ।। 

iḍā caiva tu vāmena suṣumnā madhyataḥ sthitā 
dakṣiṇe devamārgastu pitṛmārgastathottare ।। 

madhyamaḥ śivamārgastu tatra gatvā na jāyate 
dakṣiṇe sattvajāgratsthaḥ svapnastho vāmato rajaḥ ।। 

madhye tamastu vijñeyaṃ suṣuptāvastha eva ca 
brahmeśvaraśca dakṣastho vāme viṣṇusadāśivau ।। 

madhye rudraśivau proktau sarvātītaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ 
jyeṣṭhājñāne ca dakṣe ca kriyā vāmā tathottare ।। 

raudrī cecchā ca madhyasthā parā śaktiḥ parāparā 
dakṣiṇo tu sthitaḥ sūryo vāme somo virājate ।। 

pāke prakāśakatve ca madhyasthaścaiva pāvakaḥ 
pācayetsarvapākaṃ hi somādiguṇasambhavam ।। 

prakāśayetsvasāmarthyāt paratattvamanāmayam 
rāśayaśca grahāḥ sarve ṛkṣayogādayaśca ye ।। 

candrasūryapathenaiva te carantyanupūrvaśaḥ 
sūryasomau ca te sarve bhuñjate kramaśaḥ priye ।। 

somasūryātmakāste vai pathitrayavyavasthitāḥ 
vāyati tapati sūryaḥ somo varṣati cāmṛtam ।। 

somasūryātmakaṃ yasmāj jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam 
sauro dakṣiṇamārgastu uttarāyaṇasaṃjñitaḥ ।। 

vāmaḥ saumyastu yaḥ proktas tatra vai dakṣiṇāyanam 
somasūryātma viṣuvat puṭadvayaviniḥsṛtam ।। 

udaksaṃkrāntayaḥ pañca pañca vai dakṣiṇāyane 
dakṣiṇottarayormadhye saṃkrāntyā viṣuvaddvayam ।। 

sauraśca dakṣiṇo mārgas tv abhicāraprasiddhidaḥ 
āpyāyane tathā puṣṭau śāntike saumya uttaraḥ ।। 

dakṣiṇāduttaraṃ yāti uttaraddakṣiṇaṃ yadā 
dakṣiṇottarasaṃkrāntiḥ sā caivaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।। 

dakṣiṇasyāṃ yadā nāḍyaṃ saṃkrāmettu yadottaram 
yāvadardhaṃ tu tatrasthaṃ madhyenottarato vahet ।। 

tāvattadviṣuvatproktam uttaraṃ tūttarāyaṇe 
uttarāddakṣiṇāyāṃ tu saṃkrāmansa varānane ।। 

yāvadardhaṃ vahettatra ardhaṃ dakṣiṇato vahet 
viṣuvaddakṣiṇaṃ tāvad dakṣiṇāyanajaṃ priye ।। 

tatra pūjā japo homo yatkṛtaṃ muktidaṃ bhavet 
dhyānayogena dīkṣāyāṃ tatstho vai mocayedguruḥ ।। 

bāhye caiva tvahorātre adhyātmaṃ tu varānane 
caturviṃśatisaṃkrāntīḥ prāṇahaṃsastu saṃkramet ।। 

ahani dvādaśa proktā rātrau vai dvādaśa smṛtāḥ 
pūrvāhṇe viṣuvattvekaṃ madhyāhne tu dvitīyakam ।। 

tṛtīyaṃ cāparāhṇe vai ardharātre caturthakam 
caturdhā viṣuvatproktam ahorātreṇa muktidam ।। 

caturviṃśatisaṃkrāntyaḥ samadhātoḥ svabhāvataḥ 
śatāni nava vai haṃsa ekāmekāṃ vahetsadā ।। 

etanmānaṃ samākhyātaṃ anyathā pravahedyadā 
iṣṭaṃ caivāpyaniṣṭaṃ ca tadā saṃsūcayettu saḥ ।। 

ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā tasmādyogī nirūpayet 
pūrvodaye tu saṃprāpte bhāskarasya varānane ।। 

jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ caiva tadārabhya vicārayet 
susaṃyatamanā yogī vīro yogāsanasthitaḥ ।। 

saṃsmarannātmajaṃ prāṇaṃ suṣumnāntargataṃ priye 
supraśāntastadā tiṣṭhet prāṇaikagatamānasaḥ ।। 

prāṇasaṃkrāntikālo vai piṅgalaikasthito vahet 
pravāhe viṣuvaddevi jñātvā kālaṃ samādiśet ।। 

ekābdaṃ jīvitaṃ jñeyam ahorātreṇa suvrate 
abdadvayaṃ sa jīvettu ahorātradvayena tu ।। 

tryabdaṃ tu tribhirevātra caturbhiścaturabdakam 
pañcābdaṃ pañcadivasaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍvarṣameva ca ।। 

saptabhiḥ sapta varṣāṇi jīvedaṣṭāṣṭabhirdinaiḥ 
navabhirnavavarṣāṇi daśabhirdaśa eva ca ।। 

dinaikādaśakenaiva varṣaikādaśakaṃ priye 
dinairdvādaśabhiryogī jīvedvarṣāṇi dvādaśa ।। 

saptayāmapravāheṇa ṣaṇmāsānatha jīvati 
praharānṣaḍvahedyasya māsāṃstrīnvai sa jīvati ।। 

pañcapraharavāhena dvayardhamāsāyurva saḥ 
caturbhiḥ praharaidevi māsamekaṃ sa jīvati ।। 

praharatrayavāhena māsārdhaṃ caiva jīvati 
praharadvayaṃ vahedyasya dinānyaṣṭau sa jīvati ।। 

caturaḥ praharāñjīvet praharaṃ tu vahedyadā 
praharārdhaṃ vahedyasya sa jīvetpraharadvayam ।। 

sadyo mṛtyurbhavettasya yasya haṃsastrimārgagaḥ 
yadārabhya nirūpyeta prāṇe vai kālamīśvaram ।। 

māsaḥ pakṣo dinaṃ varṣaṃ tadahaḥ prabhṛti priye 
saṃlakṣyaivaṃ prayatnena tatkāle niścayo bhavet ।। 

uttarāyaṇaje kāle evaṃ te kathitaṃ mayā 
ayuktasyāpi ca prāṇe mṛtyujñānaṃ nibodha me ।। 

karṇarandhrakṛtāṅguṣṭho ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇute yadā 
maraṇaṃ tasya deveśi ṣaṇmāsena vinirdiśet ।। 

ghoṣamadhye paraṃ śabdaṃ cīravākciñcinīravam 
māsamekaṃ sa jīvettu na śṛṇoti yadā priye ।। 

utpāṭaṃ caiva kāṇaṃ ca mṛtyuyogaṃ ca me śṛṇu 
saṃkrāntipañcakaṃ prāṇo mukharandhre vahedyadā ।। 

tamutpāṭaṃ vadedyogaṃ sthānātsthānāntaraṃ vrajet 
vittanāśastathodvego rogavṛddhiśca jāyate ।। 

suhṛdgṛhavināśaśca tejohāniśca jāyate 
dakṣiṇe puṭa ekasmin dakṣiṇāyanavarjite ।। 

saṃkrāntyaṣṭakavāhena kāṇayogo bhaveddhi saḥ 
bhagandharo anugranthaśca netrarogaśca kāmalā ।। 

śūlaṃ visphoṭikā duḥkham urodoṣā bhavanti ca 
vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva saṃkrāntīśca trayodaśa ।। 

jvaraḥ śiro artiḥ śūlaṃ ca arśāsi stambha eva ca 
mūtrakṛcchraṃ pramehaśca pāṇḍurogaśca jāyate ।। 

iḍāsthaḥ śleṣmaṇā vyādhiṃ prakopayati suvrate 
yasmiṃścāre nirūpyeta tatkāladivase pare ।। 

vyādhibhiḥ pīḍyate sarvair vāmavāmetaretare 
athānyatsparśavijñānaṃ nāsādhastāttathopari ।। 

ūrdhvena spṛśataścordhvaṃ rugdoṣāḥ prākpracoditāḥ 
vācākrośābhibhavanaṃ dakṣiṇena vahedyadā ।। 

madhye madhyapuṭasparśī parābhibhavatāṃ vrajet 
itaścetaśca bahudhā saṃkrāntyekā vahedyadā ।। 

pūjanaṃ bahusaṃmānaṃ lābhastasya bhavettadā 
mandacāre suṣumnāyāṃ prāṇahaṃso vahedyadā ।। 

bhūlābho dharma aiśvaryaṃ bhaveccātra priyāgamaḥ 
dvādaśaiva tu saṃkrāntīr vahedviṣuvataikataḥ ।। 

tadaikavatsareṇaiva maraṇaṃ tu samādiśet 
hrasetsaṃkrāntirekaikā māsa eko hrasettadā ।। 

saṃkrāntyekā varārohe triṃśatprāṇakṣayodayā 
dine dine vahedbāhye yāvattriṃśaddināni tu ।। 

māsānte tu bhavenmṛtyuḥ sadya eva varānane 
mṛtyuyogaḥ samākhyāto mayā te varavarṇini ।। 

abdaṃ māsaṃ tathā pakṣaṃ tithiṃ velāṃ yadābhyaset 
yatkālāttu samārabhya tatkālaṃ tu samādiśet ।। 

iḍāsuṣumnāmārgeṇa prāṇacāraṃ vidurbudhāḥ 
dakṣiṇāyanaje kāle evaṃ te kathitaṃ śubham ।। 

evaṃ śarīraje kāle mṛtyuṃ cāśubhameva ca 
jñātvā yogī jayenmṛtyum aśubhānyapyaśeṣataḥ ।। 

dhyātvā kāleśasvacchandaṃ haṃsaṃ vā sakaleśvaram 
nāsikārandhramārgasthaḥ sa sṛjetsaṃharejjagat ।। 

tatrasthaḥ kalayetsarvaṃ sarvabhūteṣvavasthitaḥ 
tatsthaṃ dhyātvā jayenmṛtyuṃ nākalasthaṃ kaletprabhuḥ ।। 

dhyānayuktasya ṣaṇmāsāt sarvajñatvaṃ pravartate 
kālatrayaṃ vijānāti kālayuktastu yogavit ।। 

kālahaṃsaṃ sa tu japan dhyāyanvāpi maheśvari 
sa bhavetkālarūpī vai svacchandaḥ kālavaccaret ।। 

hatamṛtyurjarāṃ tyaktvā rogaiḥ sarvabhayojjhitaḥ 
vijñānaṃ śravaṇaṃ dūrān mananaṃ cāvalokanam ।। 

sarvaiśvaryaguṇāvāptir bhavetkālajayātsadā 
dakṣanāsāpuṭe dhyātvā brāhmaiśvaryamavāpnuyāt ।। 

tadāyustatsamaṃ vīryaṃ bhūtakālaṃ ca vettyataḥ 
bhaviṣyajjño bhavedvāme viṣṇutulyabalaśca saḥ ।। 

tatsamaṃ caitadaiśvaryaṃ tadāyuryogirāḍbhavet 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca sarvaṃ jānāti madhyataḥ ।। 

nityaṃ vai dhyānayogena rudrasya samatāṃ vrajet 
āyuṣā balavīryeṇa rūpaiśvaryeṇa tatsamaḥ ।। 

brahmaṇaḥ parabhāvena aiśvaraṃ padamāpnuyāt 
viṣṇoḥ sadāśivaiśvaryaṃ parabhāvādavāpnuyāt ।। 

rudrasya yaḥ paro bhāvo dhyātvā taṃ tu śivo bhavet 
evaṃ mṛtyujayaḥ khyātaḥ amṛtaṃ dhyāyato jayaḥ ।। 

nāḍibhinnālarandhrasthaṃ hṛtpadmaṃ ṣoḍaśacchadam 
dhyātvā sitaṃ suvikacaṃ kalāṣoḍaśakānvitam ।। 

saṃpūrṇāvayavaṃ candraṃ karṇikākāravigraham 
tanmadhye cintyamātmānaṃ śuddhasphaṭikanirmalam ।। 

śrīrāmṛtārṇavāvasthakallolāmṛtapūritam 
upariṣṭāddvitīyābjaṃ śaktāmṛtamahodadhau ।। 

taccādho mukhapadmaṃ tu paripūrṇendukarṇikam 
tanmadhye cintayeddhaṃsam adho binduśikhānvitam ।। 

varṣantamamṛtaṃ divyaṃ samantātsaṃvicintayet 
ātmordhvarandhramārgeṇa praviṣṭaṃ tacca cintayet ।। 

sitaṃ subahulaṃ sāndram amṛtaṃ mṛtyunāśanam 
tenāplāvitamātmānaṃ pūryamāṇaṃ vicintayet ।। 

padmanālanibaddhaiśca nāḍīrandhramukhaiḥ sadā 
amṛtāpūritaṃ dehaṃ sarvameva vicintayet ।। 

evaṃ vai nityayuktātmā amṛteśasamo bhavet 
vyādhīnmṛtyuṃ jarāṃ tyaktvā krīḍate tvaṇimādibhiḥ ।। 

evaṃ tasyāmṛtadhyānāt kālamṛtyujayo bhavet 
athavā paratattvasthaḥ sarvakālairna bādhyate ।। 

cintayetparamaṃ tattvaṃ kālacāravivarjitam 
kalākalaṅkanirmuktaṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। 

niṣkalaṃ cātmatattvaṃ tu kalaṅko deha ucyate 
saṃyuktaḥ kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvatattvasamanvitaḥ ।। 

varṇo bindustathā nādo vyāpinīśaktisaṃyutaḥ 
samanāvadhiparyantaḥ kalaṅkādhāra ucyate ।। 

ādheyaḥ paramo hyātmā tatparāpyunmanā smṛtā 
tasyāścānte paraṃ tattvaṃ sakalākalavarjitam ।। 

vyāpakaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvāntaḥ sarvatomukham 
pañcapañcakatattvastham aṣṭādaśaguṇānvitam ।। 

yadyasmiṃstu paraṃ vetti tadā mucyeta bandhanāt 
kāraṇāni ca mantrāśca nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāstathā ।। 

binduścaivārdhacandraśca nirodhī nāda ūrdhvargaḥ 
śaktiśca vyāpinī caiva samanātmā tathonmanā ।। 

pañcapañcakametaddhi kathitaṃ te varānane 
tattvānyeva tu ṣaṭtriṃśat guṇāṃścaiva nibodha me ।। 

ahaṃkāro dhīrmanaśca indriyārthāstathaiva ca 
grahaṇaṃ sparśa ādhāraḥ śaktiścaivāṣṭamī smṛtā ।। 

ete cāṣṭau guṇāḥ aṣṭau bhairavā bhairavāvṣṭakam 
prāṇahaṃsastathā śaktiḥ guṇā aṣṭādaśa tvime ।। 

eteṣu tatparaṃ tattvam uccārālambanādṛte 
akṣarākṣaranirmuktaṃ paraṃ tattvamanakṣaram ।। 

akṣareṣu kuto mokṣa ākāśo kusumaṃ kutaḥ 
yāvaduccāryate vācā yāvallekhye api tiṣṭhati ।। 

tāvatsa sakalo jñeyo niṣkalo bhedavarjitaḥ 
sṛṣṭisaṃhāranirmuktaḥ kriyākālavivarjitaḥ ।। 

adhaścāre bhavetsṛṣṭir ūrdhve saṃhāra ucyate 
adhaścāreṇa jāto asau urdhve caiva mṛto bhavet ।। 

sūtakaṃ mṛtakaṃ tyaktvā tiṣṭhedvai tattvavṛttitaḥ 
tattvavṛttiśca vyākhyātā sarvādhvopādhivarjitā ।। 

tattvādhvadharmanirmukhtaḥ kāraṇaiśca vivarjitaḥ 
tattvavṛttau sthito yogī sarvārambhavivarjitaḥ ।। 

rāgadveṣavinirmukto viṣādānandavarjitaḥ 
nākāṅkṣenna ca nindettu viṣayāṃśca kadācana ।। 

samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca brāhmaṇe śvapace samaḥ 
tulyadarśī bhavennityaṃ sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ smaret ।। 

ātmānaṃ ca tathaivaivaṃ sarvathaiva sadā smaret 
sarvatattvāni bhūtāni varṇā mantrāśca ye smṛtāḥ ।। 

nityaṃ tasya vaśāste vai śivabhāvanayānayā 
nacāsau kurute puṇyaṃ naiva pāpaṃ ca suvrate ।। 

kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasannātmā kṛtyaṃ cāsya na vidyate 
iha loke parasmiṃśca paripūrṇastu sarvadā ।। 

dharmādharmavinirmuktaḥ puṇyapāpavivarjitaḥ 
na cāsya bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ hi na peyāpeyameva ca ।। 

nāpavitraṃ hi tasyāsti na pavitraṃ hi suvrate 
nirapekṣo hyasau nityaṃ sarvāpekṣāvivarjitaḥ ।। 

nāsya kṣetraṃ nāsya tīrthaṃ niyamo yama eva ca 
kṣetraṃ tasya parā śaktir yataḥ sarvaṃ prasūyate ।। 

sarvādhvāno yato devi tatrasthāḥ pracaranti vai 
tīrthaṃ caiva paraṃ śāntaṃ nityaṃ cānandaviśvagam ।। 

yena vyāptamidaṃ viśvam anantaṃ viśvaśaktibhiḥ 
nityaṃ viraktiḥ saṃsārād yamo ayam parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

niyamo bhāvanā nityaṃ paratattvaikatānatā 
nātmano bhāvayejjātiṃ na kulaṃ na ca bāndhavān ।। 

ācaretsarvavarṇatvaṃ na ca varṇeṣu vartayet 
parabhāvanayā nityaṃ paradharmeṇa vartayet ।। 

sarvajñaḥ paritṛptaśca paripūrṇaḥ svabhāvataḥ 
svatantro aluptasāmarthyas tv anādinidhanāśritaḥ ।। 

anādibodho hyatulaḥ kālavelāvivarjitaḥ 
cāroccāravinirmuktas tv ahorātravivarjitaḥ ।। 

na divā jāgaraṃ kuryān na ca rātrau svapetkvacit 
svabhāvenaiva saṃtiṣṭhad dinarātrivivarjitaḥ ।। 

evaṃ vai vartate yogī pareṇa samatāṃ vrajet 
na ca taṃ kalayetkālaḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।। 

jīvanneva vimukto asau yasyaiṣā bhāvanā sadā 
śivo hi bhāvito nityaṃ na kālaḥ kalayecchivam ।। 

yogī svacchandayogena svacchandagaticāriṇā 
sa svacchandapade yuktaḥ svacchandasamatāṃ vrajet ।। 

svacchandaścaiva svacchandaḥ svacchando vicaretsadā 
evaṃ vai mṛtyuliṅgāni riṣṭānyanyāni yāni ca ।। 

yogājjānāti yogīndro nādajāntargatāni ca 
nirjityaitāni yogena evamuktavrameṇa tu ।। 

ayogī yāni jānāti ayukto vāpi suvrate 
bahirliṅgāni tānyatra aṅgāriṣṭāni me śṛṇu ।। 

śuṣkatālvoṣṭhakaṇṭhaśced akasmāddhūsaracchaviḥ 
skandhau ca bhaṅgamāyātaḥ ṣaṇmāsānmṛtyumāpnuyāt ।। 

sunīlaṃ maṇḍalaṃ vyomni yaḥ paśyati dine dine 
sitaṃ haritakṛṣṇaṃ ca vatsarārdhānmriyeta saḥ ।। 

viraśmiṃ paśyati raviṃ somaṃ vai lakṣmavarjitam 
tārāṃ jyotsnāṃ ca kṛṣṇāṃ vai paśyetṣaṇmāsajīvitaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyavarṇaṃ puruṣaṃ piṅgalaṃ kṛṣṇameva ca 
svapne saṃpaśyate yo vai ṣaṇmāsānso api jīvati ।। 

ātmano hyaśiracchāyāṃ paśyetṣaṇmāsajīvitaḥ 
tailābhyaṅgaṃ tathā pānaṃ raktasraganulepanam ।। 

raktāmbarāṇi kṛṣṇāni svapne paśyati vai yadā 
pretaiḥ piśācai rakṣobhiḥ śvagomāyukasūkaraiḥ ।। 

vṛtaṃ yātaṃ gṛddhrakākair mahiṣairuṣṭragardabhaiḥ 
aṅgabhakṣaṇamudvāhaṃ nagnaṃ cātīva vihvalam ।। 

svapne ca paśyate yo vai varṣamekaṃ sa jīvati 
śaṃkhāvarte bhujāmadhye gulphayormarmasandhiṣu ।। 

so avaśyaṃ vadhamāyāti yasyaitatspandanaṃ na hi 
somārkamaṇḍalaṃ dehe dhruvaṃ caiva tvarundhatīm ।। 

na paśyati mahāyānaṃ so avaśyaṃ mriyate naraḥ 
tālurandhragato dhūmo mahāyānaṃ taducyate ।। 

jihvā tvarundhatītyuktā nāsāgraṃ dhruva ucyate 
netrānte karajākrānte maṇḍalaṃ somasūryayoḥ ।। 

na paśyedgagane apyetat so avaśyaṃ mriyate naraḥ 
sthūlo akasmācca jāyeta akasmādvai bhavetkṛśaḥ ।। 

atikruddho atibhītaśca varṣamekaṃ sa jīvati 
kṛṣṇāmbaradharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ lohadaṇḍakarodyatam ।। 

naraṃ cābhimukhaṃ svapne dṛṣṭvā māsatrayāyuṣam 
hṛdayaṃ śuṣyate yasya snātamātrasya tatkṣaṇāt ।। 

gātraṃ caivāpyanuṣṇaṃ ca ṛtumekaṃ sa jīvati 
dhanurniśi divā colkā vyabhre vidyutpradarśanam ।। 

digdāho apluṣṭadeśe api māsamekaṃ sa jīvati 
cakṣuṣī sravato yasya śabdaṃ na śṛṇuyāt sphuṭam ।। 

nāghrāti gandhaṃ vāgjāḍyaṃ māsamekaṃ gatāyuṣaḥ 
raktapadmopamaṃ vaktraṃ jihvā kṛṣṇā ca yasya vai ।। 

gātre varṇānyanekāni hṛdayaṃ yasya roditi 
tālukampo atha nābheśca ardhamāsaṃ sa jīvati ।। 

pratyakṣakākanāsīro dīpadhūmaṃ na jighrati 
pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ na jānāti caturmāsaṃ sa jīvati ।। 

binduṃ yastu na paśyettu nityaṃ vaktrānugaṃ hitam 
nityaṃ vahati hikkāṃ tu varṣamekaṃ sa jīvati ।। 

bahirliṅgāni caitāni aṅgāriṣṭāni yāni ca 
pūjayā japahomena dhyānadhāraṇayā priye ।। 

kṛtarakṣāvidhānena jīyante nātra saṃśayaḥ 
nāḍīnāṃ śodhanaṃ caiva vāyūnāṃ ca jayaḥ katham ।। 

sthānaṃ rūpaṃ ca śabdaṃ ca karma brūhi mama prabho 
paramo yogasadbhāvo guhyādguhyataraḥ priye ।। 

yo na kasyacidākhyātas taṃ yogaṃ śṛṇu tattvataḥ 
supraśaste bhūpradeśe nāgnitoyasamīpataḥ ।। 

vālukāśarkarāhīne śuṣkavṛkṣavivarjite 
niḥśabdakīṭavalmīke ītibhiḥ parivarjite ।। 

puṇye dharmiṣṭhasaṃvāse tatra yogaṃ samabhyaset 
devadevaṃ samabhyarcya bhairavaṃ savināyakam ।। 

pūrvācāryānnamaskṛtya yukto dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ 
āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmakaṃ bhadrameva vā ।। 

sāpāśrayaṃ sārdhacandraṃ yogapaṭṭaṃ yathāsukham 
dahanotpūyane kṛtvā plāvayedamṛtena ca ।। 

sabāhyābhyantareṇaiva sakalīkaraṇaṃ tataḥ 
antaryāgaṃ yathāpūrvam uccāryaṃ ca paraṃ tathā ।। 

daśadhā yogamārgeṇa haṃsasvacchandamabhyaset 
mantraṃ bindumatītaṃ tu nādāntajyotirākṛtim ।। 

saṃkalpya kalpanālakṣyaṃ dhyāyedvai tena sarvagam 
apasavyena pūryeta savyenaiva virecayet ।। 

nāḍīsaṃśodhanaṃ caitan mokṣamārgapathasya ca 
recanātpūraṇādrodhāt prāṇāyāmasridhā smṛtaḥ ।। 

sāmānyā bahirete tu punaścābhyantare trayaḥ 
ābhyantareṇa recyeta pūryetābhyantareṇa tu ।। 

niṣkampaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā kāryāścābhyantarāstrayaḥ 
nābhyāṃ hṛdayasaṃcārān manaścendriyagocarāt ।। 

prāṇāyāmaścaturthastu supraśānta iti śrutaḥ 
prāṇarodhe tu saṃpūrṇe nābhau nītvā samucchvasan ।। 

śanairvimocayedvāyuṃ vāmanāsāpuṭena tu 
vāyavī dhāraṇāṅguṣṭhe āgneyī nābhimadhyataḥ ।। 

māheyī kaṇṭhadeśe tu vāruṇī ghaṇṭikāśrayā 
ākāśadhāraṇā mūrdhni sarvasiddhikarī smṛtā ।। 

ekadvitricatuṣpañcasaṃkhyoddhātaiḥ prasiddhyati 
saṃniruddhe tu vai prāṇe mūrdhni gatvā nivartate ।। 

sa udghāta iti prokto jñātavyo yogibhiḥ sadā 
rāgadveṣau prahīyete prāṇāyāmaiḥ sudhāritaiḥ ।। 

dhāraṇābhirdahetpāpaṃ pratyāhāre akṣasaṃyamaḥ 
hṛdgude nābhikaṇṭhe ca sarvasandhau tathaiva ca ।। 

prāṇādyāḥ saṃsthitā hyete rūpaṃ śabdaṃ ca me śṛṇu 
drutatāranibho rakta indragopakasaṃnibhaḥ ।। 

kṣīrābhaḥ sphaṭikābhaśca pañcānāṃ rūpalakṣaṇaṃ 
ghaṇṭākaṃsābdamadhuro gajanādo mahādhvaniḥ ।। 

prāṇādināṃ tu pañcānām ayaṃ śabda udāhṛtaḥ 
jalpitaṃ hasitaṃ gītaṃ nṛttaṃ yuddhagatiḥ kalāḥ ।। 

śilpaṃ ca sarvakarmāṇi prāṇasyaiva viceṣṭitam 
praveśayedannapānaṃ tanmalaṃ srāvayedadhaḥ ।। 

andhatvaṃ śrotrarogaṃ ca apānastu kariṣyati 
aśitaṃ līḍhapītaṃ ca samānaḥ samatāṃ nayet ।। 

kṣobho hikkā tathā chikkā udānasya viceṣṭitam 
svedaśca romaharṣaśca śūlaṃ dāho aṅgabhañjanam ।। 

vyānasyaitāni karmāṇi sparśaṃ caiva sa vindati 
aṅguṣṭhajānuhṛdaye locane mūrdhni saṃsthitāḥ ।। 

nāgādyāḥ bahurūpāśca karma tveṣāṃ nibodha me 
āhlādodvegajanakaḥ śoṣaṇastrāsanastathā ।। 

nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkaro devadattaśca pañcamaḥ 
atinidrākaraścānyo yojakaśca dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। 

śvāsasaṃkocanacchedā ghurghurotkramaṇaṃ tathā 
nāgādīnāṃ tu pañcānāṃ mṛtyukāle viceṣṭitam ।। 

na caiva yāti cotkrāntau tanuṃ tyaktvā dhanañjayaḥ 
ākuñcayati vai kūrmaḥ śoṣayecca kalevaram ।। 

prāṇameva jayetpūrvaṃ jite prāṇe jitaṃ manaḥ 
jite manasi śāntasya paraṃ tattvaṃ prakāśate ।। 

prāṇāpānaṃ gude dhyāyet prāṇasamānaṃ nābhitaḥ 
prāṇodānaṃ tu kaṇṭhe tu prāṇavyānaṃ tu sarvagam ।। 

nāgādyāḥ prāṇasaṃyuktāḥ svasthāneṣu nirodhayet 
niruddhasya ca yaḥ kālas taṃ vakṣyāmi nibodha me ।। 

tālātprabhṛti taṃ dhyāyed yāvatpañcaśataṃ gatam 
jito anilo bhavatyeva saṃkrāntyutkrāntikarmaṇi ।। 

divyā kāntiḥ śubho gandhaḥ prajñā cāsya vivardhate 
divyā dṛṣṭiśca śravaṇaṃ divyā vākca prajāyate ।। 

vāyuvadvicarellokān siddhāndevāṃśca paśyati 
manasā cintitāvāptiḥ pravarteta guṇāṣṭakam ।। 

sarvakāmasusaṃpūrṇaḥ sarvadvandvavivarjitaḥ 
saṃsārabandhanirmuktaḥ śivatulyaśca jāyate ।। 

prāṇāpānau tu saṃyojya hrasvakoṭisamanvitau 
nābhyādhāre ca yogīndraḥ svedaḥ kampaśca jāyate ।। 

punareva tu hṛtsthau hi prāṇāpānau nirodhayet 
dīrghakoṭisamāyogāt tatkṣaṇācca patedbhuvi ।। 

kaṇṭhasthaṃ ca tathaiveha prāṇameva nirodhayet 
plutakoṭisamāyogāt svapnavṛttistato bhavet ।। 

bhrūmadhye binduyogena prāṇarodhaṃ tu kārayet 
suṣuptaṃ jāyate tatra kṣaṇāccaiva prabuddhyate ।। 

mūrdhadvāraṃ samāśritya niṣkalaṃ dhyānamārabhet 
evamabhyasatastasya pratyayastu tadā bhavet ।। 

pipīlakaṇṭakāvedho mūrdhvadvāraṃ vibhindataḥ 
bhittvā krameṇa sarvaṇi unmanyantāni yāni tu ।। 

pūrvoktalakṣṇairdevi tyaktvā svacchandatāṃ vrajet 
jāyate unmanastvaṃ hi dehenānena sādhake ।। 

saṃkrāmetparadeheṣu kṣuttṛṣṇābhyāṃ na bādhyate 
atītānāgataṃ caiva trailokye yatpravartate ।। 

pratyakṣaṃ tadbhavettasya sarvajñatvaṃ ca jāyate 
prasaṅge adhyātmakālasya jñānaṃ vijñānameva ca ।। 

sarvametatsamākhyātam aṃśakāṃśca nibodha me ।। 

iti svacchandatantre saptamaḥ paṭalaḥ

aṣṭamaḥ paṭalaḥ

aṃśakaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ devi kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ 
bhāvāṃśakaḥ svabhāvāṃśaḥ puṣpapātāṃśa eva ca ।। 

mantrāṃśakaḥ smṛtaścānyas tv aṃśakāpādanaṃ dvidhā 
devānusmaraṇaṃ bhāvaḥ sahajaṃ taṃ vijānata ।। 

svabhāvaśca bhavecceṣṭā kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ 
brahmāṃśo vedabhaktastu rudrāṃśaṃ ca nibodha me ।। 

rudrabhaktaḥ suśīlaśca śivaśāstrarataḥ sadā
