śivecchayā prapadyeta dīkṣāṃ jñānamayīṃ śubhām ।। 

mantrayogātmikā divyāṃ tato mokṣaṃ vrajetpaśuḥ 
nānyathā mokṣamāyāti api jñānaśatairapi ।। 

yasya prakāśitaṃ sarvaṃ śivenānantarūpiṇā 
sa eva mokṣaṃ vrajati śivaḥ sarvamaheśvaraḥ ।। 

tenedaṃ jñānamukhyaṃ tu purā proktaṃ mayā tava 
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ naurivottāraṇaṃ param ।। 

mahāmāyāñjanātītaṃ ajñātaṃ paśugocare 
anantaṃ pāramakṣobhyaṃ subodhaṃ parameśvaram ।। 

parameśamukhodgīrṇaṃ yan mayā prāptamadbhutam 
vakṣye jñānāmṛtamidaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ priye ।। 

ūrdhvaṃ vai brahmaṇo aṇḍasya puraikādaśakaṃ sthitam 
ekādaśānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ yugāntāgnisamatviṣām ।। 

athordhve bhuvanaṃ devyāḥ kathayāmi varānane 
indranīlamayaṃ divyaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। 

tasminbhagavatī devī bhadrakālī vyavasthitā 
vasatīndīvaraśyāmā snigdhakaṅkuṣṭasaprabhā ।। 

sūryamaṇḍalarūpābhyāṃ kuṇḍalābhyāmalaṅkṛtā 
paurṇamāsyāṃ yathā sandhyā candrarkābhyāṃ virājate ।। 

rājate ca mahāhāraḥ stanābhyāmantare sthitaḥ 
asitāñjanaśailābhyāṃ madhye srotovahā yathā ।। 

caturbhiśca dhṛtaṃ pīṭhaṃ siṃhairamitavikramaiḥ 
sarvavajramaye divye divyaratnavibhūṣite ।। 

āsane suprabhe devī jātyañjanasamaprabhā 
śukle himavataḥ śṛṅge nīlamegha iva sthitā ।। 

sarvaratnamayī divyā raśanāsyā virājate 
pītamālyāṃśukavatī śarvarīvāruṇodaye ।। 

tṛtīyaṃ nayanaṃ tasyā lalāṭasthaṃ virājate 
udayastha ivādityo raśmijālavibhūṣitaḥ ।। 

ucchritenātapatreṇa sā śvetena virājate 
kṛṣṇameghoparisthena candreṇeva vibhāvarī ।। 

koṭikoṭisahasreṇa strīṇāṃ tu parivāritā 
āvṛtā candralekheva nakṣatraistu nabhastale ।। 

kumudotpalavarṇāśca hemaśyāmāśca yoṣitaḥ 
priyaṅgukalikāśyāmāś candragauryaḥ sayauvanāḥ ।। 

padmāvadātarūpiṇyaḥ pīnaśroṇipayodharāḥ 
hāvabhāvavidhijñāstu nṛttagītaviśāradāḥ ।। 

vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgādyair vaṃśavāditraniḥsvanaiḥ 
upāsīnāstu tāṃ devīṃ ramante tatra yoṣitaḥ ।। 

evaṃ viddhi jayaṃ nāma bhuvanaṃ tu varānane 
yā durgeti smṛtā loke brahmāṇḍodaravartinī ।। 

viṣṇunā tapasā pūrvam ārādhya parameśvaram 
avatāritā vadhārtāya mahiṣasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 

yena caikena śṛṅgeṇa bhagavān himavān giriḥ 
śuṣkaparṇamiva kṣiptaḥ bhagavatyā vināśitaḥ ।। 

sā taṃ vināśāyeddevī tamaḥ sūrya ivotthitaḥ 
sā devī sarvadevīnāṃ nāmarūpaiśca tiṣṭhati ।। 

yogamāyāpraticchannā kumārī lokabhāvinī 
acintyā cāprameyā ca anyatra paripaṭhyate ।। 

viṣṇunā sahitā devī kalpe kalpe punaḥ punaḥ 
bhaginītvena cāyāti nāmarūpaviparyayaiḥ ।। 

manvantare manvantare tathā caiva yuge yuge 
rakṣaṇārthaṃ hi lokānāṃ māteva hitakāriṇī ।। 

ityākhyātaṃ tu bhuvanaṃ jayaṃ nāma varānane 
tadbhaktāstatra gacchanti tasyā maṇḍaladīkṣitāḥ ।। 

nacaitattapasā prāpyaṃ nayajñairbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ 
na dānairvividhaiścāpi śakyaṃ prāptuṃ varānane ।। 

prasādāddevadevasya śaśāṅkāṅkitamaulinaḥ 
dīkṣāṃ prāpya prāpnuvanti maṇḍalaṃ cakravartinām ।। 

nirbījadīkṣayā mokṣaṃ dadāti khalu dehinām 
sā muktidīkṣā paramā vidhivatparikīrtitā ।। 

vidyeśāvaraṇe dīkṣā yavatī kriyate nṛṇām 
tāvatīṃ gatimāpnoti bhuvane atra varānane ।। 

bhuvanāni tadīśāṃśca saṃsthānāni yathākramam 
kathayiṣyāmi te sarvaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ priye ।। 

bhadrakālyāṃ paro devo rudrakrodhasamudbhavaḥ 
koṭimātreṇa deveśi yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ ।। 

yugāntāmbudavṛndotthagarjitadhvaniniḥsvanaḥ 
śatabāhurmahātejā divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

śirasīndudharaḥ śyāmo nīlāñjanasamadyutiḥ 
śikhikaṇṭhanibhaḥ kiñcit kiñcidāpāṇḍulohitaḥ ।। 

cāṣajīmūtavarṇaśca atasīpuṣpasaṃnibhaḥ 
indranīlanibhaḥ kiñcit kiñcidbhṛṅganibhākṛtiḥ ।। 

jātyañjananibhākāro rudraikādaśikānvitaḥ 
yutaṃ koṭisahasreṇa rudrāṇāṃ ca mahātmanām ।। 

bhuvanaṃ tasya devasya vijayaṃ nāma viśrutam 
indranīlanibhaṃ divyaṃ sarvavajranibhaṃ mahat ।। 

daśakoṭisahasrāṇi rudrāṇāṃ varavarṇini 
antarbhuvanasaṃghātair anyaiśca parivāritam ।। 

nīlotpaladalaśyāmaiḥ śikhikaṇṭhanibhaistathā 
rudrairdivyairmahāvīryaiḥ samantātparivāritam ।। 

stutibhirmaṅgalairgītair nṛttāvāditravāditaiḥ 
paṇavairveṇuvīṇābhir bherījhallari gomukhaiḥ ।। 

paṭahaiḥ kāhalaiścaiva śaṅkhadundubhipīlukaiḥ 
mṛddalaistaṭṭarībhiśca tālakairmurajaistathā ।। 

maundakāhalaṭaṅkaiśca tamiladraghaṭādibhiḥ 
vāditrairvalgitaistālai roṭanairmukhamṛddalaiḥ ।। 

bhūtairbhūtagaṇai rudrair jalpitaiḥ paṭhitaistathā 
dhyāyādbhiśca japadbhiśca dhāvadbhiśceṣṭitaistathā ।। 

mayūrakokilārāvān muñcadbhiśca tathāparaiḥ 
nānārutavilāsaiśca vikurvadbhirmahātmabhiḥ ।। 

āvṛtastairmahātejā mayūkhairiva bhāskaraḥ 
gajavaktraiḥ siṃhavaktrair aśvavaktraiḥ śubhānanaiḥ ।। 

gokarṇairgomukhaiścānyair dvīpiṛkṣamukhaistathā 
vyāghravānaravakaiś ca bhagavānparyupāsyate ।। 

vīrabhadro mahātejā yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ 
āsanaṃ tasya devasya sarvavajramayaṃ mahat ।। 

daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ caturasrānalaprabham 
rājate atrāṣṭabhiḥ siṃhair vṛtaṃ bhīmaparākramaiḥ ।। 

atra te puṇyakarmāṇaḥ ye smaranti maheśvaram 
jale marutsvathāgnau vā śiraśchedena vā mṛtāḥ ।। 

te yānti caiśvaraṃ bodhaṃ vīrabhadraṃ mahādyutim 
bhuvanasyāsya deveśi hy uparyāvaraṇaṃ mahat ।। 

ammayaṃ tu ghanaṃ cāpi śakracāpamiva sthitam 
vitānamiva tadbhadram antare samavasthitam ।। 

tatra cāste mahātmāsāv aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakaḥ 
tatra yojanakoṭirvai viṣkambhādūrdhvamucyate ।। 

tiryaktriguṇavistāram āpyamāvaraṇaṃ priye 
āvṛtaṃ tena tatsarvaṃ mahāmbhodhivisāriṇā ।। 

rudrāṇḍa iti vikhyātaṃ rudrāloka iti priye 
vīrabhadraniketaśca bhadrakālyālayastathā ।। 

trayodaśabhiranyaiśca bhuvānairupaśobhitam 
nānārudragaṇairdivyair nirantaramalaṃkṛtam ।। 

aṇḍaṃ vai vīrabhadrasya brahmāṇḍasadṛśaṃ priye 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharitryā bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। 

dhātrī yasminbhagavatī dharāloke sanātanī 
hairaṇyamatulaṃ prāptā ādhāraṃ yatra saṃsthitā ।। 

cakravartivimānaiśca bahubhiḥ parivāritam 
āvṛtaṃ bhūtasaṃghātair ācāryaistatparāyaṇaiḥ ।। 

divyagītaninādāḍhyair vāditraśataniḥsvanaiḥ 
antarbhuvanasaṃghātai rudrāṇāṃ parivāritam ।। 

bhuvanasyāsya madhye tu udayādityasaṃnibhaḥ 
raktotpalanibho divya aśokastabakacchaviḥ ।। 

padmarāgamayo divyaḥ prāsādo bahubhūmikaḥ 
tasya madhye bhagavatī dharitrī lokadhāriṇī ।। 

mālayā raktapuṣpasya lambayā nityabhūṣitā 
candrārkamaṇḍalākārakapolatalabhūṣitā ।। 

pītahemāṃśukavatī mahāhāravibhūṣitā 
śatayojanavistīrṇe kūrmapṛṣṭhe vyavasthitā ।। 

caturvaktrā cāṣṭabhujā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā 
rūpayauvanasaṃpannā nṛttagītaviśāradāḥ ।। 

parivāryopāsate tāṃ divyā vai mānasāḥ striyaḥ 
triṃśatkoṭyastu tāsāṃ vai divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। 

utpāditāstu śarveṇa tadarthaṃ hitamicchatā 
taptajāmbūnadanibhā divyābharaṇaśobhitāḥ ।। 

ucchritenātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena śobhitāḥ 
puraḥsthito mahātejā yo asau merurmahāgiriḥ ।। 

upāsīnastu tāṃ devīṃ tatrāste sa nagādhipaḥ 
nīlotpaladalaśyāmo nīlajīmūtasaṃnibhaḥ ।। 

nīlo nāma mahāśailaḥ pītavāsā mahādyutiḥ 
atikāntena rūpeṇa kaiṭabhāririvāparaḥ ।। 

upāsyamāno divyābhir nagarībhirnagādhipaḥ 
tasyottare candranibho nānālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

śvetātapatrī tejasvī śveto nāma mahāgiriḥ 
tasyottareṇa sūryābho mukuṭādivibhūṣitaḥ ।। 

pītāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān śṛṅgavāniti viśrutaḥ 
atikāntena rūpeṇa kusumāstra ivāparaḥ ।। 

dakṣiṇenāpi vakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvāvahitā priye 
candrāvadātadīptaujā divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān niṣadho nāma viśrutaḥ 
taptahemapratīkāśo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

atiśubhreṇa dehena pitāmaha ivāparaḥ 
pītāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān pītamālyānulepanaḥ ।। 

hemakūṭo mahātejās tejasāmiva saṅgrahaḥ 
rājate bhagavān śailaḥ sandhyāvṛta ivāṃśumān ।। 

pāṇḍurābhrapratīkāśaḥ śaṅkhagokṣīrasaṃnibhaḥ 
śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān divyakuṇḍalabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

ātapatreṇa mahatā dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani 
himavāniti vikhyāto dvitīya iva bhāskaraḥ ।। 

indragopakasaṃkāśaḥ paścime gandhamādanaḥ 
raktāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān astādristha ivāṃśumān ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śubhaḥ 
kirīṭī kuṇḍalī śrīmān mālyavānnāma parvataḥ ।। 

ityevamādibhiścānyaiḥ parvataiḥ parivāritā 
lokālokāvasānaiśca tathānyaiḥ kulaparvataiḥ ।। 

divyarūpadharā devī tanurvai pārameśvarī 
dhāraṇāṃ gandhatanmātre prāṇāṃstyaktvā tu yoginaḥ ।। 

te yānti tādṛśīṃ mūrtiṃ dharitryāḥ paramāṃ tanum 
ataḥ parataraṃ devi sāmudraṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। 

sarvavajramayaṃ divyaṃ nānāścaryaśatānvitam 
nīlotpalasamacchāyaṃ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalam ।। 

madhye tu bhuvanasyāsya maṇḍalaṃ candrasaṃnibham 
śatayojanasāhasraṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। 

tasya madhye tu puruṣo rukmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ 
kirīṭī kuṇḍalī sragvī divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

apāṃ nidherbhagavato varuṇasya parā tanuḥ 
taṃ tu devaṃ mahātmānaṃ parivārya samantataḥ ।। 

rūpayauvanasaṃpannāḥ satataṃ paryupāsate 
śuklāmbaradharā devī śuklagandhānulepanā ।। 

śuklayajñopavītā ca śuklahāropaśobhitā 
śuklainaivātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani ।। 

gaṅgā hyuttaratastasya sthitā vai paramā tanuḥ 
nīlāmbaradharā devī nīlagandhānulepanā ।। 

nīlasragdāmakaṇṭhā ca yamunā tasya dakṣiṇe 
evamādyā mahānadyaḥ parivārya mahādyutim ।। 

samudrāṣṭakaṃ ca deveśi svanadībhiḥ samāvṛtam 
upāsate sadā bhaktyā vāruṇīṃ paramāṃ tanum ।। 

nānāsarāṃsi tīrthāni tadbhaktāścāpi saṃsthitāḥ 
rasatanmātra atraiva kṛtvā samyaktu dhāraṇām ।। 

apāṃ yoniṃ parāṃ prāptāḥ vāruṇī sā parā tanuḥ 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuvanaṃ varavarṇini ।। 

śrīniketa iti khyātaṃ padmagarbha iti śrutam 
vimānaśatasaṃghātair nirantaramavasthitaiḥ ।। 

śobhitaṃ bhuvaneśaiśca rudrai rudragaṇaistathā 
sarobhirmānasairdivyair dīrghikābhiśca śobhitam ।। 

rathacakrapramāṇaiśca maṇikāñcanamaṇḍitaiḥ 
vaidūryanālaiḥ kamalair divyagandhasugandhibhiḥ ।। 

mṛdubhiḥ kāntimadbhiśca candramaṇḍalasaṃnibhaiḥ 
saṃśobhitaṃ vicitraistair vikacairvajrakesaraiḥ ।। 

udyānairvividhaiścāpi nānāvihagakūjitaiḥ 
nānākāmapradairvṛkṣaiḥ samantātsamalaṅkṛtam ।। 

nānāmaṇimayairdivyaiḥ krīḍāśailaiśca mānasaiḥ 
mānasībhiśca nārībhir divyayauvanakāntibhiḥ ।। 

hāvabhāvavilāsāḍhyadivyastrībhiralaṃkṛtam 
vicitrairmaṇipadmaiśca sitapatraiśca suvrate ।। 

vibhūṣitaṃ gajendrasthaiḥ stutimaṅgalavādibhiḥ 
gāyadbhiścātha nṛtyadbhir divyastraiṇaiḥ samākulam ।। 

tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye padmagarbhasamaprabhe 
śaradindunibhaṃ divyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ raśmisaṃkulam ।। 

tasya madhye bhagavatī śrī svayaṃ lokabhāvinī 
candrakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ yā kāntimativartate ।। 

ekatra yugapattejas tejasāṃ tu virājate 
nirvāṇamiva yā śāntā sarvānandamanoharā ।। 

rūpiṇī paramā devī mūrtiravyabhicāriṇī 
śatayojanavistīrṇe uditādityasaprabhe ।। 

candrakāntamaye padme vajrakesarakarṇike 
koṭipatre mahādivye gandhapuṣpaguṇānvite ।। 

padmāsane bhagavatī padmagarbhasamaprabhā 
upaviṣṭātra sā nityaṃ vibhūtyā parayā yutā ।। 

mahāratnaiśca sragdhāma pralambamurasā śubham 
vahantī sā tu śuśubhe jyotsneva tripathāpatham ।। 

sphuranmayūkhacalane kapolatalamaṇḍale 
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśe dhārayantī ca kuṇḍale ।। 

sphuranmayūkhasaṃghātāṃ raśanāṃ sā tu bibhratī 
hemābhā pītavasanā mahāhāravibhūṣitā ।। 

candrābbhenātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena rājitā 
upagītā ca gandharvair mānasai rudrasambhavaiḥ ।। 

parivāritā bhagavatī sā tanuḥ pārameśvarī 
yā prāptā tapasārādhya viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। 

dattā prītena rudreṇa viṣṇorurasi vāhinī 
ardhena sā bhagavatī viṣṇoraṅge pratiṣṭhātā ।। 

pādenendrasya devasya pādārdhena divi sthitā 
tadardhena punardevi pārthiveṣu vyavasthitā ।। 

tadardhena manuṣyeṣu yā sthitā vyāpya mūrtibhiḥ 
svarūpā kāmarūpā ca dvidhā sā parikīrtitā ।। 

acalā sā tanuḥ sūkṣmā akṣobhyā tatra tiṣṭhati 
rudrakrīḍāvatāreṣu prayāgādiṣu suvrate ।। 

śrīgirau ca viśeṣeṇa mṛtastadbhuvanaṃ vrajet 
satsvanyeṣvapi bhāgeṣu tv iyaṃ sā gaditā gatiḥ ।। 

prāpya tāmīdṛśīṃ devīm aiśvaryamaṇimādikam 
bhūtvā tu sāṣṭadhā divyā deveṣvapi ca tiṣṭhati ।। 

siddheṣvapi ca sā devī uttamā siddhirucyate 
yadarthaṃ tārakādyaiśca saṃgrāmastridaśeśvaraiḥ ।। 

kṛto ghorastvasaṃkhyeyaḥ tāṃ śriyaṃ prāptumicchubhiḥ 
asaṅkhyeyāśca saṃgrāmāḥ kṛtā vai cakravartibhiḥ ।। 

sā bandha evamuktānām abudhānāṃ parā smṛtā 
śrīpuraṃ tu samākhyātaṃ yathāvacca varānane ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuvanaṃ ca nibodha me 
sārasvatamiti khyātaṃ gāndharvamiti ca smṛtam ।। 

padmagarbhapuraṃ cāpi koṭimātreṇa suvrate 
yojanānāṃ samākhyātaṃ pramāṇena samantataḥ ।। 

sārvaratnamayaṃ divyaṃ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitam 
vimānairvividhākārair nānāratnamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। 

gāndharvairmānasaiścāpi gāyadbhiścāpyanekadhā 
nṛtyadbhiśca tathānyaiśca gaṇaiḥ pārśvagataistathā ।। 

strībhiḥ surūpiṇībhiśca gandharvaiśca samākulam 
tasya madhye tu deveśi śaraccandranibhaṃ śubham ।। 

raśmimālākulaṃ divyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ parimaṇḍalam 
tasya madhye bhagavatī sthitā sākṣātsarasvatī ।। 

śaraccandrasahasrasya yā kāntimativartate 
pītāmbaradharā devī padmapatrāyatekṣaṇā ।। 

nīlotpaladalaśyāmā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā 
hemapaṭṭaparīdhānā divyakuṇḍaladhāriṇī ।। 

urasā tu mahāhāram udvahantī śaśiprabham 
sphuranmayūkhasaṃghātakuṇḍaladvayamaṇḍitā ।। 

grāmatrayavalīmadhyā saptasvaratanuḥ śubhā 
tānamūrdhāruhā devī mūrcchanāṅgaruhodvahā ।। 

padāsanā tālapādā gītavarṇaprabhāvatī 
aṅgulyaḥ sandhayaścaiva lakṣaṇāni varānane ।। 

āsane parame divye vṛtā bhūtagaṇeśvaraiḥ 
sthitā sthitirivābhāti sarvasya jagataḥ śubhā ।। 

mānasībhiśca nārībhir gandharvairmānasairvṛtā 
hāhā hūhūścitrarathas tumbururnāradastathā ।। 

viśvāvasurviśvarathaḥ divyagītavicakṣaṇāḥ 
saṃyojya manasātmānaṃ tyaktvā karmaphalaspṛhām ।। 

te vai sārasvataṃ sthānaṃ prāptā vai surapūjite 
ye ca vāgdhāraṇāṃ dhyātvā prāṇānmuñcanti dehinaḥ ।। 

te vai sārasvataṃ lokaṃ prāpnuvanti narottamāḥ 
eṣā sarasvatī devī mūrtirvai pārameśvarī ।। 

yā sthitāparabhāvena brahmāṇḍodaravartinām 
brahmaloke ca sā devī pādenaikena tiṣṭhati ।। 

śākre cāpi tadardhena gandharveṣu tadardhataḥ 
siddheṣu ca tadardhena kinnareṣu tadardhataḥ ।। 

tadardhena ca nāgeṣu yakṣeṣvardhena vai punaḥ 
piśāceṣu tadardhena sā vai tiṣṭhati bhāgaśaḥ ।। 

piśācebhyaḥ sahasrāṃśān mānuṣeṣu ca tiṣṭhati 
taistu taptvā tapo ghoram ārādhya ca pinākinam ।। 

avatāritā tu sā devī rūpiṇī svarabhūṣitā 
svarāṃstu smaratastasya kalpādau brahmaṇaḥ purā ।। 

svarebhyastu viniṣkrāntā tena sā tu sarasvatī 
sā sthitā sarvaśāstreṣu kavīnāṃ kāvyamāsthitā ।। 

yā vālmīkau sthitā devī vyāse caiva nirantaram 
ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ medhābudhivivardhinī ।। 

sarvajñānadharī sā tu sarvajñā devapūjitā 
merorvāyavyadigbhāge puraṃ tasyāḥ prakīrtitam ।। 

idaṃ tu paramaṃ devyā mayā te parikīrtitam 
sārasvataṃ tu bhuvanaṃ kīrtitaṃ paramā tanuḥ ।। 

atraiva tvāpyatattve tvaṃ śṛṇu vai bhuvanottamam 
amareśaṃ prabhāsaṃ ca puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।। 

āṣāḍhiṃ ḍiṇḍimuṇḍiṃ ca bhārabhūtiṃ ca lākulam 
guhyāṣṭakamiti khyātaṃ jalāvaraṇagaṃ priye ।। 

tejastattvamataścordhvaṃ kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
agnestu bhuvanaṃ tatra kathayāmi varānane ।। 

aśokastavakānāṃ ca sarvato dīptimudvahat 
utphullakiṃśukacchāyaṃ japākusumasaṃnibham ।। 

bhuvanasyāsya madhye tu uditārkasamaprabham 
parimaṇḍalamāgneyaṃ tejomaṇḍalamucyate ।। 

tasya madhye tu bhagavāñ śivāgniḥ kāraṇaṃ param 
yo avatīryāṇḍamadhye tu sthito nityaṃ tridhā tridhā ।। 

vaktre tu dakṣiṇe tasya rudrasya paramātmanaḥ 
sthito jihvāsvarūpeṇa svayaṃbhūrnīlalohitaḥ ।। 

sa eva tu mahādevi kālāgniḥ parameśvaraḥ 
tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvāvahitā priye ।। 

raktapadmadalacchāyaḥ padmarāgasamadyutiḥ 
raktāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān raktamālyānulepanaḥ ।। 

arkabhābhyāṃ kuṇḍalābhyām alaṃkṛtaśubhānanaḥ 
mahāhāreṇa dīptena uraḥsthena virājate ।। 

kirīṭī kuṇḍalī dīpto devānāmāsyamucyate 
sarvavajramaye pīṭhe upaviṣṭaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। 

dāvāgniriva śailāgre veṇugharṣātsamutthitaḥ 
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi āgneyāstu gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। 

dakṣiṇāsyādviniṣkrāntāḥ śvasato asya svayambhuvaḥ 
hitāya sarvalokānāṃ rudrā vai sūryavarcasaḥ ।। 

tena te agniṃ mahātmāno nityaśaḥ paryupāsate 
nāryaśca vividhā divyā divyagītavicakṣaṇāḥ ।। 

gaṇā rudrā bhūtagaṇāḥ kiṅkarāśca sahasrasaḥ 
sa vai śivāgniḥ paṭhitaḥ sarvahomeśvaraḥ paraḥ ।। 

agnikāryavidhāneṣu hūyate tadvidaiḥ sadā 
tamagnimaiśvaraṃ yānti kṛtvāgneyīṃ tu dhāraṇām ।। 

sa ekadhā sa bahudhā vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
sa tejastejasāṃ yoniḥ tasmājjajñe divākaraḥ ।। 

bahudhā vyajyate cāsau kalpamanvantarādiṣu 
bhinnaśca janmabhedaiśca pañcāśadbhiśca bhūtale ।। 

tadevaṃ kīrtitaṃ samyag āgneyaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat 
bhuvanādhipāṃśca bhuvane kathayāmi tvataḥ param ।। 

hariścandraṃ ca śrīśailaṃ jalpamāmrātakeśvaram 
mahākālaṃ madhyamaṃ ca kedāraṃ bhairavaṃ tathā ।। 

atiguhyaṃ samākhyātaṃ pūrveśāntamanukramāt 
athordhve vāyvāvaraṇaṃ tatrastho vāyuravyayaḥ ।। 

prāṇasya bhuvanaṃ tatra vāyostu varavarṇini 
śaṅkhagokṣiradhavalaṃ śaratkundendusaprabham ।। 

tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye divyāścaryaśatairyute 
madhye tu maṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ śaraccandrasamaprabham ।। 

raśmimālākulaṃ divyaṃ dyotayadvai diśodaśa 
tasya madhye tu deveśi vāyostu paramā tanuḥ ।। 

kirīṭī kuṇḍalī dīpto hārakeyūrabhūṣitaḥ 
nānābharaṇacitrāṅgaś citramālyānulepanaḥ ।। 

citrāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān mahāhāravibhūṣitaḥ 
mārutā nāma vai devāḥ śatakoṭyo mahābalāḥ ।। 

upāsate mahātmānaṃ vāyumūrtiṃ mahādyutim 
yo vyāpayeccharīrāṇi ekadhā pañcadhā vibhuḥ ।। 

saptadhā saptadhā caiva tiryaggo dviguṇo vibhuḥ 
svamaṇḍalasya sā divyair vibhātyekā parā tanuḥ ।। 

tametamekaṃ daśadhā prāṇātmānaṃ tu yoginaḥ 
dhyātvā tyaktvā tu vai prāṇān kṛtvā tasminstu dhāraṇām ।। 

taṃ viśanti mahātmāno vāyubhūtāḥ khamūrtayaḥ 
iti prāṇasya bhuvanam ākhyātaṃ tava suvrate ।। 

bhuvaneśāṃstatra rudrān kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ 
gayāṃ caiva kurukṣetraṃ nākalaṃ kanakhalaṃ tathā ।। 

vimalaṃ cāṭṭahāsaṃ ca māhendra bhīmamaṣṭamam 
guhyādguhyataraṃ hy etad veditavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। 

ākāśe tu yathākāśaṃ śuddhasphaṭikanirmalam 
sūkṣmarūpo avyayo nityo madhyadeśe vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

ākāśadhāraṇāyukto yogī yujyate tatpade 
atrākāśe pravakṣyāmi ye rudrāḥ saṃvyavasthitāḥ ।। 

vastrāpadaṃ rudrakoṭim avimuktaṃ mahālayam 
gokīrṇaṃ bhadrakarṇaṃ ca svarṇākṣaṃ sthāṇumaṣṭamam ।। 

pavitrāṣṭakametaddhi samāsena prakīrtitam 
asya bāhye ahaṃkāraḥ tatra rudrānnibodha me ।। 

chagalāṇḍaṃ duraṇḍaṃ ca mākoṭaṃ maṇḍaleśvaram 
kālañjaraṃ śaṅkukarṇaṃ sthūleśvarasthaleśvarau ।। 

sthāṇvaṣṭakaṃ samākhyātaṃ pūrvādīśānagocaram 
madhyadeśesthito rudras tv ahaṃkāreśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

śvetaṃ raktaṃ tathā pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sphaṭikasaprabham 
pañcāṣṭakeṣu ye varṇāḥ samāsātkathitāstava ।। 

sitā raktāstathā kṛṣṇā nīlāḥ śyāmā balāhakāḥ 
pītāḥ śuklāśca vijñeyāḥ adhastu dhūmravarcasaḥ ।। 

śatarudrāḥ samākhyātās trinetrāḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ 
candrārdhamaulayaḥ sarve rudrāṇībhiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। 

padmākṛtīni jñeyāni citraratnayutāni ca 
śatarudrabhuvanāni bhogaiśvaryayutāni ca ।। 

pañcāṣṭake purāṇi syuḥ kūrmākārāṇi sarvataḥ 
ākāśāvaraṇādūrdhvam ahaṃkārādadhaḥ priye ।। 

bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ punaḥ 
ādau tu gandhatanmātraṃ vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ mahat ।। 

sthitaṃ vitānavaddevi yojanānekakoṭayaḥ 
śuklaraktasitāpītaharitaṃ sphaṭikaprabham ।। 

vitānamiva deveśi sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalam 
śarvo hyadhipatistatra eka eva varānane ।। 

tasmāttu jāyate pṛthvī śarveśena pracoditā 
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ rasatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। 

haritaṃ marakataśyāmaṃ cāṣapakṣanibhaṃ priye 
bhavo hyadhipatistatra eka eva varānane ।। 

tasmādāpo viniṣkrāntā bhaveśena pracoditāḥ 
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ rūpatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। 

sphuratsūryāṃśudīptābhaṃ padmarāgasamaprabham 
rudraḥ paśupatistatra eka evāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

tasmāttejo viniṣkrāntaṃ tadvai paśupatīcchayā 
tattejaḥ sarvalokānāṃ vyāpakaṃ parameśvari ।। 

tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sparśatanmātramaṇḍalam 
sandhyāruṇasamacchāyaṃ vāyavyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ priye ।। 

vitānākārasadṛśaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam 
tatraiva maṇḍale devi tv īśānaḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। 

tasmādvāyurviniṣkrānta īśecchāpreritaḥ priye 
tasmātprāṇādayaḥ pañca vāyostadvyāpakaḥ paraḥ ।। 

saptadhā saptadhā so api sa eko bahudhā gataḥ 
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ śabdatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। 

nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ svacchodakasamaprabham 
vitānasadṛśākāraṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। 

bhīmastatrādhipatyena eka evāvatiṣṭhate 
tasmānnabho viniṣkrāntaṃ bhīmecchācoditaṃ mahat ।। 

vyāpakaṃ sarvalokānāṃ parāparagataṃ priye 
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sūryamaṇḍalamucyate ।। 

sahasrādityasaṃkāśaṃ dīpyamānaṃ samantataḥ 
vitānavadraśmidīptaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। 

rudro hyadhipatistatra tv eka evāvatiṣṭhate 
sūryāstasmādviniṣkrāntāḥ kalpe kalpe varānane ।। 

tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ somamaṇḍalamucyate 
candrakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ tejasā tulyamaṇḍalam ।। 

adhipatistu mahādeva eka evāvatiṣṭhate 
tasmāccandrādime candrā mahādevena coditāḥ ।। 

asaṃkhyātāḥ sahasrāṇi kalpe kalpee vinirgatāḥ 
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ vedamaṇḍalamucyate ।। 

candrakoṭisamacchāyaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam 
vitānavatsthitaṃ divyam ugreśasamadhiṣṭhitam ।। 

saṃruddhaṃ vāmayā tattu tasmādvai nirgatāni tu 
yajamānasahasrāṇi kalpe kalpe sthitāni hi ।। 

brahmaṇastapasogreṇa ugreśena pracoditāt 
vedayajñāśca vividhā brahmaṇo anantavartmanaḥ ।। 

tasmādete pravartante yajñā yajñaphalāni ca 
tapodānādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ vāmaśaktyā niyantritāḥ ।। 

ityeṣṭau tanavastvetāḥ parā vai saṃprakīrtitāḥ 
aparā brahmaṇo aṇḍaṃ vai vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

ebhyaḥ parataraṃ cāpi maṇḍalaṃ karaṇātmakam 
śuklaraktāsitaṃ pītaṃ haritaṃ cāpi varṇataḥ ।। 

pañcādhipāstu tiṣṭhanti maṇḍale karaṇātmake 
karmadevāḥ pravartante tasmādvai sarvadehinām ।। 

vākpāṇipādapāyuśca upasthaśceti pañcamaḥ 
ebhyaḥ prakāśakaṃ nāma parataḥ sūryasaṃnibham ।। 

tasmādvai saṃpravartante pañca buddhīndriyāṇi tu 
śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā ca yathākramam ।। 

viṣayālocanaṃ vṛttiḥ tejomaṇḍalasaṃsthitāḥ 
svākyādhipatayo nityaṃ teṣveva praticodakāḥ ।। 

ebhyaḥ parataraṃ cāsti candramaṇḍalasannibham 
vistārātpariṇāhācca sarvato raśmimaṇḍalam ।। 

tasmādvai saṃpravartante pañcārthāḥ sarvadehinām 
śabdaḥ sparśastathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ ।। 

ebhyaḥ parataraṃ cāpi saumyaṃ somasya maṇḍalam 
tasmānmano viniṣkrāntaṃ raśmibhirdarśapañcabhiḥ ।। 

cittaṃ ceto manaśceti śabdādyakṣapravartakam 
tasyādhipo mahātejāś candramāḥ saumyatejasā ।। 

tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ parato maṇḍalaṃ mahat 
japākusumasaṃkāśam aruṇādityasaṃnibham ।। 

pūrvavacca pramāṇenna samantātparimaṇḍalam 
tasmāttu maṇḍalāddevi sandhyāruṇasamadyutiḥ ।। 

sadhūmo agnirivāsau vai ahaṃkāraḥ pravartate 
antaḥkaraṇamātmasthaṃ yenedaṃ raṃjitaṃ jagat ।। 

mattadvipa ivāndhastu dāvāgnirupasarpati 
tasyādhidevo rudro vai yenāyaṃ preryate sadā ।। 

chagalāṇḍādayo devi pūrvaṃ te kathitā mayā 
ahaṃkārādathordhvaṃ tu buddhyāvaraṇamucyate ।। 

sūryakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ tejasā tulyavarcasam 
aṣṭānāṃ devayonīnām atraiva bhuvanaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

kakubhaṃ nāma bhuvanaṃ sandhyāruṇasamaprabham 
mānasībhistu tatstrībhir muditābhiḥ samākulam ।। 

sthitāstatra piśācāstu sandhyāruṇasamaprābhāḥ 
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi teṣāṃ tatra nivāsinām ।। 

svanando nāma vikrāntaḥ piśāceṣvīśvaro mahān 
sandhyāruṇasamacchāyo bandhūkakusumākṛtiḥ ।। 

kuṇḍalābharaṇopeto hārakeyūrabhūṣitaḥ 
kirīṭī cāṅgadī maulī hemacīnāmbaraḥ śubhaḥ ।। 

parivṛto bhūtagaṇaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ pārśvagaistathā 
nānārūpadharairdivyair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। 

divyamālyānulepaistu divyaiśvaryasamanvitaiḥ 
parivṛto mahātejā gaṇairiva mahāgaṇaḥ ।। 

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rākṣāsaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat 
kokilākaṇṭhasadṛśaṃ nīlajīmutasaṃnibham ।। 

tasmistu bhuvane divye divyaiśvaryasamanvite 
karālo rākṣaseśo vai jātyañjananibho mahān ।। 

kiriṭī kuṇḍalī dīptaḥ śobhate tu mahādyutiḥ 
jātyañjananibhaḥ śrīmān dāvāgniriva parvate ।। 

daśakoṭisahasrāṇi muditā nāma rākṣasāḥ 
bhṛṅgajīmūtavarṇābhā vasantyatra mahāprabhāḥ ।। 

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yākṣaṃ vai bhuvanaṃ mahat 
jāmbūnadamayaṃ sarvaṃ divyaratnasamujjvalam ।। 

bhogaiśvaryasamutpannaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam 
tasmiṃstu bhuvane bhadre subhadro nāma yakṣarāṭ ।। 

taptakāñcanavarṇābho makuṭādivibhūṣitaḥ 
śatakoṭisahasraistu yakṣairamitavikramaiḥ ।। 

tairvṛto bhrājate sarvaiḥ śarvaḥ sarvagaṇairiva 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi gāndharvaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। 

pītakauśītakīprakhyaṃ campakaistu samacchavi 
tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye surūpo nāma vai priye ।। 

gandharvadevādhipati gandhamādanasannibhaḥ 
taptajāmbūnadanibhas taruṇādityasaprabhaḥ ।। 

divyagandhānuliptāṅgo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
daśakoṭisahasraistu gandharvaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। 

manaḥ śilābhaṅganibhair haritālanibhaistathā 
svakāntā nāma gandharvāś citramālyānulepanāḥ ।। 

citrāmbaradharāḥ sarve citrābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
tasmātparataraṃ vakṣye sthānam aindraṃ ca pārvati ।। 

bṛhadbhogamiti khyātaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ sarvakāmadam 
śaṅkhagokṣīradhavalaṃ śaratkundendusannibham ।। 

tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye divyāścaryaśatairyute 
vibhūtirnāma bhagavān mahendro bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। 

candramaṇḍalasaṅkāśo muktāhāravibhūṣitaḥ 
śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmāñc chuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।। 

jvalatkirīṭo dīptābhyāṃ kuṇḍalābhyāmalaṃkṛtaḥ 
hārakeyūravāñchvetaḥ śvetoṣṇīṣavibhūṣitaḥ ।। 

bhūtijā nāma vai devā vibhūtyā parayā yutāḥ 
kirīṭinaḥ kuṇḍalino divyamālyavibhūṣitāḥ ।। 

daśakoṭisahasrāṇi devāścendrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tairāvṛto mahātejā nakṣatrairiva candramāḥ ।। 

manojaṃ nāma bhuvanaṃ śaraccandranibhaṃ śubham 
śuklābhrakanibhaṃ dīptaṃ muktāhārasuvarcasam ।। 

amṛto nāma vai tatra candramāḥ paramaḥ sthitaḥ 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaḥ śrīmāñcchuklāmbarodvahaḥ ।। 

kuṇḍalairdīptisaṃkāśair bhūṣitastu virājate 
divyagandhānuliptāṅgo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

tatra vai raśmayo nāmnā raśmivyūhasamaprabhāḥ 
divyāḥ saumyāstu te jñeyāḥ somatejaḥ samudbhavāḥ ।। 

daśakoṭisahasrāṇi teṣāṃ vai saumyatejasām 
ata ūrdhvaṃ tu deveśi prājeśāṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। 

tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye prajeśastvamitadyutiḥ 
viśvarūpo viśvavarṇo viśvālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

viśvarūpaparairdevair viśvātmā parivāritaḥ 
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi viśvānāṃ bhūritejasām ।। 

parivārya mahātmānaṃ śobhane paryupāsate 
brāhmaṃ caivamato jñeyaṃ śaṅkhagokṣīrasannibham ।। 

pitāmaho yatra devaḥ śuklapadmasthasaumyadṛk 
śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmāñ chuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।। 

śuklayajñopavītī ca mahāhāravibhūṣitaḥ 
daśakoṭisahasraistu candrabimbasamaprabhaiḥ ।। 

brāhmairdevaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śāradābhrairivāṃśumān 
paiśācaṃ rākṣāsaṃ yākṣaṃ gāndharvaṃ tvaindrameva ca ।। 

saumyaṃ tathaiva prājeśaṃ brāhmaṃ vai bhuvanaṃ priye 
etāni surayonīnāṃ sthānānyeva purāṇi tu ।। 

avatīryātmajanmānaṃ dhyāyantaḥ saṃbhavanti hi 
parameśaniyogācca codyamānāśca māyayā ।। 

niyamitā niyatyā ca brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥ 
vyajyante te ca sargādau nāmarūpairanekadhā ।। 

aṃśenaiva varārohe na tyajanti niketanam 
puryaṣṭakendriyaiḥ sārdham ātmā mantrairviśodhayet ।। 

pañcāṣṭakaṃ mūrtayo aṣṭau buddhitattvamanukramāt 
viśodhyaivaṃ prayatnena krodhāṣṭakamataḥ param ।। 

saṃvartastvekavīraśca kṛtānto jananāśakaḥ 
mṛtyuhantā ca raktākṣo mahākrodhaśca durjayaḥ ।। 

nīlotpaladalābhāni teṣāṃ vai bhuvanāni tu 
ekaikasya parīvāraḥ koṭirdaśasahasrakam ।। 

krodheśvarāṣṭakādūrdhvaṃ sthitaṃ tejoṣṭakaṃ mahat 
balādhyakṣo gaṇādhyakṣas tridaśastripurāntakaḥ ।। 

sarvarūpaśca śāntaśca nimeṣonmeṣa eva ca 
sahasraiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ parivāro abhidhīyate ।। 

agnirudrāḥ smṛtā hyate tejasā kṛṣṇavarṇakāḥ 
kūrmākārāṇi citrāṇi teṣāṃ vai bhuvanāni tu ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yogāṣṭakamanuttamam 
akṛtaṃ ca kṛtaṃ caiva raibhavaṃ brāhmameva ca ।। 

vaiṣṇavaṃ tvatha kaumāram aumaṃ śraikaṇṭhameva ca 
krīḍanti yoginastatra bhuvanaiḥ sphaṭikaprabhaiḥ ।। 

tataḥ sākṣādbhagavatī jaganmātā vyavasthitā 
umā tvameyā viśvasya viśvayoniḥ svayambhavā ।। 

taptajāmbūnadanibhā hy udayādityasaprabhā 
mahāpīṭhe maṇimaye siṃhāṣṭakayute śubhe ।। 

śatayojanavistīrṇe divyasragdhāmalālite 
divyakuṇḍalinī devī mahāhāravibhūṣitā ।। 

vijayāgre mahābhāgā śrīrivottamarūpiṇī 
jayā ca padmagarbhābhā sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitā ।। 

nandā ca padmapatrākṣī hārakeyūrabhūṣitā 
sarvābharaṇacitrāṅgī sunandā ca manoharā ।। 

parivārya pratīhāryaḥ sarvataḥ samupasthitāḥ 
triṃśatkoṭisahasrāṇi triṃśatkoṭiśatāni ca ।। 

mānasyo divyanāryastās tāṃ sadā paryupāsate 
vimānakoṭirekā ca rudrāṇāṃ bhūritejasām ।। 

aumā iti samākhyātāḥ vaimānā iti te anyathā 
upāsate tu tāṃ devīṃ mātaraṃ tanayā iva ।। 

sāvatīryāṇḍamadhye tu mayā sārdhaṃ varānane 
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ prādurbhūtā sanātanī ।। 

kalpe pūrve jaganmātā jagadyonirdvitīyake 
tṛtīye śāmbhavī nāma caturthe viśvarūpiṇī ।। 

pañcame nandinī nāma ṣaṣṭhe caiva gaṇāmbikā 
vibhūtiḥ saptame kalpe subhūtiścāṣṭame tathā ।। 

ānandā navame kalpe daśame vāmalocanā 
ekādaśe varārohā dvādaśe ca sumaṅgalā ।। 

kalpe trayodaśe devi mahātanurudāhṛtā 
kalpe caturdaśe caiva anantā nāma kīrtitā ।। 

bhūtamātā pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe cottamā smṛtā 
sahasradhārā saptadaśe satī cāṣṭadaśe purā ।। 

cākṣuṣasya manoḥ kalpe dakṣasya duhitā śubhā 
avamānācca dakṣasya svāṃ tanuṃ tvajahāḥ purā ।। 

amāṃ kalāṃ tu candrasya punarāpūrya saṃsthitā 
punarhimavatārādhya duhitā tvātmanaḥ kṛtā ।। 

tvaṃ devi sādbhutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram 
māṃ bhartāraṃ punaḥ prāpya jātāsyaṅgaruhā priye ।। 

kailāsanilayaścāhaṃ tvayā sārdhaṃ varānane 
tvaṃ tanurvāmabhāgasya matto naiva viyujyase ।। 

dakṣādhvare punarjātā bhadrakālīti nāmataḥ 
ekānaṃśāparā mūrtiḥ satīśānādviniḥsṛtā ।। 

idaṃ caturyugaṃ prāpya dvāpare viṣṇunā saha 
mahiṣasya vadhārthāya utpannā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā ।। 

kātyāyanīti durgeti vividhairnāmaparyayaiḥ 
manuṣyāṇāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ varadā bhaktavatsalā ।। 

pūrvamavāvatīrṇāsi vindhyaparvatamūrdhani 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuvanaṃ varavarṇini ।। 

sucārviti tu vikhyātaṃ sahasrādityakāntimat 
kailāsaśikharākāraṃ śuddhasphaṭikasaprabham ।। 

mahāvimānakoṭībhir āvṛtaṃ cakravartinām 
tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye sūryakoṭisamadyutiḥ ।। 

sahasrabāhucaraṇaḥ sahasravadanekṣaṇaḥ 
umāpatirjagannāthaḥ sarvānugrahakṛdvaraḥ ।। 

bhogasthānaṃ samastaṃ vai tatrasthaṃ vāmabhāgataḥ 
śatayojanavistīrṇe nānāratnavibhūṣite ।। 

divyāstaraṇasaṃchanne ādityaśatasannibhe 
āsane parame divye ratnapadmavicitrite ।। 

upaviṣṭo mahātejā vṛṣabhairaṣṭabhirvṛtaḥ 
hemacīnāmbaradharo hārakeyūrabhūṣitaḥ ।। 

dhārayansupradīpte ca sūryamaṇḍalasannibhe 
sphuranmayūkhasaṃghāte kuṇḍale raśmisaṃkule ।। 

dhārayanmakuṭaṃ mūrdhni divyaratnavicitritam 
dedīpyamānamatyugraṃ kailāsaśikharopamam ।। 

pralambo asya mahāhāraḥ prabhavadraśmisaṃkulaḥ 
gāṅgo himavataḥ śṛṅgāt patito nirjharo yathā ।। 

triṃśatkoṭisahasraistu triṃśatkoṭiśataistathā 
śūlibhirjaṭibhistryakṣair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। 

nānārūpadharair rudrair vṛto bhūtagaṇaistathā 
divyābhirmānasībhiśca nārībhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। 

vimānaśatakoṭībhir āvṛtaḥ sarva eva tu 
mātaraḥ sapta rūpiṇyo nānālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ ।। 

parivārya mahātmānaṃ samantātparyavasthitāḥ 
brāhmī kamalapatrābhā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā ।। 

āgneyyāṃ diśi deveśi sthitā vai śrīrivāparā 
śaṅkhagokṣīrasaṃkāśā tv aiśānyāṃ tu varānane ।। 

māheśvarī mahātejās tiṣṭhate surapūjitā 
kaumārī padmagarbhābhā hārakeyūrabhūṣitā ।। 

diśyuttarasyāṃ deveśi kāminīparyupāsitā 
snigdhanīlotpalanibhā hārakuṇḍalamaṇḍaitā ।। 

dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi tu sā upāste parameśvaram 
vaiṣṇavīti ca vikhyātā śivena paramātmanā ।। 

nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā 
vāruṇyāṃ diśi deveśi vārāhī paryupasthitā ।। 

śaṅkhakundendudhavalā hārakuṇḍalamaṇḍitā 
aindryāṃ diśi ca sā devī indrāṇī paryupasthitā ।। 

karālavadanā dīptā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā 
nairṛtyāṃ diśi cāmuṇḍā upāste parameśvaram ।। 

na tyajanti hi tā devaṃ sarvabhāvasamanvitam 
aṃśena mānuṣaṃ lokaṃ brahmaṇā cāvatāritāḥ ।। 

asurāṇāṃ vadhārthāya manuṣyāṇāṃ hitāya ca 
tapastaptvā mahāghoraṃ brahmaṇā lokadhāriṇā ।। 

ruroścaiva vadhārthāya mayāpi tvavatāritāḥ 
svacchandāstu parāścānyāḥ paravyomni vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

svacchandaṃ paryupāsīnāḥ parāparavibhāgataḥ 
umaiva saptadhā bhūtvā nāmarūpaviparyayaiḥ ।। 

evaṃ sa bhagavāndevo mātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ 
āste paramayā lakṣmyā tatrastho dyotayañjagat ।। 

asyopari tathā cāṣṭau mūrtayastasya dhīmataḥ 
śarvo bhavaśca bhagavān rudraḥ paśupatistathā ।। 

īśānaścaiva bhīmaśca mahādevogra eva ca 
etābhiḥ kurute śarvo mūrtibhiḥ sṛṣṭimuttamām ।। 

bhūmirāpo analo vāyur ākāśaṃ sūrya eva ca 
somaśca yajamānaścety aṣṭau sṛṣṭiriyaṃ smṛtā ।। 

sarvātmanā tu te tasminn anyatraikāṃśataḥ sthitāḥ 
evamasminsthito devo brahmalokordhvatastathā ।। 

merośca mūrdhanīśāno yogāṣṭakamatheṣyate 
śrīkaṇṭha iti nāmnā ca kailāsanilayastathā ।। 

śarvādyābhiśca tanubhir aṣṭābhirvyāpya tiṣṭhati 
ye tu māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ saguṇaṃ paryupāsate ।। 

bhaktyā ca brahmacaryeṇa satyena ca damena ca 
dṛṣṭvā dehasthamātmānaṃ te atra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। 

dṛṣṭvā ca maṇḍalaṃ tasya bhaktyā ca parayā bhṛśam 
muktadvaitā yatātmānas tatra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। 

teṣāṃ caivopariṣṭāttu suśivā dvādaśa sthitāḥ 
vāmo bhīmastatheśaśca śivaḥ śarvastathaiva ca ।। 

vidyānāmadhipaścaiva ekavīraḥ pracaṇḍadhṛt 
īśānaścāpyumābhartā ajeśo ananta eva ca ।। 

tathā ekaśivaścāpi suśivā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ 
sarve kuṅkumasaṃkāśāḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhāḥ ।। 

bhuvaneṣu vicitreṣu śaṅkhākāreṣu saṃsthitāḥ 
ata ūrdhvaṃ vīrabhadro maṇḍalādhipatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

tatsāyujyamanuprāpya tenaiva saha modate 
ata ūrdhvaṃ mahādevi mahādevāṣṭakaṃ viduḥ ।। 

mahādevo mahātejā vāmadevabhavodbhavau 
ekapiṅgekṣaṇeśānau bhuvaneśapuraḥsarāḥ ।। 

aṅguṣṭhamātrasahitā mahādevāṣṭake śivāḥ 
māyāñjanavinirmuktāḥ parameśānasaṃmatāḥ ।। 

buddhitattve samāsane bhuvaneśā mayoditāḥ 
athordhvaṃ guṇatattvaṃ tu tasmiṃścaiva vyavasthitam ।। 

gurupaṅktitrayaṃ divyaṃ guṇairantaritaṃ sthitam 
prathamā tamasaḥ paṅktir upariṣṭādvyavasthitā ।। 

teṣāṃ nāmāni kathyante yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
śivaḥ prabhurvāmadevaś caṇḍaścaiva pratāpavān ।। 

prahlādaścottamo bhīmaḥ karālaḥ piṅgalastathā 
mahendro dinakṛccaiva pratodo dakṣa eva ca ।। 

kalevaraśca vikhyātas tathā caiva kaṭaṅkaṭaḥ 
ambuhartā ca nārīśaḥ śveta ṛgveda eva ca ।। 

yajurvedaḥ sāmavedas tv atharvā suśivastathā 
virūpākṣastathā jyeṣṭho vipro nārāyaṇastathā ।। 

gaṇḍo naro yamo mālī gahaneśaśca pīḍanaḥ 
prathamā paṅktiruddiṣṭā rudrairdvātriṃśatā smṛtā ।। 

rajasaścopariṣṭāttu dvitīyā paṅktirucyate 
śuklo dāsaḥ sudāsaśca lokākṣaḥ sūrya eva ca ।। 

suhotra ekapādaśca gṛhaścaiva śiveśvaraḥ 
gautamaścaiva yogīśo dadhibāhustathāparaḥ ।। 

ṛṣabhaścaiva gokarṇo devaścaiva maheśvaraḥ 
guhyeśānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca jaṭī mālī tathograkaḥ ।। 

bhṛguḥ śikhi tathā śūlī sugatiśca supālanaḥ 
aṭṭahāso dārukaśca lāṅgaliścātidaṇḍakaḥ ।। 

bhavanaśca tathā bhavyo lakuleśastathaiva ca 
triṃśadrudrāḥ samākhyātā dvitīyā paṅktiruttamā ।। 

sattvasya copariṣṭāttu tṛtīyā paṅktirucyate 
devo aruṇo dīrghabāhur atibhūtiśca sthāṇukaḥ ।। 

sadyojātastathā jhiṇṭhi ṣaṇmukhaścaturānanaḥ 
cakrapāṇiśca kūrmākhyas tv ardhanārīśvarastathā ।। 

kapālī bhūrbhuvaścaiva vaṣaṭkārastathaiva ca 
vauṣaṭkārastathā svāhā svadhā ca parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

saṃvartakaśca bhasmeśaḥ kāmanāśana eva ca 
ekaviṃśatirudrāstu paṅktireṣā tṛtīyakā ।। 

jñānayogabalopetāḥ krīḍante daiśikottamāḥ 
saṃsārapāśanirmuktāḥ mahāmohavivarjitāḥ ।। 

trinetrā guravaḥ sarve śuddhasphaṭikanirmalāḥ 
sarvajñāḥ sarvagāścaiva lokānugrahakārakāḥ ।। 

gajākārāṇi divyāni sarveṣāṃ bhuvanāni tu 
buddheḥ prakṛtiparyante ye rudrāstānnibodha me ।। 

śatadvayaṃ saptakaṃ ca bhuvanānāṃ varānane 
antarbhūtāḥ sthitāścānye ye te noktā varānane ।। 

guṇānāmupariṣṭāttu pradhānaṃ parikīrtitam 
tatra ye saṃsthitā rudrāḥ kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। 

krodheśvaraśca saṃvarto jyotiḥ piṅgalakrūradṛk 
pañcāntakaikavīrau ca śikhedasahiteśvarāḥ ।। 

tattve tu prākṛte rudra mahāvīryāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
guṇānāṃ yā parākāṣṭhā tatpradhānamihocyate ।। 

ataḥ puruṣatattve tu bhuvanāni nibodha me 
ambā ca salilā oghā vṛṣṭiḥ sārdhaṃ ca tārayā ।। 

sutārā ca sunetrā ca kumārī ca tataḥ param 
uttamāmbhasikā caiva tuṣṭayo nava kīrtitāḥ ।। 

tārā caiva sutārā ca tārayantī pramodikā 
pramoditā modamānā ramyakā ca tataḥ param ।। 

sadāpramudikā caiva siddhyaṣṭakamudāhṛtam 
aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca ।। 

prākāmyaṃ ca tatheśitvaṃ vaśitvaṃ yadudāhṛtam 
yatrakāmāvasāyitvam aṇimādyaṣṭakaṃ smṛtam ।। 

athordhvaṃ guruśiṣyāṇāṃ paṅktitrayamataḥ śṛṇu 
maskarī pūraṇaḥ kṛtsnaḥ kapilaḥ kāśa evaca ।। 

sanatkumāragautamav asiṣṭhādyāṃśakāstathā 
kaśyapo nāsiketuśca gālavo bhautikastathā ।। 

śākalyaśca samākhyāto durvāsāḥ paramas tv ṛṣiḥ 
vālmīkiśca guruśreṣṭhaḥ saparāśaragālavaḥ ।। 

pippalādāśca saumitrir vāyuputro bhadantakaḥ 
maskaryādibhadantāntā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasya vādinaḥ ।। 

dvāviṃśatirguruvarāḥ prathamā paṅktiriṣyate 
jahnuśca tṛṇabinduśca munistārkṣyastathaiva ca ।। 

dhyānāśrayo atha dīrghaśca hotā jāgara eva ca 
agastyo vasubhaumaśca upādhyāyaśca kīrtitaḥ ।। 

śukro bhṛgvagirā rāmo jamadagnisuto adhvagaḥ 
sthūlaśirā bālakhilyo manuśceti prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

vajrātreyo viśuddhaśca śivaścārurathānugaḥ 
jahnvādicāruparyantā dvitīyā paṅktiriṣyate ।। 

haro jhiṇṭhī pratodaśca amareśaścaturthakaḥ 
kṛṣṇapiṅgeśarudraśca indrajidvṛṣakaḥ śivaḥ ।। 

yamaḥ krūraśca vikhyāto gaṅgādhara umāpatiḥ 
bhūteśvaraḥ kapālīśaḥ śaṅkaraśca tathaiva ca ।। 

ardhanārīśvaraścaiva piṅgalaśca tathāparaḥ 
mahākālaśca saṃvarto maṇḍalī tvekavīrakaḥ ।। 

tathā cānyaśca vikhyāto bhārabhūteśvaro dhruvaḥ 
jahnvādicāruparyantā ṛṣayaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ ।। 

harādayo dhruvāntāśca guravo viṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ 
paṅktitrayaṃ samākhyātam ṛṣīṇāṃ guruśiṣyayoḥ ।। 

nāḍīvidyāṣṭakaṃ devi kathayāmi tvataḥ param 
iḍā ca candriṇī gaurī śāntiḥ śāntikarī tathā ।। 

mālā ca mālinī caiva svāhā caiva svadhā tathā 
athopariṣṭāddeveśi vigrahāṣṭakamucyate ।। 

kāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ caiva sukhaduḥkhakaraṃ tathā 
jñānaṃ sādhyaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ sādhanaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā ।। 

dehapāśānato vakṣye dharmaṃ ca daśadhoditam 
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryamakalkatā ।। 

akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucaṃ santoṣa ārjavam 
evaṃ daśavidho dharmo yenokto dharmakṛnnaraḥ ।। 

vikārānṣoḍaśākhyāsye parabhāvena saṃsthitān 
raso gandhaśca rūpaṃ ca sparśaḥ śabdastathaivaca ।। 

tanmātrapañcakaṃ khyātam indriyāṇi nibodha me 
vākpāṇipādaṃ pāyuśca upasthaḥ karmasaṃjñakam ।। 

śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā pañcamī smṛtā 
buddhīndriyāṇi deveśi manaḥ ṣoḍaśakaṃ smṛtam ।। 

dehapāśāḥ samākhyātāḥ atobuddhiguṇānviduḥ 
dharmojñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। 

adharmaśca tathājñānam avairāgyamanīśitā 
ahaṃkāraṃ ca trividhaṃ pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

vaikārikaṃ taijasaṃ ca bhūtādiṃ ca yathākramam 
dīkṣākāle yathā śuddhis tathā caiṣāṃ nibodha me ।। 

tamo rajastathā sattvaṃ śodhayedanupūrvaśaḥ 
śabdaḥ sparśastathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ ।। 

viṣayāśca samākhyātāḥ śodhanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ 
kāmaḥ krodhaśca lobhaśca mohaḥ paiśunyameva ca ।। 

janmamṛtyujarāvyādhikṣuttṛṭtṛṣṇāstathaiva ca 
viṣādaśca bhayaṃ caiva mado harṣaṇameva ca ।। 

rāgo dveṣaśca vaicittyaṃ kupitānṛtadrohitā 
māyā mātsaryadharmaśca adharmaścāsvatantratā ।। 

āgantukāśca bodhavyāḥ gaṇapāśānnibodha me 
devī nandimahākālau gaṇeśo vṛṣabhastathā ।। 

bhṛṅgī caṇḍīśvaraścaiva kārtikeyo aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
anantastritanuḥ sūkṣmaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaśca śivottamaḥ ।। 

śikhaṇḍī caikanetraśca ekarudrastathāparaḥ 
vidyeśvarātmakānpāśān dīkṣākāle viśodhayet ।। 

uktānuktāśca ye cātra anyatantroktalakṣaṇāḥ 
pauruṣeye tu śodhyāste tato mucyeta pudgalaḥ ।। 

athordhve niyatirjñeyā tasyāṃ rudrānnibodha me 
vāmadevastathā śarvas tathā caiva bhavodbhavau ।। 

vajradehaḥ prabhuścaiva dhātā ca kramavikramau 
suprabhedaśca daśamo niyatyāṃ śaṅkarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

yattaddhṛdi sthitaṃ padmam ātmā tatra vyavasthitaḥ 
niyatidalamahaṅkāra kesaraṃ buddhikarṇikam ।। 

kālatattve śivā jñeyā kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
śuddho buddhaḥ prabuddhaśca praśāntaḥ paramākṣaraḥ ।। 

śivaśca suśivaścaiva dhruvaścākṣaraśambhurāṭ 
daśaite tu śivā jñeyāḥ kālatattve varānane ।। 

hemābhāḥ śaṅkarāḥ proktāḥ śivaḥ sphaṭikasannibhāḥ 
ekaikasya vinirdiṣṭā parivāro yaśasvini ।। 

koṭirekā tathānyāni sahasrāṇi tu ṣoḍaśa 
kūrmākārāṇi sarveṣāṃ proktāni bhuvanāni tu ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ hariharau rāgatattve nibodha me 
suhṛṣṭaḥ suprahṛṣṭaśca surūpo rūpavardhanaḥ ।। 

manonmano mahādhīraḥ vīreśāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
rāgatattve pravakṣyāmi ye anye rudrā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

kalyāṇaḥ piṅgalo babhrur vīraśca prabbhavastathā 
medhātithiścchandakaśca dāhakaḥ śāstrakāriṇaḥ ।। 

pañcaśiṣyāstathācāryā daśaite saṃvyavasthitāḥ 
vidyātattvamataścordhvaṃ tasminvai bhuvanaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

vāmo jyeṣṭhaśca raudraśca kalo vikaraṇastathā 
balavikaraṇaścaiva balapramathanastathā ।। 

sarvabhūtadamanaśca tathā caiva manonmanaḥ 
kalātattve mahādevi mahādevatrayaṃ sthitam ।। 

mahādevo mahātejā mahājyotiḥ pratāpavān 
kalātattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ samāsena varānane ।। 

ete rudrā mahādevi trinetrāścandraśekharāḥ 
rudrakoṭisahasraistu samantātparivāritāḥ ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśāḥ yogaiśvaryabalānvitāḥ 
rāge raktāstu vijñeyā jñānayogabalotkaṭāḥ ।। 

chatrākārāstu teṣāṃ vai gṛhā ratnavicitritāḥ 
upariṣṭādbhavenmāyā kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। 

vyāpya yā vai tvadhodhvānaṃ vaiśvarūpyeṇa saṃsthitā 
tatra rudrā mahābhāgā dvādaśaiva mahābalāḥ ।। 

gahanaśca asādhyaśca tathā hariharaḥ prabhuḥ 
daśeśānaśca deveśi trigalo gopatistathā ।। 

adhaḥpuṭe tu vijñeyā māyātattve varānane 
kṣemeśo brahmaṇaḥ svāmī vidyeśānastathaiva ca ।। 

vidyeśaśca śaivaścaiva anantaḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate 
ūrdhvamāyāpuṭasthāstu rudrā ete prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

eṣāṃ madhye tu bhagavān ananteśo jagatpatiḥ 
udbhavaṃ bhāvayitvā tu svecchayā kurute prabhuḥ ।। 

sarvajñaḥ sarvakartā ca nigrahānugrahe rataḥ 
prathamena tu bhedena rudrā dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ ।। 

asmiṃstu ye yathā rudrā māyātattve vyavasthitāḥ 
tathāhaṃ kathayiṣyāmi bhedatrayavibhāgaśaḥ ।। 

gopatiśca tato devi adhogranthau vyavasthitaḥ 
granthyūrdhve saṃsthito viśvas trikalaḥ kṣema eva ca ।। 

brahmaṇo adhipatiścaiva śivaśceti sa pañcamaḥ 
adha ūrdhvamanantastu pāśāścaivātra saṃsthitāḥ ।। 

pūrvaṃ vai kathitā devi ato ṛṣikulaṃ bhavet 
yonirvāgīśvarī caiva yasyāṃ jāto na jāyate ।। 

oṃkārasādhyadhātāro damaneśastataḥ param 
dhyānaṃ bhasmeśamevāhuḥ pramāṇāni tadūrdhvataḥ ।। 

pañcārthaṃ guhyamevāhū rudrāṅkuśamataḥ param 
hṛdayaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva vyuhamākarṣameva ca ।। 

ādarśaṃ ca tathaiveha aṣṭamaṃ parikīrtitam 
ete parivṛtā devi rudrakoṭisahasrakaiḥ ।। 

nānāvarṇavicitrāśca nānābbharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
nānānārīsahasraistu ramante patyuricchayā ।। 

trinetrāḥ śūlinaḥ sarve jaṭācandrakīrīṭinaḥ 
aluptaśaktivibhavā māyātattvādhikāriṇaḥ ।। 

bhuvaneṣu vicitreṣu yonyākāreṣu saṃsthitāḥ 
ataḥ paraṃ bhavenmāyā sarvajantuvimohinī ।। 

nirvairaparipanthinyā tayā bhramitabuddhayaḥ 
idaṃ tattvamidaṃ neti vivadantīha vādinaḥ ।। 

satpathaṃ tu parityajya nayati drutamutpatham 
gurudevāgniśāstrasya ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ ।। 

asadyuktivicārajñāḥ śuṣkatarkāvalaṃbinaḥ 
bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hy amokṣe mokṣalipsayā ।। 

śivadīkṣāsinā cchinnā na prarohettu sā punaḥ 
athopari mahāvidyā sarvavidyābhavodbhavā ।। 

jagataḥ pralayotpattivibhūtinidhiravyayā 
sā eva paramā devī vāgīśīti nigadyate ।। 

aṣṭavargavibhinnā ca vidyā sā mātṛkaiva tu 
bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

vāmā jyeṣṭhā tathā raudrī kālī vikaraṇī tathā 
balavikaraṇī caiva balapramathanī tāthā ।। 

damanī sarvabhūtānāṃ tathā caiva manonmanī 
taptacāmīkarākārāḥ pañcavaktrāstrilocanāḥ ।। 

amoghavīryāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvataḥ sarvadā sthitāḥ 
sarvajñānugatāḥ sarvāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। 

sarvalakṣaṇasampannaḥ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitāḥ 
pradhānāḥ sapta koṭyastu mantrāṇāṃ yā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

ekaikasya parīvāro lakṣāyutasahasraśaḥ 
padmākāreṣu divyeṣu krīḍanti bhuvaneṣu te ।। 

triguṇī brahmavetālī sthāṇumatyambikā parā 
rūpiṇī mardinī jvālā saptasaṅkhyāstadīśvarāḥ ।। 

vidyārājñyaḥ samākhyātāḥ dīkṣākāle viśodhayet 
bāhye tasyaiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ bhuvanānyatra me śṛṇu ।। 

aṣṭavidyeśvarairyukto vītamāyo nirañjanaḥ 
sthitisaṃhārakartā vai mokṣaiśvaryapradāyakaḥ ।। 

tasyāsanaṃ tu vistīrṇaṃ sahasradalasammitam 
tisraḥ koṭyo ardhakoṭiśca mantrāstasyāsane sthitāḥ ।। 

tatrastha īśvaro devo varadaḥ sārvatomukhaḥ 
pañcavaktraḥ sutejasko daśabāhustrilocanaḥ ।। 

gokṣīradhavalaḥ saumyo nāgayajñopavītavān 
divyāmbaradharo devo divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।। 

sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
triśūlapāṇīndumaulir jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaḥ ।। 

prasannavadanaḥ kānto yogaiśvaryapradāyakaḥ 
varadābhayahastaśca dhyeyo asāvīśayogibhiḥ ।। 

tasyotsaṅgagatā vidyā sarvavidyāsamāsritā 
divyavastraparīdhānā divyamālyānulepanā ।। 

divyasragdāmamālābhir muktāhārairvibhūṣitā 
muktāphalapratīkāśā pañcavaktrā trilocanā ।। 

ārādhitā vidhānena vedayejjñāninaḥ sadā 
prahasantīva sā bhāti maheśavadanekṣaṇāt ।। 

vidyeśvarānato vakṣye pūrvādīśāntagānkramāt 
anantaścaiva sūkṣmaśca tathā caiva śivottamaḥ ।। 

ekanetraikarudrau ca trinetraśca prakīrtitaḥ 
śrīkaṇṭhaśca śikhaṇḍī ca jñeyā vidyeśvarāḥ kramāt ।। 

ato rūpamavasthānaṃ tatra rudrānnibodha me 
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aisvaryaṃ ca caturthakam ।। 

sūkṣmāvaraṇamūrdhve ataḥ tatra śaktitrayaṃ viduḥ 
vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrī ca śaktayaḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।। 

parivārastu tāsāṃ vai koṭyo anekāstu saṅkhyayā 
sarve sarvagatā mantrāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvakāmadā ।। 

śūddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśās trinetrāḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। 

sarvaiśvaryasusampūrṇāś cārucandrārdhaśekharāḥ 
śatapatrābjabhākāraiḥ śuddhahārenduraśmibhiḥ ।। 

nānāratnojjvalaiścitraiḥ prākāraistoraṇākulaiḥ 
īśvarānugatāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti bhuvaneṣu te ।। 

tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ pūjyante sarvakarmasu 
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ divyaṃ ye caranti jitendriyāḥ ।। 

bhasmaniṣṭhā japadhyānās te vrajantyeśvaraṃ padam 
tatreśvarastu bhagavān devadevo nirañjanaḥ ।। 

adhikāraṃ prakurute śivecchāvidhicoditaḥ 
daśa pañca ca śodhyāni bhuvanānīśvare kramāt ।। 

tālukordhve vijānīyād dīkṣākāle varānane 
śuddhāvaraṇamūrdhvaṃ tu tasmiñcchaktidvayaṃ smṛtam ।। 

jñānaṃ kriyā ca vikhyātaṃ dve vidye cāpyataḥ param 
bhāvasaṃjñāpyabhāvākhyā tasmiñcchaktidvaye smṛte ।। 

tejeśaśca dhruveśaśca pramāṇānāṃ paraṃ padam 
pramāṇāvaraṇe cordhve kathayāmi ca mānataḥ ।। 

brahmā rudraḥ pratodaśca anantaśca caturthakaḥ 
suśuddhāvaraṇaṃ cordhve tatra rudratrayaṃ viduḥ ।। 

ekākṣaḥ piṅgalo haṃsaḥ kathitaṃ tu samāsataḥ 
śivāvaraṇamūrdhvaṃ tu tatraiko dhruvasaṃjñakaḥ ।। 

saṃsthito rudrarājasya mokṣāvaraṇamūrdhvataḥ 
ekādaśaiva rudrāṃśca kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। 

brahmadankidiṇḍimuṇḍāḥ saurabhaśca tathaivaca 
janmamṛtyuharaścaiva praṇītaḥ sukhaduḥkhadaḥ ।। 

vijṛmbhitaḥ samākhyātā stālūrdhve tu vyavasthitāḥ 
punarūrdhve dhruvaṃ jñeyaṃ nirañjanapadaṃ śubham ।। 

īśaśaktitrayaṃ mūrdhni kathitaṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ 
icchāśaktyabhidhānāyāḥ antarbhūtāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

prabuddhāvaraṇaṃ cordhve kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
prītaḥ pramuditaścaiva pramodaśca pralambakaḥ ।। 

viṣṇurmadana evātha gahanaḥ prathitastathā 
rudrāṣṭakaṃ samākhyātaṃ vijñeyaṃ prāgdiśaḥ kramāt ।। 

samayāvaraṇaṃ cordhve kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
prabhavaḥ samayaḥ kṣudro vimalaśca śivastathā ।। 

tato ghanaḥ samākhyāto nirañjanastataḥ param 
rudroṅkārastu pañcaite tālūrdhve tu vijānata ।। 

ekonaṣaṣṭirbhuvanaṃ jñānaśaktyāditaḥ kramāt 
rudroṅkārāntamityetad dīkṣākāle viśodhayet ।। 

ekaikasya parīvāraḥ koṭyo anekāḥ sahasraśaḥ 
trinetrā varadāḥ sarve śuddhasāmarthyavigrahāḥ ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśā daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ 
triśūlapāṇayaḥ sarve jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitāḥ ।। 

sarve sarvaguṇopetāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvadeśvarāḥ 
sārvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। 

rudrakanyāsamākīrṇā divyairūpairmanoharaiḥ 
saṃkriḍante puravaraiḥ śivecchāvidhicoditāḥ ।। 

īśvarasya tathordhve tu adhaścaiva sadāśivāt 
suśivāvaraṇaṃ cordhve tasmiñjñeyaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।। 

tripañcanayano devaś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ 
vaktrapañcakasaṃyukto daśabāhurmahābalaḥ ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaḥ sphuranvai dīptatejasā 
siṃhāsanopaviṣṭastu śvetapadmāsanasthitaḥ ।। 

pañcabrahmāṅgasahitaḥ sakalādyaiḥ samanvitaḥ 
daśabhiśca śivairyukto rudrāṣṭādaśakānvitaḥ ।। 

sakalo niṣkalaḥ śūnyaḥ kalāḍhyaḥ khamalaṅkṛtaḥ 
kṣapaṇaśca kṣayāntasthaḥ kaṇṭhyauṣṭhyaścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

bhruvormadhye tu vijñeyo devadevaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
sakalādyairvṛto devaḥ oṃkāreśādibhiḥ kramāt ।। 

oṃkāreśaḥ śivo dīptaḥ kāraṇeśo daśeśakaḥ 
suśivaścaiva kāleśaḥ sūkṣmarūpaḥ sutejasaḥ ।। 

śarvaśca daśamaḥ proktaḥ ūrdhvāntaṃ saṃvyavasthitāḥ 
rudrāścāṣṭādaśa bahiḥ teṣāṃ nāmāni vai śṛṇu ।। 

vijayastvatha niḥśvāsaḥ svayambhūścāgnivīrarāṭ 
rauravo mukuṭo visaraś candro bimbaḥ pragītavān ।। 

lalitaḥ siddharudraśca santānaḥ śarva eva ca 
paraśca kiraṇaścaiva pārameśvara eva ca ।। 

sādākhyastu samākhyātaḥ sakalo mantravigrahaḥ 
sarvakāraṇamadhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ ।। 

bhuktimuktipradātā ca sādhakānāṃ kriyāvatām 
koṭayaḥ saptamantrāṇām āsane tasya saṃsthitāḥ ।। 

āsanaṃ lakṣapatrāḍhyaṃ candrakoṭyayutaprabham 
vāmādyairvibhupūrvaiśca pañcavaktraistrilocanaiḥ ।। 

tārādyaiḥ śaktibhedaiśca prāgdiśaḥ parivāritam 
jñānaśaktiḥ kriyāśaktir vāme dakṣiṇataḥ sthite ।। 

icchāśaktiḥ parādevi yayā sarvamadhiṣṭhitam 
utpattisthitisaṃhārāṃs tirobhāvamanugraham ।। 

yayā karoti deveśaḥ sarvadā sarvamadhvani 
tasyotsaṅgagatā sā tu nityaṃ caivātmavartinī ।। 

sā cecchā devadevasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ 
sa evāpararūpeṇa pañcamantramahātanuḥ ।। 

icchārūpadharaḥ śrīmān devadevaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
śaktayastasya yāḥ proktāḥ tathā vai mantranāyakāḥ ।। 

ekaikaṃ parito devi padmairarbudakoṭibhiḥ 
tathā kharvanikharvaiśca pratirūpairmahābalaiḥ ।। 

vidyārūpaiḥ svarūpāḍhair aprameyaguṇānvitaiḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। 

hāsyalāsyavilāsāḍhyair bhrūkṣeponmadavibhramaiḥ 
candrakoṭiśataprakhyaiḥ prasravadbhirivāmṛtam ।। 

tābhiḥ sārdhaṃ sadā rudrāḥ prakīḍantīcchayā prabhoḥ 
puravaraiḥ sarvatobhadraiś candrakoṭisamaprabhaiḥ ।। 

māyādharmavinirmuktā nirmalā vigatajvarāḥ 
adhikāraṃ prakurvanti sarvajñāmoghaśaktayaḥ ।। 

adhikārakṣaye śāntā jāyante sarvagāḥ śivāḥ 
parapreryāḥ punarbhūyo na bhavanti kadācana ।। 

suśivāvaraṇaṃ khyātaṃ mantragarbhaṃ varānane 
bindvāvaraṇamūrdhve ataś candrakoṭisamaprabham ।। 

tatra padmaṃ mahādīptaṃ daśakoṭisamanvitam 
tatra padme sthito devaḥ śāntyatīto mahādyutiḥ ।। 

pañcavaktro viśālākṣo daśabāhustrīlocanaḥ 
taḍitsahasrapuñjābhaḥ sphuranmāṇikyamaṇḍitaḥ ।। 

nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntistathaiva ca 
parivāraḥ smṛtastasya śāntyatītasya suvrate ।। 

tasya vāme tu digbhāge śāntyatītā vyavasthitā 
pañcavaktrāḥ smṛtāḥ sarvā daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ ।। 

bindutattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ purakoṭyarbudairvṛtam 
ardhacandrastadūrdhve tu tadūrdhve tu nirodhikā ।। 

ete dve tu mahāsthāne pañcapañcakalānvite 
jyotsnā jyotsnāvatī kāntiḥ suprabhā vimalā śivā ।। 

ardhacandre sthitāhyetā nirodhinyāṃ śṛṇu priye 
rundhanī rodhanī raudrī jñānabodhā tamopahā ।। 

ardhamātraḥ smṛto binduḥ svarūpaśca catuṣkalaḥ 
tasyāpyardhamardhacandras tv aṣṭāṃśaśca nirodhikā ।। 

nirodhayati devānsā brahmādyāṃstu varānane 
nirodhinīti vikhyātā tāṃ bhittvā tu varānane ।। 

sādākhyaparabhāvena pañcamantrakahātanuḥ 
tasyordhve tu smṛto nādaḥ sa kiñjalkarajaḥ prabhaḥ ।। 

mahadbhiḥ puruṣairvyāptaḥ sūryakoṭyayutaprabhaiḥ 
teṣāṃ vai nāyikā vaksye bhuvane pañcasaṅkhyayā ।। 

indhikā dīpikā caiva rocikā mocikā tathā 
ūrdhvagā tu samākhyātā kalātveṣā tu pañcamī ।। 

tasminpadmaṃ suvistīrṇaṃ ūrdhvageśaḥ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ 
candrārbudapratīkāśaḥ pañcavaktrastrilocanaḥ ।। 

candrārdhaśekharaḥ śānto daśabāhurmahātanuḥ 
indhikādivṛto devaḥ śūlapāṇirjaṭādharaḥ ।। 

ūrdhvagā tu kalā tasya nityamutsaṅgagāminī 
tataḥ suṣumṇābhuvanaṃ suṣumṇā tatra saṃsthitā ।। 

suṣumṇeśaḥ sthitastatra candrakoṭyayutaprabhaḥ 
daśabāhustrinetraśca śvetapadmoparisthitaḥ ।। 

śaśāṅkaśekharaḥ śrīmān pañcavaktro mahātanuḥ 
iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva vāmadakṣiṇataḥ sthite ।। 

suṣumṇā tu varārohe tuṣārakaṇadhūsarā 
śvetapadmakarā devī padmamālāvibhūṣitā ।। 

pañcavaktrā suśobhāḍhyā trinetrā śūladhāriṇī 
tasyotsaṅgagatā devī dhyātavyā sādhakādibhiḥ ।। 

grathitastu tayā sarvas tv adhvāyamadha ūrdhvagaḥ 
nāḍyādhārastu nādo vai bhittvā sarvamidaṃ jagat ।। 

adhaḥśaktyā vinirgataya yāvadbrahmāṇamūrdhvataḥ 
nāḍyā brahmabile līnas tv avyaktadhvanirakṣaraḥ ।। 

nadate sarvabhūteṣu śivaśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitaḥ 
evaṃ jñātvā varārohe śodhayettaṃ śivādhvare ।। 

tato brahmabilaṃ jñeyaṃ rudrakoṭyarbudānvitam 
tatra brahmā paro jñeyaḥ śaśāṅkaśatasaprabbhaḥ ।। 

daśabāhustrinetraśca pañcavaktrenduśekharaḥ 
triśūlapāṇirbhagavāñ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaḥ ।। 

brahmāṇi tu parā śaktir yā sā mokṣapathe sthitā 
dvāraṃ yā mokṣamārgasya rodhayitvā vyavasthitā ।। 

mokṣamārgapradātrī ca brahmotsaṅge ca saṃsthitā 
tāṃ bhittvātra varārohe gantavyamūrdhvataḥ priye ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ sthitā śaktiḥ prasuptabhujagākṛtiḥ 
ādhāro bhuvanānāṃ sā tāṃ pravakṣyāmi suvrate ।। 

sūkṣmā caiva susūkṣmā ca tathā cānyāmṛtāmitā 
vyāpinī madhyato jñeyā śeṣāḥ pūrvāditaḥ kramāt ।। 

pañcavaktrāstrinetrāśca sutejaskā mahābalāḥ 
śaktitattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ śivatattvaṃ śṛṇu priye ।। 

puraśreṣṭhairanekaistu samantātparivāritam 
hemaprākāraracitaṃ ratnamāṇikyamaṇḍitam ।। 

aśeṣabhogasampannaṃ sarvakāmaguṇodayam 
bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi tatraiva saṃsthitāni tu ।। 

vyāpakaṃ vyomarūpaṃ ca anantānāthanāśritam 
kāraṇānāṃ pañcakaṃ ca śivatattve vyavasthitam ।। 

tatra padmaṃ suvisthīrṇam anantānantasambhavam 
tasya padmasya madhyastho devaścāyamanāśritaḥ ।। 

pañcavaktradharaḥ śāntaḥ sarvajñaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
daśabāhurmahādīptaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ ।। 

sarvānugrahakartā ca praṇatārtivināśanaḥ 
bhuktimuktipradātā ca sūryakoṭyarbudaprabhaḥ ।। 

sphuranmukuṭamāṇikyaḥ samantādupaśobhitaḥ 
divyāmbaradharo devo divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।। 

padmāsanonnatoraskaḥ śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharaḥ 
ābaddhamaṇiparyaṅkaś cāmarotkṣepavījitaḥ ।। 

rudrakoṭyarbudānīkaiḥ samantādupaśobhitaḥ 
vyāpinī vyomarūpā cānantānāthātvanāśritā ।। 

pañcavaktrā mahāvīryā daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ 
trinetrāḥ śūlahastāśca kāraṇaiśca samanvitāḥ ।। 

pūrvādyuttaraparyantā etāścaiva vyavasthitāḥ 
anāśrito madhyagastu saṃsthitaḥ prabhuravyayaḥ ।। 

anāśritakalā devī tasyotsaṅge ca saṃsthitā 
evaṃ vai śivatattvaṃ tu kathitaṃ tava sundari ।। 

śodhayitvā tataścordhvaṃ śaktiścaiva parā smṛtā 
samanā nāma sā jñeyā manaścordhvaṃ na jāyate ।। 

paripāṭyā sthitānāṃ tu pṛthivyādiśivāvadhau 
sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca kartṛbhūtā vyavasthitā ।। 

bibhartyaṇḍānyanekāni śivena samadhiṣṭhitā 
tatrāruḍhastu kurute śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

sṛṣṭisthitisamāhāraṃ tirobhāvamanugraham 
hetukartā maheśānaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।। 

samanā nāma yā śaktiḥ sā tasya karaṇaṃ smṛtam 
tayādhitiṣṭheddeveśo hy adhaḥkāraṇapañcakam ।। 

anāśritasya devasya kāraṇaṃ seyamāśritā 
sa vai prerayate bhūyas tv anāthaṃ tu jagatpatim ।। 

anāthaścāpyananteśam ananto vyomarūpiṇam 
vyomavyāpī mahādevo vyāpinaṃ bodhayetprabhum ।। 

vyāpinī karaṇaṃ tasya kartā vai vyāpyasau prabhuḥ 
karmarūpā sthitā māyā yadadhaḥ śaktikuṇḍalī ।। 

nādabindvātmakaṃ kāryam ityādijagadudbhavaḥ 
yatsadāśivaparyantaṃ pārthivādyaṃ ca suvrate ।। 

tatsarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ vināśotpattisaṃyutam 
yā sā śaktiḥ purā proktā samanā tvadhvamūrdhani ।। 

sphuratsūryasahasrābhakiraṇānantabhāsvarā 
dhyātvā caitāṃ samāvāhya sthāpayettu vidhānavit ।। 

upacāraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā vāgīśyāvāhanaṃ tathā 
sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva paśoryāgaṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

garbhadhāritvajanane adhikāraṃ tathaiva ca 
yogaṃ bhogaṃ layaṃ caiva niṣkṛtiṃ tadanantaram ।। 

bhuvanādhipahomaṃ ca bhuvanādhipavāsinām 
bhuvanānāṃ yathāyogaṃ homaṃ kṛtvā varānane ।। 

tritattvaṃ śadhayeccāto avayavāṃśca yathākramam 
viśleṣapāśacchedau ca kṛtvā pūrṇāṃ tu pātayet ।। 

prāyaścittaṃ tato hutvā kartarīmabhimantrayet 
śikhāṃ cchitvā samarpyaitāṃ śiśuṃ saṃsnāpayedguruḥ ।। 

ācāryaḥ prayato bhūtvā sakalīkaraṇādikam 
sruco agre tu śikhāṃ kṛtvā hutvā snāyādanantaram ।। 

sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ācāryastu varānane 
śiśorapi vidhiṃ kṛtvā śivakumbhaṃ samarcayet ।। 

bhairavaṃ madhyadeśasthaṃ bhairavāgniṃ samarcayet 
pūrṇāṃ sampūrya vidhivad vāmamantramanusmaran ।। 

pūrvoktalakṣaṇenaiva proccarettaṃ prayatnataḥ 
heyādhvānamadhaḥ kurvan necayettaṃ varānane ।। 

yāvatsā samanā śaktiḥ tadūrdhve conmanā smṛtā 
nātra kālaḥ kalāścāro na tattvaṃ na ca devatāḥ ।। 

sunirvāṇaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ guruvaktraṃ taducyate 
tadatītaṃ varārohe paraṃ tattvamanāmayam ।। 

guruvaktraprayogeṇa tasminyojyeta śāśvate 
niṣkampe kāraṇātīte viraje nirmale śubhe ।। 

sarvajñe parame tattve vyomātīte hyatīndriye 
ityadhvā caiṣa vai proktaḥ samāsena mayānaghe ।। 

jñātvā caivaṃ mahādevi prayāti paramaṃ padam 
dehe deve ca śiṣye ca kalaśe hyagnimadhyataḥ 
evaṃ jñātvā varārohe mucyate mocayatyapi ।। 

iti svacchandatantre daśamaḥ paṭalaḥ samāptaḥ

ekādaśaḥ paṭalaḥ

adhvāyaṃ tu mayā jñātas tvatprasādāt surādhipa 
jagatsṛṣṭistvayā deva sūcitā na tu varṇitā ।। 

adhvasṛṣṭiṃ mahādeva kathayasva prasādataḥ 
yo asau sūkṣmaḥ paro devaḥ kāraṇaṃ sarvagaḥ śivaḥ ।। 

nimittakāraṇaṃ so atra kathitastava suvrate 
akāmātsaṃsṛjetsarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। 

svatejasā varārohe vyoma saṃkṣobhya līlayā 
upādānaṃ tu tatproktaṃ saṃkṣubdhaṃ samavāyataḥ ।। 

tasmācchūnyaṃ samutpannaṃ śūnyātsparśasamudbhavaḥ 
tasmānnādaḥ samutpannaḥ pūrvaṃ vai kathitastava ।। 

aṣṭadhā sa tu deveśi vyaktaḥ śabdaprabhedataḥ 
ghoṣo rāvaḥ svanaḥ śabdaḥ sphoṭākhyo dhvanireva ca ।। 

jhāṅkāro dhvaṅkṛtaścaiva aṣṭau śabdāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
navamastu mahāśabdaḥ sarveṣāṃ vyāpakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

nadatyasau sadā yasmāt sarvabhūteṣvavasthitaḥ 
tasmāt sadāśivo devo vyakto vai dṛkkriyātmakaḥ ।। 

nādādbinduḥ samutpannaḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ 
sa caiva daśadhā jñeyo daśatattvaphalapradaḥ ।। 

daśadhā varṇarūpeṇa daśadaivatasaṃyutaḥ 
bindoḥ sadāśivo jñeyaḥ so aṣṭabhedāṅgasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

pañcabrahmakalābhiśca vidyāṅgaiḥ śaktibhiryutaḥ 
pañcabhiśca mahājñānair mūrtibhiśca samanvitaḥ ।। 

sa evāpararūpeṇa paramātmā śivo avyayaḥ 
dvidhāvasthaḥ sa ca jñeyaḥ soccāroccāravarjitaḥ ।। 

mudrāmantrasvarūpeṇa sa eva ca punardvidhā 
kriyājñānasvarūpeṇa icchārūpasvarūpataḥ ।। 

śabdāvabodharūpeṇa vasturūpasvarūpataḥ 
sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraścaiva parātīto nirañjanaḥ ।। 

vyomarūpasvarūpeṇa samanonmana eva ca 
unmanātīto deveśi śivo jñeyaḥ śivāgame ।। 

unmanāsamanāsthānaṃ śivena samadhiṣṭhitam 
pañcakāraṇarūpeṇa tadadhaḥ punareva saḥ ।। 

kāraṇaṃ pañcakaṃ devi adhiṣṭhāya tvadhastataḥ 
vyāpakaḥ śaktimūrdhastho biladvāramanāśritaḥ ।। 

anantaśca suṣumneśas tv anāthaścordhvagastathā 
vyomarūpī mahādevi bindvīśaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

anāśritaḥ svayaṃ brahmā samadhiṣṭhāya saṃsthitaḥ 
anātho viṣṇurityuktas tv ananto rudra eva ca ।। 

vyomarūpīśvaraḥ prokto vyāpī caiva sadāśivaḥ 
vyāpakaśca punardevi hāṭakaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

vidyāmantragaṇairyuktaḥ saptapātālanāyakaḥ 
anantaścaiva deveśi rudraḥ kālāgnivigrahaḥ ।। 

anātho anantarūpeṇa sthitaścādhvani dhārakaḥ 
anāśrito mahādevi sthito vai hūhukaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

svaśaktyāśritaḥ sa bhavāṃs tena gītastvanāśritaḥ 
tasyāśritaṃ jagatsarvam unmanyantaṃ varānane ।। 

saṃsthitaścāmbhaso mūrdhni śaktyādhārastu hūhukaḥ 
aptattvaṃ caiva tadadha āgneyaṃ tadanantaram ।। 

vāyavyaṃ nābhasaṃ caiva tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca 
viṣayāśca manaścaiva ahaṃkārastvanukramāt ।। 

bauddhaṃ gauṇaṃ ca deveśi prākṛtaṃ pauruṣaṃ tathā 
niyatiḥ kālarāgau ca vidyā caiva kalā tathā ।। 

māyātattvaṃ tathā vidyā īśvaraśca sadāśivaḥ 
bindvardhendunirodhī ca nādo nāḍī tvataḥ param ।। 

adho brahmabilaṃ devi śaktitattvaṃ tataḥ param 
pañcakāraṇasaṃyuktā vyāpinī ca tataḥ param ।। 

samanā unmanā caiva prakriyāṇḍairyutā priye 
evaṃ vai prakriyāṇḍaṃ tu adhordhvaṃ saṃvyavasthitam ।। 

evaṃvidhānyadho adho vai ūrdhvordhvaṃ ca samantataḥ 
yathā ātmāṇavo devi asaṃkhyātā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

evaṃ vai prakriyāṇḍāni tv asaṃkhyeyānyanekaśaḥ 
ekena varṇiteneha sarvo adhvā varṇitaḥ priye ।। 

yathā hyekaṃ tathā sarvaṃ prakriyāṇḍaṃ sthitaṃ priye 
sarveṣāṃ prakriyāṇḍānāṃ svasvarūpeṇa suvrate ।। 

vyāpakastu śivaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ sthitaḥ 
sarvātiśayanirmuktaḥ sarvakāraṇavarjitaḥ ।। 

sṛṣṭisaṃhāranirmuktaḥ prapañcātītagocaraḥ 
nirmalo vimalaḥ śāntas tv adha ūrdhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

ākāśasya yathā nordhvaṃ na madhyaṃ nāpyadhaḥ kvacit 
evaṃ sarvagato devaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

vyāpya devi jagatsarvaṃ vyomasu vyomavatsthitaḥ 
evaṃ jñātvā varārohe na bhūyo janmabhāg bhavet ।। 

kāraṇānāṃ punarvyāptiṃ kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
tattve tu pārthive brahmā adhiṣṭhātā vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

aptattve tu sthito viṣṇū rudrastejasi saṃsthitaḥ 
īśvaro vāyutattve tu ākāśe tu sadāśivaḥ ।। 

ādityaśca smṛto brahmā somo viṣṇuśca suvrate 
grahāṇāmadhipo rudro nakṣatrāṇāṃ tatheśvaraḥ ।। 

yajamānastu deveśi svayaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
sadyojātastu vai brahmā vāmo viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

aghoro rudra ityuktas tathā puruṣa īśvaraḥ 
īśānastu varārohe svayaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।। 

sadyojātastu ṛgvedo vāmadevo yajuḥ smṛtaḥ 
aghoraḥ sāmavedastu puruṣo atharva ucyate ।। 

īśānaśca suraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvavidyātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
laukikaṃ devi vijñānaṃ sadyojātādvinirgatam ।। 

vaidikaṃ vāmadevāttu ādhyātmikamaghorataḥ 
puruṣāccātimārgākhyaṃ nirgataṃ tu varānane ।। 

mantrākhyaṃ tu mahājñānam īśānāttu vinirgatam 
tathā tattvavibhāgena punaśca śṛṇu suvrate ।। 

caturviṃśatitattvāni brahmā vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ 
pradhānāntaṃ tu deveśi pauruṣaṃ tu janārdanaḥ ।। 

niyateratha māyāntaṃ rudro vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ 
vidyā tathaiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ vyāptaṃ caiveśvareṇa tu ।। 

ūrdhvaṃ sadāśivo devaḥ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ 
tattvatrayavibhāgena punarvakṣyāmi suvrate ।। 

ātmatattve tu vai brahmā māyānte ca vyavasthitaḥ 
vidyātattve tathā viṣṇur yāvat sādākhyagocaram ।। 

śivatattve tathā rudro vijñeyastu varānane 
sādākhyamūrdhvamadhvānaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

raudryā adhiṣṭhitātmā vai sa rudraḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
vyāptaśca vāmayā viṣṇur jyeṣṭhayā ca pitāmahaḥ ।। 

jñānaśaktiḥ smṛto brahmā kriyāśaktirjanārdanaḥ 
icchāśaktiḥ paro rudraḥ sa śivaḥ parigīyate ।। 

viṣṇuḥ sadāśivo devo brahmā caiveśvarastathā 
sadāśivaḥ śivāddevi utpannaḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ ।। 

tasmādvidyā tato māyā vidyāyāḥ punarīśvaraḥ 
jñānaśaktikarāgreṇa svecchayā parameśvaraḥ ।। 

sapta koṭīstu mantrāṇāṃ sṛjejjñānakriyātmikāḥ 
te ca sādākhyaparyante pārthivādye tu suvrate ।। 

anugrahaṃ prakurvanti dehināṃ bhuvane sthitāḥ 
śivaśaktisamāviṣṭās trinetrāścandramaulayaḥ ।। 

rudramūrtibhireko asau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam 
jagadvyāpya sthito māyī śūlapāṇiranekadhā ।। 

jñānaśaktyā punaścaiva samālokya varānane 
icchāśaktyā samāviṣṭaḥ kriyāśaktyā tu suvrate ।। 

māyātattvaṃ jagadbījaṃ nityaṃ vibhutayāvyayam 
tatsthaṃ kṛtvātmavargaṃ tu yugapat kṣobhayetprabhuḥ ।। 

helādaṇḍāhatāyāśca badaryā vā phalāni tu 
tiryagūrdhvamadhastācca nirgacchanti samāsataḥ ।। 

muktestu bhājanaṃ ye atra anudhyātāḥ śivena tu 
ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti te sarve śivaṃ paramanirmalam ।। 

vidyāyā bhājanaṃ tiryaṅmantrarūpā bhavanti vai 
saṃsārabhājanaṃ ye tu malakarmakalānvitāḥ ।। 

adhastātte vrajantyatra ghore adhvanyatidāruṇe 
tasmātkalā samutpannā vidyā rāgastathaiva ca ।। 

kālo niyatitattvaṃ ca puṃstattvaṃ prakṛtistathā 
sattvaṃ rajastamaścaiva prakṛtestu guṇāstrayaḥ ।। 

sattvaṃ prakāśajanakaṃ pravṛttijanakaṃ rajaḥ 
tamo avaṣṭambhakaṃ proktaṃ vijñeyaṃ tu guṇatrayam ।। 

sattvaṃ brahmā rajo viṣṇus tamo rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
brahmatve sṛjate lokān viṣṇutve sthitikārakaḥ ।। 

rudratve saṃharet sarvaṃ jagadetaccarācaram 
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptaṃ ca tisro avasthāśca tadgatāḥ ।। 

guṇebhyo dhiṣaṇā jātā bhāvabhedaiḥ samanvitā 
brahmā tatrādhipatyena buddhitattve vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

sarvajñaṃ ca tamevāhur bauddhānāṃ paramaṃ padam 
guṇeṣvārahatānāṃ ca pradhānaṃ vedavādinām ।। 

pauruṣaṃ caiva sāṃkhyānāṃ sukhaduḥkhādivarjitam 
ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ ca deveśi yogaśāstre paraṃ padam ।। 

vrate pāśupate proktam aiśvaraṃ paramaṃ padam 
mausule kāruke caiva māyātattvaṃ prakīrtitam ।। 

kṣemeśo brahmaṇaḥ svāmī teṣāṃ tatparamaṃ padam 
tejeśo vaimalānāṃ ca pramāṇe ca dhruvaṃ padam ।। 

dīkṣājñānaviśuddhātmā dehāntaṃ yāva caryayā 
kapālavratamāsthāya svaṃ svaṃ gacchati tatpadam ।। 

japabhasmakriyāniṣṭhās te vrajantyaiśvaraṃ padam 
sarvādhvāno viniṣkrāntaṃ śaivānāṃ tu paraṃ padam ।। 

buddhitattvādahaṅkāraḥ punarjātastridhā priye 
sāttviko rājasaścaiva tāmasaśca prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

bhūtādirvaikṛtaścaiva taijasaśca tridhā sthitaḥ 
tanmātrāṇyatha bhūtādes tebhyo bhūtānyajījanat ।। 

śabdaḥ sparśaśca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ 
etāni pañca khyātāni tanmātrāṇi krameṇa tu ।। 

śabdādvyoma samutpannaṃ sparśadvāyustathā punaḥ 
rūpāttejaḥ samutpannam āpo jātā rasāt punaḥ ।। 

gandhāttu pṛthivī jātā samāsāt kathitaṃ tava 
karmendriyāṇi jātāni tasmādvaikārikādatha ।। 

vākpāṇipādaṃ pāyuśca upasthaśceti pañcamam 
buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiva taijasāttu bhavantyatha ।। 

śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣau jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamī 
ubhayātma manaḥ proktaṃ vyāptṛ sarvendriyāṇi tu ।। 

ātmopakārakāṇyeva kathitāni yathārthataḥ 
ātmā caivāntarātmā ca bāhyātmā caiva sundari ।। 

nirātmā parātmātmaitān kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
abudhaśca budhaścaiva budhyamānastathaiva ca ।। 

prabuddhaḥ suprabuddhaśca punaśca kathayāmi te 
pradhānasāmyamāśritya sukhaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।। 

yadā tasmin sthitvā devi tadātmā tu sa ucyate 
puryaṣṭakasamāyogāt paryaṭet sarvayoniṣu ।। 

antarātmā sa vijñeyo nibaddhastu śubhāśubhaiḥ 
buddhikarmendriyairyukto mahābhūtaiḥ samāvṛtaiḥ ।। 

bāhyātmā tu tadā devi bhuṅkte asau viṣayān sadā 
bhūtabhāvavinirmuktas tattvadharmakalojjhitaḥ ।। 

maladharmaikayuktātmā māyādharmatiraskṛtaḥ 
nirātmā tu tadā jñeyaḥ paramātmātha kathyate ।। 

malakarmakalādyaistu nirmuktaśca yadā priye 
sarvādhvasamatītaśca māyāmohojjhitaśca yaḥ ।। 

nirmalatvaṃ yadā yāti padaṃ paramamavyayam 
paramātmā tadā devi procyate prabhuravyayaḥ ।। 

abudhaṃ ca punardevi kathayāmi samāsataḥ 
tattvabhūtātmasaṃhāre kalākṣityantagocare ।। 

māyāsāmyaniśāyāṃ vai saṃhṛtya parameśvaraḥ 
nirvyāpāro bhavettāvad yāvadvai nodaya punaḥ ।। 

sukhaduḥkhādyabhāvaśca hy ātmavargasya karmaṇaḥ 
malanidrāvimūḍhātmā ruddhacaitanyadṛkkriyaḥ ।। 

na vijānāti śabdādīn ātmānaṃ ca varānane 
kāraṇaṃ na vijānāti na ca sthānaṃ svakaṃ priye ।। 

sarvametanna jānati yato luptākṣadṛkkriyaḥ 
abudhastiṣṭhate tatra yāvanmāyā aharmukham ।। 

abudhastu samākhyātaḥ budhaṃ caiva nibodha me 
paripākagate karmaṇīśvarecchākaroddhṛte ।। 

prakāśaṃ nāyanaṃ yadvad anugṛhṇāti bhāskaraḥ 
karaṇānyanugṛhṇāti tadvadīśvara ātmanām ।। 

kalonmīlitacaitanyo vidyādarśitagocaraḥ 
rāgo asya rañjakatvena viṣayānandalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

kālo vai kalayatyenaṃ tuṭyādipralayāvadhiḥ 
niyatirniścitaṃ nityaṃ yojayecca śubhāśubhe ।। 

paramāṇusahasrāṃśān na ca nyūnaṃ na cādhikam 
pumbhāvaṃ tamanuprāpya tattve ca puruṣāhvaye ।। 

puraṃ pradhānamityuktaṃ prapañcānekasaṃkulam 
tatpuraṃ poṣayedyasmāt tasmādvai puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

yataḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthastu niyatyā karmataḥ paśum 
pradhānapāśajāleva veṣṭayedasamañjasam ।। 

buddhistriguṇabandhena buddhvā vaikārikeṇa tu 
tanmātrendriyabandhena dṛḍhaṃ bhūtaiśca veṣṭitaḥ ।। 

baddhaḥ saṃcarati hyevaṃ māyādyavanigocare 
saṃsārī procyate tasmāt saṃsaredyat punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

śadbādiviṣayā yasmād vidyante viṣayī tataḥ 
viṣayāḥ paramityāha nānābhedairvisarpitāḥ ।। 

nānākarmavipākaiśca bhuṅkte tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ 
evaṃ bhuṅkte tu vai yasmāt tasmādbhoktā sa ucyate ।। 

tasmiṃstajjño varārohe kṣetre vai kārṣako yathā 
mahābilāṣamālokya kṛṣedvai lobhalāṅgalaiḥ ।। 

vapecca mohabhāvena manovākkāyikaṃ sadā 
dharmādharmamayaṃ bījaṃ pravikīrya samantataḥ ।। 

tasmādvai aṅkurotpattiḥ sukhaduḥkhaphalodayā 
vardhate kāmakrodhena siktā rāgāmbunā bhṛśam ।। 

yasmin deśe ca kāle ca vayasā yādṛśena ca 
uptaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ karma tatkāle labhate phalam ।। 

bhuṅkte tu vividhākāraṃ pūrvakarmavaśādbudhaḥ 
yasmādevaṃ vijānāti tasmāt kṣetrajña ucyate ।। 

viṣayānbudhyate yasmād budhastasmāt prakīrtitaḥ 
tadevāniṣṭarūpeṇa yadā bhāvayate pumān ।। 

budhyamānastu sa tadā adhunā kathayāmi te 
yadā jugupsate bhogān śubhāṃścaivāśubhāṃstathā ।। 

kṛtrimāneva manyeta paraṃ vairāgyamāśritaḥ 
māyādyavaniparyantam indrajālaṃ tu budhyate ।। 

putramitrakalatrāṇi suhṛtsvajanabāndhavāḥ 
yadarjitaṃ mayā dravyaṃ śubhenāpyaśubhena vā ।। 

tadbhokṣyante tvime sarve nirātaṅkā nirākulāḥ 
ekākī cāhamevaiṣa yāsyāmi yamasādanam ।। 

tasmācca na śubhā hyete vairiṇo anarthakāriṇaḥ 
svāmīyamapyayaṃ dehaṃ nityameva jugupsate ।। 

śukraśoṇitasambhūtaṃ viṣayoragadūṣitam 
nānāvyādhisamākīrṇaṃ jarāmṛtyubhayākulam ।। 

so ahamasmi malākīrṇe kathamatra ramāmyaham 
nityamudvignacittastu cintayedvai punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

kathaṃ muktirbhavedasmāt saṃsārādduratikramāt 
evaṃ prabuddho deveśi tallayastatparāyaṇaḥ ।। 

sarvārambhavinirmuktaḥ pramuktaḥ procyate tadā 
prabuddhastu samākhyātaḥ suprabuddhaṃ tu me śṛṇu ।। 

dīkṣājñānena yogena caryayāpyatha suvrate 
yadā prāptaḥ paraṃ sthānam adhvātītaṃ nirāmayam ।। 

virajo vimalaṃ śāntaṃ prapañcātītagocaram 
niṣkampaṃ kāraṇātītaṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvatomukham ।। 

sutṛptānādisambuddhaṃ svatantraṃ nityameva hi 
aluptaśaktivibhavaṃ suprabuddhaṃ sanātanam ।। 

tasmin yuktastadātmā vai tadguṇaistu samanvitaḥ 
suprabuddhaḥ sa evokto bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। 

na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yogo asti śāṅkare 
adhunā kathayiṣyāmi bhāvabhedān varānane ।। 

karaṇāni daśa trīṇi kāryaṃ ca daśadhā priye 
ekādaśendriyavadhā ahaṅkārastu vai tridhā ।। 

buddhiraṣṭavidhā caiva pañcadhā tu viparyayaḥ 
nāmānyeṣāṃ vibhāgena kathayāmi yathākramam ।। 

pṛthivyāpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca ।। 

gandho rasaśca tanmātre rūpatanmātrameva ca 
sparśaḥ śabdaśca pañcaiva tanmātrāṇīritāni tu ।। 

etatte daśadhā kāryaṃ kīrtitaṃ nāmasaṃkhyayā 
vākpāṇipādaṃ pāyuṃ ca upasthaṃ ca tathā viduḥ ।। 

śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā ceti kīrtitam 
bahiṣkaraṇakaṃ devi daśadhā saṃvyavasthitam ।। 

manohaṃkārabuddhyākhyaṃ tridhāntaḥkaraṇaṃ smṛtam 
mūkatā kauṇyapaṅgutvaṃ tathānutsargatāpi ca ।। 

nirānandaśca vijñeyo badhiratvaṃ tathaiva ca 
śīrṇatā caiva gātrasya tathā cāndhatvameva ca ।। 

anāsvādastvagandhaśca anavasthā manasyatha 
itīndriyavadhāḥ khyātā ekādaśa tu tatkramāt ।। 

taijaso vaikṛtākhyaśca bhūtādiśca tṛtīyakaḥ 
ahaṅkārastridhā prokto mayā ta varavarṇini ।। 

dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca caturthakam 
adharmaṃ ca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram ।। 

aṣṭāvete samākhyātā buddherdharmādayo guṇāḥ 
tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisro anyo viparyayaḥ ।। 

andhatāmisramityāhur evaṃ pañca viparyayāḥ 
bhāvabhedāḥ samākhyātāḥ pañcāśatte yathākramam ।। 

punaścāṣṭau tu ye buddher bhedā dharmādayaḥ sthitāḥ 
teṣāṃ bhedā yathā bhinnās tathāhaṃ kathayāmi te ।। 

badhnāti saptadhā sā tu puṃsaḥ saṃsāravartmani 
mocayejjñānabhāvena sāṃkhyajñānaratānnarān ।। 

jñānaṃ ca sāttvikaṃ proktaṃ trayo anye rājasāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tāmasāścāpyadharmādyāś catvāro vai varānane ।। 

dharmaśca daśadhā prokto jñānaṃ caivāṣṭadhā smṛtam 
vairāgyaṃ navadhā caivam aiśvaryaṃ cāṣṭadhā viduḥ ।। 

eta eva viparyastā adharmādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucaṃ santoṣa ārjavam ।। 

ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryamakalkatā 
evaṃ daśavidho dharmaḥ kathitastu varānane ।। 

tāraṃ sutāraṃ taraṇaṃ tārakaṃ ca pramodakam 
pramuditaṃ ramyakaṃ ca sadāpramuditaṃ tathā ।। 

etaj jñānaṃ samākhyātaṃ samāsāt parameśvari 
ambhā ca salilā odhā vṛṣṭisaṃjñā tathāparā ।। 

sutārā ca supārā ca sunetrā ca parā smṛtā 
aṣṭamī ca kumārī syād uttamāmbhasikā tathā ।। 

vairāgyaṃ navadhā caiva kathitaṃ tu mayā tava 
aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca ।। 

prākāmyaṃ ca tatheśitvaṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tathā param 
yatrakāmāvasāyitvam aṣṭamaṃ parikīrtitam ।। 

aiśvaryamaṣṭadhā caiva kathitaṃ tu varānane 
krodhaścāguruśuśrūṣā aśaucaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। 

asantoṣo anārjavaṃ ca hiṃsā cāsatyameva ca 
steyamabrahmacaryaṃ ca tathā caiva sakalkatā ।। 

evameṣa samākhyāto daśadhādharmasaṃgrahaḥ 
atāramasutāraṃ ca atāraṇamathāpi ca ।। 

atārakaṃ ca deveśi caturthaṃ parikīrtitam 
apramodo apramuditam aramyakamathāpi ca ।। 

asadāpramuditaṃ tad ajñānaṃ caivamaṣṭadhā 
anambhā asalilā ca anoghāvṛṣṭireva ca ।। 

asutāramasupāram asunetramataḥ param 
akumārī ca vijñeyān uttamāmbhasikā tathā ।। 

anaṇimālaghimā caivāmahimā maheśvari 
aprāptiraprākāmyaṃ cānīśitvaṃ ca tathaiva ca ।। 

avaśitvaṃ tathā caivāyatrakāmāvasāyitā 
anaiśvaryaṃ ca deveśi aṣṭadhā parikīrtitam 
anaiśvaryādibhiścaite paiśācādyā adhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। 

yathā krameṇa teṣvaṣṭau saṃsthitān kathayāmi te 
anaiśvaryaṃ hi paiśāce avairāgyaṃ ca rākṣase ।। 

yākṣe caiva tadajñānaṃ gāndharve adharma eva ca 
dharmaṃ caiva tathaindre tu jñānaṃ saumye pratiṣṭhitam ।। 

prājāpatye tu vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ brahmaṇi sthitam 
catuṣṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ caitat pade brāhme vyavasthitam ।। 

ṣaṭpañcāśadguṇaṃ tacca prājāpatye vyavasthitam 
aṣṭacatvāriṃśadguṇaṃ saumye vai parikīrtitam ।। 

catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ caiva māhendraiśvaryamucyate 
dvātriṃśadguṇitaṃ devi gāndharvaiśvaryamucyate ।। 

caturviṃśaguṇaṃ yākṣaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ rākṣasaṃ smṛtam 
aiśvaryamaṣṭaguṇitaṃ paiśācaṃ parikīrtitam ।। 

evaṃ sthitaṃ tadaiśvaryaṃ devayoniṣu suvrate 
anye saptasvarūpeṇa saṃsthitā devayoniṣu ।। 

eta eva susaṃkīrṇā mānuṣeṣu vyavasthitāḥ 
pradhānaguṇabhāvena sthāvarāntaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

guṇatrayasya vyāptiṃ vai kathayāmi yathāsthitām 
sattvenādhiṣṭhitā devā brahmādyā maghavāntakāḥ ।। 

gandharvayakṣamanujā daityāścaiva tu rājasāḥ 
yātudhānāḥ piśācāśca tāmasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। 

rajaḥsattvotkaṭā jñeyā ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ 
anyonyābhibhavāste ca pṛthivyāṃ saṃvyavasthitāḥ ।। 

atyantatamasāviṣṭāḥ sthāvarāśca sarīsṛpāḥ 
pādapādavihīnāśca tāmasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। 

sarīsṛpādyā vijñeyāḥ sthāvarāntāstu suvrate 
eṣāmantargatāścānyā anantā eva yonayaḥ ।। 

mānuṣeṣu tathānantā bhedānantyavyavasthayā 
na śakyā gadituṃ tā vai karmānantyaprabhedataḥ ।। 

guṇāstu mānuṣe loke dharmādyā eva saṃsthitāḥ 
dharmādyeṣu nibaddhāni yāni jñānāni suvrate ।। 

adharmādyeṣu yāni syus tāni te kathayāmyaham 
hetuśāstraṃ ca yalloke nityānityaviḍambakam ।। 

vādajalpavitaṇḍābhiḥ vivadante hyaniścitāḥ 
hetuniṣṭhāni vākyāni vastuśūnyāni suvrate ।। 

jñānayogavihīnāni devatārahitāni tu 
dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu niścayo naiva jāyate ।। 

ajñānena nibaddhāni tv adharmeṇa nimittataḥ 
nirayaṃ te pragacchanti ye tatrābhiratā narāḥ ।। 

avairāgyādanaiśvaryaṃ bhuñjate niraye sadā 
catvāraste varārohe duḥkhadā narake sadā ।। 

mohakāḥ sarvajantūnāṃ yataste tāmasāḥ smṛtāḥ 
dharmeṇaikena deveśi baddhaṃ jñānaṃ hi laukikam ।। 

dharmajñānanibaddhaṃ tu pāñcarātraṃ ca vaidikam 
bauddhamārahataṃ caiva vairāgyeṇaiva suvrate ।। 

jñānavairāgyasambaddhaṃ sāṃkhyajñānaṃ hi pārvati 
jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ yogajñānapratiṣṭhitam ।। 

atītaṃ buddhibhāvānām atimārgaṃ prakīrtitam 
lokātītaṃ tu tajjñānam atimārgamiti smṛtam ।। 

lokāśca paśavaḥ proktāḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravartmani 
teṣāmatītāste jñeyā ye atimārge vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

kapālavratino ye ca tathā pāśupatāśca ye 
sṛṣṭirna vidyate teṣāṃ īśvare ca dhruve sthitāḥ ।। 

yasmānmokṣaṃ gamiṣyanti apunarbhavakāraṇam 
laukikānāṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ punaḥ saṃhāra eva ca ।। 

saṃsāracakramārūḍhā bhramanti ghaṭayantravat 
dharmādyarakasaṃyuktam aṣṭāraṃ cakrakaṃ priye ।। 

īśvarādhiṣṭhitaṃ devi nityatyādaṇḍakāhatam 
malakarmakalāviddhaṃ bhramate kālavegataḥ ।। 

laukikādyeṣu jñāneṣu ye teṣvabhiratāḥ priye 
hetuśāstraparā ye tu ye cānye pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।। 

te sarve cāsya cakrasya nāntaṃ paśyanti mohitāḥ 
laukikādyeṣu ye sādhyā atimārgāntagocare ।। 

līlayā sādhayet sarvān śivajñāne mahodaye 
na sarvaiḥ sādhyate tadvai yato atīva sunirmalam ।। 

yato yojayate devi abhāve parame pade 
abhāvaṃ bhāvanātītaṃ prapañcātītagocaram ।। 

manobuddhyādinirmuktaṃ hetuvādavivarjitam 
pratyakṣādipramāṇaiśca vyatītaṃ prabhu cāvyayam ।। 

sarvatarkāgamātītaṃ pāśamantravivarjitam 
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ śāntaṃ nirmalaṃ nirupaplavam ।। 

sarvaśaktyātmakaṃ hyekaṃ svatantrānāthanādimat 
sarvātiśayanirmuktam anādibhavavarjitam ।। 

sarvajñānapadātītaṃ śaivaṃ jñānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam 
evaṃ sṛṣṭāni tattvāni jñānāni ca varānane ।। 

tattvairetairjagatsarvaṃ visṛṣṭaṃ sacarācaram 
bhuvanāni vicitrāṇi śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। 

tattvābhyantarasaṃsthāni śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca 
vijñānaṃ kuhakaṃ śilpaṃ siddhisandohalakṣaṇam ।। 

sarvaṃ tattveṣu boddhavyaṃ sarvatattveṣu dṛśyate 
prakriyā śivadīkṣā ca tattvairetairhi labhyate ।। 

nāsti dīkṣāsamo mokṣo na vidyā mātṛkā parā 
na prakriyāparaṃ jñānaṃ nāsti yogastvalakṣakaḥ ।। 

tatsarvaṃ kathitaṃ devi śivajñānamahodadhau 
evaṃ sṛṣṭiḥ samākhyātā sthitiḥ saṃhāra ucyate ।। 

mānuṣākṣinimeṣasya aṣṭamāṃśaḥ kṣaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
kṣaṇadvayaṃ tuṭirjñeyā taddvayaṃ tu lavaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

lavadvayaṃ nimeṣastu jñātavyo gaṇitakramāt 
daśa pañca nimeṣāśca kāṣṭhā caiva prakīrtitā ।। 

triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā jñeyā muhūrtastriṃśadeva tāḥ 
muhūrtastu punastriṃśad ahorātrastu mānuṣaḥ ।। 

ahorātraśataiścaiva tribhiḥ ṣaṣṭyadhikaiḥ priye 
saṃvatsarastu vijñeyo mānuṣaḥ kamalekṣaṇe ।। 

saṃvatsaraśataṃ pūrṇam āyurjñeyaṃ tu mānuṣam 
daśa pañca tvahorātrāḥ pakṣastu parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

pakṣadvayena māsastu ṛturdviguṇa eva saḥ 
ṛtudvayena kālaḥ syād ayanaṃ ca tribhistribhiḥ ।। 

tābhyāṃ dvyābhyāṃ varārohe varṣaṃ tu parigīyate 
dakṣiṇaṃ cāyanaṃ rātrir uttaraṃ cāyanaṃ dinam ।। 

pitṝṇāṃ tadahorātram anenābdastu pūrvavat 
evaṃ daivastvahorātras tatrāpyabdādi pūrvavat ।। 

dvādaśābdasahasrāṇi vijñeyaṃ tu caturyugam 
caturbhistu kṛtaṃ devi sahasraistu yathākramam ।। 

tretā jñeyā tribhirdevi dvābhyāṃ vai dvāparaḥ smṛtaḥ 
sahasreṇaiva varṣāṇāṃ vijñeyastu kaliḥ priye ।। 

sandhyādvayasya mānaṃ tu kathayāmi yuge yuge 
śatāni catvāri kṛte tv ādirantaśca kīrtyate ।। 

trete śatatrayaṃ jñeyaṃ dvāpare tu śatadvayam 
kalau cāpi śataṃ jñeyaṃ sandhyāmānamidaṃ smṛtam ।। 

laukikena tu mānena punaśca kathayāmi te 
tricatvāriṃśallakṣāṇi sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ ।। 

laukikena tu mānena tv iyaṃ saṃkhyā caturyuge 
ekaikasya punardevi yugasya kathayāmi te ।। 

daśa sapta ca lakṣāṇi sahasrāṇyaṣṭaviṃśatiḥ 
kṛtasyaitadbhavenmānaṃ tretāyāṃ kathayāmi te ।। 

ṣaṇṇavatiḥ sahasrāṇi lakṣāṇi dvādaśaiva tu 
tretāyugasya mānaṃ tu dvāparasya nibodha me ।। 

catuṣṣaṣṭiḥ sahasrāṇi hy aṣṭau lakṣāṇi suvrate 
dvāparasya tu mānaṃ ca kalestu kathayāmi te ।। 

dvātriṃśattu sahasrāṇi lakṣāṇāṃ ca catuṣṭayam 
etanmānaṃ kaleḥ proktaṃ samāsāttava suvrate ।। 

varṣaistu mānavairdevi mānametadyuge yuge 
caturyugaikasaptatyā bhavenmanvantaraṃ punaḥ ।। 

sandhyāmānavihīnaṃ tu yugairmānaṃ prakīrtitam 
etaddivyena mānena mānaṃ manvantare smṛtam ।। 

varṣamānaiḥ punaścaiva laukikaiḥ kathayāmi te 
saptaṣaṣṭistu lakṣāṇi triṃśatkoṭyo varānane ।। 

sahasraviṃśatirjñeyaṃ mānaṃ manvantare priye 
caturdaśabhirdeveśi kalpo manvantare bhavet ।। 

manvantare vyatikrānte cānyasmin punarāgate 
pañca varṣasahasrāṇi madhye sandhyā bhavet sadā ।। 

ādau sahasraṃ sarveṣām ante cāpi punastathā 
kalpo brahmadinaṃ proktaṃ caturyugasahasrakam ।। 

varṣamānena divyena punaśca kathayāmi te 
koṭirekā tu varṣāṇāṃ lakṣāṇāṃ caiva viṃśatiḥ ।। 

divyenaiva tu mānena brahmaṇastu dinaṃ bhavet 
ṣaṇṇavatyā sahasraistu sandhyākālaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

laukikena tu mānena adhunā kathayāmi te 
varṣavṛndāni catvāri tv arbudatrayameva ca ।। 

koṭidvayaṃ ca deveśi dinaṃ paitāmahaṃ smṛtam 
sandhyā koṭitrayaṃ caiva pañca lakṣāṇi kīrtitā ।। 

catvāriṃśattathā ṣaṣṭiḥ sahasrāṇi tathaiva ca 
paścimaḥ sandhirevaṃ hi pūrvasandhyāpi tatsamā ।। 

narakaiḥ saha saptānāṃ pātālānāṃ tathā priye 
lokānāṃ caiva saptānāṃ sthitireṣā prakīrtitā ।। 

saṃhāraṃ ca punardevi śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te 
brahmaṇaḥ svadinānte vai kalpaḥ saṃhāra ucyate ।। 

dinenaikena brāhmeṇa indrāścaiva caturdaśa 
rājyaṃ kṛtvā kramādyānti manvantaravyavasthayā ।। 

tataḥ saṃharate viśvaṃ saptalokāntagocaram 
supte pitāmahe devi ūrdhvaṃ kālāgnirīkṣate ।। 

tasya vai dakṣiṇaṃ vaktraṃ mahājvālāṃ vinikṣipet 
tasmādvaktrānmahājvālā lakṣayojanavistṛtā ।। 

ūrdhvaṃ prayāti sā dīptā tīvravegā suduḥsahā 
lokeṣu ye sthitā lokā ye ca pātālavāsinaḥ ।। 

sukhaduḥkhobhaye kṣīṇe mohaṃ bhūyiṣṭhamāgate 
sattāmātrāstu te sarve bhavanti brahmaviṣṭape ।। 

yāvannodayanaṃ bhūyaḥ sukhaduḥkhādikarmaṇām 
tāvattiṣṭhanti te mūḍhā yāvadbrahmā na budhyate ।। 

rudralokādhipatayaḥ pātālapatayaśca ye 
kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakādyāstu te tisṭhantyatinirmalāḥ ।। 

nirvyāpārāstu te tāvad yāvat sṛṣṭiḥ punarbhavet 
śūnyabhūteṣu lokeṣu jvālā dahati durdharā ।। 

sā dahennarakān devi pātālāni samantataḥ 
trīṃllokāṃścaiva dahati bhūrbhuvaḥsvaḥpadāntikān ।। 

dhūmena ca trayo lokā vinaśyanti varānane 
mahojanastapaḥsaṃjñāḥ satyaloko api suvrate ।। 

tiṣṭhanti mohitātmāno nidrayā te mṛtopamāḥ 
evaṃ dagdghā jagatsarvaṃ jvālā vaktraṃ viśet punaḥ ।। 

tato vānti mahāvātā brahmaniḥśvāsasambhavāḥ 
nāśayanti ca tadbhasma jagaddāhodbhavaṃ priye ।। 

brahmaprasvedajaṃ vāri tajjagat plāvayet punaḥ 
tenaiva vāriṇā devi jagadekārṇavaṃ bhavet ।। 

niśākṣaye punaḥ sthitvā sukhaduḥkhaphalodaye 
karmataḥ sarvalokasya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। 

śūnyabhūtāṃ samālokya bhagavān prabhuricchayā 
ṣaḍvidhāṃ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ yathāpūrvavyavasthayā ।। 

prathamāṃ tāmasīṃ sṛṣṭiṃ karoti tamasotkaṭān 
narakān vividhākārān paśūn vai sthāvarāntagān ।। 

tamorajaḥsamāveśān mānavān saṃsṛjet punaḥ 
rajaḥsattvasamāviṣṭaḥ sṛjenmunivareśvaram ।। 

gatanidraḥ prabuddhaśca sattvaniṣṭho jagatpatiḥ 
sṛjeddevān salokāṃśca pūrvayaiva vyavasthayā ।। 

tato rudrendrasūryendunakṣatrāṇi graheśvarāḥ 
adhikāraṃ prakurvanti sve sve viṣayagocare ।। 

dine dine sṛjatyevaṃ saṃharecca dinakṣaye 
dinamānaṃ ca yatproktaṃ rātrisaṃkhyā ca tāvatī ।। 

ahorātreṇa cānena abdaṃ vai pūrvavat smṛtam 
abdānāṃ tu śate pūrṇe mahākalpaḥ sa ucyate ।। 

brāhme varṣaśate devi divyānyabdāni me śṛṇu 
ekanavatikoṭistu tathā lakṣāṇi viṃśatiḥ ।। 

tathā saptaiva kharvāṇi nikharvāṣṭakameva ca 
brāhmaṃ varṣaśataṃ caitaj jñātavyaṃ kālavedinā ।। 

daivikena tu mānena mānamitthaṃ prakīrtitam 
laukikena tu mānena punaścaiva nibodha me ।। 

dvātriṃśadabdakoṭyastu tathā kharvāṣṭakaṃ priye 
kharvadvayaṃ ca deveśi nikharvāḥ pañca eva tu ।। 

śaṅkutrayaṃ padmamekaṃ sāgaratrayameva ca 
etaddevi samākhyātaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca mumukṣubhiḥ ।। 

etallaukikamānena brāhmamabdaśataṃ smṛtam 
ekaṃ daśaguṇaṃ pūrvaṃ śataṃ daśaguṇaṃ tu tat ।। 

śataṃ daśaguṇaṃ kṛtvā sahasraṃ parikīrtitam 
sahasraṃ daśaguṇitam ayutaṃ taddhi kīrtitam ।। 

daśāyutāni lakṣaṃ tu niyutaṃ daśatāni ca 
daśa tāni ca koṭiḥ syād daśa koṭistathārbudam ।। 

arbudairdaśabhirvṛndaṃ kharvaṃ daśabhireva taiḥ 
daśabhistairnikharvaṃ tu śaṅkuḥ syāddaśa tāni tu ।। 

śaṅkubhirdaśabhiḥ padmaṃ daśa padmāni sāgaraḥ 
sāgarairdaśabhirmadhyam antyaṃ tairdaśabhiḥ smṛtam ।। 

antyaṃ daśāhataṃ kṛtvā parārdhaṃ parikīrtitam 
evamaṣṭādaśaitāni sthānāni gaṇitasya tu ।। 

mahākalpasya paryante brahmā yāti pare layam 
viṣṇośca taddinaṃ proktaṃ rātrirvai tatsamā bhavet ।। 

anena parimāṇena tasyābdaṃ tu vidhīyate 
varṣāṇāṃ ca śate pūrṇe so api yāti pare layam ।। 

viṣṇorāyuryadevoktaṃ rudrasyaitaddinaṃ bhavet
