dine dine sṛjatyanyau brahmaviṣṇū prajāpatī ।। 

brāhmī ca vaiṣṇavī śaktir adhikārapadaṃ gatā 
yaṃ cādhitiṣṭhatyātmānaṃ tatsaṃjñāṃ sa prapadyate ।। 

tadādhikāraṃ kurute icchayā paramātmanaḥ 
brahmaviṣṇvindrarudrāśca vidyeśā īśvarastathā ।। 

lokādhipāśca deveśi tathā ca bhuvanādhipāḥ 
grahādimātaro rudrā yoganakṣatrarāśayaḥ ।। 

śaktiyuktāstu te sarve bhavanti tadadhiṣṭhitāḥ 
tatparākramavīryāstu svakīye tu pade sthitāḥ ।। 

śivasyaikā mahāśaktiḥ śivaścaiko hyanādimān 
sā śaktirbhidyate devi bhedairānantyasambhavaiḥ ।। 

evaṃ vai kurute sṛṣṭiṃ rudraścaiva dine dine 
saṃhāraṃ ca dinānte vai rātrirvai tatsamā bhavet ।। 

dinarātripramāṇenā-nena syādvatsaro asya ca 
vatsarāṇāṃ śate pūrṇe śatarudradinakṣayāt ।। 

so api yāti paraṃ sthānaṃ yadgatvā niṣkalo bhavet 
tasmin sthāne punaścānyas tatsamaśca prabhurbhavet ।। 

raudraśaktisamāyogād brahmaviṣṇvindranāyakaḥ 
śatarudrāstu deveśi svābdānāṃ tu śatakṣaye ।। 

te prayānti paraṃ tattvaṃ tato aṇḍaṃ tu vinaśyati 
sarvabhūtaguṇādhāraṃ sarvatattvālayālayam ।। 

saparvatavanodyānadvīpasāgaramaṇḍitam 
vimānamālākulitaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍitam ।। 

devadānavagandharvasiddhavidyādharoragaiḥ 
ṛṣibhirmānuṣādyaiśca saptalokanivāsibhiḥ ।। 

narakaiścaiva pātālair yuktaṃ bhuvanamaṇḍitam 
aśeṣabhuvanādhāramaṇḍamapsu pralīyate ।। 

tataḥ kālāgnirudraśca kālatattve layaṃ vrajet 
aptattvāttu samārabhya yāvanmāyāntagocaram ।। 

tatsarvaṃ saṃharet kālaḥ svayameva carācaram 
tadūrdhvaṃ śuddhamadhvānaṃ yāvacchaktyantagocaram ।। 

tatsarvaṃ saṃharedghoram aghoro ghoranāśanaḥ 
triṣvevaṃ saṃsthito rudraḥ kālarūpī maheśvaraḥ ।। 

tataḥ saṃharate toyam amareśaśatātyaye 
evaṃ bhūtādyāvaraṇapatayaśca śatātyaye ।। 

saṃharanti ca deveśi sṛjanti ca parasparam 
āpastejasi līyante tattejaścānile punaḥ ।। 

tathānilo ambaraṃ prāpya saha tenaiva līyate 
tanmātreṣu pralīyante yathotpannāni ca kramāt ।। 

tanmātrāṇyapyahaṅkāre sendriyāṇi yathākramam 
sa buddhau sā ca gahane guṇasāmye pralīyate ।। 

guṇasāmyamanirdeśyam apratarkyamanaupamam 
tasmin jagadaśeṣaṃ tu prasuptamiva tiṣṭhati ।। 

paramāṇupramāṇena līnaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate jagat 
ṣaḍviṃśakasya rudrasya caitaddinamiha smṛtam ।। 

prajāḥ prajānāṃ patayaḥ pitaro mānavaiḥ saha 
sāṅkhyajñānena ye siddhāḥ vedena brahmavādinaḥ ।। 

chandaḥ sāmāni coṅkāro buddhistaddevatāḥ priye 
ahni tiṣṭhanti te sarve parameśasya dhīmataḥ ।। 

dinānte tu pralīyante rātryante viśvasambhavaḥ 
ṣaṭtriṃśattu sahasrāṇi brahmaṇāṃ pralayodbhavāḥ ।। 

avyakte ca dinaṃ proktaṃ rudrāṇāṃ tannivāsinām 
tasmin saṃharate sarvaṃ pradhānasya dinakṣaye ।। 

rātryante ca sṛjedbhūyaḥ śrīkaṇṭho viśvanāyakaḥ 
tasyāpyanena nyāyena parimāṇasthitirbhave ।। 

yasmāt pralayakoṭyaśca vyatītāśca sahasraśaḥ 
tato niyatikālau ca rāgo vidyā kalā tathā ।। 

parasparaṃ layaṃ yānti kramāt sarve svamānataḥ 
kalādyavaniparyantaṃ gahaneśadinakṣaye ।। 

nānābhuvanavinyāsaracanādivibhūṣitam 
saguṇādhāraparyantarudrakṣetrajñasaṅkulam ।। 

gahaneśe layaṃ yāti mūlaprakṛtikāraṇe 
rātryante jāyate bhūyo gahaneśapracodanāt ।। 

ahorātrastvayaṃ proktaḥ prākṛtaḥ parameśvari 
pralayaśca sa evokto bhūtānāṃ parameśvari ।। 

prādhānikaparārdhena daśadhāguṇitena tu 
māyā saṃharate sarvaṃ punaścaiva sṛjejjagat ।। 

māyākālaparārdhasya śatadhāguṇitasya ca 
īśvaraḥ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ punaśca saṃharejjagat ।। 

tataḥ sadāśivo devaḥ svamānena ca saṃharet 
sṛjate ca punarbhūya ātmīye devyaharmukhe ।। 

mahāpralaya evoktaḥ sādākhye tu dinadvaye 
bindutattve layaṃ yāti pañcamantramahātanuḥ ।। 

binduṃ caivārdhacandraṃ tu bhittvā caiva nirodhikām 
nādatattve layaṃ yāti gṛhītvā sacarācaram ।। 

nādaḥ sauṣumnamārgeṇa bhittvā brahmabilaṃ priye 
śaktitattve layaṃ yāti śaktitattvadinakṣaye ।। 

parārdhaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ kālastu varavarṇini 
tacca śivatattvasthasya vyāpīśasyāpyaharmukham ।। 

tataśca saṃsṛjedbhūyo vyāpī vyomasvarūpiṇi 
līyate so apyananteśe so anāthe so apyanāśrite ।। 

śaktikālaparārdhasya koṭidhāguṇitasya ca 
anāśritasya devasya dinametat prakīrtitam ।। 

anena parimāṇena parārdhaguṇitena tu 
so api yāti paraṃ sthānaṃ kāraṇaṃ svamanāśrayam ।। 

sa kālaḥ sāmyasaṃjñaśca janmamṛtyubhayāpahaḥ 
tato apyūrdhvamameyastu kālaḥ syāt paramāvadhiḥ ।। 

nityo nityodito devi akalyaśca na kalyate 
sa cādhaḥ kalayet sarvaṃ vyāpinyādiṃ dharāvadhim ।। 

tuṭyādibhiḥ kalābhiśca devyadhvānaṃ carācaram 
ūrdhvamunmanaso yacca tatra kālo na vidyate ।। 

na kalyaḥ kalyate kaścin niṣkalaḥ kālavarjitaḥ 
yaḥ śāṅkaryunmanātītaḥ sa nityo vyāpako avyayaḥ ।। 

tasyādau yādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ kalpānte caiva tādṛśam 
arūpā rūpanirmuktaḥ so anādirbhavavarjitaḥ ।। 

sarvajñaḥ sarvakartā ca dānādiguṇavarjitaḥ 
sa evāpararūpeṇa unmanyā mūrdhni saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

devadevo jagannāthaḥ paramātmā śivo avyayaḥ 
paryānukramayogena so akāmāt sṛjate jagat ।। 

akāmasya kriyā nāsti niṣkriyaśca sṛjet katham 
evaṃ praśnavaraṃ guhyaṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। 

ādityasya maṇeryadvat tāpitādraviraśmibhiḥ 
vahniḥ saṃjāyate tasmād ravestatra na kāmitā ।। 

maṇerapi na kāmitvaṃ tadvaddevasya ceṣṭitam 
ādityavacchivo jñeyaḥ śaktirmaṇiriva sthitā ।। 

ṛtukālamitādvṛkṣāt kālo aṅkuraniyojakaḥ 
yadvacchivasamāyogāt tadvacchakterjagatsthitiḥ ।। 

iti svacchandatantre ekādaśaḥ paṭalaḥ samāptaḥ

sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhāras tattvānāṃ kathitastvayā 
jagatsaṃbhavahetuśca tvatprasādācchrutaṃ mayā ।। 

tattvavijñānamākhyāhi siddhisteṣu yathā bhavet 
pṛthivyādi śivāntaṃ ca kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। 

pṛthvī kaṭhinarūpeṇa śṛṇu dehe yathā sthitā 
māṃse asthiṣu tathā caiva snāyulomanakheṣu ca ।। 

majjāntreṣu ca vijñeyā pṛthvī pañcaguṇotkaṭā 
kaphāsṛgāmamūtreṣu rasasvedavasāsu ca ।। 

śukre ca saṃgrahe caiva sthitā āpaścaturguṇāḥ 
pacane dahane caiva tejasyūṣmaṇi saṃsthitam ।। 

tejastvevaṃ sthitaṃ devi prakāśe ca trilakṣaṇam 
vāyurucchvāsaniḥśvāsasparśanavyūhalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

mūtroccāravisargeṣu annapānapraveśane 
vāyurebhiḥ sthito dehe vijñeyastu dvilakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

ekalakṣaṇamākāśaṃ kathayāmi yathā sthitam 
suṣirātmakaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ navadhā cchidralakṣaṇam ।। 

śabdātmakaṃ guṇaṃ h yetat kathitaṃ tava suvrate 
vāgindriyaṃ vadedvāṇīṃ sā ca vāṇī caturvidhā ।। 

saṃskṛtā prākṛtī caiva apabhraṣṭānunāsikā 
chedanaṃ bhedanaṃ dānaṃ vyadhanaṃ śilpayojanam ।। 

grahaṇaṃ vijayaścaiva sarvaṃ hastendriye sthitam 
samanimnonnatāścaiva loṣṭakaṇṭakavālukāḥ ।। 

kardamo jaladurgāṇi rathyāṭṭālakaparvatāḥ 
pādendriyeṇa gamyante deśāntaragamāgame ।। 

utsarge pardite caiva pāyurvai ceṣṭate sadā 
ānandakṛdupasthaśca gamyāgamyapravartakaḥ ।। 

karmasvetāni vartante tena karmendriyāṇi tu 
buddhīndriyāṇi deveśi vartante buddhiyogataḥ ।। 

ṣaḍjākhyarṣabhagāndhāramadhyamāḥ pañcamaḥ priye 
dhaivato niṣadhaścaiva svarāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ ।। 

gāndhāro madhyamaḥ ṣaḍjas trayo grāmāśca pārvati 
saptasvarāstrayo grāmā mūrchanāścaikaviṃśatiḥ ।। 

tāna ekonapañcāśad ityetatsuramaṇḍalam 
sūkṣmaśabdāḥ smṛtā hyete carācararavasthitāḥ ।। 

sthūlāṃścaiva pravakṣyāmi yathāvattānnibodha me 
bherīpaṭahaśaṅkhottho mṛdaṅgapaṇavotthitaḥ ।। 

veṇugomukhaśabdaśca mandalo darduro dhvaniḥ 
tantrīvādyāni citrāṇi karavādyāni yāni ca ।। 

saṃyogajaviyogotthāḥ kāṣṭhapāṣāṇavārijāḥ 
apabhraṃśo anunāsikyaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ prākṛto ravaḥ ।। 

saptasvarapratiṣṭhāni vyaktāvyaktāni caiva hi 
uktānuktāni gṛhṇāti śravaṇendriyayogataḥ ।। 

śabdo asya viṣayo hyeṣa yena budhyeta pudgalaḥ 
mṛduṃ ca kaṭhinaṃ caiva karkaśaṃ śītalaṃ tathā ।। 

uṣṇaṃ ca picchilaṃ loṣṭaṃ kardamaṃ vālukāstathā 
śarakuntāsighātādi tāḍanaṃ chedanaṃ tathā ।। 

etāni vai vijānāti sparśanaṃ ca tvagindriyam 
sparśo asya viṣayo hyeṣa yena budhyeta pudgalaḥ ।। 

cakṣurindriyakarmāṇi kathyamānāni me śṛṇu 
sitaṃ raktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ haritadhūmrakam ।। 

kapilaṃ piṅgalaṃ babhru anyānyapi viśeṣataḥ 
naranārīpaśumṛgāñ jyotiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। 

rūpākṛtiviviktāni cakṣuḥ paśyati sarvadā 
rūpākhyo viṣayo hyasya yenātmā pratibuddhyate ।। 

madhurāmlarasaṃ caiva lavaṇaṃ kaṭu tiktakam 
kaṣāyamiśraṃ svāduṃ ca jihvā vedayate rasam ।। 

raso asya viṣayo hyeṣa yena buddhyeta pudgalaḥ 
surabhirdivyagandhaśca durgandhaścāpyanekadhā ।। 

ubhau jighrati nāsāgre viṣayo gandhasaṃjñitaḥ 
yenāsau budhyate kṣetrī ahaṅkāreṇa mohitaḥ ।। 

saṃkalpe ca vikalpe ca daśadhākṣeṣu dhāvati 
anivāritasandeham ajayyaṃ sarvadehinām ।। 

manaśca kathitaṃ hyetad dharmādharmanibandhakam 
svarūpadharmaṃ vakṣyāmi tanmātrāṇāṃ yathārthataḥ ।। 

gandhaṃ tu gandhatanmātraṃ nāsikāgreṇa jighrati 
jihvayā rasatanmātraṃ rasaṃ gṛhṇāti saṃsthitam ।। 

cakṣuṣā rūpatanmātraṃ rūpaṃ gṛhṇātyupāgatam 
gṛhṇāti sparśatanmātraṃ tvacā sparśamupāgatam ।। 

śabdaṃ ca śabdatanmātraṃ gṛhṇāti śravaṇena tu 
sūkṣmastanmātradharmo ayaṃ bhūtānāṃ prakṛtikramāt ।। 

vaikārikastataścordhvaṃ budhyate yena pudgalaḥ 
ahaṃ vidvānahaṃ bhogī tv ahaṃ jāto mahākule ।। 

ahaṃ dātā ca bhoktā ca tejasvī balavānaham 
ahaṃ yoddhā ca saṃgrāme śatravaśca mayā jitāḥ ।। 

dharmaśīlaśca guṇavān śreyaskartā hyahaṃ param 
ahaṃ pāpī durācāro mūrkhaścāhaṃ durākṛtiḥ ।। 

na dattaṃ na mayā bhuktaṃ matsamo nāsti duḥkhitaḥ 
ityahaṅkāracittānāṃ mamatvavaśavartinām ।। 

ahaṅkāro nibadhnāti saṃsāre dṛḍhabandhanaiḥ 
trividhasyāpyayaṃ dharmo ahaṅkārasya prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

buddhidharmāṃstato vakṣye dharmādīṃstava suvrate 
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca catuṣṭayam ।। 

adharmaśca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram 
badhnāti saptadhā sā tu jñānabhāvena mohayet ।। 

buddhiścādhyavasāyaṃ ca karoti vividheṣvapi 
dharmādīnāmathāṣṭānāṃ lakṣaṇāni śṛṇu priye ।। 

upavāso japo maunam akrodho asteyamārjavam 
satyaṃ śaucaṃ ca dānaṃ ca dayā kṣāntiśca sarvadā ।। 

vidyābhyāsaśca lajja ca indriyāṇāṃ ca nigrahaḥ 
iṣṭāpūrtaṃ tīrthasevā pitṛṇāṃ caiva tarpaṇam ।। 

abhayaṃ sarvasattvebhyo jīvitasya ca rakṣaṇam 
dhīguṇaḥ prathamo hyeṣa dharma ityabhidhīyate ।। 

dharmakarmanibaddhānāṃ saṃsāramanuvartinām 
punarmārtyaṃ punaḥ svargyaṃ tīryak tvaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

dharmabhāvaḥ samākhyātaḥ jñānabhāvaṃ ca me śṛṇu 
caturviṃśatikaḥ piṇḍaḥ karaṇendriyasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

prākṛtaḥ sa tu vijñeyo dharmādharmapravartakaḥ 
akartā nirguṇaścāhaṃ na me bandho asti prākṛtaḥ ।। 

prakṛtyā kāritaṃ manye vāsanādeva mucyate 
sāṅkhyajñānaṃ mayā proktaṃ prakṛteryena mucyate ।। 

muktaṃ prakṛtibandhāttaṃ punarbadhnāti ceśvaraḥ 
baddhaḥ saṃsarate bhūyo yāvaddevaṃ na vindati ।। 

īśvaraṃ sṛṣṭikartāraṃ sarvajantunibandhakam 
vairāgyātsantyajetputrān dārāniṣṭānsusaṃmatān ।। 

hastyaśvarathayānāni suhṛdbhogadhanāni ca 
upavāsaṃ japaṃ tīrthaṃ pañcāgniṃ jalaśāyitām ।। 

upāsyaitāni ghorāṇi dehaṃ santyajati kṣaṇāt 
girivṛkṣajalāgnibhyaḥ prahārodbandhanāśanaiḥ ।। 

vairāgyaṃ tu samāśritya kurute sāhasānyapi 
aiśvaryabhāvamāpanno dravyaistṛptiṃ na gacchati ।। 

na dārairna dhanairbhāgaiḥ parivārairna vāhanaiḥ 
tapo vratāni mantrāṃśca aiśvaryārthe tu sādhayet ।। 

yuddhaṃ dyutaṃ tathā māyāṃ cauryaṃ cānṛtahiṃsanam 
anyānyapi tvayuktāni visrambhacchalaghātitām ।। 

aiśvaryabhāvamāpannaḥ karoti ca bahūnyapi 
prāṇihiṃsārato nityaṃ caurikānṛtadambhavān ।। 

yācako duḥkhadātā ca bhaveccādharmaceṣṭitam 
nāstidharmo na cādharmaḥ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ ca ko gataḥ ।। 

ajñānabhāvamāpannaḥ sarvaṃ mithyeti bhāṣate 
nityaṃ duḥkhī parapreṣyo bhāraṃ yānaṃ vahannapi ।। 

kṛcchrajīvī ca satatam avairāgye na khidyate 
rājyaṃ kṛtvā tu sāmantaḥ sāmantyādgrāmabhugbhavet ।। 

grāmādbhraṣṭastadardhena vartate asāvanīśvaraḥ 
na śocati na codvignaḥ krīḍate pūrvarājyavat ।। 

anaiśvaryasya bhāvo ayam evaṃ te samudāhṛtaḥ 
avyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ vakṣye saṃsārasya pravartakam ।। 

yasmācca jagadutpattiḥ prakṛtistena cocyate 
asya dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi rajaḥ sattvatamo abhidham ।। 

prakāśabhāvaḥ sattvaṃ ca dharmaḥ sattvasamāśritaḥ 
saṃvibhāgī ca satataṃ nityaṃ sattvopakārakaḥ ।। 

kṣamādayāsamāyukto jñānavijñānapāragaḥ 
prītirdānaṃ dhṛtirmedhā tapaḥ śaucaṃ damastathā ।। 

ṛtavāksamadṛṣṭiśca divyabuddhiprabodhanam 
yasminnete sadā dharmā bhavanti puruṣottame ।। 

sa sāttvikastu vijñeyaḥ rajodharmāṃśca me śṛṇu 
nistriṃśaścātilobhī ca vidveṣī krodhanastathā ।। 

kāmī harṣasamāviṣṭo duḥkhārtaḥ paryaṭetsadā 
mānī dambhasamāyukto apyahaṅkāre vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

nityaṃ yuddharataḥ śūraḥ rājasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam 
kāmakrodhābhibhūtatvaṃ lobhena ca samanvayaḥ ।। 

īrśyā dambho viṣādaśca mada unmāda eva ca 
nidrālasya makarmitvaṃ daurmedhyājñānite tathā ।। 

adharmatābuddhimattvaṃ nāstikyaṃ chalacittatā 
tamaḥ cihnāni caitāni dṛśyante yatra mānave ।। 

tāmasaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ puruṣaḥ kaluṣāśayaḥ 
etatriguṇamavyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ sāmudāhṛtam ।। 

etatsamyagviditvā tu mucyate prākṛtairguṇaiḥ 
guṇadharmā na caivāhaṃ buddhyahāṃkṛdguṇo nahi ।। 

karaṇendriyahīnaśca bhūtatanmātravarjitaḥ 
akartā nirguṇaścāhaṃ cinmātraḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

mānasaṃ vācikaṃ caiva śārīraṃ karma yatkṛtam 
prakṛtyā kāritāṃ manye akartā puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

evaṃ saṃnyasya karmāṇi vartate naca nityaśaḥ 
nāhaṃ kartā na me bandha evaṃ budhyeta yo naraḥ ।। 

prakṛteḥ sa vimucyeta yāvanna sṛjatīśvaraḥ 
sāṅkhyajñānena saṃmūdho muktirityabhimanyate ।। 

na hi muktirbhavettasya kaṃcitkālaṃ videhatā 
tiṣṭhetprakṛtinirmuktaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravarjitaḥ ।। 

yāvatkarotyasau sṛṣṭim īśvaraḥ parameśvaraḥ 
tāvatprakṛtibandhena saṃsāre kṣipyate punāḥ ।। 

kṣiptaḥ saṃsarate bhūyaḥ saṃsāre ghorasāgare 
dharmādhārmanibaddhastu sāṅkhyajñānena mohitaḥ ।। 

ahaṃ kartā ca bhoktā ca īśvarobalavānaham 
mamatvenaiva saṃmūḍho bhrāmyate ghaṭayantravat ।। 

sāṅkhyajñānaṃ mayā proktaṃ śṛṇu dhyānādhidaivatam 
pṛthvīṃ kaṭhinarūpeṇa catuḥ sāgaramekhalām ।। 

saparvatavanākīrṇāṃ mṛgapakṣisamākulām 
susthitāṃ pītavarṇābhām ūbījena samanvitām ।। 

dhyātvā tatsiddhimabhyeti viṣasattvānnivārayet 
acālyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yathaiva vasudhā bhavet ।। 

jalāpūritasarvāṅgo jaladhyānena pūrayet 
evamabhyasyamānastu viṣasattvānvināśayet ।। 

tṛṣṇādāhavinirmukta ītibhiśca vivarjitaḥ 
jagadāpūrayetsiddhaḥ pūrvabījasamanvitaḥ ।। 

kuryātkarmasahasrāṇi svabījena tu bījitaḥ 
kṛṣṇareṇvātmako vāyur dhyeyo bījena saṃyutaḥ ।। 

pūrayedvai jagaddehān siddhaścāścaryakārakaḥ 
suṣirātmakaṃ svadehaṃ tu jagacca suṣirātmakam ।। 

dhyāyetprakṛtibījena citrakarmāṇi kārayet 
vāgindriye tathā vahnir dhyāto vāksiddhidāyakaḥ ।। 

indraḥ pāṇāvabhidhyātaḥ bāhuśālī tvajeyakaḥ 
pādayordūrasaṃcāraṃ dhyāto viṣṇuḥ prayacchati ।। 

pāyau mitraḥ sito dhyātaḥ pāyuvyādhivināśakaḥ 
śiśne prajāpatiṃ śyāmaṃ dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।। 

jitendriyaśca bhavati tv icchayā ramate śatam 
śrotrendriye diśaścitrā dhyāyedvījena saṃyutāḥ ।। 

sakṛduktaṃ ca gṛhṇāti digyātrā caiva siddhyati 
mārutaṃ kṛṣṇarūpeṇa dhyāyettu tvaci saṃsthitam ।। 

yaḥ sa daṃṣṭrādyabhedyaḥ syāt na kvaciñjāyate vyathā 
ādityaṃ cakṣuṣi dhyāyej jihvāyāṃ varuṇaṃ tathā ।। 

nāsāyāṃ pṛthivīṃ pītāṃ manasīnduṃ tathaiva ca 
pītakaṃ gandhatanmātraṃ rasatanmātrakaṃ sitam ।। 

raktaṃ tu rūpatanmātraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tu sparśasaṃjñitam 
arūpaṃ śabdatanmātraṃ dhyātavyaṃ bindurūpi ca ।। 

viṣayeṣvīpsitāṃ siddhiṃ jānāti ca vicintitam 
vaikārike tathā rudro dhyātavyaḥ siddhimicchatā ।। 

dhyānātsiddhimavāpnoti muktāhaṅkārabandhanām 
brahmāṇaṃ buddhisaṃsthaṃ tu dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।। 

smaranvai pūrvabījena jñānaughaḥ saṃpravartate 
divyā ca jāyate buddhiḥ saṃśayocchittikārikā ।। 

bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca pratyakṣaṃ saṃprajāyate 
prakṛtiḥ kṛṣṇavarṇā tu raktaśuklā virājate ।। 

raktaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ tasyāḥ bahupādabhujānanā 
dhyātavyā tattvabījena yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ ।। 

siddhaścaiva svatantraśca divyadṛṣṭiśca jāyete 
ṣaṇmāsābhyāsayogena divyā dṛṣṭiḥ pravartate ।। 

trailokye yatpravarteta pratyakṣaṃ tasya jāyate 
eṣa te prākṛto yoga uktaḥ mokṣakaraḥ paraḥ ।। 

ataḥ paraṃ tu puruṣaḥ padmamadhye vyavasthitaḥ 
citsvarūpaśca sarveṣu dehamāpūrya saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

sa jīva iti vikhyāto yena jīvati tatpuram 
nirgatena mṛtā yena acetāḥ śīryate tanuḥ ।। 

badhyate mucyate asau vai sukhaduḥkhāni vetti ca 
na tasya rūpaṃ varṇo vā pramāṇaṃ dṛśyate kvacit ।। 

na śakyaḥ kathituṃ vāpi sūkṣmaścānantavigrahaḥ 
vālāgraśatabhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya tu ।। 

tasya sūkṣmataro jīvaḥ sa cānantyāya kalpate 
ādityavarṇaṃ rukmābham abbindumiva puṣkare ।। 

paśyanti tārakamiva yogino divyacakṣuṣā 
rāgavidyākalopetaḥ kālabaddho hi rūpavān ।। 

śyāmavarṇena vijñeyā sthitā jīvasya devatā 
dakṣiṇena sitāṅgī tu vāmenāsitarūpiṇī ।। 

tadvarṇāni ca vaktrāṇi maṇḍalāni viśeṣataḥ 
karmabandhena badhnāti sukhaduḥkhaṃ prayacchati ।। 

niyatiṃ ca vijānīyād anivāryāṃ surāsuraiḥ 
pūrvabījasahadhyānā dvirūpeṇa samanvitā ।। 

dhyānātsiddhimavāpnoti niyateśca vimucyate 
trinetraṃ ca caturvaktraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ caturbhujam ।। 

saṃharantaṃ durādharṣam anantaṃ kālamīśvaram 
svabījadhyānarūpajñaḥ kālena nahi kalyate ।। 

cakravatparivartante kāladhyānavivarjitāḥ 
evaṃ kālaṃ sadā dhyāyet dhyeyasiddhiśca jāyate ।। 

rāgaṃ tu raktavarṇaṃ vai vidyāṃ śyāmāṃ sulocanām 
sitavarṇāṃ kalāṃ dhyāyec cetanyonmīlinīṃ tu tām ।। 

kṛṣṇavarṇā ca raktākṣī dīrghadantā sulocanā 
kacordhvapiṅgakeśī ca sthūlakāyā mahodarī ।। 

yā pātayati bhūtāni brahmādyāni punaḥ punaḥ 
nirvairaparipanthitvān māyā granthirduruttarā ।। 

sāṅkhyavedapurāṇajñā anyaśāstravidaśca ye 
na tāṃ laṅghayituṃ śaktā ye cānye mokṣavādinaḥ ।। 

kliśyanti māyayā bhrāntā amokṣe mokṣalipsayā 
svabījadhyānayogena pūrvadhyānasvarūpataḥ ।। 

dīkṣāsinā ca tāṃ chittvā viśanti śivamavyayam 
caturvarṇā bhavedvidyā sā varṇavyāpinī smṛtā ।। 

sitaraktapītakṛṣṇā dhyātavyā suṣirātmikā 
ākāśavāyumārūḍhā rūpayauvanaśālinī ।। 

svabījena tu sā dhyeyā tatsiddhiścaiva jāyate 
divyā siddhiramoghā tu siddhavidyaśca jāyate ।। 

veda lokāṃstataḥ sarvān kāmarūpī sa gacchati 
kuṅkumābhaṃ ca nāreśaṃ trinetraṃ tu jaṭādharam ।। 

pūrvānanamabhidhyāyet vāyubhakṣasya yatphalam 
tatpuṇyaphalamāpnoti aśvamedhāyutasya ca ।। 

jagacca vaśamāyāti kramate siddhimeti ca 
ṣaḍbhirmāsairasandehaḥ dakṣiṇaṃ ca tathaiva hi ।। 

nīlāmbudapratīkāśaṃ piṅgabhrūśmaśrulocanam 
bhrukuṭīkarālavaktraṃ ca kapālāhi vibhūṣitam ।। 

bahurūpajaṭādhāraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tasya cintayet 
sukhaduḥkhavināśāya ītijvaravināśanam ।। 

viṣagrahādi sarvaṃ tu dhyānānnāśayate kṣaṇāt 
agnivajjvalate yogī jarāmṛtyuvivarjitaḥ ।। 

kramate sarvalokānvai siddhaśca samatāṃ vrajet 
sitaṃ trinayanaṃ devi sākṣāsūtrakamaṇḍalu ।। 

paścimaṃ vadanaṃ dhyāyed divyasiddhipradāyakam 
hatvā prāṇisahasrāṇi paradāraśatāni ca ।। 

alepako viśuddhātmā siddhiṃ prāpya śivo bhavet 
trinetramuttaraṃ vaktraṃ raktotpalasamadyuti ।। 

dhyānāttasya jagatsarvaṃ vaśameti na saṃśayaḥ 
tapate varṣate caiva sṛjate saṃharatyapi ।। 

īpsitāṃ labhate siddhiṃ yo abdamekaṃ tu cintayet 
sitamūrdhvaṃ sadā dhyāyec chūlahastaṃ jaṭādharam ।। 

vyāghracarmapārīdhānaṃ sākṣāsūtrakamaṇḍalu 
vīṇāḍamaruhastaṃ ca nāgayajñopavītakam ।। 

candramūrdhordhvaliṅgaṃ ca dhyāyennityaṃ maheśvaram 
anenaiva tu dehena sarvajñaḥ kāmarūpavān ।। 

ghaṇṭānādasya vā dhyānāt siddhiḥ ṣāṇmāsikī bhavet 
īpsitā martyaloke tu siddhistasya prajāyate ।। 

liṅgadhyānaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pūrvabījena saṃyutam 
māsenaikena paśyetsa sūkṣmaṃ liṅgaṃ tanūpari ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ taddṛṣṭvā tu vimucyate 
siddhistu mānuṣe loke ṣaṇmāsena prajāyate ।। 

trailokyadarśane buddhiḥ pratyakṣā tasya jāyate 
ākrāmetsarvalokāṃśca īśvareṇa samo bhavet ।। 

somārkau cakṣuṣī syātāṃ cakre vai dhī rathasya tu 
tanmātrāṇi hayāstasya manaḥ sārathi coditaḥ ।। 

ahaṃkāro bhavedyoddhā guṇaścāsya mahādhanuḥ 
indriyāṇi śarāstasya mṛgo dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

evaṃ sa krīḍate yogī paramātmani hṛtsthite 
puṇyapāpairvartamāna icchayā parameśvari ।। 

nāhaṃ kartā na me bandhaḥ sarvamīśvarakāraṇam 
matvā ceśvaravijñānaṃ sarvakarmaṇi santyajet ।। 

dharmādharmasya kartṛtve prerako hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ 
tamahaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpto na me bandho asti kaṛtṛtā ।। 

sadāśivo aṣṭabhedena pūrvabījasamanvitaḥ 
dhyeyaḥ pūrvoktarūpeṇa tatsiddhiphalamicchatā ।। 

nādaṃ vai vyāpakaṃ dhyāyed ahorātrāyaneṣu ca 
dakṣiṇottarasaṃkrāntyā viṣuvajjñasya mokṣadaḥ ।। 

vaṃśadhvanisamaprakhyaḥ śāntanādastu sa smṛtaḥ 
sadāśivaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ dhyānātsiddhiphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। 

māsamātreṇa tejasvī vāgīśastu dvitīyake 
tṛtīye paśyate siddhān divyadṛṣṭiścaturthake ।। 

siddhistu mānuṣe loke vatsarārdhe na saṃśayaḥ 
divyāsiddhistathābdena sāyujyaṃ tu dvitīyake ।। 

ṣaṇmukhīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyeddevaṃ sadāśivam 
aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ śrutī netre tarjanīmadhyamākramāt ।। 

śeṣābhyāṃ vṛṇuyādghrāṇe ṣaṇmukhe kila baddhadhīḥ 
daśadhā varṇarūpeṇa dṛśyate ca sadāśivaḥ ।। 

sitaṃ raktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ haritapiṅgalam 
nīlaṃ citrakavarṇaṃ tu sphaṭikābhaṃ manoramam ।। 

dṛṣṭvā sarvāṇi rūpāṇi tyajettani vicakṣaṇaḥ 
ekameva tu gṛhṇīyād anye tu guṇarūpakāḥ ।। 

candramaṇḍalasaṅkāśaṃ vidyutpuñjanibhekṣaṇam 
tārakācalitākāraṃ bindumevaṃ vilakṣayet ।। 

nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntistathaiva ca 
ābhiḥ kalābhiḥ saṃyukto dhyātavyo bindurīśvaraḥ ।। 

bindudhyānaṃ samākhyātaṃ śaktilakṣaṃ nibodha me 
khaṃ vīkṣya mīlitākṣo yad udyadbhāskarasannibham ।। 

īkṣate ca mahattejaḥ śaktiḥ prabhvīti sā smṛtā 
pītā raktā tathā kṛṣṇā sphaṭikābhā manoramā ।। 

draṣṭavyā pāramā śaktiḥ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā śivatāṃ vrajet 
vyāpinīṃ ca tataścordhve pañcarūpāṃ vicintayet ।। 

kāraṇaiḥ svaiḥ samopetāṃ dhyātvā svacchandatāṃ vrajet 
samanāmunmanāṃ coktāṃ dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।। 

dhyānātsiddhimavāpnoti vyāpakaḥ prabhurakhyayaḥ 
tataścordhve śivaḥ śāntaḥ pūrvaṃ vai kathito mayā ।। 

cakṣuṣā yaśca dṛśyeta vāco vā yaśca gocaraḥ 
manaścintayate yāni buddhiryāni vyavasyati ।। 

ahaṃkṛtāni yānyeva yacca vedyatayā sthitam 
yaśca nāsti sa tatraiva tv anveṣṭavyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। 

yatra tatra sthito deśe yatra tatrāśrame rataḥ 
sukhāsīnaḥ saṃyatātmā ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। 

svacchandaṃ samanusmṛtya abhāvaṃ bhāvayetsadā 
bhāvanāttasya tattvasya tatsamaścaiva jāyate ।। 

ye dharmāstasya cākhyātāḥ pūrvaṃ te varavarṇini 
taistu dharmaiḥ samāyukti yogī vai bhavati priye ।। 

svarūparūpakadhyānaṃ tattvānāṃ kathitaṃ mayā 
evaṃ jñātvā ca dhyātvā ca siddhyate mucyate api ca ।। 

iti svacchandatantre dvādaśaḥ paṭalaḥ

sāraṃ yadasya tantrasya yāgaṃ tu parameśvara 
tamākhyāhi samāsena sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai ।। 

mūlabījākṣaraṃ mantranāyakaṃ paramīśvaram 
praṇavāsanamārūḍham aṅgavaktraiḥ samanvitam ।। 

pūrvoktadravyasaṃghātaiḥ pūjayet parameśvaram 
sa eva homavinyāsaḥ dīkṣā saiva prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

daśalakṣaṃ japedyastu ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ 
samudragasarittīre sahāyaiḥ parivarjitaḥ ।। 

homayennaramāṃsasya lakṣamekaṃ saguggulam 
jitendriyaikacittastu brahmacarye vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

asādhyaṃ sādhayeddevi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
yāni kānīha karmāṇi catuṣpīṭhasthitāni ca ।। 

adhamānyatha madhyāni hy uttamāni varānane 
tāni siddhyanti deveśi bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। 

athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi kārikākośamuttamam 
yaṃ jñātvā devadeveśi vicarantīha sādhakāḥ ।। 

abhimukhakhaḍgani pātitaśūraśiraḥ śoṣitaṃ samādāya ।
raktālaktakalikhitaṃ sādhyatanau mantrayuktamabhidhānam ।। 

pretānale sutaptaṃ vidhāya niśi yatkṛte śataṃ japati ।
asurendracakravartinamasurendraguruṃ vā tamānayatyanilavegāt ।। 

pretālaktakalikhitaṃ naraśirasi pretavahnisantaptam ।
yamalokādapyacirādānayati balena pūrvavat sādhyam ।। 

mṛtanāryā vāmapadādudbaddhāyāstu pāṃsulīṃ samādāya ।
rudhirālaktakarocanayā sādhyatanuṃ mantrasaṃyuktām ।। 

khadirānale sutaptāṃ rātryardhe sammukho japaśatena ।
ānayati śacīmahalyāmathavā divasasya śatabhāgāt ।। 

udbaddhastrītanuvāmāṅghreḥ pāṃsulīṃ samādāya ।
pretālaktakanijarudhirarocanābhirvilikhya sādhyatanum ।। 

pretānale sutaptāṃ śatābhijaptāṃ svanāmamantrayutām ।
kṛtvā yakṣasurāsurapannaganārīḥ samānayatyāśu ।। 

nijavāmakare alaktakarocanayā sādhyanāma parilikhitam ।
mantravidarbhitametajjapaśatayuktaṃ sutāpitaṃ rātrau ।। 

khadirānale vidhūme asuragurumapyānayatyanilavegāt ।
sādhyamabhidhānalikhitaṃ bhūmitale gairikeṇa raktena ।। 

gandhodvartitavāmahastena tu tattvabījayuktena ।
ākramya bhūmilikhitaṃ sādhyābhimukho ardharātrakāle tu ।। 

kṣitipatimapi sāmātyaṃ cānayati nimeṣaśatabhāgāt ।
nṛkapālamadhyalikhitaṃ rocanayā raktamiśrayā sādhyam ।। 

nāma ca tasya lalāṭe mantreṇa vidarbhitaṃ samālikhya ।
gandhodakena liptaṃ nṛkapālaṃ vai dvitīyamādāya ।। 

kṛtvā kapālasampuṭamatha mṛtasūtreṇa veṣṭayet samyak ।
khadirāṅgārasutaptaṃ sikthakaliptaṃ tu tatpunaḥ kṛtvā ।। 

yāvat sikthakametat kapālalagnaṃ vilīyate tāvat ।
surapatimapyākarṣati japaśatayogānnimeṣamātreṇa ।। 

bhittau gairikalikhitaṃ mantrārṇavidarbhitaṃ tadabhidhānam ।
sādhyābhimukho rātrau vāmakarākrāntamatha japan kruddhaḥ ।। 

kroṅkārāṅkuśayogādānayati surāsurān kṣipram ।
raṇaśastraghātapatitaṃ narapiśitaṃ trimadhusaṃyutaṃ juhuyāt ।। 

viparītacakramudrāṃ baddhvā sādhyaṃ tu nikṣipenmadhye ।
sampīḍitakarasampuṭavihvalavaktraṃ karāntare dhyātvā ।। 

ānayati mahāpuruṣaṃ kṣitipatimapi divasaśatabhāgāt ।
śitaśastrapātarahitadhvajanaraśīrṣaṃ pragṛhya lakṣamayutam ।। 

tatra trirūpagaditaṃ dhāma likhitvābhipūjayedyastu ।
tasya haripavanakamalajadhanadayamendrāḥ sasiddhagandharvāḥ ।। 

vividhavarasiddhijātaṃ vidadhati vicitrāstathāparāḥ siddhīḥ ।
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tathā vyaktamavyaktaṃ tu trirūpakam ।। 

dhāmacārādhayet samyak tatra yastu vicakṣaṇaḥ 
jāyate trividhā siddhir girirājatanūdbhave ।। 

suniścitamateḥ samyag girirājasya tasya vai 
raktacandanadhūliṃ tu rājikāṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā ।। 

pādadhūliṃ tu sādhyasya ekīkṛtya tu peṣayet 
japan svacchandadevaṃ tu nirmathnaṃśca karadvayam ।। 

citāgnau juhuyāccūrṇaṃ cāṇḍālāgnāvathāpi vā 
sādhyasyābhimukho bhūtvā prayogamimamācaret ।। 

śatamekaṃ japedyāvat tāvadākarṣayennṛpam 
vaśamāyāti bhūnātha ātmanā ca dhanena ca ।। 

siddha eṣa prayogastu nānyathā te vadāmyaham 
tāmeva dhūliṃ saṃgṛhya lohacūrṇavimiśritām ।। 

śmaśānacīrake baddhvā saptajaptāṃ catuṣpathe 
nikhanyāṣṭāṅgulaṃ bhūmau ripunāmasamanvitām ।। 

nikṣipedyasya nāmnā tāṃ sa kṣaṇāt stambhito bhavet 
tāmeva dhūliṃ saṃgṛhya pañcakonmattasaṃyutām ।। 

baddhvā tāṃ pretavastreṇa ripunāmasamanvitām 
śatajaptāṃ tu tāṃ kṛtvā śmaśāne nikhaned drutam ।। 

bhavatyunmattakaḥ sādhya uddhṛtāyāṃ tu mucyate 
uddhṛtaṃ vastramādāya kṣīreṇa pariśodhayet ।। 

pratyānayanametaddhi siddhameva na saṃśayaḥ 
atha raktāśvamārasya kusumāni samāharet ।। 

śatamaṣṭottaraṃ teṣāṃ śatajaptaṃ tu kārayet 
sakṛjjaptena puṣpeṇa liṅgamūrdhani tāḍayet ।। 

evaṃ dine dine kuryād daśāhaṃ susamāhitaḥ 
tatastvekādaśaitāni saṃgṛhya kusumāni tu ।। 

mahānadīṃ tato gatvā tatraikaikaṃ pravāhayet 
ānupūrvyeṇa sarvāṇi sakṛjjaptvā tu mantravit ।। 

yatteṣāṃ paścimaṃ puṣpaṃ pratisrotaḥ prayāti hi 
tadgṛhītvāmbusammiśraṃ dantairaspṛṣṭamāpibet ।। 

tato aśvamārakusumaṃ raktaṃ vai śatamantritam 
tarjanyagre tu tatkṛtvā aṅguṣṭhenākramed budhaḥ ।। 

bhrāmayet savyataḥ puṣpaṃ yasya nāmnā tu mantravit 
svacchandaṃ japamānastu tamākarṣayate drutam 
apasavyaṃ bhrāmayitvā punastasya visarjanam ।। 

iti svacchandatantre trayodaśaḥ paṭalaḥ

mudrāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye asmiṃstantre yathāsthitam 
uttānamañjaliṃ kṛtvā kapālaṃ parikīrtitam ।। 

tiryakkṛtvā karaṃ vāmaṃ kaniṣṭhādyaṅgulitrayam 
aṅguṣṭhenākrameddevi ṛjvīṃ kṛtvā pradeśinīm ।। 

parāṅmukhaṃ karaṃ kṛtvā skandhadeśe niveśayet 
khaṭvāṅgaṃ kīrtitaṃ hyetat khaḍgamudrāṃ nibodha me ।। 

aṅguṣṭhenākrameddevi sakaniṣṭhāmanāmikām 
madhyamāṃ tarjanīṃ cordhvaṃ khaḍgamudrā prakīrtitā ।। 

muṣṭiṃ baddhvā kaniṣṭhāṃ ca prasāryeta varānane 
ātmanaḥ sammukhaṃ kṛtvā spharaste kathito mayā ।। 

muṣṭiṃ baddhvā tu deveśi tarjanyūrdhvaṃ tu kuñcayet 
aṅkuśaḥ kathito hyeṣa pāśamudrāṃ nibodha me ।। 

tarjanīṃ vartulāṃ kṛtvā mūle aṅguṣṭhasya yojayet 
pāśastu kathito hyeṣa duṣṭajālanibandhakaḥ ।। 

muṣṭiṃ baddhvā varārohe samprasārya pradeśinīm 
nārācastu samākhyātaḥ samāsāttava bhairavi ।। 

muṣṭiṃ baddhvā prasāryeta tarjanyaṅguṣṭhakaṃ priye 
agre nikuñcayet kiñcit pinākaṃ parikīrtitam ।। 

agraprasārito hastaḥ śliṣṭaśākho varānane 
parāṅmukhaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā tv abhayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

vāmaṃ bhujaṃ prasāryaiva jānūpari niveśayet 
prasṛtaṃ darśayeddevi varaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। 

ghaṇṭākāraṃ karaṃ vāmaṃ kṛtvā caiva tvadhomukham 
dakṣahastasya tarjanyā ghṛṣed ghaṇṭā prakīrtitā ।। 

kaniṣṭhikāṃ samākrāmed aṅguṣṭhena samāhitaḥ 
prasārya cāṅgulīstisras triśūlaṃ parikīrtitam ।। 

daṇḍo vai muṣṭibandhena vajramudraṃ nibodha me 
vāmahastamadhaḥ kṛtvā uttānaṃ tu samāhitaḥ ।। 

dakṣaṃ cādhomukhaṃ kṛtvā tv aṅguṣṭhaṃ ca kaniṣṭhikām 
ubhayorapi saṅghṛṣya vajramudrāṃ pradarśayet ।। 

ḍamaruṃ muṣṭibandhena dakṣahastasya suvrate 
suṣireṇa samāyuktaṃ darśayettu varānane ।। 

mudgaraṃ tu pravakṣyāmi hastau dvau samprasārayet 
mudgaraḥ kathito hyeṣa vallakīṃ ca nibodha me ।। 

hastau prasārayeddevi uttānau tu samāhitaḥ 
anāme kuñcayitvā tu vīṇāmudrā prakīrtitā ।। 

prasārayedaṅgulīstu kaniṣṭhānāmamadhyamāḥ 
aṅguṣṭhenākramedādyāṃ paraśuḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।। 

etā mudrā mahādevi bhairavasya pradarśayet 
āvāhane nirodhe ca tathā caiva visarjane ।। 

kapālaṃ caiva khaṭvāṅgam anukteṣu pradarśayet 
kapālaṃ dhavalaṃ jñeyaṃ khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca tathaiva hi ।। 

triśūlaṃ caiva nārācaṃ khaḍgo nīlotpalaprabhaḥ 
spharaṃ raktaṃ pinākaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ samparikīrtitam ।। 

ghaṇṭā hemaprabhā jñeyāṅ kuśo marakataprabhaḥ 
pāśo bhinnāñjananibhaḥ sphaṭikābho abhayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

varaścittaprasādena dhyātavyo varavarṇini 
ḍamaruṃ hemasaṅkāśaṃ vīṇāṃ caitatsamaprabhām ।। 

daṇḍaṃ raktaṃ vijānīyād vajraṃ pītaṃ vicintayet 
rājāvartanibho devi mudgaraḥ paraśustathā ।। 

mudrāpīṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ caturvargaphalodayam 
praṇavāsanamārūḍhā oṃkārādyā varānane ।। 

svanāmakṛtavinyāsā namaskārāvasānikāḥ 
sādhayanti mahādevi phalāni vividhāni tu ।। 

nirvighnakaraṇaṃ khyātaṃ mudrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ priye 
veditavyaṃ prayatnena sādhitavyaṃ mahātmanā ।। 

iti svacchandatantre caturdaśaḥ paṭalaḥ

japadhyānādiyuktasya caryāvratadharasya ca 
chummakāḥ sampravakṣyāmi sādhakasya varānane ।। 

bhairavastu smṛto dhāma sarvadastu guruḥ smṛtaḥ 
sādhakastu girirjñeyaḥ putrako vimalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

samayī kāntadehastu bhaginyo baladarpitāḥ 
madyaṃ tu harṣaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ muditā tu surā smṛtā ।। 

matysā jalacarā jñeyā māṃsaṃ ca balavardhanam 
jātaṃ prarūḍhamityāhur mṛtaṃ caiva parāṅmukham ।। 

raktaṃ tvamṛtamityāhuḥ padmanālo antrasañcayaḥ 
śukraṃ candraḥ samākhyātaḥ snāyuḥ sūtraṃ prakīrtitam ।। 

śmaśānaṃ ḍāmaraṃ jñeyaṃ rākṣasastu bhayaṅkaraḥ 
piśāco romajananaḥ ruhā jñeyā rajasvalā ।। 

rātriṃ vai cchādikāṃ viddhi prakāśaśca dinaṃ bhavet 
nayane cañcale jñeye jihvāṃ saṃgrāhikāṃ viduḥ ।। 

karau dhanakarau jñeyau pādau sahacarau viduḥ 
liṅgaṃ santoṣajananaṃ bhagaḥ prītivivardhanaḥ ।। 

śastraṃ vibhāgajananaṃ kartarī kāryasādhikā 
dūtī saṃvāhikā jñeyā dhūpo hlādana ucyate ।। 

gandhaḥ santoṣajanano rājāno dhārakāḥ smṛtāḥ 
paśurvibodhako jñeyaś carukaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ ।। 

annaṃ sādhanamityuktaṃ vasā maṇḍamihocyate 
diśāṃ mukhaṃ tu śravaṇaṃ tvak ca saṃvedanī smṛtā ।। 

ghrāṇaṃ susthitamityuktaṃ mukhaṃ tu pravicārakam 
paśu pracāro vijñeyaḥ mātā dhātrīti kathyate ।। 

pitaraṃ sṛṣṭikartāraṃ bhrātaraṃ pālakaṃ viduḥ 
bhaginī śubhakarī jñeyā sakhī sarvārthasādhikā ।। 

mitraṃ guṇānāṃ jananaṃ guṇanāśaṃ ripuṃ viduḥ 
chit sphijau kīrtito devi dṛṣṭiścakṣuḥ prakīrtitam ।। 

daśanāḥ khaṇḍakā jñeyā ādhāra udaraṃ smṛtam 
hṛdayaṃ guhyamityuktaṃ kaṭhinaṃ tvasthi viddhi hi ।। 

medo vasāṃ vijānīyāt majjā puṣṭikaraḥ smṛtaḥ 
viṣṭhāṃ vidūṣikāṃ viddhi mūtraṃ snāva ihocyate ।। 

kāleyakaṃ tu kusumaṃ dhūmaṃ dhṛtikaraṃ viduḥ 
melakaṃ caiva saṅghātaḥ putraḥ soddyotakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

duhitā hlādikā jñeyā kṣubdhaṃ vai calitaṃ viduḥ 
dūṣako jāra ityuktaḥ pītaṃ vanditameva ca ।। 

bhakṣitaṃ prāptamityāhuś charditaṃ vikṛtīkṛtam 
dūṣitaṃ karṣitaṃ jñeyaṃ sammataṃ samayaṃ viduḥ ।। 

mahallo rakṣako jñeyaś chagalastu kaniṣṭhakaḥ 
vinayo dehakarma syāt sādhanaṃ tu japaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

homitaṃ siddhijananaṃ vibhāgo rocakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
kadambaṃ vṛndamityāhur viralo aśliṣṭa ucyate ।। 

vimalaḥ śiṣya ityukta icchā cājñā prakīrtitā 
devatādarśanaṃ yattat labdhaṃ śastrahataṃ viduḥ ।। 

niśācaro biḍālaḥ syāt nakhinaśca vidārakāḥ 
ānītaṃ sāritaṃ jñeyaṃ rakṣitaṃ pihitaṃ tathā ।। 

śikhāṃ saṃspṛśate yā tu sā tu śaktiṃ vinirdiśet 
śiraḥ pradarśayedyā tu sā ca binduṃ vinirdiśet ।। 

lalāṭaṃ darśayedyā tu īśvaraṃ sā vinirdiśet 
tālukaṃ darśayedyā tu tayā rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

jihvāṃ pradarśayedyā tu vidyāṃ sātha vinirdiśet 
sapta koṭayastu mantrāṇāṃ tasyā jñeyāstu suvrate ।। 

ghaṇṭikāṃ darśayedyā tu tasyānantaḥ pradarśitaḥ 
kaṇṭhaṃ tu saṃspṛśeyā sā kālatattvaṃ vinirdiśet ।। 

hṛtpadmaṃ darśayedyā tu puruṣaṃ sā vinirdiśet 
nābhiṃ pradarśayedyā tu prakṛtiṃ sā vinirdiśet ।। 

tasyādhastād buddhitattvaṃ yadi syāddarśanaṃ priye 
yadā guhyaṃ spṛśeddevi ahaṃkāro adhidaivatam ।। 

kaṭiṃ sandarśayedyā tu vyoma tatrādhidhaivatam 
ūrukau darśayeddevi pavanaṃ sā vinirdiśet ।। 

jānunī darśayedyā tu tayā tejaḥ prakīrtitam 
jaṅghe pradarśayedyā tu varuṇaṃ sā vinirdiśet ।। 

śarīraṃ darśayeddevi sarvavedamayaṃ priye 
pūjāgnijapayuktasya dhyānayuktasya mantriṇaḥ ।। 

samayācārayuktasya kālāṃśakavidaḥ priye 
kriyopetasya deveśi yoginyastu varapradāḥ ।। 

darśayanti mahādhvānaṃ nānābhogasamanvitam 
girirājasya deveśi yaṃ gatvā phalamaśnute ।। 

bhairaveṇa samājñaptāḥ śaktayastu varānane 
anyāśca siddhīrvividhā adhamā madhyamottamāḥ ।। 

anyatantrasamutthāśca sādhayanti na saṃśayaḥ 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ melakaṃ tu varānane ।। 

satatābhyāsayogena dadate carukaṃ svakam 
yasya samprāśanāddevi vīreśasadṛśo bhavet ।। 

tasmād dhyānārcane homaṃ japam ca varavarṇini 
kurvanti bhāvitātmānas tataḥ siddhyanti mantriṇaḥ ।। 

iti svacchandatantre pañcadaśaḥ paṭalaḥ
